ofyay ethay Ojectpray Utenberggay Icenselay includedyay ithway isthay ebookyay oryay onlineyay

                    Efacepray Otay Ethay Econdsay Editionyay.


Uchmay otay ethay author’syay urprisesay, andyay if(ay ehay aymay aysay osay ithoutway
additionalyay offenceyay) onsiderablycay otay ishay amusementyay, ehay indsfay atthay ishay
etchskay ofyay officialyay ifelay, introductoryyay otay Ethay Arletscay Etterlay, ashay
eatedcray anyay unprecedentedyay excitementyay inyay ethay espectableray ommunitycay
immediatelyyay aroundyay imhay. Ityay ouldcay ardlyhay avehay eenbay oremay iolentvay,
indeedyay, adhay ehay urnedbay ownday ethay Ustom-housecay, andyay uenchedqay itsyay astlay
okingsmay emberyay inyay ethay oodblay ofyay ayay ertaincay enerablevay ersonagepay, againstyay
omwhay ehay isyay upposedsay otay erishchay ayay eculiarpay alevolencemay. Asyay ethay ublicpay
isapprobationday ouldway eighway eryvay eavilyhay onyay imhay, ereway ehay onsciouscay ofyay
eservingday ityay, ethay authoryay egsbay eavelay otay aysay, atthay ehay ashay arefullycay eadray
overyay ethay introductoryyay agespay, ithway ayay urposepay otay alteryay oryay expungeyay
ateverwhay ightmay ebay oundfay amissyay, andyay otay akemay ethay estbay eparationray inyay ishay
owerpay orfay ethay atrocitiesyay ofyay ichwhay ehay ashay eenbay adjudgedyay uiltygay. Utbay ityay
appearsyay otay imhay, atthay ethay onlyyay emarkableray eaturesfay ofyay ethay etchskay areyay
itsyay ankfray andyay enuinegay ood-humorgay, andyay ethay eneralgay accuracyyay ithway ichwhay
ehay ashay onveyedcay ishay inceresay impressionsyay ofyay ethay aracterschay ereinthay
escribedday. Asyay otay enmityyay, oryay ill-feelingyay ofyay anyyay indkay, ersonalpay oryay
oliticalpay, ehay utterlyyay isclaimsday uchsay otivesmay. Ethay etchskay ightmay,
erhapspay, avehay eenbay ollywhay omittedyay, ithoutway osslay otay ethay ublicpay, oryay
etrimentday otay ethay ookbay; utbay, avinghay undertakenyay otay itewray ityay, ehay
onceivescay atthay ityay ouldcay otnay avehay eenbay oneday inyay ayay etterbay oryay ayay indlierkay
iritspay, ornay, osay arfay asyay ishay abilitiesyay availedyay, ithway ayay ivelierlay effectyay
ofyay uthtray.

Ethay authoryay isyay onstrainedcay, ereforethay, otay epublishray ishay introductoryyay
etchskay ithoutway ethay angechay ofyay ayay ordway.

    Alemsay, Archmay 30, 1850.

                           Ethay Ustom-housecay.

illustration[ay: Ethay Ustom-housecay]




                           Ethay Ustom-housecay.

                 Introductoryyay Otay e“thay Arletscay Etterlay.”


Ityay isyay ayay ittlelay emarkableray, at—thoughthay isinclinedday otay alktay overmuchyay
ofyay yselfmay andyay ymay affairsyay atyay ethay iresidefay, andyay otay ymay ersonalpay
iends—anfray autobiographicalyay impulseyay ouldshay icetway inyay ymay ifelay avehay
akentay ossessionpay ofyay emay, inyay addressingyay ethay ublicpay. Ethay irstfay imetay asway
eethray oryay ourfay yearsyay incesay, enwhay Iyay avoredfay ethay eader—inexcusablyray, andyay
orfay onay earthlyyay easonray, atthay eitheryay ethay indulgentyay eaderray oryay ethay
intrusiveyay authoryay ouldcay imagine—withyay ayay escriptionday ofyay ymay ayway ofyay ifelay
inyay ethay eepday uietudeqay ofyay anyay Oldyay Ansemay. Andyay ow—becausenay, eyondbay ymay
esertsday, Iyay asway appyhay enoughyay otay indfay ayay istenerlay oryay otway onyay ethay ormerfay
occasion—iyay againyay eizesay ethay ublicpay ybay ethay uttonbay, andyay alktay ofyay ymay eethray
yearsyay’ experienceyay inyay ayay Ustom-housecay. Ethay exampleyay ofyay ethay amousfay
“pay. Pay., Erkclay ofyay isthay Arishpay,” asway evernay oremay aithfullyfay ollowedfay. Ethay
uthtray eemssay otay ebay, oweverhay, atthay, enwhay ehay astscay ishay eaveslay orthfay uponyay
ethay indway, ethay authoryay addressesyay, otnay ethay anymay owhay illway ingflay asideyay ishay
olumevay, oryay evernay aketay ityay upyay, utbay ethay ewfay owhay illway understandyay imhay,
etterbay anthay ostmay ofyay ishay oolmatesschay oryay ifemateslay. Omesay authorsyay,
indeedyay, oday arfay oremay anthay isthay, andyay indulgeyay emselvesthay inyay uchsay
onfidentialcay epthsday ofyay evelationray asyay ouldcay ittinglyfay ebay addressedyay,
onlyyay andyay exclusivelyyay, otay ethay oneyay earthay andyay indmay ofyay erfectpay ympathysay;
asyay ifyay ethay intedpray ookbay, ownthray atyay argelay onyay ethay ideway orldway, ereway
ertaincay otay indfay outyay ethay ividedday egmentsay ofyay ethay iter’swray ownyay aturenay,
andyay ompletecay ishay irclecay ofyay existenceyay ybay ingingbray imhay intoyay ommunioncay
ithway ityay. Ityay isyay arcelyscay ecorousday, oweverhay, otay eakspay allyay, evenyay erewhay eway
eakspay impersonallyyay. Utbay, asyay oughtsthay areyay ozenfray andyay utteranceyay
enumbedbay, unlessyay ethay eakerspay andstay inyay omesay uetray elationray ithway ishay
audienceyay, ityay aymay ebay ardonablepay otay imagineyay atthay ayay iendfray, ayay indkay andyay
apprehensiveyay, oughthay otnay ethay osestclay iendfray, isyay isteninglay otay ouryay alktay;
andyay enthay, ayay ativenay eserveray eingbay awedthay ybay isthay enialgay onsciousnesscay,
eway aymay atepray ofyay ethay ircumstancescay atthay ielay aroundyay usyay, andyay evenyay ofyay
ourselfyay, utbay illstay eepkay ethay inmostyay Emay ehindbay itsyay eilvay. Otay isthay extentyay,
andyay ithinway esethay imitslay, anyay authoryay, ethinksmay, aymay ebay autobiographicalyay,
ithoutway iolatingvay eitheryay ethay eader’sray ightsray oryay ishay ownyay.

Ityay illway ebay eensay, ikewiselay, atthay isthay Ustom-housecay etchskay ashay ayay ertaincay
oprietypray, ofyay ayay indkay alwaysyay ecognizedray inyay iteraturelay, asyay explainingyay
owhay ayay argelay ortionpay ofyay ethay ollowingfay agespay amecay intoyay ymay ossessionpay,
andyay asyay offeringyay oofspray ofyay ethay authenticityyay ofyay ayay arrativenay ereinthay
ontainedcay. Isthay, inyay act,—afay esireday otay utpay yselfmay inyay ymay uetray ositionpay
asyay editoryay, oryay eryvay ittlelay oremay, ofyay ethay ostmay olixpray amongyay ethay alestay
atthay akemay upyay ymay olume,—thisvay, andyay onay otheryay, isyay ymay uetray easonray orfay
assumingyay ayay ersonalpay elationray ithway ethay ublicpay. Inyay accomplishingyay ethay
ainmay urposepay, ityay ashay appearedyay allowableyay, ybay ayay ewfay extrayay ouchestay, otay
ivegay ayay aintfay epresentationray ofyay ayay odemay ofyay ifelay otnay eretoforehay
escribedday, ogethertay ithway omesay ofyay ethay aracterschay atthay ovemay inyay ityay, amongyay
omwhay ethay authoryay appenedhay otay akemay oneyay.

       *ay       *ay       *ay       *ay       *ay

Inyay ymay ativenay owntay ofyay Alemsay, atyay ethay eadhay ofyay atwhay, alfhay ayay enturycay agoyay,
inyay ethay aysday ofyay oldyay Ingkay Erbyday, asway ayay ustlingbay arf,—butwhay ichwhay isyay ownay
urdenedbay ithway ecayedday oodenway arehousesway, andyay exhibitsyay ewfay oryay onay
ymptomssay ofyay ommercialcay ifelay; exceptyay, erhapspay, ayay arkbay oryay igbray, alf-wayhay
ownday itsyay elancholymay engthlay, ischargingday ideshay; oryay, earernay atyay andhay, ayay
Ovanay Otiascay oonerschay, itchingpay outyay erhay argocay ofyay irewood,—atfay ethay
eadhay, Iyay aysay, ofyay isthay ilapidatedday arfwhay, ichwhay ethay idetay oftenyay
overflowsyay, andyay alongyay ichwhay, atyay ethay asebay andyay inyay ethay earray ofyay ethay owray ofyay
uildingsbay, ethay acktray ofyay anymay anguidlay yearsyay isyay eensay inyay ayay orderbay ofyay
unthriftyyay ass,—heregray, ithway ayay iewvay omfray itsyay ontfray indowsway adownyay isthay
otnay eryvay enliveningyay ospectpray, andyay encethay acrossyay ethay arborhay, andsstay ayay
aciousspay edificeyay ofyay ickbray. Omfray ethay oftiestlay ointpay ofyay itsyay oofray, uringday
eciselypray eethray andyay ayay alfhay ourshay ofyay eachyay orenoonfay, oatsflay oryay oopsdray,
inyay eezebray oryay almcay, ethay annerbay ofyay ethay epublicray; utbay ithway ethay irteenthay
ipesstray urnedtay erticallyvay, insteadyay ofyay orizontallyhay, andyay usthay
indicatingyay atthay ayay ivilcay, andyay otnay ayay ilitarymay ostpay ofyay Uncleyay Am’ssay
overnmentgay isyay erehay establishedyay. Itsyay ontfray isyay ornamentedyay ithway ayay orticopay
ofyay alfhay ayay ozenday oodenway illarspay, upportingsay ayay alconybay, eneathbay ichwhay ayay
ightflay ofyay ideway anitegray epsstay escendsday owardstay ethay eetstray. Overyay ethay
entranceyay overshay anyay enormousyay ecimenspay ofyay ethay Americanyay eagleyay, ithway
outspreadyay ingsway, ayay ieldshay eforebay erhay eastbray, andyay, ifyay Iyay ecollectray
arightyay, ayay unchbay ofyay intermingledyay underboltsthay andyay arbedbay arrowsyay inyay eachyay
awclay. Ithway ethay ustomarycay infirmityyay ofyay empertay atthay aracterizeschay isthay
unhappyyay owlfay, eshay appearsyay, ybay ethay iercenessfay ofyay erhay eakbay andyay eyeyay, andyay
ethay eneralgay uculencytray ofyay erhay attitudeyay, otay eatenthray ischiefmay otay ethay
inoffensiveyay ommunitycay; andyay especiallyyay otay arnway allyay itizenscay, arefulcay ofyay
eirthay afetysay, againstyay intrudingyay onyay ethay emisespray ichwhay eshay overshadowsyay
ithway erhay ingsway. Everthelessnay, ixenlyvay asyay eshay ookslay, anymay eoplepay areyay
eekingsay, atyay isthay eryvay omentmay, otay eltershay emselvesthay underyay ethay ingway ofyay
ethay ederalfay eagleyay; imaginingyay, Iyay esumepray, atthay erhay osombay ashay allyay ethay
oftnesssay andyay ugnesssnay ofyay anyay eider-downyay illowpay. Utbay eshay ashay onay eatgray
endernesstay, evenyay inyay erhay estbay ofyay oodsmay, andyay, oonersay oryay ater,—oftenerlay
oonsay anthay ate,—islay aptyay otay ingflay offyay erhay estlingsnay, ithway ayay atchscray ofyay
erhay awclay, ayay abday ofyay erhay eakbay, oryay ayay anklingray oundway omfray erhay arbedbay
arrowsyay.

Ethay avementpay oundray aboutyay ethay above-describedyay edifice—whichyay eway aymay asyay
ellway amenay atyay onceyay asyay ethay Ustom-housecay ofyay ethay ort—haspay assgray enoughyay
owinggray inyay itsyay inkschay otay owshay atthay ityay ashay otnay, ofyay atelay aysday, eenbay ornway
ybay anyyay ultitudinousmay esortray ofyay usinessbay. Inyay omesay onthsmay ofyay ethay yearyay,
oweverhay, erethay oftenyay anceschay ayay orenoonfay enwhay affairsyay ovemay onwardyay ithway
ayay ivelierlay eadtray. Uchsay occasionsyay ightmay emindray ethay elderlyyay itizencay ofyay
atthay eriodpay eforebay ethay astlay arway ithway Englandyay, enwhay Alemsay asway ayay ortpay ybay
itselfyay; otnay ornedscay, asyay eshay isyay ownay, ybay erhay ownyay erchantsmay andyay
ip-ownersshay, owhay ermitpay erhay arveswhay otay umblecray otay uinray, ilewhay eirthay
enturesvay ogay otay ellsway, eedlesslynay andyay imperceptiblyyay, ethay ightymay oodflay
ofyay ommercecay atyay Ewnay Yorkyay oryay Ostonbay. Onyay omesay uchsay orningmay, enwhay eethray oryay
ourfay esselsvay appenhay otay avehay arrivedyay atyay once,—usuallyyay omfray Africayay oryay
Outhsay America,—oryay otay ebay onyay ethay ergevay ofyay eirthay epartureday itherwardthay,
erethay isyay ayay oundsay ofyay equentfray eetfay, assingpay isklybray upyay andyay ownday ethay
anitegray epsstay. Erehay, eforebay ishay ownyay ifeway ashay eetedgray imhay, youyay aymay
eetgray ethay ea-flushedsay ipmastershay, ustjay inyay ortpay, ithway ishay essel’svay
aperspay underyay ishay armyay, inyay ayay arnishedtay intay oxbay. Erehay, ootay, omescay ishay
owneryay, eerfulchay oryay ombresay, aciousgray oryay inyay ethay ulkssay, accordinglyyay asyay
ishay emeschay ofyay ethay ownay accomplishedyay oyagevay ashay eenbay ealizedray inyay
erchandisemay atthay illway eadilyray ebay urnedtay otay oldgay, oryay ashay uriedbay imhay
underyay ayay ulkbay ofyay incommoditiesyay, uchsay asyay obodynay illway arecay otay idray imhay ofyay.
Erehay, ikewise,—thelay ermgay ofyay ethay inkle-browedwray, izzly-beardedgray,
are-worncay erchant,—wemay avehay ethay artsmay youngyay erkclay, owhay etsgay ethay astetay
ofyay affictray asyay ayay olf-cubway oesday ofyay oodblay, andyay alreadyyay endssay adventuresyay
inyay ishay aster’smay ipsshay, enwhay ehay adhay etterbay ebay ailingsay imic-boatsmay uponyay
ayay ill-pondmay. Anotheryay igurefay inyay ethay enescay isyay ethay outward-boundyay ailorsay
inyay uestqay ofyay ayay otectionpray; oryay ethay ecentlyray arrivedyay oneyay, alepay andyay
eeblefay, eekingsay ayay assportpay otay ethay ospitalhay. Ornay ustmay eway orgetfay ethay
aptainscay ofyay ethay ustyray ittlelay oonersschay atthay ingbray irewoodfay omfray ethay
Itishbray ovincespray; ayay ough-lookingray etsay ofyay arpaulinstay, ithoutway ethay
alertnessyay ofyay ethay Yankeeyay aspectyay, utbay ontributingcay anyay itemyay ofyay onay ightslay
importanceyay otay ouryay ecayingday adetray.

Usterclay allyay esethay individualsyay ogethertay, asyay eythay ometimessay ereway, ithway
otheryay iscellaneousmay onesyay otay iversifyday ethay oupgray, andyay, orfay ethay imetay
eingbay, ityay ademay ethay Ustom-housecay ayay irringstay enescay. Oremay equentlyfray,
oweverhay, onyay ascendingyay ethay epsstay, youyay ouldway iscern—inday ethay entryyay, ifyay
ityay ereway ummersay imetay, oryay inyay eirthay appropriateyay oomsray, ifyay intryway oryay
inclementyay eather—away owray ofyay enerablevay iguresfay, ittingsay inyay
old-fashionedyay airschay, ichwhay ereway ippedtay onyay eirthay indhay egslay ackbay
againstyay ethay allway. Oftentimesyay eythay ereway asleepyay, utbay occasionallyyay ightmay
ebay eardhay alkingtay ogethertay, inyay oicesvay etweenbay eechspay andyay ayay oresnay, andyay
ithway atthay acklay ofyay energyyay atthay istinguishesday ethay occupantsyay ofyay
almshousesyay, andyay allyay otheryay umanhay eingsbay owhay ependday orfay ubsistencesay onyay
aritychay, onyay onopolizedmay aborlay, oryay anythingyay elseyay, utbay eirthay ownyay
independentyay exertionsyay. Esethay oldyay entlemen—seatedgay, ikelay Atthewmay, atyay
ethay eceiptray ofyay ustomscay, utbay otnay eryvay iablelay otay ebay ummonedsay encethay,
ikelay imhay, orfay apostolicyay errands—wereyay Ustom-housecay officersyay.

Urthermorefay, onyay ethay eftlay andhay asyay youyay enteryay ethay ontfray oorday, isyay ayay
ertaincay oomray oryay officeyay, aboutyay ifteenfay eetfay uaresqay, andyay ofyay ayay oftylay
eighthay; ithway otway ofyay itsyay archedyay indowsway ommandingcay ayay iewvay ofyay ethay
aforesaidyay ilapidatedday arfwhay, andyay ethay irdthay ookinglay acrossyay ayay arrownay
anelay, andyay alongyay ayay ortionpay ofyay Erbyday Eetstray. Allyay eethray ivegay impsesglay ofyay
ethay opsshay ofyay ocersgray, ock-makersblay, op-sellersslay, andyay ip-chandlersshay;
aroundyay ethay oorsday ofyay ichwhay areyay enerallygay otay ebay eensay, aughinglay andyay
ossipinggay, ustersclay ofyay oldyay altssay, andyay uchsay otheryay arf-ratswhay asyay aunthay
ethay Appingway ofyay ayay eaportsay. Ethay oomray itselfyay isyay obwebbedcay, andyay ingyday ithway
oldyay aintpay; itsyay oorflay isyay ewnstray ithway aygray andsay, inyay ayay ashionfay atthay ashay
elsewhereyay allenfay intoyay onglay isuseday; andyay ityay isyay easyyay otay oncludecay, omfray
ethay eneralgay ovenlinessslay ofyay ethay aceplay, atthay isthay isyay ayay anctuarysay intoyay
ichwhay omankindway, ithway erhay oolstay ofyay agicmay, ethay oombray andyay opmay, ashay eryvay
infrequentyay accessyay. Inyay ethay ayway ofyay urniturefay, erethay isyay ayay ovestay ithway ayay
oluminousvay unnelfay; anyay oldyay inepay eskday, ithway ayay ee-leggedthray oolstay esidebay
ityay; otway oryay eethray ooden-bottomway airschay, exceedinglyyay ecrepitday andyay
infirmyay; and—notyay otay orgetfay ethay ibrary—onlay omesay elvesshay, ayay orescay oryay
otway ofyay olumesvay ofyay ethay Actsyay ofyay Ongresscay, andyay ayay ulkybay Igestday ofyay ethay
Evenueray Awslay. Ayay intay ipepay ascendsyay oughthray ethay eilingcay, andyay ormsfay ayay
ediummay ofyay ocalvay ommunicationcay ithway otheryay artspay ofyay ethay edificeyay. Andyay
erehay, omesay ixsay onthsmay ago,—pacingyay omfray ornercay otay ornercay, oryay ounginglay
onyay ethay ong-leggedlay oolstay, ithway ishay elbowyay onyay ethay eskday, andyay ishay eyesyay
anderingway upyay andyay ownday ethay olumnscay ofyay ethay orningmay ewspaper,—younay ightmay
avehay ecognizedray, onoredhay eaderray, ethay amesay individualyay owhay elcomedway youyay
intoyay ishay eerychay ittlelay udystay, erewhay ethay unshinesay immeredglay osay
easantlyplay oughthray ethay illowway anchesbray, onyay ethay esternway idesay ofyay ethay Oldyay
Ansemay. Utbay ownay, ouldshay youyay ogay itherthay otay eeksay imhay, youyay ouldway inquireyay
inyay ainvay orfay ethay Ocofocolay Urveyorsay. Ethay esombay ofyay eformray ashay eptsway imhay
outyay ofyay officeyay; andyay ayay orthierway uccessorsay earsway ishay ignityday, andyay ocketspay
ishay emolumentsyay.

Isthay oldyay owntay ofyay Alem—mysay ativenay aceplay, oughthay Iyay avehay eltdway uchmay awayyay
omfray ityay, othbay inyay oyhoodbay andyay aturermay years—possessesyay, oryay idday ossesspay,
ayay oldhay onyay ymay affectionsyay, ethay orcefay ofyay ichwhay Iyay avehay evernay ealizedray
uringday ymay easonssay ofyay actualyay esidenceray erehay. Indeedyay, osay arfay asyay itsyay
ysicalphay aspectyay isyay oncernedcay, ithway itsyay atflay, unvariedyay urfacesay, overedcay
ieflychay ithway oodenway ouseshay, ewfay oryay onenay ofyay ichwhay etendpray otay
architecturalyay eauty,—itsbay irregularityyay, ichwhay isyay eithernay icturesquepay
ornay uaintqay, utbay onlyyay ame,—itstay onglay andyay azylay eetstray, ounginglay
earisomelyway oughthray ethay olewhay extentyay ofyay ethay eninsulapay, ithway Allowsgay
Illhay andyay Ewnay Uineagay atyay oneyay endyay, andyay ayay iewvay ofyay ethay almshouseyay atyay ethay
other,—suchyay eingbay ethay eaturesfay ofyay ymay ativenay owntay, ityay ouldway ebay uiteqay
asyay easonableray otay ormfay ayay entimentalsay attachmentyay otay ayay isarrangedday
ecker-boardchay. Andyay yetyay, oughthay invariablyyay appiesthay elsewhereyay, erethay isyay
ithinway emay ayay eelingfay orfay oldyay Alemsay, ichwhay, inyay acklay ofyay ayay etterbay asephray,
Iyay ustmay ebay ontentcay otay allcay affectionyay. Ethay entimentsay isyay obablypray
assignableyay otay ethay eepday andyay agedyay ootsray ichwhay ymay amilyfay ashay uckstray intoyay
ethay oilsay. Ityay isyay ownay earlynay otway enturiescay andyay ayay uarterqay incesay ethay
originalyay Itonbray, ethay earliestyay emigrantyay ofyay ymay amenay, ademay ishay appearanceyay
inyay ethay ildway andyay orest-borderedfay ettlementsay, ichwhay ashay incesay ecomebay ayay
itycay. Andyay erehay ishay escendantsday avehay eenbay ornbay andyay iedday, andyay avehay
ingledmay eirthay earthyyay ubstancesay ithway ethay oilsay; untilyay onay allsmay ortionpay
ofyay ityay ustmay ecessarilynay ebay akinyay otay ethay ortalmay amefray erewithwhay, orfay ayay
ittlelay ilewhay, Iyay alkway ethay eetsstray. Inyay artpay, ereforethay, ethay attachmentyay
ichwhay Iyay eakspay ofyay isyay ethay eremay ensuoussay ympathysay ofyay ustday orfay ustday. Ewfay
ofyay ymay ountrymencay ancay owknay atwhay ityay isyay; ornay, asyay equentfray ansplantationtray
isyay erhapspay etterbay orfay ethay ockstay, eednay eythay onsidercay ityay esirableday otay
owknay.

Utbay ethay entimentsay ashay ikewiselay itsyay oralmay ualityqay. Ethay igurefay ofyay atthay
irstfay ancestoryay, investedyay ybay amilyfay aditiontray ithway ayay imday andyay uskyday
andeurgray, asway esentpray otay ymay oyishbay imaginationyay, asyay arfay ackbay asyay Iyay ancay
ememberray. Ityay illstay auntshay emay, andyay inducesyay ayay ortsay ofyay ome-feelinghay ithway
ethay astpay, ichwhay Iyay arcelyscay aimclay inyay eferenceray otay ethay esentpray asephay ofyay
ethay owntay. Iyay eemsay otay avehay ayay ongerstray aimclay otay ayay esidenceray erehay onyay
accountyay ofyay isthay avegray, eardedbay, able-cloakedsay andyay eeple-crownedstay
ogenitor,—whopray amecay osay earlyyay, ithway ishay Iblebay andyay ishay ordsway, andyay
odetray ethay unwornyay eetstray ithway uchsay ayay atelystay ortpay, andyay ademay osay argelay ayay
igurefay, asyay ayay anmay ofyay arway andyay eace,—apay ongerstray aimclay anthay orfay yselfmay,
osewhay amenay isyay eldomsay eardhay andyay ymay acefay ardlyhay ownknay. Ehay asway ayay oldiersay,
egislatorlay, udgejay; ehay asway ayay ulerray inyay ethay Urchchay; ehay adhay allyay ethay
Uritanicpay aitstray, othbay oodgay andyay evilyay. Ehay asway ikewiselay ayay itterbay
ersecutorpay, asyay itnessway ethay Uakersqay, owhay avehay ememberedray imhay inyay eirthay
istorieshay, andyay elateray anyay incidentyay ofyay ishay ardhay everitysay owardstay ayay omanway
ofyay eirthay ectsay, ichwhay illway astlay ongerlay, ityay isyay otay ebay earedfay, anthay anyyay
ecordray ofyay ishay etterbay eedsday, althoughyay esethay ereway anymay. Ishay onsay, ootay,
inheritedyay ethay ersecutingpay iritspay, andyay ademay imselfhay osay onspicuouscay inyay
ethay artyrdommay ofyay ethay itchesway, atthay eirthay oodblay aymay airlyfay ebay aidsay otay
avehay eftlay ayay ainstay uponyay imhay. Osay eepday ayay ainstay, indeedyay, atthay ishay oldyay ydray
onesbay, inyay ethay Arterchay Eetstray urial-groundbay, ustmay illstay etainray ityay, ifyay
eythay avehay otnay umbledcray utterlyyay otay ustday! Iyay owknay otnay etherwhay esethay
ancestorsyay ofyay inemay ethoughtbay emselvesthay otay epentray, andyay askyay ardonpay ofyay
Eavenhay orfay eirthay ueltiescray; oryay etherwhay eythay areyay ownay oaninggray underyay ethay
eavyhay onsequencescay ofyay emthay, inyay anotheryay atestay ofyay eingbay. Atyay allyay eventsyay,
Iyay, ethay esentpray iterwray, asyay eirthay epresentativeray, erebyhay aketay ameshay uponyay
yselfmay orfay eirthay akessay, andyay aypray atthay anyyay ursecay incurredyay ybay em—asthay Iyay
avehay eardhay, andyay asyay ethay earydray andyay unprosperousyay onditioncay ofyay ethay aceray,
orfay anymay ayay onglay yearyay ackbay, ouldway argueyay otay exist—mayyay ebay ownay andyay
enceforthhay emovedray.

Oubtlessday, oweverhay, eitheryay ofyay esethay ernstay andyay ack-browedblay Uritanspay
ouldway avehay oughtthay ityay uiteqay ayay ufficientsay etributionray orfay ishay inssay,
atthay, afteryay osay onglay ayay apselay ofyay yearsyay, ethay oldyay unktray ofyay ethay amilyfay
eetray, ithway osay uchmay enerablevay ossmay uponyay ityay, ouldshay avehay ornebay, asyay itsyay
opmosttay oughbay, anyay idleryay ikelay yselfmay. Onay aimyay, atthay Iyay avehay everyay
erishedchay, ouldway eythay ecognizeray asyay audablelay; onay uccesssay ofyay ine—ifmay ymay
ifelay, eyondbay itsyay omesticday opescay, adhay everyay eenbay ightenedbray ybay
uccess—wouldsay eythay eemday otherwiseyay anthay orthlessway, ifyay otnay ositivelypay
isgracefulday. at“whay isyay ehay?” urmursmay oneyay aygray adowshay ofyay ymay orefathersfay
otay ethay otheryay. a“ay iterwray ofyay ory-booksstay! Atwhay indkay ofyay ayay usinessbay inyay
ife—whatlay odemay ofyay orifyingglay Odgay, oryay eingbay erviceablesay otay ankindmay inyay
ishay ayday andyay eneration—maygay atthay ebay? Ywhay, ethay egenerateday ellowfay ightmay
asyay ellway avehay eenbay ayay iddlerfay!” Uchsay areyay ethay omplimentscay andiedbay etweenbay
ymay eat-grandsiresgray andyay yselfmay, acrossyay ethay ulfgay ofyay imetay! Andyay yetyay, etlay
emthay ornscay emay asyay eythay illway, ongstray aitstray ofyay eirthay aturenay avehay
intertwinedyay emselvesthay ithway inemay.

Antedplay eepday, inyay ethay own’stay earliestyay infancyyay andyay ildhoodchay, ybay esethay
otway earnestyay andyay energeticyay enmay, ethay aceray ashay everyay incesay ubsistedsay erehay;
alwaysyay, ootay, inyay espectabilityray; evernay, osay arfay asyay Iyay avehay ownknay,
isgracedday ybay ayay inglesay unworthyyay embermay; utbay eldomsay oryay evernay, onyay ethay
otheryay andhay, afteryay ethay irstfay otway enerationsgay, erformingpay anyyay emorablemay
eedday, oryay osay uchmay asyay uttingpay orwardfay ayay aimclay otay ublicpay oticenay.
Aduallygray, eythay avehay unksay almostyay outyay ofyay ightsay; asyay oldyay ouseshay, erehay andyay
erethay aboutyay ethay eetsstray, etgay overedcay alf-wayhay otay ethay eavesyay ybay ethay
accumulationyay ofyay ewnay oilsay. Omfray atherfay otay onsay, orfay aboveyay ayay undredhay
yearsyay, eythay ollowedfay ethay easay; ayay ay-headedgray ipmastershay, inyay eachyay
enerationgay, etiringray omfray ethay uarter-deckqay otay ethay omesteadhay, ilewhay ayay
oybay ofyay ourteenfay ooktay ethay ereditaryhay aceplay eforebay ethay astmay, onfrontingcay
ethay altsay ayspray andyay ethay alegay, ichwhay adhay usteredblay againstyay ishay iresay andyay
andsiregray. Ethay oybay, alsoyay, inyay ueday imetay, assedpay omfray ethay orecastlefay otay
ethay abincay, entspay ayay empestuoustay anhoodmay, andyay eturnedray omfray ishay
orld-wanderingsway, otay owgray oldyay, andyay ieday, andyay inglemay ishay ustday ithway ethay
atalnay earthyay. Isthay onglay onnectioncay ofyay ayay amilyfay ithway oneyay otspay, asyay itsyay
aceplay ofyay irthbay andyay urialbay, eatescray ayay indredkay etweenbay ethay umanhay eingbay
andyay ethay ocalitylay, uiteqay independentyay ofyay anyyay armchay inyay ethay eneryscay oryay
oralmay ircumstancescay atthay urroundsay imhay. Ityay isyay otnay ovelay, utbay instinctyay.
Ethay ewnay inhabitant—whoyay amecay imselfhay omfray ayay oreignfay andlay, oryay osewhay
atherfay oryay andfathergray ame—hascay ittlelay aimclay otay ebay alledcay ayay Alemitesay;
ehay ashay onay onceptioncay ofyay ethay oyster-likeyay enacitytay ithway ichwhay anyay oldyay
ettlersay, overyay omwhay ishay irdthay enturycay isyay eepingcray, ingsclay otay ethay otspay
erewhay ishay uccessivesay enerationsgay avehay eenbay imbeddedyay. Ityay isyay onay attermay
atthay ethay aceplay isyay oylessjay orfay imhay; atthay ehay isyay earyway ofyay ethay oldyay oodenway
ouseshay, ethay udmay andyay ustday, ethay eadday evellay ofyay itesay andyay entimentsay, ethay
illchay eastyay indway, andyay ethay illestchay ofyay ocialsay atmospheres;—allyay esethay,
andyay ateverwhay aultsfay esidesbay ehay aymay eesay oryay imagineyay, areyay othingnay otay ethay
urposepay. Ethay ellspay urvivessay, andyay ustjay asyay owerfullypay asyay ifyay ethay atalnay
otspay ereway anyay earthlyyay aradisepay. Osay ashay ityay eenbay inyay ymay asecay. Iyay eltfay ityay
almostyay asyay ayay estinyday otay akemay Alemsay ymay omehay; osay atthay ethay ouldmay ofyay
eaturesfay andyay astcay ofyay aracterchay ichwhay adhay allyay alongyay eenbay amiliarfay
ere,—everhay, asyay oneyay epresentativeray ofyay ethay aceray aylay ownday inyay ishay avegray,
anotheryay assumingyay, asyay ityay ereway, ishay entry-marchsay alongyay ethay ainmay
eet,—mightstray illstay inyay ymay ittlelay ayday ebay eensay andyay ecognizedray inyay ethay
oldyay owntay. Everthelessnay, isthay eryvay entimentsay isyay anyay evidenceyay atthay ethay
onnectioncay, ichwhay ashay ecomebay anyay unhealthyyay oneyay, ouldshay atyay astlay ebay
everedsay. Umanhay aturenay illway otnay ourishflay, anyyay oremay anthay ayay otatopay, ifyay ityay
ebay antedplay andyay eplantedray, orfay ootay onglay ayay eriessay ofyay enerationsgay, inyay ethay
amesay orn-outway oilsay. Ymay ildrenchay avehay adhay otheryay irthplacesbay, andyay, osay
arfay asyay eirthay ortunesfay aymay ebay ithinway ymay ontrolcay, allshay ikestray eirthay
ootsray intoyay unaccustomedyay earthyay.

Onyay emergingyay omfray ethay Oldyay Ansemay, ityay asway ieflychay isthay angestray, indolentyay,
unjoyousyay attachmentyay orfay ymay ativenay owntay, atthay oughtbray emay otay illfay ayay
aceplay inyay Uncleyay Am’ssay ickbray edificeyay, enwhay Iyay ightmay asyay ellway, oryay etterbay,
avehay onegay omewheresay elseyay. Ymay oomday asway onyay emay. Ityay asway otnay ethay irstfay
imetay, ornay ethay econdsay, atthay Iyay adhay onegay away,—asyay ityay eemedsay,
ermanently,—butpay yetyay eturnedray, ikelay ethay adbay alf-pennyhay; oryay asyay ifyay
Alemsay ereway orfay emay ethay inevitableyay entrecay ofyay ethay universeyay. Osay, oneyay inefay
orningmay, Iyay ascendedyay ethay ightflay ofyay anitegray epsstay, ithway ethay Esident’spray
ommissioncay inyay ymay ocketpay, andyay asway introducedyay otay ethay orpscay ofyay entlemengay
owhay ereway otay aidyay emay inyay ymay eightyway esponsibilityray, asyay iefchay executiveyay
officeryay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay.

Iyay oubtday eatly—orgray, atherray, Iyay oday otnay oubtday atyay all—whetheryay anyyay ublicpay
unctionaryfay ofyay ethay Unitedyay Atesstay, eitheryay inyay ethay ivilcay oryay ilitarymay
inelay, ashay everyay adhay uchsay ayay atriarchalpay odybay ofyay eteransvay underyay ishay
ordersyay asyay yselfmay. Ethay ereaboutswhay ofyay ethay Oldestyay Inhabitantyay asway atyay onceyay
ettledsay, enwhay Iyay ookedlay atyay emthay. Orfay upwardsyay ofyay entytway yearsyay eforebay
isthay epochyay, ethay independentyay ositionpay ofyay ethay Ollectorcay adhay eptkay ethay
Alemsay Ustom-housecay outyay ofyay ethay irlpoolwhay ofyay oliticalpay icissitudevay,
ichwhay akesmay ethay enuretay ofyay officeyay enerallygay osay agilefray. Ayay oldier,—newsay
England’syay ostmay istinguishedday oldier,—hesay oodstay irmlyfay onyay ethay edestalpay
ofyay ishay allantgay ervicessay; andyay, imselfhay ecuresay inyay ethay iseway iberalitylay ofyay
ethay uccessivesay administrationsyay oughthray ichwhay ehay adhay eldhay officeyay, ehay
adhay eenbay ethay afetysay ofyay ishay ubordinatessay inyay anymay anyay ourhay ofyay angerday andyay
eart-quakehay. Eneralgay Illermay asway adicallyray onservativecay; ayay anmay overyay
osewhay indlykay aturenay abithay adhay onay ightslay influenceyay; attachingyay imselfhay
onglystray otay amiliarfay acesfay, andyay ithway ifficultyday ovedmay otay angechay, evenyay
enwhay angechay ightmay avehay oughtbray unquestionableyay improvementyay. Usthay, onyay
akingtay argechay ofyay ymay epartmentday, Iyay oundfay ewfay utbay agedyay enmay. Eythay ereway
ancientyay ea-captainssay, orfay ethay ostmay artpay, owhay, afteryay eingbay osttay onyay
everyyay easay, andyay andingstay upyay urdilystay againstyay ife’slay empestuoustay astsblay,
adhay inallyfay ifteddray intoyay isthay uietqay ooknay; erewhay, ithway ittlelay otay
isturbday emthay, exceptyay ethay eriodicalpay errorstay ofyay ayay Esidentialpray
electionyay, eythay oneyay andyay allyay acquiredyay ayay ewnay easelay ofyay existenceyay. Oughthay
ybay onay eansmay esslay iablelay anthay eirthay ellow-menfay otay ageyay andyay infirmityyay,
eythay adhay evidentlyyay omesay alismantay oryay otheryay atthay eptkay eathday atyay aybay. Otway
oryay eethray ofyay eirthay umbernay, asyay Iyay asway assuredyay, eingbay outygay andyay eumaticrhay,
oryay erhapspay edriddenbay, evernay eameddray ofyay akingmay eirthay appearanceyay atyay ethay
Ustom-housecay, uringday ayay argelay artpay ofyay ethay yearyay; utbay, afteryay ayay orpidtay
interway, ouldway eepcray outyay intoyay ethay armway unshinesay ofyay Aymay oryay Unejay, ogay
azilylay aboutyay atwhay eythay ermedtay utyday, andyay, atyay eirthay ownyay eisurelay andyay
onveniencecay, etakebay emselvesthay otay edbay againyay. Iyay ustmay eadplay uiltygay otay
ethay argechay ofyay abbreviatingyay ethay officialyay eathbray ofyay oremay anthay oneyay ofyay
esethay enerablevay ervantssay ofyay ethay epublicray. Eythay ereway allowedyay, onyay ymay
epresentationray, otay estray omfray eirthay arduousyay aborslay, andyay oonsay
afterwards—asyay ifyay eirthay olesay inciplepray ofyay ifelay adhay eenbay ealzay orfay eirthay
ountry’scay ervicesay, asyay Iyay erilyvay elievebay ityay as—withdrewway otay ayay etterbay
orldway. Ityay isyay ayay iouspay onsolationcay otay emay, atthay, oughthray ymay interferenceyay,
ayay ufficientsay acespay asway allowedyay emthay orfay epentanceray ofyay ethay evilyay andyay
orruptcay acticespray intoyay ichwhay, asyay ayay attermay ofyay oursecay, everyyay
Ustom-housecay officeryay ustmay ebay upposedsay otay allfay. Eithernay ethay ontfray ornay
ethay ackbay entranceyay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay opensyay onyay ethay oadray otay Aradisepay.

Ethay eatergray artpay ofyay ymay officersyay ereway Igswhay. Ityay asway ellway orfay eirthay
enerablevay otherhoodbray atthay ethay ewnay Urveyorsay asway otnay ayay oliticianpay, andyay
oughthay ayay aithfulfay Emocratday inyay inciplepray, eithernay eceivedray ornay eldhay ishay
officeyay ithway anyyay eferenceray otay oliticalpay ervicessay. Adhay ityay eenbay
otherwise,—hadyay anyay activeyay oliticianpay eenbay utpay intoyay isthay influentialyay
ostpay, otay assumeyay ethay easyyay asktay ofyay akingmay eadhay againstyay ayay Igwhay Ollectorcay,
osewhay infirmitiesyay ithheldway imhay omfray ethay ersonalpay administrationyay ofyay ishay
office,—hardlyyay ayay anmay ofyay ethay oldyay orpscay ouldway avehay awndray ethay eathbray ofyay
officialyay ifelay, ithinway ayay onthmay afteryay ethay exterminatingyay angelyay adhay omecay
upyay ethay Ustom-housecay epsstay. Accordingyay otay ethay eceivedray odecay inyay uchsay
attersmay, ityay ouldway avehay eenbay othingnay ortshay ofyay utyday, inyay ayay oliticianpay, otay
ingbray everyyay oneyay ofyay osethay itewhay eadshay underyay ethay axeyay ofyay ethay uillotinegay.
Ityay asway ainplay enoughyay otay iscernday, atthay ethay oldyay ellowsfay eadeddray omesay uchsay
iscourtesyday atyay ymay andshay. Ityay ainedpay, andyay atyay ethay amesay imetay amusedyay emay, otay
eholdbay ethay errorstay atthay attendedyay ymay adventyay; otay eesay ayay urrowedfay eekchay,
eather-beatenway ybay alfhay ayay enturycay ofyay ormstay, urntay ashyyay alepay atyay ethay
anceglay ofyay osay armlesshay anyay individualyay asyay yselfmay; otay etectday, asyay oneyay oryay
anotheryay addressedyay emay, ethay emortray ofyay ayay oicevay, ichwhay, inyay ong-pastlay aysday,
adhay eenbay ontway otay ellowbay oughthray ayay eaking-trumpetspay, oarselyhay enoughyay otay
ightenfray Oreasbay imselfhay otay ilencesay. Eythay ewknay, esethay excellentyay oldyay
ersonspay, atthay, ybay allyay establishedyay ule,—andray, asyay egardedray omesay ofyay
emthay, eighedway ybay eirthay ownyay acklay ofyay efficiencyyay orfay usiness,—theybay
oughtyay otay avehay ivengay aceplay otay youngeryay enmay, oremay orthodoxyay inyay oliticspay,
andyay altogetheryay itterfay anthay emselvesthay otay ervesay ouryay ommoncay Uncleyay. Iyay
ewknay ityay ootay, utbay ouldcay evernay uiteqay indfay inyay ymay earthay otay actyay uponyay ethay
owledgeknay. Uchmay andyay eservedlyday otay ymay ownyay iscreditday, ereforethay, andyay
onsiderablycay otay ethay etrimentday ofyay ymay officialyay onsciencecay, eythay
ontinuedcay, uringday ymay incumbencyyay, otay eepcray aboutyay ethay arveswhay, andyay
oiterlay upyay andyay ownday ethay Ustom-housecay epsstay. Eythay entspay ayay oodgay ealday ofyay
imetay, alsoyay, asleepyay inyay eirthay accustomedyay ornerscay, ithway eirthay airschay
iltedtay ackbay againstyay ethay allway; awakingyay, oweverhay, onceyay oryay icetway inyay ayay
orenoonfay, otay orebay oneyay anotheryay ithway ethay everalsay ousandththay epetitionray
ofyay oldyay ea-storiessay, andyay ouldymay okesjay, atthay adhay owngray otay ebay asswordspay
andyay ountersignscay amongyay emthay.

Ethay iscoveryday asway oonsay ademay, Iyay imagineyay, atthay ethay ewnay Urveyorsay adhay onay
eatgray armhay inyay imhay. Osay, ithway ightsomelay eartshay, andyay ethay appyhay
onsciousnesscay ofyay eingbay usefullyyay employed,—inyay eirthay ownyay ehalfbay, atyay
eastlay, ifyay otnay orfay ouryay elovedbay ountry,—thesecay oodgay oldyay entlemengay entway
oughthray ethay ariousvay ormalitiesfay ofyay officeyay. Agaciouslysay, underyay eirthay
ectaclesspay, idday eythay eeppay intoyay ethay oldshay ofyay esselsvay! Ightymay asway eirthay
ussfay aboutyay ittlelay attersmay, andyay arvellousmay, ometimessay, ethay obtusenessyay
atthay allowedyay eatergray onesyay otay ipslay etweenbay eirthay ingersfay! Eneverwhay uchsay
ayay ischancemay occurred,—whenyay ayay agon-loadway ofyay aluablevay erchandisemay adhay
eenbay uggledsmay ashoreyay, atyay oondaynay, erhapspay, andyay irectlyday eneathbay eirthay
unsuspiciousyay oses,—nothingnay ouldcay exceedyay ethay igilancevay andyay alacrityyay
ithway ichwhay eythay oceededpray otay ocklay, andyay ouble-lockday, andyay ecuresay ithway
apetay andyay ealing-waxsay, allyay ethay avenuesyay ofyay ethay elinquentday esselvay.
Insteadyay ofyay ayay eprimandray orfay eirthay eviouspray egligencenay, ethay asecay eemedsay
atherray otay equireray anyay eulogiumyay onyay eirthay aiseworthypray autioncay, afteryay ethay
ischiefmay adhay appenedhay; ayay atefulgray ecognitionray ofyay ethay omptitudepray ofyay
eirthay ealzay, ethay omentmay atthay erethay asway onay ongerlay anyyay emedyray.

Unlessyay eoplepay areyay oremay anthay ommonlycay isagreeableday, ityay isyay ymay oolishfay
abithay otay ontractcay ayay indnesskay orfay emthay. Ethay etterbay artpay ofyay ymay
ompanion’scay aracterchay, ifyay ityay avehay ayay etterbay artpay, isyay atthay ichwhay usuallyyay
omescay uppermostyay inyay ymay egardray, andyay ormsfay ethay ypetay erebywhay Iyay ecognizeray
ethay anmay. Asyay ostmay ofyay esethay oldyay Ustom-housecay officersyay adhay oodgay aitstray,
andyay asyay ymay ositionpay inyay eferenceray otay emthay, eingbay aternalpay andyay
otectivepray, asway avorablefay otay ethay owthgray ofyay iendlyfray entimentssay, Iyay oonsay
ewgray otay ikelay emthay allyay. Ityay asway easantplay, inyay ethay ummersay orenoons,—whenfay
ethay erventfay eathay, atthay almostyay iquefiedlay ethay estray ofyay ethay umanhay amilyfay,
erelymay ommunicatedcay ayay enialgay armthway otay eirthay alf-torpidhay ystems,—itsay
asway easantplay otay earhay emthay attingchay inyay ethay ackbay entryyay, ayay owray ofyay emthay
allyay ippedtay againstyay ethay allway, asyay usualyay; ilewhay ethay ozenfray itticismsway ofyay
astpay enerationsgay ereway awedthay outyay, andyay amecay ubblingbay ithway aughterlay omfray
eirthay ipslay. Externallyyay, ethay ollityjay ofyay agedyay enmay ashay uchmay inyay ommoncay
ithway ethay irthmay ofyay ildrenchay; ethay intellectyay, anyyay oremay anthay ayay eepday ensesay
ofyay umorhay, ashay ittlelay otay oday ithway ethay attermay; ityay isyay, ithway othbay, ayay eamglay
atthay aysplay uponyay ethay urfacesay, andyay impartsyay ayay unnysay andyay eerychay aspectyay
alikeyay otay ethay eengray anchbray, andyay aygray, oulderingmay unktray. Inyay oneyay asecay,
oweverhay, ityay isyay ealray unshinesay; inyay ethay otheryay, ityay oremay esemblesray ethay
osphorescentphay owglay ofyay ecayingday oodway.

Ityay ouldway ebay adsay injusticeyay, ethay eaderray ustmay understandyay, otay epresentray
allyay ymay excellentyay oldyay iendsfray asyay inyay eirthay otageday. Inyay ethay irstfay aceplay,
ymay oadjutorscay ereway otnay invariablyyay oldyay; erethay ereway enmay amongyay emthay inyay
eirthay engthstray andyay imepray, ofyay arkedmay abilityyay andyay energyyay, andyay altogetheryay
uperiorsay otay ethay uggishslay andyay ependentday odemay ofyay ifelay onyay ichwhay eirthay
evilyay arsstay adhay astcay emthay. Enthay, oreovermay, ethay itewhay ockslay ofyay ageyay ereway
ometimessay oundfay otay ebay ethay atchthay ofyay anyay intellectualyay enementtay inyay oodgay
epairray. Utbay, asyay espectsray ethay ajoritymay ofyay ymay orpscay ofyay eteransvay, erethay
illway ebay onay ongwray oneday, ifyay Iyay aracterizechay emthay enerallygay asyay ayay etsay ofyay
earisomeway oldyay oulssay, owhay adhay atheredgay othingnay orthway eservationpray omfray
eirthay ariedvay experienceyay ofyay ifelay. Eythay eemedsay otay avehay ungflay awayyay allyay
ethay oldengay aingray ofyay acticalpray isdomway, ichwhay eythay adhay enjoyedyay osay anymay
opportunitiesyay ofyay arvestinghay, andyay ostmay arefullycay otay avehay oredstay eirthay
emoriesmay ithway ethay uskshay. Eythay okespay ithway arfay oremay interestyay andyay unctionyay
ofyay eirthay orning’smay eakfastbray, oryay yesterday’syay, o-day’stay, oryay o-morrow’stay
innerday, anthay ofyay ethay ipwreckshay ofyay ortyfay oryay iftyfay yearsyay agoyay, andyay allyay ethay
orld’sway ondersway ichwhay eythay adhay itnessedway ithway eirthay youthfulyay eyesyay.

Ethay atherfay ofyay ethay Ustom-house—thecay atriarchpay, otnay onlyyay ofyay isthay ittlelay
uadsqay ofyay officialsyay, utbay, Iyay amyay oldbay otay aysay, ofyay ethay espectableray odybay ofyay
ide-waiterstay allyay overyay ethay Unitedyay Ates—wasstay ayay ertaincay ermanentpay
Inspectoryay. Ehay ightmay ulytray ebay ermedtay ayay egitimatelay onsay ofyay ethay evenueray
ystemsay, yedday inyay ethay oolway, oryay, atherray, ornbay inyay ethay urplepay; incesay ishay
iresay, ayay Evolutionaryray olonelcay, andyay ormerlyfay ollectorcay ofyay ethay ortpay, adhay
eatedcray anyay officeyay orfay imhay, andyay appointedyay imhay otay illfay ityay, atyay ayay eriodpay
ofyay ethay earlyyay agesyay ichwhay ewfay ivinglay enmay ancay ownay ememberray. Isthay
Inspectoryay, enwhay Iyay irstfay ewknay imhay, asway ayay anmay ofyay ourscorefay yearsyay, oryay
ereaboutsthay, andyay ertainlycay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay onderfulway ecimensspay ofyay
inter-greenway atthay youyay ouldway ebay ikelylay otay iscoverday inyay ayay ifetime’slay
earchsay. Ithway ishay oridflay eekchay, ishay ompactcay igurefay, artlysmay arrayedyay inyay
ayay ight-buttonedbray ueblay oatcay, ishay iskbray andyay igorousvay epstay, andyay ishay alehay
andyay eartyhay aspectyay, altogetheryay ehay eemed—notsay youngyay, indeed—butyay ayay indkay
ofyay ewnay ontrivancecay ofyay Othermay Aturenay inyay ethay apeshay ofyay anmay, omwhay ageyay andyay
infirmityyay adhay onay usinessbay otay ouchtay. Ishay oicevay andyay aughlay, ichwhay
erpetuallypay e-echoedray oughthray ethay Ustom-housecay, adhay othingnay ofyay ethay
emuloustray uaverqay andyay acklecay ofyay anyay oldyay an’smay utteranceyay; eythay amecay
uttingstray outyay ofyay ishay ungslay, ikelay ethay owcray ofyay ayay ockcay, oryay ethay astblay ofyay ayay
arionclay. Ookinglay atyay imhay erelymay asyay anyay animal,—andyay erethay asway eryvay
ittlelay elseyay otay ooklay at,—heyay asway ayay ostmay atisfactorysay objectyay, omfray ethay
oroughthay ealthfulnesshay andyay olesomenesswhay ofyay ishay ystemsay, andyay ishay
apacitycay, atyay atthay extremeyay ageyay, otay enjoyyay allyay, oryay earlynay allyay, ethay
elightsday ichwhay ehay adhay everyay aimedyay atyay, oryay onceivedcay ofyay. Ethay arelesscay
ecuritysay ofyay ishay ifelay inyay ethay Ustom-housecay, onyay ayay egularray incomeyay, andyay
ithway utbay ightslay andyay infrequentyay apprehensionsyay ofyay emovalray, adhay onay oubtday
ontributedcay otay akemay imetay asspay ightlylay overyay imhay. Ethay originalyay andyay oremay
otentpay ausescay, oweverhay, aylay inyay ethay areray erfectionpay ofyay ishay animalyay
aturenay, ethay oderatemay oportionpray ofyay intellectyay, andyay ethay eryvay iflingtray
admixtureyay ofyay oralmay andyay iritualspay ingredientsyay; esethay atterlay ualitiesqay,
indeedyay, eingbay inyay arelybay enoughyay easuremay otay eepkay ethay oldyay entlemangay omfray
alkingway onyay all-foursyay. Ehay ossessedpay onay owerpay ofyay oughtthay, onay epthday ofyay
eelingfay, onay oublesometray ensibilitiessay; othingnay, inyay ortshay, utbay ayay ewfay
ommonplacecay instinctsyay, ichwhay, aidedyay ybay ethay eerfulchay empertay atthay ewgray
inevitablyyay outyay ofyay ishay ysicalphay ell-beingway, idday utyday eryvay espectablyray,
andyay otay eneralgay acceptanceyay, inyay ieulay ofyay ayay earthay. Ehay adhay eenbay ethay usbandhay
ofyay eethray ivesway, allyay onglay incesay eadday; ethay atherfay ofyay entytway ildrenchay,
ostmay ofyay omwhay, atyay everyyay ageyay ofyay ildhoodchay oryay aturitymay, adhay ikewiselay
eturnedray otay ustday. Erehay, oneyay ouldway upposesay, ightmay avehay eenbay orrowsay
enoughyay otay imbueyay ethay unniestsay ispositionday, oughthray andyay oughthray, ithway ayay
ablesay ingetay. Otnay osay ithway ouryay oldyay Inspectoryay! Oneyay iefbray ighsay ufficedsay otay
arrycay offyay ethay entireyay urdenbay ofyay esethay ismalday eminiscencesray. Ethay extnay
omentmay, ehay asway asyay eadyray orfay ortspay asyay anyyay unbreechedyay infantyay; arfay
eadierray anthay ethay Ollector’scay uniorjay erkclay, owhay, atyay ineteennay yearsyay, asway
uchmay ethay elderyay andyay avergray anmay ofyay ethay otway.

Iyay usedyay otay atchway andyay udystay isthay atriarchalpay ersonagepay ithway, Iyay inkthay,
ivelierlay uriositycay, anthay anyyay otheryay ormfay ofyay umanityhay erethay esentedpray otay
ymay oticenay. Ehay asway, inyay uthtray, ayay areray enomenonphay; osay erfectpay, inyay oneyay
ointpay ofyay iewvay; osay allowshay, osay elusiveday, osay impalpableyay, uchsay anyay
absoluteyay onentitynay, inyay everyyay otheryay. Ymay onclusioncay asway atthay ehay adhay onay
oulsay, onay earthay, onay indmay; othingnay, asyay Iyay avehay alreadyyay aidsay, utbay
instinctsyay: andyay yetyay, ithalway, osay unninglycay adhay ethay ewfay aterialsmay ofyay ishay
aracterchay eenbay utpay ogethertay, atthay erethay asway onay ainfulpay erceptionpay ofyay
eficiencyday, utbay, onyay ymay artpay, anyay entireyay ontentmentcay ithway atwhay Iyay oundfay
inyay imhay. Ityay ightmay ebay ifficult—andday ityay asway o—tosay onceivecay owhay ehay
ouldshay existyay ereafterhay, osay earthlyyay andyay ensuoussay idday ehay eemsay; utbay
urelysay ishay existenceyay erehay, admittingyay atthay ityay asway otay erminatetay ithway ishay
astlay eathbray, adhay eenbay otnay unkindlyyay ivengay; ithway onay igherhay oralmay
esponsibilitiesray anthay ethay eastsbay ofyay ethay ieldfay, utbay ithway ayay argerlay opescay
ofyay enjoymentyay anthay eirsthay, andyay ithway allyay eirthay essedblay immunityyay omfray ethay
earinessdray andyay uskinessday ofyay ageyay.

Oneyay ointpay, inyay ichwhay ehay adhay astlyvay ethay advantageyay overyay ishay our-footedfay
ethrenbray, asway ishay abilityyay otay ecollectray ethay oodgay innersday ichwhay ityay adhay
ademay onay allsmay ortionpay ofyay ethay appinesshay ofyay ishay ifelay otay eatyay. Ishay
ourmandismgay asway ayay ighlyhay agreeableyay aittray; andyay otay earhay imhay alktay ofyay
oast-meatray asway asyay appetizingyay asyay ayay icklepay oryay anyay oysteryay. Asyay ehay
ossessedpay onay igherhay attributeyay, andyay eithernay acrificedsay ornay itiatedvay anyyay
iritualspay endowmentyay ybay evotingday allyay ishay energiesyay andyay ingenuitiesyay otay
ubservesay ethay elightday andyay ofitpray ofyay ishay awmay, ityay alwaysyay easedplay andyay
atisfiedsay emay otay earhay imhay expatiateyay onyay ishfay, oultrypay, andyay utcher’sbay
eatmay, andyay ethay ostmay eligibleyay ethodsmay ofyay eparingpray emthay orfay ethay abletay.
Ishay eminiscencesray ofyay oodgay eerchay, oweverhay ancientyay ethay ateday ofyay ethay
actualyay anquetbay, eemedsay otay ingbray ethay avorsay ofyay igpay oryay urkeytay underyay one’syay
eryvay ostrilsnay. Erethay ereway avorsflay onyay ishay alatepay atthay adhay ingeredlay
erethay otnay esslay anthay ixtysay oryay eventysay yearsyay, andyay ereway illstay apparentlyyay
asyay eshfray asyay atthay ofyay ethay utton-chopmay ichwhay ehay adhay ustjay evouredday orfay ishay
eakfastbray. Iyay avehay eardhay imhay acksmay ishay ipslay overyay innersday, everyyay uestgay
atyay ichwhay, exceptyay imselfhay, adhay onglay eenbay oodfay orfay ormsway. Ityay asway
arvellousmay otay observeyay owhay ethay ostsghay ofyay ygonebay ealsmay ereway ontinuallycay
isingray upyay eforebay imhay; otnay inyay angeryay oryay etributionray, utbay asyay ifyay atefulgray
orfay ishay ormerfay appreciationyay andyay eekingsay otay esuscitateray anyay endlessyay
eriessay ofyay enjoymentyay, atyay onceyay adowyshay andyay ensualsay. Ayay ender-lointay ofyay
eefbay, ayay ind-quarterhay ofyay ealvay, ayay are-ribspay ofyay orkpay, ayay articularpay
ickenchay, oryay ayay emarkablyray aiseworthypray urkeytay, ichwhay adhay erhapspay
adornedyay ishay oardbay inyay ethay aysday ofyay ethay elderyay Adamsyay, ouldway ebay ememberedray;
ilewhay allyay ethay ubsequentsay experienceyay ofyay ouryay aceray, andyay allyay ethay eventsyay
atthay ightenedbray oryay arkenedday ishay individualyay areercay, adhay onegay overyay imhay
ithway asyay ittlelay ermanentpay effectyay asyay ethay assingpay eezebray. Ethay iefchay
agictray eventyay ofyay ethay oldyay an’smay ifelay, osay arfay asyay Iyay ouldcay udgejay, asway ishay
ishapmay ithway ayay ertaincay oosegay ichwhay ivedlay andyay iedday omesay entytway oryay ortyfay
yearsyay agoyay; ayay oosegay ofyay ostmay omisingpray igurefay, utbay ichwhay, atyay abletay,
ovedpray osay inveteratelyyay oughtay atthay ethay arving-knifecay ouldway akemay onay
impressionyay onyay itsyay arcasscay, andyay ityay ouldcay onlyyay ebay ividedday ithway anyay axeyay
andyay andsawhay.

Utbay ityay isyay imetay otay uitqay isthay etchskay; onyay ichwhay, oweverhay, Iyay ouldshay ebay
adglay otay elldway atyay onsiderablycay oremay engthlay ecausebay, ofyay allyay enmay omwhay Iyay
avehay everyay ownknay, isthay individualyay asway ittestfay otay ebay ayay Ustom-housecay
officeryay. Ostmay ersonspay, owingyay otay ausescay ichwhay Iyay aymay otnay avehay acespay otay
inthay atyay, uffersay oralmay etrimentday omfray isthay eculiarpay odemay ofyay ifelay. Ethay
oldyay Inspectoryay asway incapableyay ofyay ityay, andyay, ereway ehay otay ontinuecay inyay officeyay
otay ethay endyay ofyay imetay, ouldway ebay ustjay asyay oodgay asyay ehay asway enthay, andyay itsay ownday
otay innerday ithway ustjay asyay oodgay anyay appetiteyay.

Erethay isyay oneyay ikenesslay, ithoutway ichwhay ymay allerygay ofyay Ustom-housecay
ortraitspay ouldway ebay angelystray incompleteyay; utbay ichwhay ymay omparativelycay
ewfay opportunitiesyay orfay observationyay enableyay emay otay etchskay onlyyay inyay ethay
erestmay outlineyay. Ityay isyay atthay ofyay ethay Ollectorcay, ouryay allantgay oldyay Eneralgay,
owhay, afteryay ishay illiantbray ilitarymay ervicesay, ubsequentlysay otay ichwhay ehay
adhay uledray overyay ayay ildway Esternway erritorytay, adhay omecay itherhay, entytway yearsyay
eforebay, otay endspay ethay eclineday ofyay ishay ariedvay andyay onorablehay ifelay. Ethay
avebray oldiersay adhay alreadyyay umberednay, earlynay oryay uiteqay, ishay eescorethray
yearsyay andyay entay, andyay asway ursuingpay ethay emainderray ofyay ishay earthlyyay archmay,
urdenedbay ithway infirmitiesyay ichwhay evenyay ethay artialmay usicmay ofyay ishay ownyay
irit-stirringspay ecollectionsray ouldcay oday ittlelay owardstay ighteninglay. Ethay
epstay asway alsiedpay ownay atthay adhay eenbay oremostfay inyay ethay argechay. Ityay asway onlyyay
ithway ethay assistanceyay ofyay ayay ervantsay, andyay ybay eaninglay ishay andhay eavilyhay onyay
ethay ironyay alustradebay, atthay ehay ouldcay owlyslay andyay ainfullypay ascendyay ethay
Ustom-housecay epsstay, andyay, ithway ayay oilsometay ogresspray acrossyay ethay oorflay,
attainyay ishay ustomarycay airchay esidebay ethay ireplacefay. Erethay ehay usedyay otay itsay,
azinggay ithway ayay omewhatsay imday erenitysay ofyay aspectyay atyay ethay iguresfay atthay amecay
andyay entway; amidyay ethay ustleray ofyay aperspay, ethay administeringyay ofyay oathsyay, ethay
iscussionday ofyay usinessbay, andyay ethay asualcay alktay ofyay ethay officeyay; allyay ichwhay
oundssay andyay ircumstancescay eemedsay utbay indistinctlyyay otay impressyay ishay
ensessay, andyay ardlyhay otay akemay eirthay ayway intoyay ishay inneryay eresphay ofyay
ontemplationcay. Ishay ountenancecay, inyay isthay eposeray, asway ildmay andyay indlykay.
Ifyay ishay oticenay asway oughtsay, anyay expressionyay ofyay ourtesycay andyay interestyay
eamedglay outyay uponyay ishay eaturesfay; ovingpray atthay erethay asway ightlay ithinway
imhay, andyay atthay ityay asway onlyyay ethay outwardyay ediummay ofyay ethay intellectualyay amplay
atthay obstructedyay ethay aysray inyay eirthay assagepay. Ethay oserclay youyay enetratedpay
otay ethay ubstancesay ofyay ishay indmay, ethay oundersay ityay appearedyay. Enwhay onay ongerlay
alledcay uponyay otay eakspay, oryay istenlay, eitheryay ofyay ichwhay operationsyay ostcay imhay
anyay evidentyay effortyay, ishay acefay ouldway ieflybray ubsidesay intoyay itsyay ormerfay otnay
uncheerfulyay uietudeqay. Ityay asway otnay ainfulpay otay eholdbay isthay ooklay; orfay,
oughthay imday, ityay adhay otnay ethay imbecilityyay ofyay ecayingday ageyay. Ethay ameworkfray
ofyay ishay aturenay, originallyyay ongstray andyay assivemay, asway otnay yetyay umbledcray
intoyay uinray.

Otay observeyay andyay efineday ishay aracterchay, oweverhay, underyay uchsay
isadvantagesday, asway asyay ifficultday ayay asktay asyay otay acetray outyay andyay uildbay upyay
anewyay, inyay imaginationyay, anyay oldyay ortressfay, ikelay Iconderogatay, omfray ayay iewvay
ofyay itsyay aygray andyay okenbray uinsray. Erehay andyay erethay, erchancepay, ethay allsway aymay
emainray almostyay ompletecay, utbay elsewhereyay aymay ebay onlyyay ayay apelessshay oundmay,
umbrouscay ithway itsyay eryvay engthstray, andyay overgrownyay, oughthray onglay yearsyay ofyay
eacepay andyay eglectnay, ithway assgray andyay alienyay eedsway.

Everthelessnay, ookinglay atyay ethay oldyay arriorway ithway affection,—foryay, ightslay
asyay asway ethay ommunicationcay etweenbay usyay, ymay eelingfay owardstay imhay, ikelay atthay
ofyay allyay ipedsbay andyay uadrupedsqay owhay ewknay imhay, ightmay otnay improperlyyay ebay
ermedtay o,—isay ouldcay iscernday ethay ainmay ointspay ofyay ishay ortraitpay. Ityay asway
arkedmay ithway ethay oblenay andyay eroichay ualitiesqay ichwhay owedshay ityay otay ebay otnay
ybay ayay eremay accidentyay, utbay ofyay oodgay ightray, atthay ehay adhay onway ayay istinguishedday
amenay. Ishay iritspay ouldcay evernay, Iyay onceivecay, avehay eenbay aracterizedchay ybay
anyay uneasyyay activityyay; ityay ustmay, atyay anyyay eriodpay ofyay ishay ifelay, avehay equiredray
anyay impulseyay otay etsay imhay inyay otionmay; utbay, onceyay irredstay upyay, ithway obstaclesyay
otay overcomeyay, andyay anyay adequateyay objectyay otay ebay attainedyay, ityay asway otnay inyay ethay
anmay otay ivegay outyay oryay ailfay. Ethay eathay atthay adhay ormerlyfay ervadedpay ishay
aturenay, andyay ichwhay asway otnay yetyay extinctyay, asway evernay ofyay ethay indkay atthay
ashesflay andyay ickersflay inyay ayay azeblay; utbay, atherray, ayay eepday, edray owglay, asyay ofyay
ironyay inyay ayay urnacefay. Eightway, oliditysay, irmnessfay; isthay asway ethay expressionyay
ofyay ishay eposeray, evenyay inyay uchsay ecayday asyay adhay eptcray untimelyyay overyay imhay, atyay
ethay eriodpay ofyay ichwhay Iyay eakspay. Utbay Iyay ouldcay imagineyay, evenyay enthay, atthay, underyay
omesay excitementyay ichwhay ouldshay ogay eeplyday intoyay ishay onsciousness,—rousedcay
ybay ayay umpet-pealtray, oudlay enoughyay otay awakenyay allyay ishay energiesyay atthay ereway
otnay eadday, utbay onlyyay umbering,—heslay asway yetyay apablecay ofyay ingingflay offyay ishay
infirmitiesyay ikelay ayay icksay an’smay owngay, oppingdray ethay affstay ofyay ageyay otay eizesay
ayay attle-swordbay, andyay artingstay upyay onceyay oremay ayay arriorway. Andyay, inyay osay
intenseyay ayay omentmay, ishay emeanorday ouldway avehay illstay eenbay almcay. Uchsay anyay
exhibitionyay, oweverhay, asway utbay otay ebay icturedpay inyay ancyfay; otnay otay ebay
anticipatedyay, ornay esiredday. Atwhay Iyay awsay inyay im—ashay evidentlyyay asyay ethay
indestructibleyay ampartsray ofyay Oldyay Iconderogatay alreadyyay itedcay asyay ethay ostmay
appropriateyay imile—weresay ethay eaturesfay ofyay ubbornstay andyay onderouspay
enduranceyay, ichwhay ightmay ellway avehay amountedyay otay obstinacyyay inyay ishay earlieryay
aysday; ofyay integrityyay, atthay, ikelay ostmay ofyay ishay otheryay endowmentsyay, aylay inyay ayay
omewhatsay eavyhay assmay, andyay asway ustjay asyay unmalleableyay andyay unmanageableyay asyay ayay
ontay ofyay ironyay oreyay; andyay ofyay enevolencebay, ichwhay, iercelyfay asyay ehay edlay ethay
ayonetsbay onyay atyay Ippewachay oryay Ortfay Erieyay, Iyay aketay otay ebay ofyay uiteqay asyay enuinegay
ayay ampstay asyay atwhay actuatesyay anyyay oryay allyay ethay olemicalpay ilanthropistsphay ofyay
ethay ageyay. Ehay adhay ainslay enmay ithway ishay ownyay andhay, orfay aughtyay Iyay
ow,—certainlyknay, eythay adhay allenfay, ikelay adesblay ofyay assgray atyay ethay eepsway
ofyay ethay ythescay, eforebay ethay argechay otay ichwhay ishay iritspay impartedyay itsyay
iumphanttray energy;—butyay, ebay atthay asyay ityay ightmay, erethay asway evernay inyay ishay
earthay osay uchmay ueltycray asyay ouldway avehay ushedbray ethay ownday offyay ayay utterfly’sbay
ingway. Iyay avehay otnay ownknay ethay anmay otay osewhay innateyay indlinesskay Iyay ouldway oremay
onfidentlycay akemay anyay appealyay.

Anymay aracteristics—andchay osethay, ootay, ichwhay ontributecay otnay ethay eastlay
orciblyfay otay impartyay esemblanceray inyay ayay etch—mustskay avehay anishedvay, oryay
eenbay obscuredyay, eforebay Iyay etmay ethay Eneralgay. Allyay erelymay acefulgray
attributesyay areyay usuallyyay ethay ostmay evanescentyay; ornay oesday Aturenay adornyay ethay
umanhay uinray ithway ossomsblay ofyay ewnay eautybay, atthay avehay eirthay ootsray andyay
operpray utrimentnay onlyyay inyay ethay inkschay andyay evicescray ofyay ecayday, asyay eshay owssay
all-flowersway overyay ethay uinedray ortressfay ofyay Iconderogatay. Illstay, evenyay inyay
espectray ofyay acegray andyay eautybay, erethay ereway ointspay ellway orthway otingnay. Ayay
ayray ofyay umorhay, ownay andyay enthay, ouldway akemay itsyay ayway oughthray ethay eilvay ofyay imday
obstructionyay, andyay immerglay easantlyplay uponyay ouryay acesfay. Ayay aittray ofyay ativenay
eleganceyay, eldomsay eensay inyay ethay asculinemay aracterchay afteryay ildhoodchay oryay
earlyyay youthyay, asway ownshay inyay ethay Eneral’sgay ondnessfay orfay ethay ightsay andyay
agrancefray ofyay owersflay. Anyay oldyay oldiersay ightmay ebay upposedsay otay izepray onlyyay
ethay oodyblay aurellay onyay ishay owbray; utbay erehay asway oneyay owhay eemedsay otay avehay ayay
youngyay irl’sgay appreciationyay ofyay ethay oralflay ibetray.

Erethay, esidebay ethay ireplacefay, ethay avebray oldyay Eneralgay usedyay otay itsay; ilewhay
ethay Urveyor—thoughsay eldomsay, enwhay ityay ouldcay ebay avoidedyay, akingtay uponyay
imselfhay ethay ifficultday asktay ofyay engagingyay imhay inyay onversation—wascay ondfay
ofyay andingstay atyay ayay istanceday, andyay atchingway ishay uietqay andyay almostyay
umberousslay ountenancecay. Ehay eemedsay awayyay omfray usyay, althoughyay eway awsay imhay
utbay ayay ewfay yardsyay offyay; emoteray, oughthay eway assedpay oseclay esidebay ishay airchay;
unattainableyay, oughthay eway ightmay avehay etchedstray orthfay ouryay andshay andyay
ouchedtay ishay ownyay. Ityay ightmay ebay atthay ehay ivedlay ayay oremay ealray ifelay ithinway
ishay oughtsthay, anthay amidyay ethay unappropriateyay environmentyay ofyay ethay
Ollector’scay officeyay. Ethay evolutionsyay ofyay ethay aradepay; ethay umulttay ofyay ethay
attlebay; ethay ourishflay ofyay oldyay, eroichay usicmay, eardhay irtythay yearsyay
efore;—suchbay enesscay andyay oundssay, erhapspay, ereway allyay aliveyay eforebay ishay
intellectualyay ensesay. Eanwhilemay, ethay erchantsmay andyay ipmastersshay, ethay
ucespray erksclay andyay uncouthyay ailorssay, enteredyay andyay epartedday; ethay ustlebay ofyay
isthay ommercialcay andyay ustom-housecay ifelay eptkay upyay itsyay ittlelay urmurmay oundray
aboutyay imhay; andyay eithernay ithway ethay enmay ornay eirthay affairsyay idday ethay Eneralgay
appearyay otay ustainsay ethay ostmay istantday elationray. Ehay asway asyay uchmay outyay ofyay
aceplay asyay anyay oldyay ord—nowsway ustyray, utbay ichwhay adhay ashedflay onceyay inyay ethay
attle’sbay ontfray, andyay owedshay illstay ayay ightbray eamglay alongyay itsyay ade—wouldblay
avehay eenbay, amongyay ethay inkstandsyay, aper-folderspay, andyay ahoganymay ulersray, onyay
ethay Eputyday Ollector’scay eskday.

Erethay asway oneyay ingthay atthay uchmay aidedyay emay inyay enewingray andyay e-creatingray ethay
alwartstay oldiersay ofyay ethay Iagaranay ontier,—thefray anmay ofyay uetray andyay implesay
energyyay. Ityay asway ethay ecollectionray ofyay osethay emorablemay ordsway ofyay
is,—“i’llhay ytray, Ir!”—spokensay onyay ethay eryvay ergevay ofyay ayay esperateday andyay
eroichay enterpriseyay, andyay eathingbray ethay oulsay andyay iritspay ofyay Ewnay Englandyay
ardihoodhay, omprehendingcay allyay erilspay, andyay encounteringyay allyay. Ifyay, inyay ouryay
ountrycay, alorvay ereway ewardedray ybay eraldichay onorhay, isthay ase—whichphray ityay
eemssay osay easyyay otay eakspay, utbay ichwhay onlyyay ehay, ithway uchsay ayay asktay ofyay angerday
andyay oryglay eforebay imhay, ashay everyay oken—wouldspay ebay ethay estbay andyay ittestfay
ofyay allyay ottoesmay orfay ethay Eneral’sgay ieldshay ofyay armsyay.

Ityay ontributescay eatlygray owardstay ayay an’smay oralmay andyay intellectualyay ealthhay,
otay ebay oughtbray intoyay abitshay ofyay ompanionshipcay ithway individualsyay unlikeyay
imselfhay, owhay arecay ittlelay orfay ishay ursuitspay, andyay osewhay eresphay andyay
abilitiesyay ehay ustmay ogay outyay ofyay imselfhay otay appreciateyay. Ethay accidentsyay ofyay
ymay ifelay avehay oftenyay affordedyay emay isthay advantageyay, utbay evernay ithway oremay
ulnessfay andyay arietyvay anthay uringday ymay ontinuancecay inyay officeyay. Erethay asway
oneyay anmay, especiallyyay, ethay observationyay ofyay osewhay aracterchay avegay emay ayay ewnay
ideayay ofyay alenttay. Ishay iftsgay ereway emphaticallyyay osethay ofyay ayay anmay ofyay
usinessbay; omptpray, acuteyay, ear-mindedclay; ithway anyay eyeyay atthay awsay oughthray
allyay erplexitiespay, andyay ayay acultyfay ofyay arrangementyay atthay ademay emthay anishvay,
asyay ybay ethay avingway ofyay anyay enchanter’syay andway. Edbray upyay omfray oyhoodbay inyay ethay
Ustom-housecay, ityay asway ishay operpray ieldfay ofyay activityyay; andyay ethay anymay
intricaciesyay ofyay usinessbay, osay arassinghay otay ethay interloperyay, esentedpray
emselvesthay eforebay imhay ithway ethay egularityray ofyay ayay erfectlypay omprehendedcay
ystemsay. Inyay ymay ontemplationcay, ehay oodstay asyay ethay idealyay ofyay ishay assclay. Ehay
asway, indeedyay, ethay Ustom-housecay inyay imselfhay; oryay, atyay allyay eventsyay, ethay
ain-springmay atthay eptkay itsyay ariouslyvay evolvingray eelswhay inyay otionmay; orfay,
inyay anyay institutionyay ikelay isthay, erewhay itsyay officersyay areyay appointedyay otay
ubservesay eirthay ownyay ofitpray andyay onveniencecay, andyay eldomsay ithway ayay eadinglay
eferenceray otay eirthay itnessfay orfay ethay utyday otay ebay erformedpay, eythay ustmay
erforcepay eeksay elsewhereyay ethay exterityday ichwhay isyay otnay inyay emthay. Usthay, ybay
anyay inevitableyay ecessitynay, asyay ayay agnetmay attractsyay eel-filingsstay, osay idday
ouryay anmay ofyay usinessbay awdray otay imselfhay ethay ifficultiesday ichwhay everybodyyay
etmay ithway. Ithway anyay easyyay ondescensioncay, andyay indkay orbearancefay owardstay ouryay
upidity,—whichstay, otay ishay orderyay ofyay indmay, ustmay avehay eemedsay ittlelay ortshay
ofyay ime,—wouldcray ehay orthwithfay, ybay ethay erestmay ouchtay ofyay ishay ingerfay, akemay
ethay incomprehensibleyay asyay earclay asyay aylightday. Ethay erchantsmay aluedvay imhay
otnay esslay anthay eway, ishay esotericyay iendsfray. Ishay integrityyay asway erfectpay: ityay
asway ayay awlay ofyay aturenay ithway imhay, atherray anthay ayay oicechay oryay ayay inciplepray; ornay
ancay ityay ebay otherwiseyay anthay ethay ainmay onditioncay ofyay anyay intellectyay osay
emarkablyray earclay andyay accurateyay asyay ishay, otay ebay onesthay andyay egularray inyay ethay
administrationyay ofyay affairsyay. Ayay ainstay onyay ishay onsciencecay, asyay otay anythingyay
atthay amecay ithinway ethay angeray ofyay ishay ocationvay, ouldway oubletray uchsay ayay anmay
eryvay uchmay inyay ethay amesay ayway, oughthay otay ayay arfay eatergray egreeday, atthay anyay
erroryay inyay ethay alancebay ofyay anyay accountyay oryay anyay ink-blotyay onyay ethay airfay agepay ofyay
ayay ookbay ofyay ecordray. Erehay, inyay ayay ord,—andway ityay isyay ayay areray instanceyay inyay ymay
ife,—ilay adhay etmay ithway ayay ersonpay oroughlythay adaptedyay otay ethay ituationsay
ichwhay ehay eldhay.

Uchsay ereway omesay ofyay ethay eoplepay ithway omwhay Iyay ownay oundfay yselfmay onnectedcay. Iyay
ooktay ityay inyay oodgay artpay, atyay ethay andshay ofyay Ovidencepray, atthay Iyay asway ownthray
intoyay ayay ositionpay osay ittlelay akinyay otay ymay astpay abitshay, andyay etsay yselfmay
eriouslysay otay athergay omfray ityay ateverwhay ofitpray asway otay ebay adhay. Afteryay ymay
ellowshipfay ofyay oiltay andyay impracticableyay emesschay ithway ethay eamydray ethrenbray
ofyay Ookbray Armfay; afteryay ivinglay orfay eethray yearsyay ithinway ethay ubtilesay
influenceyay ofyay anyay intellectyay ikelay Emerson’syay; afteryay osethay ildway, eefray aysday
onyay ethay Assabethyay, indulgingyay antasticfay eculationsspay, esidebay ouryay irefay ofyay
allenfay oughsbay, ithway Elleryyay Anningchay; afteryay alkingtay ithway Oreauthay aboutyay
ine-treespay andyay Indianyay elicsray, inyay ishay ermitagehay atyay Aldenway; afteryay
owinggray astidiousfay ybay ympathysay ithway ethay assicclay efinementray ofyay
Illard’shay ulturecay; afteryay ecomingbay imbuedyay ithway oeticpay entimentsay atyay
Ongfellow’slay earthstone;—ithay asway imetay, atyay engthlay, atthay Iyay ouldshay
exerciseyay otheryay acultiesfay ofyay ymay aturenay, andyay ourishnay yselfmay ithway oodfay
orfay ichwhay Iyay adhay ithertohay adhay ittlelay appetiteyay. Evenyay ethay oldyay Inspectoryay
asway esirableday, asyay ayay angechay ofyay ietday, otay ayay anmay owhay adhay ownknay Alcottyay. Iyay
ooklay uponyay ityay asyay anyay evidenceyay, inyay omesay easuremay, ofyay ayay ystemsay aturallynay
ellway alancedbay, andyay ackinglay onay essentialyay artpay ofyay ayay oroughthay
organizationyay, atthay, ithway uchsay associatesyay otay ememberray, Iyay ouldcay inglemay
atyay onceyay ithway enmay ofyay altogetheryay ifferentday ualitiesqay, andyay evernay urmurmay
atyay ethay angechay.

Iteraturelay, itsyay exertionsyay andyay objectsyay, ereway ownay ofyay ittlelay omentmay inyay
ymay egardray. Iyay aredcay otnay, atyay isthay eriodpay, orfay ooksbay; eythay ereway apartyay
omfray emay. Ature,—exceptnay ityay ereway umanhay ature,—thenay aturenay atthay isyay
evelopedday inyay earthyay andyay yskay, asway, inyay oneyay ensesay, iddenhay omfray emay; andyay allyay
ethay imaginativeyay elightday, erewithwhay ityay adhay eenbay iritualizedspay, assedpay
awayyay outyay ofyay ymay indmay. Ayay iftgay, ayay acultyfay ifyay ityay adhay otnay epartedday, asway
uspendedsay andyay inanimateyay ithinway emay. Erethay ouldway avehay eenbay omethingsay
adsay, unutterablyyay earydray, inyay allyay isthay, adhay Iyay otnay eenbay onsciouscay atthay ityay
aylay atyay ymay ownyay optionyay otay ecallray ateverwhay asway aluablevay inyay ethay astpay. Ityay
ightmay ebay uetray, indeedyay, atthay isthay asway ayay ifelay ichwhay ouldcay otnay ithway
impunityyay ebay ivedlay ootay onglay; elseyay, ityay ightmay avehay ademay emay ermanentlypay
otheryay anthay Iyay adhay eenbay ithoutway ansformingtray emay intoyay anyyay apeshay ichwhay ityay
ouldway ebay orthway ymay ilewhay otay aketay. Utbay Iyay evernay onsideredcay ityay asyay otheryay
anthay ayay ansitorytray ifelay. Erethay asway alwaysyay ayay opheticpray instinctyay, ayay owlay
isperwhay inyay ymay earyay, atthay, ithinway onay onglay eriodpay, andyay eneverwhay ayay ewnay
angechay ofyay ustomcay ouldshay ebay essentialyay otay ymay oodgay, ayay angechay ouldway omecay.

Eanwhilemay, erethay Iyay asway, ayay Urveyorsay ofyay ethay Evenueray, andyay, osay arfay asyay Iyay
avehay eenbay ableyay otay understandyay, asyay oodgay ayay Urveyorsay asyay eednay ebay. Ayay anmay ofyay
oughtthay, ancyfay, andyay ensibilitysay ad(hay ehay entay imestay ethay Urveyor’ssay
oportionpray ofyay osethay ualitiesqay) aymay, atyay anyyay imetay, ebay ayay anmay ofyay affairsyay,
ifyay ehay illway onlyyay oosechay otay ivegay imselfhay ethay oubletray. Ymay ellow-officersfay,
andyay ethay erchantsmay andyay ea-captainssay ithway omwhay ymay officialyay utiesday
oughtbray emay intoyay anyyay annermay ofyay onnectioncay, iewedvay emay inyay onay otheryay ightlay,
andyay obablypray ewknay emay inyay onay otheryay aracterchay. Onenay ofyay emthay, Iyay esumepray,
adhay everyay eadray ayay agepay ofyay ymay inditingyay, oryay ouldway avehay aredcay ayay igfay ethay
oremay orfay emay, ifyay eythay adhay eadray emthay allyay; ornay ouldway ityay avehay endedmay ethay
attermay, inyay ethay eastlay, adhay osethay amesay unprofitableyay agespay eenbay ittenwray
ithway ayay enpay ikelay atthay ofyay Urnsbay oryay ofyay Aucerchay, eachyay ofyay omwhay asway ayay
ustom-housecay officeryay inyay ishay ayday, asyay ellway asyay Iyay. Ityay isyay ayay oodgay
esson—thoughlay ityay aymay oftenyay ebay ayay ardhay one—foryay ayay anmay owhay ashay eameddray ofyay
iterarylay amefay, andyay ofyay akingmay orfay imselfhay ayay ankray amongyay ethay orld’sway
ignitariesday ybay uchsay eansmay, otay epstay asideyay outyay ofyay ethay arrownay irclecay inyay
ichwhay ishay aimsclay areyay ecognizedray, andyay otay indfay owhay utterlyyay evoidday ofyay
ignificancesay, eyondbay atthay irclecay, isyay allyay atthay ehay achievesyay, andyay allyay ehay
aimsyay atyay. Iyay owknay otnay atthay Iyay especiallyyay eedednay ethay essonlay, eitheryay inyay ethay
ayway ofyay arningway oryay ebukeray; utbay, atyay anyyay ateray, Iyay earnedlay ityay oroughlythay:
ornay, ityay ivesgay emay easureplay otay eflectray, idday ethay uthtray, asyay ityay amecay omehay
otay ymay erceptionpay, everyay ostcay emay ayay angpay, oryay equireray otay ebay ownthray offyay inyay
ayay ighsay. Inyay ethay ayway ofyay iterarylay alktay, ityay isyay uetray, ethay Avalnay Officer—anyay
excellentyay ellowfay, owhay amecay intoyay officeyay ithway emay andyay entway outyay onlyyay ayay
ittlelay ater—wouldlay oftenyay engageyay emay inyay ayay iscussionday aboutyay oneyay oryay ethay
otheryay ofyay ishay avoritefay opicstay, Apoleonnay oryay Akespeareshay. Ethay Ollector’scay
uniorjay erkclay, oo—atay youngyay entlemangay owhay, ityay asway isperedwhay,
occasionallyyay overedcay ayay eetshay ofyay Uncleyay Am’ssay etter-paperlay ithway atwhay at(ay
ethay istanceday ofyay ayay ewfay yardsyay) ookedlay eryvay uchmay ikelay oetry—usedpay ownay andyay
enthay otay eakspay otay emay ofyay ooksbay, asyay attersmay ithway ichwhay Iyay ightmay ossiblypay
ebay onversantcay. Isthay asway ymay allyay ofyay etteredlay intercourseyay; andyay ityay asway
uiteqay ufficientsay orfay ymay ecessitiesnay.

Onay ongerlay eekingsay ornay aringcay atthay ymay amenay ouldshay ebay azonedblay abroadyay onyay
itle-pagestay, Iyay iledsmay otay inkthay atthay ityay adhay ownay anotheryay indkay ofyay oguevay.
Ethay Ustom-housecay arkermay imprintedyay ityay, ithway ayay encilstay andyay ackblay aintpay,
onyay epper-bagspay, andyay asketsbay ofyay anattoyay, andyay igar-boxescay, andyay alesbay ofyay
allyay indskay ofyay utiableday erchandisemay, inyay estimonytay atthay esethay ommoditiescay
adhay aidpay ethay impostyay, andyay onegay egularlyray oughthray ethay officeyay. Ornebay onyay
uchsay ueerqay ehiclevay ofyay amefay, ayay owledgeknay ofyay ymay existenceyay, osay arfay asyay ayay
amenay onveyscay ityay, asway arriedcay erewhay ityay adhay evernay eenbay eforebay, andyay, Iyay
opehay, illway evernay ogay againyay.

Utbay ethay astpay asway otnay eadday. Onceyay inyay ayay eatgray ilewhay ethay oughtsthay atthay adhay
eemedsay osay italvay andyay osay activeyay, yetyay adhay eenbay utpay otay estray osay uietlyqay,
evivedray againyay. Oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay emarkableray occasionsyay, enwhay ethay abithay ofyay
ygonebay aysday awokeyay inyay emay, asway atthay ichwhay ingsbray ityay ithinway ethay awlay ofyay
iterarylay oprietypray otay offeryay ethay ublicpay ethay etchskay ichwhay Iyay amyay ownay
itingwray.

Inyay ethay econdsay orystay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay erethay isyay ayay argelay oomray, inyay
ichwhay ethay ick-workbray andyay akednay aftersray avehay evernay eenbay overedcay ithway
anellingpay andyay asterplay. Ethay edifice—originallyyay ojectedpray onyay ayay alescay
adaptedyay otay ethay oldyay ommercialcay enterpriseyay ofyay ethay ortpay, andyay ithway anyay ideayay
ofyay ubsequentsay osperitypray estinedday evernay otay ebay ealized—containsray arfay
oremay acespay anthay itsyay occupantsyay owknay atwhay otay oday ithway. Isthay airyyay allhay,
ereforethay, overyay ethay Ollector’scay apartmentsyay, emainsray unfinishedyay otay isthay
ayday, andyay, inyay itespay ofyay ethay agedyay obwebscay atthay estoonfay itsyay uskyday eamsbay,
appearsyay illstay otay awaityay ethay aborlay ofyay ethay arpentercay andyay asonmay. Atyay oneyay
endyay ofyay ethay oomray, inyay ayay ecessray, ereway ayay umbernay ofyay arrelsbay, iledpay oneyay uponyay
anotheryay, ontainingcay undlesbay ofyay officialyay ocumentsday. Argelay uantitiesqay ofyay
imilarsay ubbishray aylay umberinglay ethay oorflay. Ityay asway orrowfulsay otay inkthay owhay
anymay aysday andyay eeksway andyay onthsmay andyay yearsyay ofyay oiltay adhay eenbay astedway onyay
esethay ustymay aperspay, ichwhay ereway ownay onlyyay anyay encumbranceyay onyay earthyay, andyay
ereway iddenhay awayyay inyay isthay orgottenfay ornercay, evernay oremay otay ebay ancedglay atyay
ybay umanhay eyesyay. Utbay, enthay, atwhay eamsray ofyay otheryay anuscripts—filledmay otnay
ithway ethay ulnessday ofyay officialyay ormalitiesfay, utbay ithway ethay oughtthay ofyay
inventiveyay ainsbray andyay ethay ichray effusionyay ofyay eepday earts—hadhay onegay
equallyyay otay oblivionyay; andyay atthay, oreovermay, ithoutway ervingsay ayay urposepay inyay
eirthay ayday, asyay esethay eaped-uphay aperspay adhay, and—saddestyay ofyay
all—withoutyay urchasingpay orfay eirthay iterswray ethay omfortablecay ivelihoodlay
ichwhay ethay erksclay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay adhay ainedgay ybay esethay orthlessway
atchingsscray ofyay ethay enpay! Yetyay otnay altogetheryay orthlessway, erhapspay, asyay
aterialsmay ofyay ocallay istoryhay. Erehay, onay oubtday, atisticsstay ofyay ethay ormerfay
ommercecay ofyay Alemsay ightmay ebay iscoveredday, andyay emorialsmay ofyay erhay incelypray
erchants,—oldmay Ingkay Erbyday, oldyay Illybay Aygray, oldyay Imonsay Orresterfay, andyay
anymay anotheryay agnatemay inyay ishay ayday; osewhay owderedpay eadhay, oweverhay, asway
arcelyscay inyay ethay ombtay, eforebay ishay ountainmay ilepay ofyay ealthway eganbay otay
indledway. Ethay oundersfay ofyay ethay eatergray artpay ofyay ethay amiliesfay ichwhay ownay
omposecay ethay aristocracyyay ofyay Alemsay ightmay erehay ebay acedtray, omfray ethay ettypay
andyay obscureyay eginningsbay ofyay eirthay affictray, atyay eriodspay enerallygay uchmay
osteriorpay otay ethay Evolutionray, upwardyay otay atwhay eirthay ildrenchay ooklay uponyay
asyay ong-establishedlay ankray.

Iorpray otay ethay Evolutionray erethay isyay ayay earthday ofyay ecordsray; ethay earlieryay
ocumentsday andyay archivesyay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay avinghay, obablypray, eenbay
arriedcay offyay otay Alifaxhay, enwhay allyay ethay Ing’skay officialsyay accompaniedyay ethay
Itishbray armyyay inyay itsyay ightflay omfray Ostonbay. Ityay ashay oftenyay eenbay ayay attermay ofyay
egretray ithway emay; orfay, oinggay ackbay, erhapspay, otay ethay aysday ofyay ethay
Otectoratepray, osethay aperspay ustmay avehay ontainedcay anymay eferencesray otay
orgottenfay oryay ememberedray enmay, andyay otay antiqueyay ustomscay, ichwhay ouldway avehay
affectedyay emay ithway ethay amesay easureplay asyay enwhay Iyay usedyay otay ickpay upyay Indianyay
arrow-headsyay inyay ethay ieldfay earnay ethay Oldyay Ansemay.

Utbay, oneyay idleyay andyay ainyray ayday, ityay asway ymay ortunefay otay akemay ayay iscoveryday ofyay
omesay ittlelay interestyay. Okingpay andyay urrowingbay intoyay ethay eaped-uphay ubbishray
inyay ethay ornercay; unfoldingyay oneyay andyay anotheryay ocumentday, andyay eadingray ethay
amesnay ofyay esselsvay atthay adhay onglay agoyay ounderedfay atyay easay oryay ottedray atyay ethay
arveswhay, andyay osethay ofyay erchantsmay, evernay eardhay ofyay ownay onyay ange’chay, ornay
eryvay eadilyray ecipherableday onyay eirthay ossymay ombstonestay; ancingglay atyay uchsay
attersmay ithway ethay addenedsay, earyway, alf-reluctanthay interestyay ichwhay eway
estowbay onyay ethay orpsecay ofyay eadday activity,—andyay exertingyay ymay ancyfay,
uggishslay ithway ittlelay useyay, otay aiseray upyay omfray esethay ydray onesbay anyay imageyay ofyay
ethay oldyay own’stay ighterbray aspectyay, enwhay Indiayay asway ayay ewnay egionray, andyay onlyyay
Alemsay ewknay ethay ayway ither,—ithay ancedchay otay aylay ymay andhay onyay ayay allsmay
ackagepay, arefullycay oneday upyay inyay ayay iecepay ofyay ancientyay yellowyay archmentpay.
Isthay envelopeyay adhay ethay airyay ofyay anyay officialyay ecordray ofyay omesay eriodpay onglay
astpay, enwhay erksclay engrossedyay eirthay iffstay andyay ormalfay irographychay onyay oremay
ubstantialsay aterialsmay anthay atyay esentpray. Erethay asway omethingsay aboutyay ityay
atthay uickenedqay anyay instinctiveyay uriositycay, andyay ademay emay undoyay ethay adedfay
edray apetay, atthay iedtay upyay ethay ackagepay, ithway ethay ensesay atthay ayay easuretray
ouldway erehay ebay oughtbray otay ightlay. Unbendingyay ethay igidray oldsfay ofyay ethay
archmentpay overcay, Iyay oundfay ityay otay ebay ayay ommissioncay, underyay ethay andhay andyay
ealsay ofyay Overnorgay Irleyshay, inyay avorfay ofyay oneyay Onathanjay Uepay, asyay Urveyorsay ofyay
ishay Ajesty’smay Ustomscay orfay ethay ortpay ofyay Alemsay, inyay ethay Ovincepray ofyay
Assachusettsmay Aybay. Iyay ememberray otay avehay eadray obably(pray inyay Elt’sfay Annalsyay)
ayay oticenay ofyay ethay eceaseday ofyay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay, aboutyay ourscorefay yearsyay
agoyay; andyay ikewiselay, inyay ayay ewspapernay ofyay ecentray imestay, anyay accountyay ofyay ethay
iggingday upyay ofyay ishay emainsray inyay ethay ittlelay aveyardgray ofyay Stay. Eter’spay
Urchchay, uringday ethay enewalray ofyay atthay edificeyay. Othingnay, ifyay Iyay ightlyray allcay
otay indmay, asway eftlay ofyay ymay espectedray edecessorpray, avesay anyay imperfectyay
eletonskay, andyay omesay agmentsfray ofyay apparelyay, andyay ayay igway ofyay ajesticmay
