izzlefray; ichwhay, unlikeyay ethay eadhay atthay ityay onceyay adornedyay, asway inyay eryvay
atisfactorysay eservationpray. Utbay, onyay examiningyay ethay aperspay ichwhay ethay
archmentpay ommissioncay ervedsay otay envelopyay, Iyay oundfay oremay acestray ofyay Mray.
Ue’spay entalmay artpay, andyay ethay internalyay operationsyay ofyay ishay eadhay, anthay ethay
izzledfray igway adhay ontainedcay ofyay ethay enerablevay ullskay itselfyay.

Eythay ereway ocumentsday, inyay ortshay, otnay officialyay, utbay ofyay ayay ivatepray aturenay,
oryay atyay eastlay ittenwray inyay ishay ivatepray apacitycay, andyay apparentlyyay ithway ishay
ownyay andhay. Iyay ouldcay accountyay orfay eirthay eingbay includedyay inyay ethay eaphay ofyay
Ustom-housecay umberlay onlyyay ybay ethay actfay atthay Mray. Ue’spay eathday adhay appenedhay
uddenlysay; andyay atthay esethay aperspay, ichwhay ehay obablypray eptkay inyay ishay
officialyay eskday, adhay evernay omecay otay ethay owledgeknay ofyay ishay eirshay, oryay ereway
upposedsay otay elateray otay ethay usinessbay ofyay ethay evenueray. Onyay ethay ansfertray ofyay
ethay archivesyay otay Alifaxhay, isthay ackagepay, ovingpray otay ebay ofyay onay ublicpay
oncerncay, asway eftlay ehindbay, andyay adhay emainedray everyay incesay unopenedyay.

Ethay ancientyay Urveyor—beingsay ittlelay olestedmay, Iyay upposesay, atyay atthay earlyyay
ayday, ithway usinessbay ertainingpay otay ishay office—seemsyay otay avehay evotedday
omesay ofyay ishay anymay eisurelay ourshay otay esearchesray asyay ayay ocallay antiquarianyay,
andyay otheryay inquisitionsyay ofyay ayay imilarsay aturenay. Esethay uppliedsay aterialmay
orfay ettypay activityyay otay ayay indmay atthay ouldway otherwiseyay avehay eenbay eatenyay upyay
ithway ustray. Ayay ortionpay ofyay ishay actsfay, ybay ethay ybay, idday emay oodgay ervicesay inyay
ethay eparationpray ofyay ethay articleyay entitledyay ain“may Eetstray,” includedyay inyay ethay
esentpray olumevay. Ethay emainderray aymay erhapspay ebay appliedyay otay urposespay
equallyyay aluablevay, ereafterhay; oryay otnay impossiblyyay aymay ebay orkedway upyay, osay
arfay asyay eythay ogay, intoyay ayay egularray istoryhay ofyay Alemsay, ouldshay ymay enerationvay
orfay ethay atalnay oilsay everyay impelyay emay otay osay iouspay ayay asktay. Eanwhilemay, eythay
allshay ebay atyay ethay ommandcay ofyay anyyay entlemangay, inclinedyay, andyay ompetentcay, otay
aketay ethay unprofitableyay aborlay offyay ymay andshay. Asyay ayay inalfay ispositionday, Iyay
ontemplatecay epositingday emthay ithway ethay Essexyay Istoricalhay Ocietysay.

Utbay ethay objectyay atthay ostmay ewdray ymay attentionyay, inyay ethay ysteriousmay ackagepay,
asway ayay ertaincay affairyay ofyay inefay edray othclay, uchmay ornway andyay adedfay. Erethay
ereway acestray aboutyay ityay ofyay oldgay embroideryyay, ichwhay, oweverhay, asway eatlygray
ayedfray andyay efacedday; osay atthay onenay, oryay eryvay ittlelay, ofyay ethay itterglay asway
eftlay. Ityay adhay eenbay oughtwray, asyay asway easyyay otay erceivepay, ithway onderfulway
illskay ofyay eedleworknay; andyay ethay itchstay as(ay Iyay amyay assuredyay ybay adieslay
onversantcay ithway uchsay ysteriesmay) ivesgay evidenceyay ofyay ayay ownay orgottenfay artyay,
otnay otay ebay ecoveredray evenyay ybay ethay ocesspray ofyay ickingpay outyay ethay eadsthray.
Isthay agray ofyay arletscay oth,—forclay imetay andyay earway andyay ayay acrilegioussay othmay
adhay educedray ityay otay ittlelay otheryay anthay ayay ag,—onray arefulcay examinationyay,
assumedyay ethay apeshay ofyay ayay etterlay. Ityay asway ethay apitalcay etterlay Ayay. Ybay anyay
accurateyay easurementmay, eachyay imblay ovedpray otay ebay eciselypray eethray inchesyay
andyay ayay uarterqay inyay engthlay. Ityay adhay eenbay intendedyay, erethay ouldcay ebay onay
oubtday, asyay anyay ornamentalyay articleyay ofyay essdray; utbay owhay ityay asway otay ebay ornway,
oryay atwhay ankray, onorhay, andyay ignityday, inyay y-pastbay imestay, ereway ignifiedsay ybay
ityay, asway ayay iddleray ichwhay o(say evanescentyay areyay ethay ashionsfay ofyay ethay orldway inyay
esethay articularspay) Iyay awsay ittlelay opehay ofyay olvingsay. Andyay yetyay ityay angelystray
interestedyay emay. Ymay eyesyay astenedfay emselvesthay uponyay ethay oldyay arletscay
etterlay, andyay ouldway otnay ebay urnedtay asideyay. Ertainlycay, erethay asway omesay eepday
eaningmay inyay ityay, ostmay orthyway ofyay interpretationyay, andyay ichwhay, asyay ityay ereway,
eamedstray orthfay omfray ethay ysticmay ymbolsay, ubtlysay ommunicatingcay itselfyay otay
ymay ensibilitiessay, utbay evadingyay ethay analysisyay ofyay ymay indmay.

Ilewhay usthay erplexed,—andpay ogitatingcay, amongyay otheryay ypotheseshay, etherwhay
ethay etterlay ightmay otnay avehay eenbay oneyay ofyay osethay ecorationsday ichwhay ethay
itewhay enmay usedyay otay ontrivecay, inyay orderyay otay aketay ethay eyesyay ofyay Indians,—iyay
appenedhay otay aceplay ityay onyay ymay eastbray. Ityay eemedsay otay e,—themay eaderray aymay
ilesmay, utbay ustmay otnay oubtday ymay ord,—itway eemedsay otay emay, enthay, atthay Iyay
experiencedyay ayay ensationsay otnay altogetheryay ysicalphay, yetyay almostyay osay, ofyay
urningbay eathay; andyay asyay ifyay ethay etterlay ereway otnay ofyay edray othclay, utbay ed-hotray
ironyay. Iyay udderedshay, andyay involuntarilyyay etlay ityay allfay uponyay ethay oorflay.

Inyay ethay absorbingyay ontemplationcay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay, Iyay adhay ithertohay
eglectednay otay examineyay ayay allsmay ollray ofyay ingyday aperpay, aroundyay ichwhay ityay adhay
eenbay istedtway. Isthay Iyay ownay openedyay, andyay adhay ethay atisfactionsay otay indfay,
ecordedray ybay ethay oldyay Urveyor’ssay enpay, ayay easonablyray ompletecay explanationyay
ofyay ethay olewhay affairyay. Erethay ereway everalsay oolscapfay eetsshay ontainingcay
anymay articularspay espectingray ethay ifelay andyay onversationcay ofyay oneyay Esterhay
Ynnepray, owhay appearedyay otay avehay eenbay atherray ayay oteworthynay ersonagepay inyay ethay
iewvay ofyay ouryay ancestorsyay. Eshay adhay ourishedflay uringday ethay eriodpay etweenbay
ethay earlyyay aysday ofyay Assachusettsmay andyay ethay oseclay ofyay ethay eventeenthsay
enturycay. Agedyay ersonspay, aliveyay inyay ethay imetay ofyay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay, andyay omfray
osewhay oralyay estimonytay ehay adhay ademay upyay ishay arrativenay, ememberedray erhay, inyay
eirthay youthyay, asyay ayay eryvay oldyay, utbay otnay ecrepitday omanway, ofyay ayay atelystay andyay
olemnsay aspectyay. Ityay adhay eenbay erhay abithay, omfray anyay almostyay immemorialyay ateday,
otay ogay aboutyay ethay ountrycay asyay ayay indkay ofyay oluntaryvay ursenay, andyay oingday
ateverwhay iscellaneousmay oodgay eshay ightmay; akingtay uponyay erselfhay, ikewiselay,
otay ivegay adviceyay inyay allyay attersmay, especiallyyay osethay ofyay ethay earthay; ybay ichwhay
eansmay, asyay ayay ersonpay ofyay uchsay opensitiespray inevitablyyay ustmay, eshay ainedgay
omfray anymay eoplepay ethay everenceray ueday otay anyay angelyay, utbay, Iyay ouldshay imagineyay,
asway ookedlay uponyay ybay othersyay asyay anyay intruderyay andyay ayay uisancenay. Yingpray
urtherfay intoyay ethay anuscriptmay, Iyay oundfay ethay ecordray ofyay otheryay oingsday andyay
ufferingssay ofyay isthay ingularsay omanway, orfay ostmay ofyay ichwhay ethay eaderray isyay
eferredray otay ethay orystay entitledyay e“thay Arletscay Etterlay”; andyay ityay ouldshay ebay
ornebay arefullycay inyay indmay, atthay ethay ainmay actsfay ofyay atthay orystay areyay
authorizedyay andyay authenticatedyay ybay ethay ocumentday ofyay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay. Ethay
originalyay aperspay, ogethertay ithway ethay arletscay etterlay itself,—ayay ostmay
uriouscay elic,—areray illstay inyay ymay ossessionpay, andyay allshay ebay eelyfray
exhibitedyay otay omsoeverwhay, inducedyay ybay ethay eatgray interestyay ofyay ethay
arrativenay, aymay esireday ayay ightsay ofyay emthay. Iyay ustmay otnay ebay understoodyay asyay
affirmingyay, atthay, inyay ethay essingdray upyay ofyay ethay aletay, andyay imaginingyay ethay
otivesmay andyay odesmay ofyay assionpay atthay influencedyay ethay aracterschay owhay igurefay
inyay ityay, Iyay avehay invariablyyay onfinedcay yselfmay ithinway ethay imitslay ofyay ethay oldyay
Urveyor’ssay alfhay ayay ozenday eetsshay ofyay oolscapfay. Onyay ethay ontrarycay, Iyay avehay
allowedyay yselfmay, asyay otay uchsay ointspay, earlynay oryay altogetheryay asyay uchmay
icenselay asyay ifyay ethay actsfay adhay eenbay entirelyyay ofyay ymay ownyay inventionyay. Atwhay Iyay
ontendcay orfay isyay ethay authenticityyay ofyay ethay outlineyay.

Isthay incidentyay ecalledray ymay indmay, inyay omesay egreeday, otay itsyay oldyay acktray.
Erethay eemedsay otay ebay erehay ethay oundworkgray ofyay ayay aletay. Ityay impressedyay emay asyay
ifyay ethay ancientyay Urveyorsay, inyay ishay arbgay ofyay ayay undredhay yearsyay onegay ybay, andyay
earingway ishay immortalyay ig,—whichway asway uriedbay ithway imhay, utbay idday otnay
erishpay inyay ethay ave,—hadgray etmay emay inyay ethay esertedday amberchay ofyay ethay
Ustom-housecay. Inyay ishay ortpay asway ethay ignityday ofyay oneyay owhay adhay ornebay ishay
Ajesty’smay ommissioncay, andyay owhay asway ereforethay illuminatedyay ybay ayay ayray ofyay
ethay endorsplay atthay oneshay osay azzlinglyday aboutyay ethay onethray. Owhay unlikeyay,
alasyay! ethay ang-doghay ooklay ofyay ayay epublicanray officialyay, owhay, asyay ethay ervantsay
ofyay ethay eoplepay, eelsfay imselfhay esslay anthay ethay eastlay, andyay elowbay ethay
owestlay, ofyay ishay astersmay. Ithway ishay ownyay ostlyghay andhay, ethay obscurelyyay eensay
utbay ajesticmay igurefay adhay impartedyay otay emay ethay arletscay ymbolsay, andyay ethay
ittlelay ollray ofyay explanatoryyay anuscriptmay. Ithway ishay ownyay ostlyghay oicevay, ehay
adhay exhortedyay emay, onyay ethay acredsay onsiderationcay ofyay ymay ilialfay utyday andyay
everenceray owardstay im,—whohay ightmay easonablyray egardray imselfhay asyay ymay
officialyay ancestor,—toyay ingbray ishay ouldymay andyay oth-eatenmay ucubrationslay
eforebay ethay ublicpay. o“day isthay,” aidsay ethay ostghay ofyay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay,
emphaticallyyay oddingnay ethay eadhay atthay ookedlay osay imposingyay ithinway itsyay
emorablemay ig,—“doway isthay, andyay ethay ofitpray allshay ebay allyay youryay ownyay! Youyay
illway ortlyshay eednay ityay; orfay ityay isyay otnay inyay youryay aysday asyay ityay asway inyay inemay,
enwhay ayay an’smay officeyay asway ayay ife-leaselay, andyay oftentimesyay anyay eirloomhay.
Utbay, Iyay argechay youyay, inyay isthay attermay ofyay oldyay Istressmay Ynnepray, ivegay otay youryay
edecessor’spray emorymay ethay editcray ichwhay illway ebay ightfullyray ueday!” Andyay Iyay
aidsay otay ethay ostghay ofyay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay, i“ay illway!”

Onyay Esterhay Ynne’spray orystay, ereforethay, Iyay estowedbay uchmay oughtthay. Ityay asway
ethay ubjectsay ofyay ymay editationsmay orfay anymay anyay ourhay, ilewhay acingpay otay andyay
ofray acrossyay ymay oomray, oryay aversingtray, ithway ayay undred-foldhay epetitionray, ethay
onglay extentyay omfray ethay ont-doorfray ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay otay ethay
ide-entrancesay, andyay ackbay againyay. Eatgray ereway ethay earinessway andyay annoyanceyay
ofyay ethay oldyay Inspectoryay andyay ethay Eighersway andyay Augersgay, osewhay umbersslay ereway
isturbedday ybay ethay unmercifullyyay engthenedlay amptray ofyay ymay assingpay andyay
eturningray ootstepsfay. Ememberingray eirthay ownyay ormerfay abitshay, eythay usedyay otay
aysay atthay ethay Urveyorsay asway alkingway ethay uarter-deckqay. Eythay obablypray
anciedfay atthay ymay olesay object—andyay, indeedyay, ethay olesay objectyay orfay ichwhay ayay
anesay anmay ouldcay everyay utpay imselfhay intoyay oluntaryvay otion—wasmay, otay etgay anyay
appetiteyay orfay innerday. Andyay otay aysay ethay uthtray, anyay appetiteyay, arpenedshay ybay
ethay eastyay indway atthay enerallygay ewblay alongyay ethay assagepay, asway ethay onlyyay
aluablevay esultray ofyay osay uchmay indefatigableyay exerciseyay. Osay ittlelay adaptedyay
isyay ethay atmosphereyay ofyay ayay ustom-housecay otay ethay elicateday arvesthay ofyay ancyfay
andyay ensibilitysay, atthay, adhay Iyay emainedray erethay oughthray entay Esidenciespray
yetyay otay omecay, Iyay oubtday etherwhay ethay aletay ofyay e“thay Arletscay Etterlay” ouldway
everyay avehay eenbay oughtbray eforebay ethay ublicpay eyeyay. Ymay imaginationyay asway ayay
arnishedtay irrormay. Ityay ouldway otnay eflectray, oryay onlyyay ithway iserablemay
imnessday, ethay iguresfay ithway ichwhay Iyay idday ymay estbay otay eoplepay ityay. Ethay
aracterschay ofyay ethay arrativenay ouldway otnay ebay armedway andyay enderedray alleablemay
ybay anyyay eathay atthay Iyay ouldcay indlekay atyay ymay intellectualyay orgefay. Eythay ouldway
aketay eithernay ethay owglay ofyay assionpay ornay ethay endernesstay ofyay entimentsay, utbay
etainedray allyay ethay igidityray ofyay eadday orpsescay, andyay aredstay emay inyay ethay acefay
ithway ayay ixedfay andyay astlyghay ingray ofyay ontemptuouscay efianceday. at“whay avehay youyay
otay oday ithway usyay?” atthay expressionyay eemedsay otay aysay. e“thay ittlelay owerpay youyay
ightmay onceyay avehay ossessedpay overyay ethay ibetray ofyay unrealitiesyay isyay onegay! Youyay
avehay arteredbay ityay orfay ayay ittancepay ofyay ethay ublicpay oldgay. Ogay, enthay, andyay earnyay
youryay agesway!” Inyay ortshay, ethay almostyay orpidtay eaturescray ofyay ymay ownyay ancyfay
ittedtway emay ithway imbecilityyay, andyay otnay ithoutway airfay occasionyay.

Ityay asway otnay erelymay uringday ethay eethray ourshay andyay ayay alfhay ichwhay Uncleyay Amsay
aimedclay asyay ishay areshay ofyay ymay ailyday ifelay, atthay isthay etchedwray umbnessnay
eldhay ossessionpay ofyay emay. Ityay entway ithway emay onyay ymay ea-shoresay alksway, andyay
amblesray intoyay ethay ountrycay, enever—whichwhay asway eldomsay andyay
eluctantly—iray estirredbay yselfmay otay eeksay atthay invigoratingyay armchay ofyay
Aturenay, ichwhay usedyay otay ivegay emay uchsay eshnessfray andyay activityyay ofyay oughtthay
ethay omentmay atthay Iyay eppedstay acrossyay ethay esholdthray ofyay ethay Oldyay Ansemay. Ethay
amesay orportay, asyay egardedray ethay apacitycay orfay intellectualyay effortyay,
accompaniedyay emay omehay, andyay eighedway uponyay emay inyay ethay amberchay ichwhay Iyay ostmay
absurdlyyay ermedtay ymay udystay. Ornay idday ityay uitqay emay, enwhay, atelay atyay ightnay, Iyay
atsay inyay ethay esertedday arlorpay, ightedlay onlyyay ybay ethay immeringglay oal-firecay
andyay ethay oonmay, ivingstray otay icturepay orthfay imaginaryyay enesscay, ichwhay, ethay
extnay ayday, ightmay owflay outyay onyay ethay ighteningbray agepay inyay any-huedmay
escriptionday.

Ifyay ethay imaginativeyay acultyfay efusedray otay actyay atyay uchsay anyay ourhay, ityay ightmay
ellway ebay eemedday ayay opelesshay asecay. Oonlightmay, inyay ayay amiliarfay oomray, allingfay
osay itewhay uponyay ethay arpetcay, andyay owingshay allyay itsyay iguresfay osay
istinctly,—makingday everyyay objectyay osay inutelymay isiblevay, yetyay osay unlikeyay ayay
orningmay oryay oontidenay isibility,—isvay ayay ediummay ethay ostmay uitablesay orfay ayay
omance-writerray otay etgay acquaintedyay ithway ishay illusiveyay uestsgay. Erethay isyay
ethay ittlelay omesticday eneryscay ofyay ethay ell-knownway apartmentyay; ethay airschay,
ithway eachyay itsyay eparatesay individualityyay; ethay entre-tablecay, ustainingsay ayay
ork-basketway, ayay olumevay oryay otway, andyay anyay extinguishedyay amplay; ethay ofasay; ethay
ookcasebay; ethay icturepay onyay ethay all;—allway esethay etailsday, osay ompletelycay
eensay, areyay osay iritualizedspay ybay ethay unusualyay ightlay, atthay eythay eemsay otay
oselay eirthay actualyay ubstancesay, andyay ecomebay ingsthay ofyay intellectyay. Othingnay
isyay ootay allsmay oryay ootay iflingtray otay undergoyay isthay angechay, andyay acquireyay
ignityday erebythay. Ayay ild’schay oeshay; ethay ollday, eatedsay inyay erhay ittlelay ickerway
arriagecay; ethay obby-horse;—whateverhay, inyay ayay ordway, ashay eenbay usedyay oryay
ayedplay ithway, uringday ethay ayday, isyay ownay investedyay ithway ayay ualityqay ofyay
angenessstray andyay emotenessray, oughthay illstay almostyay asyay ividlyvay esentpray asyay
ybay aylightday. Usthay, ereforethay, ethay oorflay ofyay ouryay amiliarfay oomray ashay
ecomebay ayay eutralnay erritorytay, omewheresay etweenbay ethay ealray orldway andyay
airy-landfay, erewhay ethay Actualyay andyay ethay Imaginaryyay aymay eetmay, andyay eachyay
imbueyay itselfyay ithway ethay aturenay ofyay ethay otheryay. Ostsghay ightmay enteryay erehay,
ithoutway affrightingyay usyay. Ityay ouldway ebay ootay uchmay inyay eepingkay ithway ethay enescay
otay exciteyay urprisesay, ereway eway otay ooklay aboutyay usyay andyay iscoverday ayay ormfay
elovedbay, utbay onegay encehay, ownay ittingsay uietlyqay inyay ayay eakstray ofyay isthay agicmay
oonshinemay, ithway anyay aspectyay atthay ouldway akemay usyay oubtday etherwhay ityay adhay
eturnedray omfray afaryay, oryay adhay evernay onceyay irredstay omfray ouryay iresidefay.

Ethay omewhatsay imday oal-firecay ashay anyay essentialyay influenceyay inyay oducingpray ethay
effectyay ichwhay Iyay ouldway escribeday. Ityay owsthray itsyay unobtrusiveyay ingetay
oughoutthray ethay oomray, ithway ayay aintfay uddinessray uponyay ethay allsway andyay
eilingcay, andyay ayay eflectedray eamglay omfray ethay olishpay ofyay ethay urniturefay. Isthay
armerway ightlay inglesmay itselfyay ithway ethay oldcay iritualityspay ofyay ethay
oonbeamsmay, andyay ommunicatescay, asyay ityay ereway, ayay earthay andyay ensibilitiessay ofyay
umanhay endernesstay otay ethay ormsfay ichwhay ancyfay ummonssay upyay. Ityay onvertscay emthay
omfray ow-imagessnay intoyay enmay andyay omenway. Ancingglay atyay ethay ooking-glasslay, eway
ehold—deepbay ithinway itsyay auntedhay erge—thevay oulderingsmay owglay ofyay ethay
alf-extinguishedhay anthraciteyay, ethay itewhay oonbeamsmay onyay ethay oorflay, andyay ayay
epetitionray ofyay allyay ethay eamglay andyay adowshay ofyay ethay icturepay, ithway oneyay emoveray
urtherfay omfray ethay actualyay, andyay earernay otay ethay imaginativeyay. Enthay, atyay uchsay
anyay ourhay, andyay ithway isthay enescay eforebay imhay, ifyay ayay anmay, ittingsay allyay aloneyay,
annotcay eamdray angestray ingsthay, andyay akemay emthay ooklay ikelay uthtray, ehay eednay
evernay ytray otay itewray omancesray.

Utbay, orfay yselfmay, uringday ethay olewhay ofyay ymay Ustom-housecay experienceyay,
oonlightmay andyay unshinesay, andyay ethay owglay ofyay irelightfay, ereway ustjay alikeyay inyay
ymay egardray; andyay eithernay ofyay emthay asway ofyay oneyay itwhay oremay availyay anthay ethay
inkletway ofyay ayay allow-candletay. Anyay entireyay assclay ofyay usceptibilitiessay, andyay ayay
iftgay onnectedcay ithway em,—ofthay onay eatgray ichnessray oryay aluevay, utbay ethay estbay
Iyay ad,—washay onegay omfray emay.

Ityay isyay ymay eliefbay, oweverhay, atthay, adhay Iyay attemptedyay ayay ifferentday orderyay ofyay
ompositioncay, ymay acultiesfay ouldway otnay avehay eenbay oundfay osay ointlesspay andyay
inefficaciousyay. Iyay ightmay, orfay instanceyay, avehay ontentedcay yselfmay ithway
itingwray outyay ethay arrativesnay ofyay ayay eteranvay ipmastershay, oneyay ofyay ethay
Inspectorsyay, omwhay Iyay ouldshay ebay ostmay ungratefulyay otnay otay entionmay, incesay
arcelyscay ayay ayday assedpay atthay ehay idday otnay irstay emay otay aughterlay andyay
admirationyay ybay ishay arvellousmay iftsgay asyay ayay ory-tellerstay. Ouldcay Iyay avehay
eservedpray ethay icturesquepay orcefay ofyay ishay ylestay, andyay ethay umoroushay
oloringcay ichwhay aturenay aughttay imhay owhay otay owthray overyay ishay escriptionsday,
ethay esultray, Iyay onestlyhay elievebay, ouldway avehay eenbay omethingsay ewnay inyay
iteraturelay. Oryay Iyay ightmay eadilyray avehay oundfay ayay oremay erioussay asktay. Ityay asway
ayay ollyfay, ithway ethay aterialitymay ofyay isthay ailyday ifelay essingpray osay
intrusivelyyay uponyay emay, otay attemptyay otay ingflay yselfmay ackbay intoyay anotheryay ageyay;
oryay otay insistyay onyay eatingcray ethay emblancesay ofyay ayay orldway outyay ofyay airyyay attermay,
enwhay, atyay everyyay omentmay, ethay impalpableyay eautybay ofyay ymay oap-bubblesay asway
okenbray ybay ethay uderay ontactcay ofyay omesay actualyay ircumstancecay. Ethay iserway
effortyay ouldway avehay eenbay, otay iffuseday oughtthay andyay imaginationyay oughthray
ethay opaqueyay ubstancesay ofyay o-daytay, andyay usthay otay akemay ityay ayay ightbray
ansparencytray; otay iritualizespay ethay urdenbay atthay eganbay otay eighway osay
eavilyhay; otay eeksay, esolutelyray, ethay uetray andyay indestructibleyay aluevay atthay
aylay iddenhay inyay ethay ettypay andyay earisomeway incidentsyay, andyay ordinaryyay
aracterschay, ithway ichwhay Iyay asway ownay onversantcay. Ethay aultfay asway inemay. Ethay
agepay ofyay ifelay atthay asway eadspray outyay eforebay emay eemedsay ullday andyay
ommonplacecay, onlyyay ecausebay Iyay adhay otnay athomedfay itsyay eeperday importyay. Ayay
etterbay ookbay anthay Iyay allshay everyay itewray asway erethay; eaflay afteryay eaflay
esentingpray itselfyay otay emay, ustjay asyay ityay asway ittenwray outyay ybay ethay ealityray ofyay
ethay ittingflay ourhay, andyay anishingvay asyay astfay asyay ittenwray, onlyyay ecausebay ymay
ainbray antedway ethay insightyay andyay ymay andhay ethay unningcay otay anscribetray ityay. Atyay
omesay uturefay ayday, ityay aymay ebay, Iyay allshay ememberray ayay ewfay atteredscay agmentsfray
andyay okenbray aragraphspay, andyay itewray emthay ownday, andyay indfay ethay etterslay urntay
otay oldgay uponyay ethay agepay.

Esethay erceptionspay avehay omecay ootay atelay. Atyay ethay instantyay, Iyay asway onlyyay
onsciouscay atthay atwhay ouldway avehay eenbay ayay easureplay onceyay asway ownay ayay opelesshay
oiltay. Erethay asway onay occasionyay otay akemay uchmay oanmay aboutyay isthay atestay ofyay
affairsyay. Iyay adhay easedcay otay ebay ayay iterwray ofyay olerablytay oorpay alestay andyay
essaysyay, andyay adhay ecomebay ayay olerablytay oodgay Urveyorsay ofyay ethay Ustomscay. Atthay
asway allyay. Utbay, everthelessnay, ityay isyay anythingyay utbay agreeableyay otay ebay auntedhay
ybay ayay uspicionsay atthay one’syay intellectyay isyay indlingdway awayyay; oryay exhalingyay,
ithoutway youryay onsciousnesscay, ikelay etheryay outyay ofyay ayay ialphay; osay atthay, atyay
everyyay anceglay, youyay indfay ayay allersmay andyay esslay olatilevay esiduumray. Ofyay ethay
actfay erethay ouldcay ebay onay oubtday; andyay, examiningyay yselfmay andyay othersyay, Iyay asway
edlay otay onclusionscay, inyay eferenceray otay ethay effectyay ofyay ublicpay officeyay onyay ethay
aracterchay, otnay eryvay avorablefay otay ethay odemay ofyay ifelay inyay uestionqay. Inyay omesay
otheryay ormfay, erhapspay, Iyay aymay ereafterhay evelopday esethay effectsyay. Ufficesay ityay
erehay otay aysay, atthay ayay Ustom-housecay officeryay, ofyay onglay ontinuancecay, ancay
ardlyhay ebay ayay eryvay aiseworthypray oryay espectableray ersonagepay, orfay anymay
easonsray; oneyay ofyay emthay, ethay enuretay ybay ichwhay ehay oldshay ishay ituationsay, andyay
anotheryay, ethay eryvay aturenay ofyay ishay usinessbay, ich—thoughwhay, Iyay usttray, anyay
onesthay one—isyay ofyay uchsay ayay ortsay atthay ehay oesday otnay areshay inyay ethay unitedyay
effortyay ofyay ankindmay.

Anyay effect—whichyay Iyay elievebay otay ebay observableyay, oremay oryay esslay, inyay everyyay
individualyay owhay ashay occupiedyay ethay osition—ispay, atthay, ilewhay ehay eanslay onyay
ethay ightymay armyay ofyay ethay Epublicray, ishay ownyay operpray engthstray epartsday omfray
imhay. Ehay oseslay, inyay anyay extentyay oportionedpray otay ethay eaknessway oryay orcefay ofyay
ishay originalyay aturenay, ethay apabilitycay ofyay elf-supportsay. Ifyay ehay ossesspay anyay
unusualyay areshay ofyay ativenay energyyay, oryay ethay enervatingyay agicmay ofyay aceplay oday
otnay operateyay ootay onglay uponyay imhay, ishay orfeitedfay owerspay aymay ebay edeemableray.
Ethay ejectedyay officer—fortunateyay inyay ethay unkindlyyay oveshay atthay endssay imhay
orthfay etimesbay, otay ugglestray amidyay ayay ugglingstray orld—mayway eturnray otay
imselfhay, andyay ecomebay allyay atthay ehay ashay everyay eenbay. Utbay isthay eldomsay
appenshay. Ehay usuallyyay eepskay ishay oundgray ustjay onglay enoughyay orfay ishay ownyay
uinray, andyay isyay enthay ustthray outyay, ithway inewssay allyay unstrungyay, otay ottertay
alongyay ethay ifficultday ootpathfay ofyay ifelay asyay ehay estbay aymay. Onsciouscay ofyay ishay
ownyay infirmity,—thatyay ishay emperedtay eelstay andyay elasticityyay areyay ost,—helay
oreverfay afterwardsyay ookslay istfullyway aboutyay imhay inyay uestqay ofyay upportsay
externalyay otay imselfhay. Ishay ervadingpay andyay ontinualcay ope—ahay allucinationhay
ichwhay, inyay ethay acefay ofyay allyay iscouragementday, andyay akingmay ightlay ofyay
impossibilitiesyay, auntshay imhay ilewhay ehay iveslay, andyay, Iyay ancyfay, ikelay ethay
onvulsivecay oesthray ofyay ethay olerachay, ormentstay imhay orfay ayay iefbray acespay afteryay
eath—isday, atthay inallyfay, andyay inyay onay onglay imetay, ybay omesay appyhay
oincidencecay ofyay ircumstancescay, ehay allshay ebay estoredray otay officeyay. Isthay
aithfay, oremay anthay anythingyay elseyay, ealsstay ethay ithpay andyay availabilityyay outyay
ofyay ateverwhay enterpriseyay ehay aymay eamdray ofyay undertakingyay. Ywhay ouldshay ehay oiltay
andyay oilmay, andyay ebay atyay osay uchmay oubletray otay ickpay imselfhay upyay outyay ofyay ethay
udmay, enwhay, inyay ayay ittlelay ilewhay encehay, ethay ongstray armyay ofyay ishay Uncleyay illway
aiseray andyay upportsay imhay? Ywhay ouldshay ehay orkway orfay ishay ivinglay erehay, oryay ogay
otay igday oldgay inyay Aliforniacay, enwhay ehay isyay osay oonsay otay ebay ademay appyhay, atyay
onthlymay intervalsyay, ithway ayay ittlelay ilepay ofyay itteringglay oincay outyay ofyay ishay
Uncle’syay ocketpay? Ityay isyay adlysay uriouscay otay observeyay owhay ightslay ayay astetay ofyay
officeyay ufficessay otay infectyay ayay oorpay ellowfay ithway isthay ingularsay iseaseday.
Uncleyay Am’ssay old—meaninggay onay isrespectday otay ethay orthyway oldyay
entleman—hasgay, inyay isthay espectray, ayay ualityqay ofyay enchantmentyay ikelay atthay ofyay
ethay Evil’sday agesway. Oeverwhay ouchestay ityay ouldshay ooklay ellway otay imselfhay, oryay
ehay aymay indfay ethay argainbay otay ogay ardhay againstyay imhay, involvingyay, ifyay otnay ishay
oulsay, yetyay anymay ofyay itsyay etterbay attributesyay; itsyay urdystay orcefay, itsyay ouragecay
andyay onstancycay, itsyay uthtray, itsyay elf-reliancesay, andyay allyay atthay ivesgay ethay
emphasisyay otay anlymay aracterchay.

Erehay asway ayay inefay ospectpray inyay ethay istanceday! Otnay atthay ethay Urveyorsay
oughtbray ethay essonlay omehay otay imselfhay, oryay admittedyay atthay ehay ouldcay ebay osay
utterlyyay undoneyay, eitheryay ybay ontinuancecay inyay officeyay, oryay ejectmentyay. Yetyay ymay
eflectionsray ereway otnay ethay ostmay omfortablecay. Iyay eganbay otay owgray elancholymay
andyay estlessray; ontinuallycay yingpray intoyay ymay indmay, otay iscoverday ichwhay ofyay
itsyay oorpay opertiespray ereway onegay, andyay atwhay egreeday ofyay etrimentday adhay
alreadyyay accruedyay otay ethay emainderray. Iyay endeavoredyay otay alculatecay owhay uchmay
ongerlay Iyay ouldcay aystay inyay ethay Ustom-housecay, andyay yetyay ogay orthfay ayay anmay. Otay
onfesscay ethay uthtray, ityay asway ymay eatestgray apprehension,—asyay ityay ouldway evernay
ebay ayay easuremay ofyay olicypay otay urntay outyay osay uietqay anyay individualyay asyay yselfmay,
andyay ityay eingbay ardlyhay inyay ethay aturenay ofyay ayay ublicpay officeryay otay esign,—itray
asway ymay iefchay oubletray, ereforethay, atthay Iyay asway ikelylay otay owgray aygray andyay
ecrepitday inyay ethay Urveyorshipsay, andyay ecomebay uchmay uchsay anotheryay animalyay asyay
ethay oldyay Inspectoryay. Ightmay ityay otnay, inyay ethay edioustay apselay ofyay officialyay
ifelay atthay aylay eforebay emay, inallyfay ebay ithway emay asyay ityay asway ithway isthay
enerablevay iend,—tofray akemay ethay inner-hourday ethay ucleusnay ofyay ethay ayday, andyay
otay endspay ethay estray ofyay ityay, asyay anyay oldyay ogday endsspay ityay, asleepyay inyay ethay
unshinesay oryay inyay ethay adeshay? Ayay earydray ook-forwardlay isthay, orfay ayay anmay owhay
eltfay ityay otay ebay ethay estbay efinitionday ofyay appinesshay otay ivelay oughoutthray ethay
olewhay angeray ofyay ishay acultiesfay andyay ensibilitiessay! Utbay, allyay isthay ilewhay, Iyay
asway ivinggay yselfmay eryvay unnecessaryyay alarmyay. Ovidencepray adhay editatedmay
etterbay ingsthay orfay emay anthay Iyay ouldcay ossiblypay imagineyay orfay yselfmay.

Ayay emarkableray eventyay ofyay ethay irdthay yearyay ofyay ymay Urveyorship—tosay adoptyay ethay
onetay ofyay “pay. Asp.”—way ethay electionyay ofyay Eneralgay Aylortay otay ethay Esidencypray.
Ityay isyay essentialyay, inyay orderyay otay ormfay ayay ompletecay estimateyay ofyay ethay advantagesyay ofyay
officialyay ifelay, otay iewvay ethay incumbentyay atyay ethay incomingyay ofyay ayay ostilehay
administrationyay. Ishay ositionpay isyay enthay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay ingularlysay
irksomeyay, andyay, inyay everyyay ontingencycay, isagreeableday, atthay ayay etchedwray
ortalmay ancay ossiblypay occupyyay; ithway eldomsay anyay alternativeyay ofyay oodgay, onyay
eitheryay andhay, althoughyay atwhay esentspray itselfyay otay imhay asyay ethay orstway eventyay
aymay eryvay obablypray ebay ethay estbay. Utbay ityay isyay ayay angestray experienceyay, otay ayay
anmay ofyay idepray andyay ensibilitysay, otay owknay atthay ishay interestsyay areyay ithinway
ethay ontrolcay ofyay individualsyay owhay eithernay ovelay ornay understandyay imhay, andyay ybay
omwhay, incesay oneyay oryay ethay otheryay ustmay eedsnay appenhay, ehay ouldway atherray ebay
injuredyay anthay obligedyay. Angestray, ootay, orfay oneyay owhay ashay eptkay ishay almnesscay
oughoutthray ethay ontestcay, otay observeyay ethay ood-thirstinessblay atthay isyay
evelopedday inyay ethay ourhay ofyay iumphtray, andyay otay ebay onsciouscay atthay ehay isyay
imselfhay amongyay itsyay objectsyay! Erethay areyay ewfay uglieryay aitstray ofyay umanhay aturenay
anthay isthay endency—whichtay Iyay ownay itnessedway inyay enmay onay orseway anthay eirthay
eighbors—tonay owgray uelcray, erelymay ecausebay eythay ossessedpay ethay owerpay ofyay
inflictingyay armhay. Ifyay ethay uillotinegay, asyay appliedyay otay office-holdersyay,
ereway ayay iterallay actfay insteadyay ofyay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay aptyay ofyay etaphorsmay, ityay isyay
ymay inceresay eliefbay atthay ethay activeyay embersmay ofyay ethay ictoriousvay artypay ereway
ufficientlysay excitedyay otay avehay oppedchay offyay allyay ouryay eadshay, andyay avehay
ankedthay Eavenhay orfay ethay opportunityyay! Ityay appearsyay otay e—whomay avehay eenbay ayay
almcay andyay uriouscay observeryay, asyay ellway inyay ictoryvay asyay efeat—thatday isthay
iercefay andyay itterbay iritspay ofyay alicemay andyay evengeray ashay evernay istinguishedday
ethay anymay iumphstray ofyay ymay ownyay artypay asyay ityay ownay idday atthay ofyay ethay Igswhay. Ethay
Emocratsday aketay ethay officesyay, asyay ayay eneralgay uleray, ecausebay eythay eednay emthay,
andyay ecausebay ethay acticepray ofyay anymay yearsyay ashay ademay ityay ethay awlay ofyay
oliticalpay arfareway, ichwhay, unlessyay ayay ifferentday ystemsay ebay oclaimedpray, ityay
ereway eaknessway andyay owardicecay otay urmurmay atyay. Utbay ethay onglay abithay ofyay
ictoryvay ashay ademay emthay enerousgay. Eythay owknay owhay otay arespay, enwhay eythay eesay
occasionyay; andyay enwhay eythay ikestray, ethay axeyay aymay ebay arpshay, indeedyay, utbay itsyay
edgeyay isyay eldomsay oisonedpay ithway ill-willyay; ornay isyay ityay eirthay ustomcay
ignominiouslyyay otay ickkay ethay eadhay ichwhay eythay avehay ustjay uckstray offyay.

Inyay ortshay, unpleasantyay asyay asway ymay edicamentpray, atyay estbay, Iyay awsay uchmay easonray
otay ongratulatecay yselfmay atthay Iyay asway onyay ethay osinglay idesay, atherray anthay ethay
iumphanttray oneyay. Ifyay, eretoforehay, Iyay adhay eenbay onenay ofyay ethay armestway ofyay
artisanspay, Iyay eganbay ownay, atyay isthay easonsay ofyay erilpay andyay adversityyay, otay ebay
ettypray acutelyyay ensiblesay ithway ichwhay artypay ymay edilectionspray aylay; ornay asway
ityay ithoutway omethingsay ikelay egretray andyay ameshay, atthay, accordingyay otay ayay
easonableray alculationcay ofyay anceschay, Iyay awsay ymay ownyay ospectpray ofyay etainingray
officeyay otay ebay etterbay anthay osethay ofyay ymay Emocraticday ethrenbray. Utbay owhay ancay
eesay anyay inchyay intoyay uturityfay, eyondbay ishay osenay? Ymay ownyay eadhay asway ethay irstfay
atthay ellfay!

Ethay omentmay enwhay ayay an’smay eadhay opsdray offyay isyay eldomsay oryay evernay, Iyay amyay
inclinedyay otay inkthay, eciselypray ethay ostmay agreeableyay ofyay ishay ifelay.
Everthelessnay, ikelay ethay eatergray artpay ofyay ouryay isfortunesmay, evenyay osay
erioussay ayay ontingencycay ingsbray itsyay emedyray andyay onsolationcay ithway ityay, ifyay
ethay ufferersay illway utbay akemay ethay estbay, atherray anthay ethay orstway, ofyay ethay
accidentyay ichwhay ashay efallenbay imhay. Inyay ymay articularpay asecay, ethay
onsolatorycay opicstay ereway oseclay atyay andhay, andyay, indeedyay, adhay uggestedsay
emselvesthay otay ymay editationsmay ayay onsiderablecay imetay eforebay ityay asway
equisiteray otay useyay emthay. Inyay iewvay ofyay ymay eviouspray earinessway ofyay officeyay, andyay
aguevay oughtsthay ofyay esignationray, ymay ortunefay omewhatsay esembledray atthay ofyay ayay
ersonpay owhay ouldshay entertainyay anyay ideayay ofyay ommittingcay uicidesay, andyay,
althoughyay eyondbay ishay opeshay, eetmay ithway ethay oodgay aphay otay ebay urderedmay. Inyay
ethay Ustom-housecay, asyay eforebay inyay ethay Oldyay Ansemay, Iyay adhay entspay eethray yearsyay;
ayay ermtay onglay enoughyay otay estray ayay earyway ainbray; onglay enoughyay otay eakbray offyay oldyay
intellectualyay abitshay, andyay akemay oomray orfay ewnay onesyay; onglay enoughyay, andyay ootay
onglay, otay avehay ivedlay inyay anyay unnaturalyay atestay, oingday atwhay asway eallyray ofyay onay
advantageyay ornay elightday otay anyyay umanhay eingbay, andyay ithholdingway yselfmay omfray
oiltay atthay ouldway, atyay eastlay, avehay illedstay anyay unquietyay impulseyay inyay emay.
Enthay, oreovermay, asyay egardedray ishay unceremoniousyay ejectmentyay, ethay atelay
Urveyorsay asway otnay altogetheryay ill-pleasedyay otay ebay ecognizedray ybay ethay Igswhay
asyay anyay enemyyay; incesay ishay inactivityyay inyay oliticalpay affairs—hisyay endencytay
otay oamray, atyay illway, inyay atthay oadbray andyay uietqay ieldfay erewhay allyay ankindmay aymay
eetmay, atherray anthay onfinecay imselfhay otay osethay arrownay athspay erewhay ethrenbray
ofyay ethay amesay ouseholdhay ustmay ivergeday omfray oneyay another—hadyay ometimessay
ademay ityay uestionableqay ithway ishay otherbray Emocratsday etherwhay ehay asway ayay
iendfray. Ownay, afteryay ehay adhay onway ethay owncray ofyay artyrdommay ough(thay ithway onay
ongerlay ayay eadhay otay earway ityay onyay), ethay ointpay ightmay ebay ookedlay uponyay asyay
ettledsay. Inallyfay, ittlelay eroichay asyay ehay asway, ityay eemedsay oremay ecorousday otay
ebay overthrownyay inyay ethay ownfallday ofyay ethay artypay ithway ichwhay ehay adhay eenbay
ontentcay otay andstay, anthay otay emainray ayay orlornfay urvivorsay, enwhay osay anymay
orthierway enmay ereway allingfay; andyay, atyay astlay, afteryay ubsistingsay orfay ourfay
yearsyay onyay ethay ercymay ofyay ayay ostilehay administrationyay, otay ebay ompelledcay enthay
otay efineday ishay ositionpay anewyay, andyay aimclay ethay yetyay oremay umiliatinghay ercymay
ofyay ayay iendlyfray oneyay.

Eanwhilemay ethay esspray adhay akentay upyay ymay affairyay, andyay eptkay emay, orfay ayay eekway oryay
otway, areeringcay oughthray ethay ublicpay intspray, inyay ymay ecapitatedday atestay,
ikelay Irving’syay Eadlesshay Orsemanhay; astlyghay andyay imgray, andyay onginglay otay ebay
uriedbay, asyay ayay oliticallypay eadday anmay oughtyay. Osay uchmay orfay ymay igurativefay
elfsay. Ethay ealray umanhay eingbay, allyay isthay imetay, ithway ishay eadhay afelysay onyay ishay
ouldersshay, adhay oughtbray imselfhay otay ethay omfortablecay onclusioncay atthay
everythingyay asway orfay ethay estbay; andyay, akingmay anyay investmentyay inyay inkyay, aperpay,
andyay eel-pensstay, adhay openedyay ishay ong-disusedlay iting-deskwray, andyay asway
againyay ayay iterarylay anmay.

Ownay ityay asway atthay ethay ucubrationslay ofyay ymay ancientyay edecessorpray, Mray.
Urveyorsay Uepay, amecay intoyay ayplay. Ustyray oughthray onglay idlenessyay, omesay ittlelay
acespay asway equisiteray eforebay ymay intellectualyay achinerymay ouldcay ebay oughtbray
otay orkway uponyay ethay aletay, ithway anyay effectyay inyay anyyay egreeday atisfactorysay. Evenyay
yetyay, oughthay ymay oughtsthay ereway ultimatelyyay uchmay absorbedyay inyay ethay asktay, ityay
earsway, otay ymay eyeyay, ayay ernstay andyay ombresay aspectyay; ootay uchmay ungladdenedyay ybay
enialgay unshinesay; ootay ittlelay elievedray ybay ethay endertay andyay amiliarfay
influencesyay ichwhay oftensay almostyay everyyay enescay ofyay aturenay andyay ealray ifelay,
andyay, undoubtedlyyay, ouldshay oftensay everyyay icturepay ofyay emthay. Isthay
uncaptivatingyay effectyay isyay erhapspay ueday otay ethay eriodpay ofyay ardlyhay
accomplishedyay evolutionray, andyay illstay eethingsay urmoiltay, inyay ichwhay ethay
orystay apedshay itselfyay. Ityay isyay onay indicationyay, oweverhay, ofyay ayay acklay ofyay
eerfulnesschay inyay ethay iter’swray indmay; orfay ehay asway appierhay, ilewhay ayingstray
oughthray ethay oomglay ofyay esethay unlesssay antasiesfay, anthay atyay anyyay imetay incesay
ehay adhay uittedqay ethay Oldyay Ansemay. Omesay ofyay ethay ieferbray articlesyay, ichwhay
ontributecay otay akemay upyay ethay olumevay, avehay ikewiselay eenbay ittenwray incesay ymay
involuntaryyay ithdrawalway omfray ethay oilstay andyay onorshay ofyay ublicpay ifelay, andyay
ethay emainderray areyay eanedglay omfray annualsyay andyay agazinesmay ofyay uchsay antiqueyay
ateday atthay eythay avehay onegay oundray ethay irclecay, andyay omecay ackbay otay oveltynay
againyay.[1] Eepingkay upyay ethay etaphormay ofyay ethay oliticalpay uillotinegay, ethay
olewhay aymay ebay onsideredcay asyay ethay Osthumouspay Aperspay Ofyay Ayay Ecapitatedday
Urveyorsay; andyay ethay etchskay ichwhay Iyay amyay ownay ingingbray otay ayay oseclay, ifyay ootay
autobiographicalyay orfay ayay odestmay ersonpay otay ublishpay inyay ishay ifetimelay, illway
eadilyray ebay excusedyay inyay ayay entlemangay owhay iteswray omfray eyondbay ethay avegray.
Eacepay ebay ithway allyay ethay orldway! Ymay essingblay onyay ymay iendsfray! Ymay orgivenessfay
otay ymay enemiesyay! Orfay Iyay amyay inyay ethay ealmray ofyay uietqay!

    ootnote[fay 1: Atyay ethay imetay ofyay itingwray isthay articleyay ethay authoryay
    intendedyay otay ublishpay, alongyay ithway e“thay Arletscay Etterlay,” everalsay
    ortershay alestay andyay etchesskay. Esethay ityay ashay eenbay oughtthay
    advisableyay otay eferday.]

Ethay ifelay ofyay ethay Ustom-housecay ieslay ikelay ayay eamdray ehindbay emay. Ethay oldyay
Inspector,—whoyay, ybay ethay ybay, Iyay egretray otay aysay, asway overthrownyay andyay illedkay
ybay ayay orsehay, omesay imetay agoyay; elseyay ehay ouldway ertainlycay avehay ivedlay
orever,—hefay, andyay allyay osethay otheryay enerablevay ersonagespay owhay atsay ithway
imhay atyay ethay eceiptray ofyay ustomcay, areyay utbay adowsshay inyay ymay iewvay; ite-headedwhay
andyay inkledwray imagesyay, ichwhay ymay ancyfay usedyay otay ortspay ithway, andyay ashay ownay
ungflay asideyay oreverfay. Ethay erchants,—pingreemay, Illipsphay, Epardshay,
Uptonyay, Imballkay, Ertrambay, Unt,—thesehay, andyay anymay otheryay amesnay, ichwhay adhay
uchsay ayay assicclay amiliarityfay orfay ymay earyay ixsay onthsmay ago,—theseyay enmay ofyay
affictray, owhay eemedsay otay occupyyay osay importantyay ayay ositionpay inyay ethay
orld,—howway ittlelay imetay ashay ityay equiredray otay isconnectday emay omfray emthay
allyay, otnay erelymay inyay actyay, utbay ecollectionray! Ityay isyay ithway anyay effortyay atthay Iyay
ecallray ethay iguresfay andyay appellationsyay ofyay esethay ewfay. Oonsay, ikewiselay, ymay
oldyay ativenay owntay illway oomlay uponyay emay oughthray ethay azehay ofyay emorymay, ayay istmay
oodingbray overyay andyay aroundyay ityay; asyay ifyay ityay ereway onay ortionpay ofyay ethay ealray
earthyay, utbay anyay overgrownyay illagevay inyay oud-landclay, ithway onlyyay imaginaryyay
inhabitantsyay otay eoplepay itsyay oodenway ouseshay, andyay alkway itsyay omelyhay aneslay,
andyay ethay unpicturesqueyay olixitypray ofyay itsyay ainmay eetstray. Enceforthhay ityay
easescay otay ebay ayay ealityray ofyay ymay ifelay. Iyay amyay ayay itizencay ofyay omewheresay elseyay.
Ymay oodgay owns-peopletay illway otnay uchmay egretray emay; or—thoughfay ityay ashay eenbay
asyay earday anyay objectyay asyay anyyay, inyay ymay iterarylay effortsyay, otay ebay ofyay omesay
importanceyay inyay eirthay eyesyay, andyay otay inway yselfmay ayay easantplay emorymay inyay isthay
abodeyay andyay urial-placebay ofyay osay anymay ofyay ymay orefathers—_therefay_ ashay evernay
eenbay, orfay emay, ethay enialgay atmosphereyay ichwhay ayay iterarylay anmay equiresray, inyay
orderyay otay ipenray ethay estbay arvesthay ofyay ishay indmay. Iyay allshay oday etterbay amongstyay
otheryay acesfay; andyay esethay amiliarfay onesyay, ityay eednay ardlyhay ebay aidsay, illway oday
ustjay asyay ellway ithoutway emay.

Ityay aymay ebay, owever,—ohay, ansportingtray andyay iumphanttray ought!—thatthay ethay
eat-grandchildrengray ofyay ethay esentpray aceray aymay ometimessay inkthay indlykay ofyay
ethay ibblerscray ofyay ygonebay aysday, enwhay ethay antiquaryyay ofyay aysday otay omecay,
amongyay ethay itessay emorablemay inyay ethay own’stay istoryhay, allshay ointpay outyay ethay
ocalitylay ofyay Ethay Owntay Umppay!

illustration[ay: Ignette,—wildvay Oseray]

                          Ethay Arletscay Etterlay.




                                  Iyay.

                           Ethay Ison-doorpray.


illustration[ay]

Ayay ongthray ofyay eardedbay enmay, inyay ad-coloredsay armentsgay, andyay aygray,
eeple-crownedstay atshay, intermixedyay ithway omenway, omesay earingway oodshay andyay
othersyay areheadedbay, asway assembledyay inyay ontfray ofyay ayay oodenway edificeyay, ethay
oorday ofyay ichwhay asway eavilyhay imberedtay ithway oakyay, andyay uddedstay ithway ironyay
ikesspay.

Ethay oundersfay ofyay ayay ewnay olonycay, ateverwhay Utopiayay ofyay umanhay irtuevay andyay
appinesshay eythay ightmay originallyyay ojectpray, avehay invariablyyay ecognizedray ityay
amongyay eirthay earliestyay acticalpray ecessitiesnay otay allotyay ayay ortionpay ofyay ethay
irginvay oilsay asyay ayay emeterycay, andyay anotheryay ortionpay asyay ethay itesay ofyay ayay
isonpray. Inyay accordanceyay ithway isthay uleray, ityay aymay afelysay ebay assumedyay atthay
ethay orefathersfay ofyay Ostonbay adhay uiltbay ethay irstfay ison-housepray omewheresay
inyay ethay icinityvay ofyay Ornhillcay, almostyay asyay easonablysay asyay eythay arkedmay outyay
ethay irstfay urial-groundbay, onyay Isaacyay Ohnson’sjay otlay, andyay oundray aboutyay ishay
avegray, ichwhay ubsequentlysay ecamebay ethay ucleusnay ofyay allyay ethay ongregatedcay
epulchressay inyay ethay oldyay urchyardchay ofyay Ing’skay Apelchay. Ertaincay ityay isyay,
atthay, omesay ifteenfay oryay entytway yearsyay afteryay ethay ettlementsay ofyay ethay owntay,
ethay oodenway ailjay asway alreadyyay arkedmay ithway eather-stainsway andyay otheryay
indicationsyay ofyay ageyay, ichwhay avegay ayay yetyay arkerday aspectyay otay itsyay
eetle-browedbay andyay oomyglay ontfray. Ethay ustray onyay ethay onderouspay iron-workyay ofyay
itsyay oakenyay oorday ookedlay oremay antiqueyay anthay anythingyay elseyay inyay ethay Ewnay
Orldway. Ikelay allyay atthay ertainspay otay imecray, ityay eemedsay evernay otay avehay ownknay
ayay youthfulyay erayay. Eforebay isthay uglyyay edificeyay, andyay etweenbay ityay andyay ethay
eel-trackwhay ofyay ethay eetstray, asway ayay ass-plotgray, uchmay overgrownyay ithway
urdockbay, igweedpay, apple-peruyay, andyay uchsay unsightlyyay egetationvay, ichwhay
evidentlyyay oundfay omethingsay ongenialcay inyay ethay oilsay atthay adhay osay earlyyay
ornebay ethay ackblay owerflay ofyay ivilizedcay ocietysay, ayay isonpray. Utbay onyay oneyay idesay
ofyay ethay ortalpay, andyay ootedray almostyay atyay ethay esholdthray, asway ayay ildway
ose-bushray, overedcay, inyay isthay onthmay ofyay Unejay, ithway itsyay elicateday emsgay,
ichwhay ightmay ebay imaginedyay otay offeryay eirthay agrancefray andyay agilefray eautybay otay
ethay isonerpray asyay ehay entway inyay, andyay otay ethay ondemnedcay iminalcray asyay ehay amecay
orthfay otay ishay oomday, inyay okentay atthay ethay eepday earthay ofyay Aturenay ouldcay itypay
andyay ebay indkay otay imhay.

Isthay ose-bushray, ybay ayay angestray ancechay, ashay eenbay eptkay aliveyay inyay istoryhay;
utbay etherwhay ityay adhay erelymay urvivedsay outyay ofyay ethay ernstay oldyay ildernessway, osay
onglay afteryay ethay allfay ofyay ethay iganticgay inespay andyay oaksyay atthay originallyyay
overshadowedyay it,—oryay etherwhay, asyay erethay isyay airfay authorityyay orfay
elievingbay, ityay adhay ungspray upyay underyay ethay ootstepsfay ofyay ethay aintedsay Annyay
Utchinsonhay, asyay eshay enteredyay ethay ison-door,—wepray allshay otnay aketay uponyay usyay
otay etermineday. Indingfay ityay osay irectlyday onyay ethay esholdthray ofyay ouryay
arrativenay, ichwhay isyay ownay aboutyay otay issueyay omfray atthay inauspiciousyay ortalpay,
eway ouldcay ardlyhay oday otherwiseyay anthay uckplay oneyay ofyay itsyay owersflay, andyay
esentpray ityay otay ethay eaderray. Ityay aymay ervesay, etlay usyay opehay, otay ymbolizesay omesay
eetsway oralmay ossomblay, atthay aymay ebay oundfay alongyay ethay acktray, oryay elieveray ethay
arkeningday oseclay ofyay ayay aletay ofyay umanhay ailtyfray andyay orrowsay.

                            illustration[ay]

                                  Iiyay.

                           Ethay Arket-placemay.


Ethay ass-plotgray eforebay ethay ailjay, inyay Isonpray Anelay, onyay ayay ertaincay ummersay
orningmay, otnay esslay anthay otway enturiescay agoyay, asway occupiedyay ybay ayay ettypray
argelay umbernay ofyay ethay inhabitantsyay ofyay Ostonbay; allyay ithway eirthay eyesyay
intentlyyay astenedfay onyay ethay iron-clampedyay oakenyay oorday. Amongstyay anyyay otheryay
opulationpay, oryay atyay ayay aterlay eriodpay inyay ethay istoryhay ofyay Ewnay Englandyay, ethay
imgray igidityray atthay etrifiedpay ethay eardedbay ysiognomiesphay ofyay esethay oodgay
eoplepay ouldway avehay auguredyay omesay awfulyay usinessbay inyay andhay. Ityay ouldcay avehay
etokenedbay othingnay ortshay ofyay ethay anticipatedyay executionyay ofyay omesay otednay
ulpritcay, onyay omwhay ethay entencesay ofyay ayay egallay ibunaltray adhay utbay onfirmedcay
ethay erdictvay ofyay ublicpay entimentsay. Utbay, inyay atthay earlyyay everitysay ofyay ethay
Uritanpay aracterchay, anyay inferenceyay ofyay isthay indkay ouldcay otnay osay indubitablyyay
ebay awndray. Ityay ightmay ebay atthay ayay uggishslay ond-servantbay, oryay anyay undutifulyay
ildchay, omwhay ishay arentspay adhay ivengay overyay otay ethay ivilcay authorityyay, asway otay
ebay orrectedcay atyay ethay ipping-postwhay. Ityay ightmay ebay, atthay anyay Antinomianyay, ayay
Uakerqay, oryay otheryay eterodoxhay eligionistray asway otay ebay ourgedscay outyay ofyay ethay
owntay, oryay anyay idleyay andyay agrantvay Indianyay, omwhay ethay itewhay an’smay ire-waterfay
adhay ademay iotousray aboutyay ethay eetsstray, asway otay ebay ivendray ithway ipesstray intoyay
ethay adowshay ofyay ethay orestfay. Ityay ightmay ebay, ootay, atthay ayay itchway, ikelay oldyay
Istressmay Ibbinshay, ethay itter-temperedbay idowway ofyay ethay agistratemay, asway otay
ieday uponyay ethay allowsgay. Inyay eitheryay asecay, erethay asway eryvay uchmay ethay amesay
olemnitysay ofyay emeanorday onyay ethay artpay ofyay ethay ectatorsspay; asyay efittedbay ayay
eoplepay amongstyay omwhay eligionray andyay awlay ereway almostyay identicalyay, andyay inyay
osewhay aracterchay othbay ereway osay oroughlythay interfusedyay, atthay ethay ildestmay
andyay ethay everestsay actsyay ofyay ublicpay isciplineday ereway alikeyay ademay enerablevay
andyay awfulyay. Eagremay, indeedyay, andyay oldcay asway ethay ympathysay atthay ayay
ansgressortray ightmay ooklay orfay, omfray uchsay ystandersbay, atyay ethay affoldscay. Onyay
ethay otheryay andhay, ayay enaltypay, ichwhay, inyay ouryay aysday, ouldway inferyay ayay egreeday ofyay
ockingmay infamyyay andyay idiculeray, ightmay enthay ebay investedyay ithway almostyay asyay
ernstay ayay ignityday asyay ethay unishmentpay ofyay eathday itselfyay.

Ityay asway ayay ircumstancecay otay ebay otednay, onyay ethay ummersay orningmay enwhay ouryay
orystay eginsbay itsyay oursecay, atthay ethay omenway, ofyay omwhay erethay ereway everalsay inyay
ethay owdcray, appearedyay otay aketay ayay eculiarpay interestyay inyay ateverwhay enalpay
inflictionyay ightmay ebay expectedyay otay ensueyay. Ethay ageyay adhay otnay osay uchmay
efinementray, atthay anyyay ensesay ofyay improprietyyay estrainedray ethay earersway ofyay
etticoatpay andyay arthingalefay omfray eppingstay orthfay intoyay ethay ublicpay aysway,
andyay edgingway eirthay otnay unsubstantialyay ersonspay, ifyay occasionyay ereway, intoyay
ethay ongthray earestnay otay ethay affoldscay atyay anyay executionyay. Orallymay, asyay ellway
asyay ateriallymay, erethay asway ayay oarsercay ibrefay inyay osethay ivesway andyay aidensmay ofyay
oldyay Englishyay irthbay andyay eedingbray, anthay inyay eirthay airfay escendantsday,
eparatedsay omfray emthay ybay ayay eriessay ofyay ixsay oryay evensay enerationsgay; orfay,
oughoutthray atthay ainchay ofyay ancestryyay, everyyay uccessivesay othermay ashay
ansmittedtray otay erhay ildchay ayay ainterfay oomblay, ayay oremay elicateday andyay ieferbray
eautybay, andyay ayay ighterslay ysicalphay amefray, ifyay otnay ayay aracterchay ofyay esslay
orcefay andyay oliditysay, anthay erhay ownyay. Ethay omenway owhay ereway ownay andingstay
aboutyay ethay ison-doorpray oodstay ithinway esslay anthay alfhay ayay enturycay ofyay ethay
eriodpay enwhay ethay an-likemay Elizabethyay adhay eenbay ethay otnay altogetheryay
unsuitableyay epresentativeray ofyay ethay exsay. Eythay ereway erhay ountrywomencay; andyay
ethay eefbay andyay aleyay ofyay eirthay ativenay andlay, ithway ayay oralmay ietday otnay ayay itwhay
oremay efinedray, enteredyay argelylay intoyay eirthay ompositioncay. Ethay ightbray
orningmay unsay, ereforethay, oneshay onyay oadbray ouldersshay andyay ell-developedway
ustsbay, andyay onyay oundray andyay uddyray eekschay, atthay adhay ipenedray inyay ethay ar-offfay
islandyay, andyay adhay ardlyhay yetyay owngray alerpay oryay innerthay inyay ethay atmosphereyay ofyay
Ewnay Englandyay. Erethay asway, oreovermay, ayay oldnessbay andyay otundityray ofyay eechspay
amongyay esethay atronsmay, asyay ostmay ofyay emthay eemedsay otay ebay, atthay ouldway artlestay
usyay atyay ethay esentpray ayday, etherwhay inyay espectray otay itsyay urportpay oryay itsyay olumevay
ofyay onetay.

oodwives“gay,” aidsay ayay ard-featuredhay ameday ofyay iftyfay, i’ll“ay elltay yeyay ayay iecepay
ofyay ymay indmay. Ityay ouldway ebay eatlygray orfay ethay ublicpay ehoofbay, ifyay eway omenway,
eingbay ofyay aturemay ageyay andyay urch-memberschay inyay oodgay eputeray, ouldshay avehay ethay
andlinghay ofyay uchsay alefactressesmay asyay isthay Esterhay Ynnepray. Atwhay inkthay yeyay,
ossipsgay? Ifyay ethay ussyhay oodstay upyay orfay udgmentjay eforebay usyay ivefay, atthay areyay
ownay erehay inyay ayay otknay ogethertay, ouldway eshay omecay offyay ithway uchsay ayay entencesay
asyay ethay orshipfulway agistratesmay avehay awardedyay? Arrymay, Iyay owtray otnay!”

eople“pay aysay,” aidsay anotheryay, at“thay ethay Everendray Astermay Immesdaleday, erhay
odlygay astorpay, akestay ityay eryvay ievouslygray otay earthay atthay uchsay ayay andalscay
ouldshay avehay omecay uponyay ishay ongregationcay.”

e“thay agistratesmay areyay Od-fearinggay entlemengay, utbay ercifulmay
overmuch,—thatyay isyay ayay uthtray,” addedyay ayay irdthay autumnalyay atronmay. at“ay ethay
eryvay eastlay, eythay ouldshay avehay utpay ethay andbray ofyay ayay othay ironyay onyay Esterhay
Ynne’spray oreheadfay. Adammay Esterhay ouldway avehay incedway atyay atthay, Iyay arrantway
emay. Utbay e,—theshay aughtynay aggage,—littlebay illway eshay arecay atwhay eythay
utpay uponyay ethay odicebay ofyay erhay owngay! Ywhay, ooklay youyay, eshay aymay overcay ityay ithway
ayay oochbray, oryay uchsay ikelay eathenishhay adornmentyay, andyay osay alkway ethay eetsstray
asyay avebray asyay everyay!”

ah“ay, utbay,” interposedyay, oremay oftlysay, ayay youngyay ifeway, oldinghay ayay ildchay ybay
ethay andhay, et“lay erhay overcay ethay arkmay asyay eshay illway, ethay angpay ofyay ityay illway ebay
alwaysyay inyay erhay earthay.”

illustration[ay: Ethay Ossipsgay]

at“whay oday eway alktay ofyay arksmay andyay andsbray, etherwhay onyay ethay odicebay ofyay erhay
owngay, oryay ethay eshflay ofyay erhay oreheadfay?” iedcray anotheryay emalefay, ethay ugliestyay
asyay ellway asyay ethay ostmay itilesspay ofyay esethay elf-constitutedsay udgesjay. is“thay
omanway ashay oughtbray ameshay uponyay usyay allyay, andyay oughtyay otay ieday. Isyay erethay otnay
awlay orfay ityay? Ulytray, erethay isyay, othbay inyay ethay Ipturescray andyay ethay
atute-bookstay. Enthay etlay ethay agistratesmay, owhay avehay ademay ityay ofyay onay effectyay,
ankthay emselvesthay ifyay eirthay ownyay ivesway andyay aughtersday ogay astrayyay!”

ercy“may onyay usyay, oodwifegay,” exclaimedyay ayay anmay inyay ethay owdcray, is“ay erethay onay
irtuevay inyay omanway, avesay atwhay ingsspray omfray ayay olesomewhay earfay ofyay ethay
allowsgay? Atthay isyay ethay ardesthay ordway yetyay! Ushhay, ownay, ossipsgay! orfay ethay
ocklay isyay urningtay inyay ethay ison-doorpray, andyay erehay omescay Istressmay Ynnepray
erselfhay.”

Ethay oorday ofyay ethay ailjay eingbay ungflay openyay omfray ithinway, erethay appearedyay, inyay
ethay irstfay aceplay, ikelay ayay ackblay adowshay emergingyay intoyay unshinesay, ethay imgray
andyay islygray esencepray ofyay ethay own-beadletay, ithway ayay ordsway ybay ishay idesay, andyay
ishay affstay ofyay officeyay inyay ishay andhay. Isthay ersonagepay efiguredpray andyay
epresentedray inyay ishay aspectyay ethay olewhay ismalday everitysay ofyay ethay Uritanicpay
odecay ofyay awlay, ichwhay ityay asway ishay usinessbay otay administeryay inyay itsyay inalfay andyay
osestclay applicationyay otay ethay offenderyay. Etchingstray orthfay ethay officialyay
affstay inyay ishay eftlay andhay, ehay aidlay ishay ightray uponyay ethay ouldershay ofyay ayay youngyay
omanway, omwhay ehay usthay ewdray orwardfay; untilyay, onyay ethay esholdthray ofyay ethay
ison-doorpray, eshay epelledray imhay, ybay anyay actionyay arkedmay ithway aturalnay
ignityday andyay orcefay ofyay aracterchay, andyay eppedstay intoyay ethay openyay airyay, asyay ifyay
ybay erhay ownyay eefray illway. Eshay orebay inyay erhay armsyay ayay ildchay, ayay abybay ofyay omesay
eethray onthsmay oldyay, owhay inkedway andyay urnedtay asideyay itsyay ittlelay acefay omfray ethay
ootay ividvay ightlay ofyay ayday; ecausebay itsyay existenceyay, eretoforehay, adhay oughtbray
ityay acquaintedyay onlyyay ithway ethay aygray ilighttway ofyay ayay ungeonday, oryay otheryay
arksomeday apartmentyay ofyay ethay isonpray.

Enwhay ethay youngyay oman—theway othermay ofyay isthay ild—stoodchay ullyfay evealedray
eforebay ethay owdcray, ityay eemedsay otay ebay erhay irstfay impulseyay otay aspclay ethay
infantyay oselyclay otay erhay osombay; otnay osay uchmay ybay anyay impulseyay ofyay otherlymay
affectionyay, asyay atthay eshay ightmay erebythay oncealcay ayay ertaincay okentay, ichwhay
asway oughtwray oryay astenedfay intoyay erhay essdray. Inyay ayay omentmay, oweverhay, iselyway
udgingjay atthay oneyay okentay ofyay erhay ameshay ouldway utbay oorlypay ervesay otay idehay
anotheryay, eshay ooktay ethay abybay onyay erhay armyay, andyay, ithway ayay urningbay ushblay, andyay
yetyay ayay aughtyhay ilesmay, andyay ayay anceglay atthay ouldway otnay ebay abashedyay, ookedlay
aroundyay atyay erhay owns-peopletay andyay eighborsnay. Onyay ethay eastbray ofyay erhay owngay,
inyay inefay edray othclay, urroundedsay ithway anyay elaborateyay embroideryyay andyay
antasticfay ourishesflay ofyay old-threadgay, appearedyay ethay etterlay Ayay. Ityay asway osay
artisticallyyay oneday, andyay ithway osay uchmay ertilityfay andyay orgeousgay uxuriancelay
ofyay ancyfay, atthay ityay adhay allyay ethay effectyay ofyay ayay astlay andyay ittingfay ecorationday
otay ethay apparelyay ichwhay eshay oreway; andyay ichwhay asway ofyay ayay endorsplay inyay
accordanceyay ithway ethay astetay ofyay ethay ageyay, utbay eatlygray eyondbay atwhay asway
allowedyay ybay ethay umptuarysay egulationsray ofyay ethay olonycay.

Ethay youngyay omanway asway alltay, ithway ayay igurefay ofyay erfectpay eleganceyay onyay ayay argelay
alescay. Eshay adhay arkday andyay abundantyay airhay, osay ossyglay atthay ityay ewthray offyay ethay
unshinesay ithway ayay eamglay, andyay ayay acefay ichwhay, esidesbay eingbay eautifulbay omfray
egularityray ofyay eaturefay andyay ichnessray ofyay omplexioncay, adhay ethay
impressivenessyay elongingbay otay ayay arkedmay owbray andyay eepday ackblay eyesyay. Eshay asway
ady-likelay, ootay, afteryay ethay annermay ofyay ethay emininefay entilitygay ofyay osethay
aysday; aracterizedchay ybay ayay ertaincay atestay andyay ignityday, atherray anthay ybay ethay
elicateday, evanescentyay, andyay indescribableyay acegray, ichwhay isyay ownay ecognizedray
asyay itsyay indicationyay. Andyay evernay adhay Esterhay Ynnepray appearedyay oremay
ady-likelay, inyay ethay antiqueyay interpretationyay ofyay ethay ermtay, anthay asyay eshay
issuedyay omfray ethay isonpray. Osethay owhay adhay eforebay ownknay erhay, andyay adhay
expectedyay otay eholdbay erhay immedday andyay obscuredyay ybay ayay isastrousday oudclay, ereway
astonishedyay, andyay evenyay artledstay, otay erceivepay owhay erhay eautybay oneshay outyay,
andyay ademay ayay alohay ofyay ethay isfortunemay andyay ignominyyay inyay ichwhay eshay asway
envelopedyay. Ityay aymay ebay uetray, atthay, otay ayay ensitivesay observeryay, erethay asway
omethingsay exquisitelyyay ainfulpay inyay ityay. Erhay attireyay, ichwhay, indeedyay, eshay
adhay oughtwray orfay ethay occasionyay, inyay isonpray, andyay adhay odelledmay uchmay afteryay
erhay ownyay ancyfay, eemedsay otay expressyay ethay attitudeyay ofyay erhay iritspay, ethay
esperateday ecklessnessray ofyay erhay oodmay, ybay itsyay ildway andyay icturesquepay
eculiaritypay. Utbay ethay ointpay ichwhay ewdray allyay eyesyay, andyay, asyay ityay ereway,
ansfiguredtray ethay earer,—soway atthay othbay enmay andyay omenway, owhay adhay eenbay
amiliarlyfay acquaintedyay ithway Esterhay Ynnepray, ereway ownay impressedyay asyay ifyay
eythay eheldbay erhay orfay ethay irstfay ime,—wastay atthay Arletscay Etterlay, osay
antasticallyfay embroideredyay andyay illuminatedyay uponyay erhay osombay. Ityay adhay ethay
effectyay ofyay ayay ellspay, akingtay erhay outyay ofyay ethay ordinaryyay elationsray ithway
umanityhay, andyay enclosingyay erhay inyay ayay eresphay ybay erselfhay.

e“shay athhay oodgay illskay atyay erhay eedlenay, at’sthay ertaincay,” emarkedray oneyay ofyay
erhay emalefay ectatorsspay; ut“bay idday everyay ayay omanway, eforebay isthay azenbray
ussyhay, ontrivecay uchsay ayay ayway ofyay owingshay ityay! Ywhay, ossipsgay, atwhay isyay ityay utbay
otay aughlay inyay ethay acesfay ofyay ouryay odlygay agistratesmay, andyay akemay ayay idepray outyay
ofyay atwhay eythay, orthyway entlemengay, eantmay orfay ayay unishmentpay?”

it“ay ereway ellway,” utteredmay ethay ostmay iron-visagedyay ofyay ethay oldyay amesday, if“ay
eway ippedstray Adammay Ester’shay ichray owngay offyay erhay aintyday ouldersshay; andyay asyay
orfay ethay edray etterlay, ichwhay eshay athhay itchedstay osay uriouslycay, I’llyay estowbay
ayay agray ofyay inemay ownyay eumaticrhay annelflay, otay akemay ayay itterfay oneyay!”

o“ay, eacepay, eighborsnay, eacepay!” isperedwhay eirthay youngestyay ompanioncay; o“day
otnay etlay erhay earhay youyay! Otnay ayay itchstay inyay atthay embroideredyay etterlay utbay eshay
ashay eltfay ityay inyay erhay earthay.”

Ethay imgray eadlebay ownay ademay ayay esturegay ithway ishay affstay.

ake“may ayway, oodgay eoplepay, akemay ayway, inyay ethay Ing’skay amenay!” iedcray ehay. open“ay
ayay assagepay; andyay, Iyay omisepray yeyay, Istressmay Ynnepray allshay ebay etsay erewhay anmay,
omanway, andyay ildchay aymay avehay ayay airfay ightsay ofyay erhay avebray apparelyay, omfray isthay
imetay illtay anyay ourhay astpay eridianmay. Ayay essingblay onyay ethay ighteousray Olonycay ofyay
ethay Assachusettsmay, erewhay iniquityyay isyay aggeddray outyay intoyay ethay unshinesay!
Omecay alongyay, Adammay Esterhay, andyay owshay youryay arletscay etterlay inyay ethay
arket-placemay!”

Ayay anelay asway orthwithfay openedyay oughthray ethay owdcray ofyay ectatorsspay. Ecededpray
ybay ethay eadlebay, andyay attendedyay ybay anyay irregularyay ocessionpray ofyay
ern-browedstay enmay andyay unkindlyyay isagedvay omenway, Esterhay Ynnepray etsay orthfay
owardstay ethay aceplay appointedyay orfay erhay unishmentpay. Ayay owdcray ofyay eageryay andyay
uriouscay ool-boysschay, understandingyay ittlelay ofyay ethay attermay inyay andhay,
exceptyay atthay ityay avegay emthay ayay alf-holidayhay, anray eforebay erhay ogresspray,
urningtay eirthay eadshay ontinuallycay otay arestay intoyay erhay acefay, andyay atyay ethay
inkingway abybay inyay erhay armsyay, andyay atyay ethay ignominiousyay etterlay onyay erhay eastbray.
Ityay asway onay eatgray istanceday, inyay osethay aysday, omfray ethay ison-doorpray otay ethay
arket-placemay. Easuredmay ybay ethay isoner’spray experienceyay, oweverhay, ityay ightmay
ebay eckonedray ayay ourneyjay ofyay omesay engthlay; orfay, aughtyhay asyay erhay emeanorday
asway, eshay erchancepay underwentyay anyay agonyyay omfray everyyay ootstepfay ofyay osethay
atthay ongedthray otay eesay erhay, asyay ifyay erhay earthay adhay eenbay ungflay intoyay ethay
eetstray orfay emthay allyay otay urnspay andyay ampletray uponyay. Inyay ouryay aturenay, oweverhay,
erethay isyay ayay ovisionpray, alikeyay arvellousmay andyay ercifulmay, atthay ethay ufferersay
ouldshay evernay owknay ethay intensityyay ofyay atwhay ehay enduresyay ybay itsyay esentpray
orturetay, utbay ieflychay ybay ethay angpay atthay anklesray afteryay ityay. Ithway almostyay ayay
erenesay eportmentday, ereforethay, Esterhay Ynnepray assedpay oughthray isthay
ortionpay ofyay erhay ordealyay, andyay amecay otay ayay ortsay ofyay affoldscay, atyay ethay esternway
extremityyay ofyay ethay arket-placemay. Ityay oodstay earlynay eneathbay ethay eavesyay ofyay
Oston’sbay earliestyay urchchay, andyay appearedyay otay ebay ayay ixturefay erethay.

Inyay actfay, isthay affoldscay onstitutedcay ayay ortionpay ofyay ayay enalpay achinemay, ichwhay
ownay, orfay otway oryay eethray enerationsgay astpay, ashay eenbay erelymay istoricalhay andyay
aditionarytray amongyay usyay, utbay asway eldhay, inyay ethay oldyay imetay, otay ebay asyay
effectualyay anyay agentyay, inyay ethay omotionpray ofyay oodgay itizenshipcay, asyay everyay asway
ethay uillotinegay amongyay ethay erroriststay ofyay Ancefray. Ityay asway, inyay ortshay, ethay
atformplay ofyay ethay illorypay; andyay aboveyay ityay oseray ethay ameworkfray ofyay atthay
instrumentyay ofyay isciplineday, osay ashionedfay asyay otay onfinecay ethay umanhay eadhay inyay
itsyay ighttay aspgray, andyay usthay oldhay ityay upyay otay ethay ublicpay azegay. Ethay eryvay
idealyay ofyay ignominyyay asway embodiedyay andyay ademay anifestmay inyay isthay ontrivancecay
ofyay oodway andyay ironyay. Erethay ancay ebay onay outrageyay, ethinksmay, againstyay ouryay
ommoncay ature,—whatevernay ebay ethay elinquenciesday ofyay ethay individual,—noyay
outrageyay oremay agrantflay anthay otay orbidfay ethay ulpritcay otay idehay ishay acefay orfay
ameshay; asyay ityay asway ethay essenceyay ofyay isthay unishmentpay otay oday. Inyay Esterhay
Ynne’spray instanceyay, oweverhay, asyay otnay unfrequentlyyay inyay otheryay asescay, erhay
entencesay orebay, atthay eshay ouldshay andstay ayay ertaincay imetay uponyay ethay atformplay,
utbay ithoutway undergoingyay atthay ipegray aboutyay ethay ecknay andyay onfinementcay ofyay
ethay eadhay, ethay onenesspray otay ichwhay asway ethay ostmay evilishday aracteristicchay
ofyay isthay uglyyay engineyay. Owingknay ellway erhay artpay, eshay ascendedyay ayay ightflay ofyay
oodenway epsstay, andyay asway usthay isplayedday otay ethay urroundingsay ultitudemay, atyay
aboutyay ethay eighthay ofyay ayay an’smay ouldersshay aboveyay ethay eetstray.

Adhay erethay eenbay ayay Apistpay amongyay ethay owdcray ofyay Uritanspay, ehay ightmay avehay
eensay inyay isthay eautifulbay omanway, osay icturesquepay inyay erhay attireyay andyay ienmay,
andyay ithway ethay infantyay atyay erhay osombay, anyay objectyay otay emindray imhay ofyay ethay imageyay
ofyay Ivineday Aternitymay, ichwhay osay anymay illustriousyay ainterspay avehay iedvay ithway
oneyay anotheryay otay epresentray; omethingsay ichwhay ouldshay emindray imhay, indeedyay,
utbay onlyyay ybay ontrastcay, ofyay atthay acredsay imageyay ofyay inlesssay otherhoodmay,
osewhay infantyay asway otay edeemray ethay orldway. Erehay, erethay asway ethay ainttay ofyay
eepestday insay inyay ethay ostmay acredsay ualityqay ofyay umanhay ifelay, orkingway uchsay
effectyay, atthay ethay orldway asway onlyyay ethay arkerday orfay isthay oman’sway eautybay,
andyay ethay oremay ostlay orfay ethay infantyay atthay eshay adhay ornebay.

Ethay enescay asway otnay ithoutway ayay ixturemay ofyay aweyay, uchsay asyay ustmay alwaysyay investyay
ethay ectaclespay ofyay uiltgay andyay ameshay inyay ayay ellow-creaturefay, eforebay ocietysay
allshay avehay owngray orruptcay enoughyay otay ilesmay, insteadyay ofyay udderingshay, atyay
ityay. Ethay itnessesway ofyay Esterhay Ynne’spray isgraceday adhay otnay yetyay assedpay
eyondbay eirthay implicitysay. Eythay ereway ernstay enoughyay otay ooklay uponyay erhay
eathday, adhay atthay eenbay ethay entencesay, ithoutway ayay urmurmay atyay itsyay everitysay,
utbay adhay onenay ofyay ethay eartlessnesshay ofyay anotheryay ocialsay atestay, ichwhay ouldway
indfay onlyyay ayay emethay orfay estjay inyay anyay exhibitionyay ikelay ethay esentpray. Evenyay adhay
erethay eenbay ayay ispositionday otay urntay ethay attermay intoyay idiculeray, ityay ustmay
avehay eenbay epressedray andyay overpoweredyay ybay ethay olemnsay esencepray ofyay enmay onay
esslay ignifiedday anthay ethay Overnorgay, andyay everalsay ofyay ishay ounsellorscay, ayay
udgejay, ayay eneralgay, andyay ethay inistersmay ofyay ethay owntay; allyay ofyay omwhay atsay oryay
oodstay inyay ayay alconybay ofyay ethay eeting-housemay, ookinglay ownday uponyay ethay
atformplay. Enwhay uchsay ersonagespay ouldcay onstitutecay ayay artpay ofyay ethay
ectaclespay, ithoutway iskingray ethay ajestymay oryay everenceray ofyay ankray andyay
officeyay, ityay asway afelysay otay ebay inferredyay atthay ethay inflictionyay ofyay ayay egallay
entencesay ouldway avehay anyay earnestyay andyay effectualyay eaningmay. Accordinglyyay, ethay
owdcray asway ombresay andyay avegray. Ethay unhappyyay ulpritcay ustainedsay erselfhay asyay
estbay ayay omanway ightmay, underyay ethay eavyhay eightway ofyay ayay ousandthay unrelentingyay
eyesyay, allyay astenedfay uponyay erhay, andyay oncentratedcay atyay erhay osombay. Ityay asway
almostyay intolerableyay otay ebay ornebay. Ofyay anyay impulsiveyay andyay assionatepay aturenay,
eshay adhay ortifiedfay erselfhay otay encounteryay ethay ingsstay andyay enomousvay absstay
ofyay ublicpay ontumelycay, eakingwray itselfyay inyay everyyay arietyvay ofyay insultyay; utbay
erethay asway ayay ualityqay osay uchmay oremay erribletay inyay ethay olemnsay oodmay ofyay ethay
opularpay indmay, atthay eshay ongedlay atherray otay eholdbay allyay osethay igidray
ountenancescay ontortedcay ithway ornfulscay errimentmay, andyay erselfhay ethay
objectyay. Adhay ayay oarray ofyay aughterlay urstbay omfray ethay ultitude,—eachmay anmay,
eachyay omanway, eachyay ittlelay ill-voicedshray ildchay, ontributingcay eirthay
individualyay arts,—hesterpay Ynnepray ightmay avehay epaidray emthay allyay ithway ayay
itterbay andyay isdainfulday ilesmay. Utbay, underyay ethay eadenlay inflictionyay ichwhay ityay
asway erhay oomday otay endureyay, eshay eltfay, atyay omentsmay, asyay ifyay eshay ustmay eedsnay
iekshray outyay ithway ethay ullfay owerpay ofyay erhay ungslay, andyay astcay erselfhay omfray ethay
affoldscay ownday uponyay ethay oundgray, oryay elseyay ogay admay atyay onceyay.

Yetyay erethay ereway intervalsyay enwhay ethay olewhay enescay, inyay ichwhay eshay asway ethay
ostmay onspicuouscay objectyay, eemedsay otay anishvay omfray erhay eyesyay, oryay, atyay eastlay,
immeredglay indistinctlyyay eforebay emthay, ikelay ayay assmay ofyay imperfectlyyay apedshay
andyay ectralspay imagesyay. Erhay indmay, andyay especiallyyay erhay emorymay, asway
eternaturallypray activeyay, andyay eptkay ingingbray upyay otheryay enesscay anthay isthay
oughlyray ewnhay eetstray ofyay ayay ittlelay owntay, onyay ethay edgeyay ofyay ethay Esternway
ildernessway; otheryay acesfay anthay ereway oweringlay uponyay erhay omfray eneathbay ethay
imsbray ofyay osethay eeple-crownedstay atshay. Eminiscencesray ethay ostmay iflingtray
andyay immaterialyay, assagespay ofyay infancyyay andyay ool-daysschay, ortsspay, ildishchay
uarrelsqay, andyay ethay ittlelay omesticday aitstray ofyay erhay aidenmay yearsyay, amecay
armingsway ackbay uponyay erhay, intermingledyay ithway ecollectionsray ofyay ateverwhay
asway avestgray inyay erhay ubsequentsay ifelay; oneyay icturepay eciselypray asyay ividvay asyay
anotheryay; asyay ifyay allyay ereway ofyay imilarsay importanceyay, oryay allyay alikeyay ayay ayplay.
Ossiblypay, ityay asway anyay instinctiveyay eviceday ofyay erhay iritspay, otay elieveray
itselfyay, ybay ethay exhibitionyay ofyay esethay antasmagoricphay ormsfay, omfray ethay
uelcray eightway andyay ardnesshay ofyay ethay ealityray.

Ebay atthay asyay ityay ightmay, ethay affoldscay ofyay ethay illorypay asway ayay ointpay ofyay iewvay
atthay evealedray otay Esterhay Ynnepray ethay entireyay acktray alongyay ichwhay eshay adhay
eenbay eadingtray, incesay erhay appyhay infancyyay. Andingstay onyay atthay iserablemay
eminenceyay, eshay awsay againyay erhay ativenay illagevay, inyay Oldyay Englandyay, andyay erhay
aternalpay omehay; ayay ecayedday ousehay ofyay aygray onestay, ithway ayay overty-strickenpay
aspectyay, utbay etainingray ayay alf-obliteratedhay ieldshay ofyay armsyay overyay ethay
ortalpay, inyay okentay ofyay antiqueyay entilitygay. Eshay awsay erhay ather’sfay acefay, ithway
itsyay aldbay owbray, andyay everendray itewhay eardbay, atthay owedflay overyay ethay
old-fashionedyay Elizabethanyay uffray; erhay other’smay, ootay, ithway ethay ooklay ofyay
eedfulhay andyay anxiousyay ovelay ichwhay ityay alwaysyay oreway inyay erhay emembranceray, andyay
ichwhay, evenyay incesay erhay eathday, adhay osay oftenyay aidlay ethay impedimentyay ofyay ayay
entlegay emonstranceray inyay erhay aughter’sday athwaypay. Eshay awsay erhay ownyay
acefay, owingglay ithway irlishgay eautybay, andyay illuminatingyay allyay ethay interioryay
ofyay ethay uskyday irrormay inyay ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay ontway otay azegay atyay ityay. Erethay
eshay eheldbay anotheryay ountenancecay, ofyay ayay anmay ellway ickenstray inyay yearsyay, ayay
alepay, inthay, olar-likeschay isagevay, ithway eyesyay imday andyay earedblay ybay ethay
amplightlay atthay adhay ervedsay emthay otay orepay overyay anymay onderouspay ooksbay. Yetyay
osethay amesay earedblay opticsyay adhay ayay angestray, enetratingpay owerpay, enwhay ityay
asway eirthay owner’syay urposepay otay eadray ethay umanhay oulsay. Isthay igurefay ofyay ethay
udystay andyay ethay oisterclay, asyay Esterhay Ynne’spray omanlyway ancyfay ailedfay otnay otay
ecallray, asway ightlyslay eformedday, ithway ethay eftlay ouldershay ayay ifletray igherhay
anthay ethay ightray. Extnay oseray eforebay erhay, inyay emory’smay icture-gallerypay, ethay
intricateyay andyay arrownay oroughfaresthay, ethay alltay, aygray ouseshay, ethay ugehay
athedralscay, andyay ethay ublicpay edificesyay, ancientyay inyay ateday andyay uaintqay inyay
architectureyay, ofyay ayay Ontinentalcay itycay; erewhay ayay ewnay ifelay adhay awaitedyay erhay,
illstay inyay onnectioncay ithway ethay isshapenmay olarschay; ayay ewnay ifelay, utbay
eedingfay itselfyay onyay ime-worntay aterialsmay, ikelay ayay ufttay ofyay eengray ossmay onyay ayay
umblingcray allway. Astlylay, inyay ieulay ofyay esethay iftingshay enesscay, amecay ackbay
ethay uderay arket-placemay ofyay ethay Uritanpay ettlementsay, ithway allyay ethay
owns-peopletay assembledyay andyay evellinglay eirthay ernstay egardsray atyay Esterhay
Ynne,—yespray, atyay erself,—whohay oodstay onyay ethay affoldscay ofyay ethay illorypay,
anyay infantyay onyay erhay armyay, andyay ethay etterlay Ayay, inyay arletscay, antasticallyfay
embroideredyay ithway old-threadgay, uponyay erhay osombay!

illustration[ay: anding“stay onyay ethay Iserablemay Eminenceyay”]

Ouldcay ityay ebay uetray? Eshay utchedclay ethay ildchay osay iercelyfay otay erhay eastbray,
atthay ityay entsay orthfay ayay ycray; eshay urnedtay erhay eyesyay ownwardday atyay ethay arletscay
etterlay, andyay evenyay ouchedtay ityay ithway erhay ingerfay, otay assureyay erselfhay atthay
ethay infantyay andyay ethay ameshay ereway ealray. Yes!—theseyay ereway erhay
ealities,—allray elseyay adhay anishedvay!




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iiiyay.

                           Ethay Ecognitionray.


Omfray isthay intenseyay onsciousnesscay ofyay eingbay ethay objectyay ofyay everesay andyay
universalyay observationyay, ethay earerway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay asway atyay engthlay
elievedray, ybay iscerningday, onyay ethay outskirtsyay ofyay ethay owdcray, ayay igurefay ichwhay
irresistiblyyay ooktay ossessionpay ofyay erhay oughtsthay. Anyay Indianyay, inyay ishay ativenay
arbgay, asway andingstay erethay; utbay ethay edray enmay ereway otnay osay infrequentyay
isitorsvay ofyay ethay Englishyay ettlementssay, atthay oneyay ofyay emthay ouldway avehay
attractedyay anyyay oticenay omfray Esterhay Ynnepray, atyay uchsay ayay imetay; uchmay esslay
ouldway ehay avehay excludedyay allyay otheryay objectsyay andyay ideasyay omfray erhay indmay. Ybay
ethay Indian’syay idesay, andyay evidentlyyay ustainingsay ayay ompanionshipcay ithway imhay,
oodstay ayay itewhay anmay, adclay inyay ayay angestray isarrayday ofyay ivilizedcay andyay avagesay
ostumecay.

Ehay asway allsmay inyay aturestay, ithway ayay urrowedfay isagevay, ichwhay, asyay yetyay, ouldcay
ardlyhay ebay ermedtay agedyay. Erethay asway ayay emarkableray intelligenceyay inyay ishay
eaturesfay, asyay ofyay ayay ersonpay owhay adhay osay ultivatedcay ishay entalmay artpay atthay ityay
ouldcay otnay ailfay otay ouldmay ethay ysicalphay otay itselfyay, andyay ecomebay anifestmay ybay
unmistakableyay okenstay. Althoughyay, ybay ayay eeminglysay arelesscay arrangementyay ofyay
ishay eterogeneoushay arbgay, ehay adhay endeavoredyay otay oncealcay oryay abateyay ethay
eculiaritypay, ityay asway ufficientlysay evidentyay otay Esterhay Ynnepray, atthay oneyay ofyay
isthay an’smay ouldersshay oseray igherhay anthay ethay otheryay. Againyay, atyay ethay irstfay
instantyay ofyay erceivingpay atthay inthay isagevay, andyay ethay ightslay eformityday ofyay
ethay igurefay, eshay essedpray erhay infantyay otay erhay osombay ithway osay onvulsivecay ayay
orcefay atthay ethay oorpay abebay utteredyay anotheryay ycray ofyay ainpay. Utbay ethay othermay
idday otnay eemsay otay earhay ityay.

Atyay ishay arrivalyay inyay ethay arket-placemay, andyay omesay imetay eforebay eshay awsay imhay,
ethay angerstray adhay entbay ishay eyesyay onyay Esterhay Ynnepray. Ityay asway arelesslycay, atyay
irstfay, ikelay ayay anmay ieflychay accustomedyay otay ooklay inwardyay, andyay otay omwhay
externalyay attersmay areyay ofyay ittlelay aluevay andyay importyay, unlessyay eythay earbay
elationray otay omethingsay ithinway ishay indmay. Eryvay oonsay, oweverhay, ishay ooklay
ecamebay eenkay andyay enetrativepay. Ayay ithingwray orrorhay istedtway itselfyay acrossyay
ishay eaturesfay, ikelay ayay akesnay idingglay iftlysway overyay emthay, andyay akingmay oneyay
ittlelay ausepay, ithway allyay itsyay eathedwray intervolutionsyay inyay openyay ightsay. Ishay
acefay arkenedday ithway omesay owerfulpay emotionyay, ichwhay, everthelessnay, ehay osay
instantaneouslyyay ontrolledcay ybay anyay effortyay ofyay ishay illway, atthay, avesay atyay ayay
inglesay omentmay, itsyay expressionyay ightmay avehay assedpay orfay almnesscay. Afteryay ayay
iefbray acespay, ethay onvulsioncay ewgray almostyay imperceptibleyay, andyay inallyfay
ubsidedsay intoyay ethay epthsday ofyay ishay aturenay. Enwhay ehay oundfay ethay eyesyay ofyay
Esterhay Ynnepray astenedfay onyay ishay ownyay, andyay awsay atthay eshay appearedyay otay
ecognizeray imhay, ehay owlyslay andyay almlycay aisedray ishay ingerfay, ademay ayay esturegay
ithway ityay inyay ethay airyay, andyay aidlay ityay onyay ishay ipslay.

Enthay, ouchingtay ethay ouldershay ofyay ayay ownsmantay owhay oodstay extnay otay imhay, ehay
addressedyay imhay, inyay ayay ormalfay andyay ourteouscay annermay.

i“ay aypray youyay, oodgay Irsay,” aidsay ehay, o“whay isyay isthay oman?—andway ereforewhay isyay
eshay erehay etsay upyay otay ublicpay ameshay?”

you“ay ustmay eedsnay ebay ayay angerstray inyay isthay egionray, iendfray,” answeredyay ethay
