ownsmantay, ookinglay uriouslycay atyay ethay uestionerqay andyay ishay avagesay
ompanioncay, else“ay youyay ouldway urelysay avehay eardhay ofyay Istressmay Esterhay
Ynnepray, andyay erhay evilyay oingsday. Eshay athhay aisedray ayay eatgray andalscay, Iyay
omisepray youyay, inyay odlygay Astermay Immesdale’sday urchchay.”

you“ay aysay ulytray,” epliedray ethay otheryay. i“ay amyay ayay angerstray, andyay avehay eenbay ayay
andererway, orelysay againstyay ymay illway. Iyay avehay etmay ithway ievousgray ishapsmay ybay
easay andyay andlay, andyay avehay eenbay onglay eldhay inyay ondsbay amongyay ethay eathen-folkhay,
otay ethay outhwardsay; andyay amyay ownay oughtbray itherhay ybay isthay Indianyay, otay ebay
edeemedray outyay ofyay ymay aptivitycay. Illway ityay easeplay youyay, ereforethay, otay elltay
emay ofyay Esterhay Ynne’s,—havepray Iyay erhay amenay ightly?—ofray isthay oman’sway
offencesyay, andyay atwhay ashay oughtbray erhay otay yonderyay affoldscay?”

uly“tray, iendfray; andyay ethinksmay ityay ustmay addenglay youryay earthay, afteryay youryay
oublestray andyay ojournsay inyay ethay ildernessway,” aidsay ethay ownsmantay, o“tay indfay
yourselfyay, atyay engthlay, inyay ayay andlay erewhay iniquityyay isyay earchedsay outyay, andyay
unishedpay inyay ethay ightsay ofyay ulersray andyay eoplepay; asyay erehay inyay ouryay odlygay Ewnay
Englandyay. Yonderyay omanway, Irsay, youyay ustmay owknay, asway ethay ifeway ofyay ayay ertaincay
earnedlay anmay, Englishyay ybay irthbay, utbay owhay adhay onglay eltdway inyay Amsterdamyay,
encewhay, omesay oodgay imetay agoneyay, ehay asway indedmay otay osscray overyay andyay astcay inyay
ishay otlay ithway usyay ofyay ethay Assachusettsmay. Otay isthay urposepay, ehay entsay ishay
ifeway eforebay imhay, emainingray imselfhay otay ooklay afteryay omesay ecessarynay
affairsyay. Arrymay, oodgay Irsay, inyay omesay otway yearsyay, oryay esslay, atthay ethay omanway
ashay eenbay ayay ellerdway erehay inyay Ostonbay, onay idingstay avehay omecay ofyay isthay
earnedlay entlemangay, Astermay Ynnepray; andyay ishay youngyay ifeway, ooklay youyay, eingbay
eftlay otay erhay ownyay isguidancemay—”

ah!—aha!—i“ay onceivecay youyay,” aidsay ethay angerstray, ithway ayay itterbay ilesmay.
o“say earnedlay ayay anmay asyay youyay eakspay ofyay ouldshay avehay earnedlay isthay ootay inyay ishay
ooksbay. Andyay owhay, ybay youryay avorfay, Irsay, aymay ebay ethay atherfay ofyay yonderyay
abe—itbay isyay omesay eethray oryay ourfay onthsmay oldyay, Iyay ouldshay udge—whichjay
Istressmay Ynnepray isyay oldinghay inyay erhay armsyay?”

of“ay ayay uthtray, iendfray, atthay attermay emainethray ayay iddleray; andyay ethay Anielday
owhay allshay expoundyay ityay isyay yetyay a-wantingyay,” answeredyay ethay ownsmantay. adam“may
Esterhay absolutelyyay efusethray otay eakspay, andyay ethay agistratesmay avehay aidlay
eirthay eadshay ogethertay inyay ainvay. Eradventurepay ethay uiltygay oneyay andsstay
ookinglay onyay atyay isthay adsay ectaclespay, unknownyay ofyay anmay, andyay orgettingfay atthay
Odgay eessay imhay.”

e“thay earnedlay anmay,” observedyay ethay angerstray, ithway anotheryay ilesmay, ould“shay
omecay imselfhay, otay ooklay intoyay ethay ysterymay.”

it“ay ehoovesbay imhay ellway, ifyay ehay ebay illstay inyay ifelay,” espondedray ethay
ownsmantay. ow“nay, oodgay Irsay, ouryay Assachusettsmay agistracymay, ethinkingbay
emselvesthay atthay isthay omanway isyay youthfulyay andyay airfay, andyay oubtlessday asway
onglystray emptedtay otay erhay all,—andfay atthay, oreovermay, asyay isyay ostmay ikelylay,
erhay usbandhay aymay ebay atyay ethay ottombay ofyay ethay ea,—theysay avehay otnay eenbay oldbay
otay utpay inyay orcefay ethay extremityyay ofyay ouryay ighteousray awlay againstyay erhay. Ethay
enaltypay ereofthay isyay eathday. Utbay inyay eirthay eatgray ercymay andyay endernesstay ofyay
earthay, eythay avehay oomedday Istressmay Ynnepray otay andstay onlyyay ayay acespay ofyay eethray
ourshay onyay ethay atformplay ofyay ethay illorypay, andyay enthay andyay ereafterthay, orfay ethay
emainderray ofyay erhay aturalnay ifelay, otay earway ayay arkmay ofyay ameshay uponyay erhay
osombay.”

a“ay iseway entencesay!” emarkedray ethay angerstray, avelygray owingbay ishay eadhay.
us“thay eshay illway ebay ayay ivinglay ermonsay againstyay insay, untilyay ethay ignominiousyay
etterlay ebay engravedyay uponyay erhay ombstonetay. Ityay irksyay emay, everthelessnay, atthay
ethay artnerpay ofyay erhay iniquityyay ouldshay otnay, atyay eastlay, andstay onyay ethay
affoldscay ybay erhay idesay. Utbay ehay illway ebay own!—heknay illway ebay own!—heknay
illway ebay ownknay!”

Ehay owedbay ourteouslycay otay ethay ommunicativecay ownsmantay, andyay, isperingwhay ayay
ewfay ordsway otay ishay Indianyay attendantyay, eythay othbay ademay eirthay ayway oughthray
ethay owdcray.

Ilewhay isthay assedpay, Esterhay Ynnepray adhay eenbay andingstay onyay erhay edestalpay,
illstay ithway ayay ixedfay azegay owardstay ethay angerstray; osay ixedfay ayay azegay, atthay,
atyay omentsmay ofyay intenseyay absorptionyay, allyay otheryay objectsyay inyay ethay isiblevay
orldway eemedsay otay anishvay, eavinglay onlyyay imhay andyay erhay. Uchsay anyay interviewyay,
erhapspay, ouldway avehay eenbay oremay erribletay anthay evenyay otay eetmay imhay asyay eshay
ownay idday, ithway ethay othay, id-daymay unsay urningbay ownday uponyay erhay acefay, andyay
ightinglay upyay itsyay ameshay; ithway ethay arletscay okentay ofyay infamyyay onyay erhay eastbray;
ithway ethay in-bornsay infantyay inyay erhay armsyay; ithway ayay olewhay eoplepay, awndray orthfay
asyay otay ayay estivalfay, aringstay atyay ethay eaturesfay atthay ouldshay avehay eenbay eensay
onlyyay inyay ethay uietqay eamglay ofyay ethay iresidefay, inyay ethay appyhay adowshay ofyay ayay
omehay, oryay eneathbay ayay atronlymay eilvay, atyay urchchay. Eadfuldray asyay ityay asway, eshay
asway onsciouscay ofyay ayay eltershay inyay ethay esencepray ofyay esethay ousandthay
itnessesway. Ityay asway etterbay otay andstay usthay, ithway osay anymay etwixtbay imhay andyay
erhay, anthay otay eetgray imhay, acefay otay acefay, eythay otway aloneyay. Eshay edflay orfay
efugeray, asyay ityay ereway, otay ethay ublicpay exposureyay, andyay eadeddray ethay omentmay
enwhay itsyay otectionpray ouldshay ebay ithdrawnway omfray erhay. Involvedyay inyay esethay
oughtsthay, eshay arcelyscay eardhay ayay oicevay ehindbay erhay, untilyay ityay adhay epeatedray
erhay amenay oremay anthay onceyay, inyay ayay oudlay andyay olemnsay onetay, audibleyay otay ethay
olewhay ultitudemay.

earken“hay untoyay emay, Esterhay Ynnepray!” aidsay ethay oicevay.

Ityay ashay alreadyyay eenbay oticednay, atthay irectlyday overyay ethay atformplay onyay ichwhay
Esterhay Ynnepray oodstay asway ayay indkay ofyay alconybay, oryay openyay allerygay, appendedyay
otay ethay eeting-housemay. Ityay asway ethay aceplay encewhay oclamationspray ereway ontway
otay ebay ademay, amidstyay anyay assemblageyay ofyay ethay agistracymay, ithway allyay ethay
eremonialcay atthay attendedyay uchsay ublicpay observancesyay inyay osethay aysday. Erehay,
otay itnessway ethay enescay ichwhay eway areyay escribingday, atsay Overnorgay Ellinghambay
imselfhay, ithway ourfay ergeantssay aboutyay ishay airchay, earingbay alberdshay, asyay ayay
uardgay ofyay onorhay. Ehay oreway ayay arkday eatherfay inyay ishay athay, ayay orderbay ofyay
embroideryyay onyay ishay oakclay, andyay ayay ackblay elvetvay unictay eneathbay; ayay
entlemangay advancedyay inyay yearsyay, ithway ayay ardhay experienceyay ittenwray inyay ishay
inkleswray. Ehay asway otnay illyay ittedfay otay ebay ethay eadhay andyay epresentativeray ofyay ayay
ommunitycay, ichwhay owedyay itsyay originyay andyay ogresspray, andyay itsyay esentpray atestay
ofyay evelopmentday, otnay otay ethay impulsesyay ofyay youthyay, utbay otay ethay ernstay andyay
emperedtay energiesyay ofyay anhoodmay, andyay ethay ombresay agacitysay ofyay ageyay;
accomplishingyay osay uchmay, eciselypray ecausebay ityay imaginedyay andyay opedhay osay
ittlelay. Ethay otheryay eminentyay aracterschay, ybay omwhay ethay iefchay ulerray asway
urroundedsay, ereway istinguishedday ybay ayay ignityday ofyay ienmay, elongingbay otay ayay
eriodpay enwhay ethay ormsfay ofyay authorityyay ereway eltfay otay ossesspay ethay acrednesssay
ofyay Ivineday institutionsyay. Eythay ereway, oubtlessday, oodgay enmay, ustjay andyay agesay.
Utbay, outyay ofyay ethay olewhay umanhay amilyfay, ityay ouldway otnay avehay eenbay easyyay otay
electsay ethay amesay umbernay ofyay iseway andyay irtuousvay ersonspay, owhay ouldshay ebay
esslay apablecay ofyay ittingsay inyay udgmentjay onyay anyay erringyay oman’sway earthay, andyay
isentanglingday itsyay eshmay ofyay oodgay andyay evilyay, anthay ethay agessay ofyay igidray
aspectyay owardstay omwhay Esterhay Ynnepray ownay urnedtay erhay acefay. Eshay eemedsay
onsciouscay, indeedyay, atthay ateverwhay ympathysay eshay ightmay expectyay aylay inyay ethay
argerlay andyay armerway earthay ofyay ethay ultitudemay; orfay, asyay eshay iftedlay erhay eyesyay
owardstay ethay alconybay, ethay unhappyyay omanway ewgray alepay andyay embledtray.

Ethay oicevay ichwhay adhay alledcay erhay attentionyay asway atthay ofyay ethay everendray andyay
amousfay Ohnjay Ilsonway, ethay eldestyay ergymanclay ofyay Ostonbay, ayay eatgray olarschay,
ikelay ostmay ofyay ishay ontemporariescay inyay ethay ofessionpray, andyay ithalway ayay anmay ofyay
indkay andyay enialgay iritspay. Isthay astlay attributeyay, oweverhay, adhay eenbay esslay
arefullycay evelopedday anthay ishay intellectualyay iftsgay, andyay asway, inyay uthtray,
atherray ayay attermay ofyay ameshay anthay elf-congratulationsay ithway imhay. Erethay ehay
oodstay, ithway ayay orderbay ofyay izzledgray ockslay eneathbay ishay ull-capskay; ilewhay
ishay aygray eyesyay, accustomedyay otay ethay adedshay ightlay ofyay ishay udystay, ereway
inkingway, ikelay osethay ofyay Ester’shay infantyay, inyay ethay unadulteratedyay
unshinesay. Ehay ookedlay ikelay ethay arklyday engravedyay ortraitspay ichwhay eway eesay
efixedpray otay oldyay olumesvay ofyay ermonssay; andyay adhay onay oremay ightray anthay oneyay ofyay
osethay ortraitspay ouldway avehay, otay epstay orthfay, asyay ehay ownay idday, andyay eddlemay
ithway ayay uestionqay ofyay umanhay uiltgay, assionpay, andyay anguishyay.

ester“hay Ynnepray,” aidsay ethay ergymanclay, i“ay avehay ivenstray ithway ymay youngyay
otherbray erehay, underyay osewhay eachingpray ofyay ethay ordway youyay avehay eenbay
ivilegedpray otay it,”—heresay Mray. Ilsonway aidlay ishay andhay onyay ethay ouldershay ofyay
ayay alepay youngyay anmay esidebay im,—“ihay avehay oughtsay, Iyay aysay, otay ersuadepay isthay
odlygay youthyay, atthay ehay ouldshay ealday ithway youyay, erehay inyay ethay acefay ofyay Eavenhay,
andyay eforebay esethay iseway andyay uprightyay ulersray, andyay inyay earinghay ofyay allyay ethay
eoplepay, asyay ouchingtay ethay ilenessvay andyay acknessblay ofyay youryay insay. Owingknay
youryay aturalnay empertay etterbay anthay Iyay, ehay ouldcay ethay etterbay udgejay atwhay
argumentsyay otay useyay, etherwhay ofyay endernesstay oryay errortay, uchsay asyay ightmay
evailpray overyay youryay ardnesshay andyay obstinacyyay; insomuchyay atthay youyay ouldshay onay
ongerlay idehay ethay amenay ofyay imhay owhay emptedtay youyay otay isthay ievousgray allfay. Utbay
ehay opposesyay otay emay ith(way ayay youngyay an’smay over-softnessyay, albeityay iseway eyondbay
ishay yearsyay), atthay ityay ereway ongingwray ethay eryvay aturenay ofyay omanway otay orcefay
erhay otay aylay openyay erhay eart’shay ecretssay inyay uchsay oadbray aylightday, andyay inyay
esencepray ofyay osay eatgray ayay ultitudemay. Ulytray, asyay Iyay oughtsay otay onvincecay imhay,
ethay ameshay aylay inyay ethay ommissioncay ofyay ethay insay, andyay otnay inyay ethay owingshay ofyay
ityay orthfay. Atwhay aysay youyay otay ityay, onceyay againyay, Otherbray Immesdaleday? Ustmay ityay
ebay outhay, oryay Iyay, atthay allshay ealday ithway isthay oorpay inner’ssay oulsay?”

Erethay asway ayay urmurmay amongyay ethay ignifiedday andyay everendray occupantsyay ofyay ethay
alconybay; andyay Overnorgay Ellinghambay avegay expressionyay otay itsyay urportpay,
eakingspay inyay anyay authoritativeyay oicevay, althoughyay emperedtay ithway espectray
owardstay ethay youthfulyay ergymanclay omwhay ehay addressedyay.

ood“gay Astermay Immesdaleday,” aidsay ehay, e“thay esponsibilityray ofyay isthay oman’sway
oulsay ieslay eatlygray ithway youyay. Ityay ehoovesbay youyay, ereforethay, otay exhortyay erhay
otay epentanceray, andyay otay onfessioncay, asyay ayay oofpray andyay onsequencecay ereofthay.”

Ethay irectnessday ofyay isthay appealyay ewdray ethay eyesyay ofyay ethay olewhay owdcray uponyay
ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday; ayay youngyay ergymanclay, owhay adhay omecay omfray oneyay
ofyay ethay eatgray Englishyay universitiesyay, ingingbray allyay ethay earninglay ofyay ethay
ageyay intoyay ouryay ildway orest-landfay. Ishay eloquenceyay andyay eligiousray ervorfay adhay
alreadyyay ivengay ethay earnestyay ofyay ighhay eminenceyay inyay ishay ofessionpray. Ehay asway ayay
ersonpay ofyay eryvay ikingstray aspectyay, ithway ayay itewhay, oftylay, andyay impendingyay
owbray, argelay ownbray, elancholymay eyesyay, andyay ayay outhmay ichwhay, unlessyay enwhay ehay
orciblyfay ompressedcay ityay, asway aptyay otay ebay emuloustray, expressingyay othbay
ervousnay ensibilitysay andyay ayay astvay owerpay ofyay elf-restraintsay.
Otwithstandingnay ishay ighhay ativenay iftsgay andyay olar-likeschay attainmentsyay,
erethay asway anyay airyay aboutyay isthay youngyay inister,—anmay apprehensiveyay, ayay
artledstay, ayay alf-frightenedhay ook,—aslay ofyay ayay eingbay owhay eltfay imselfhay
uiteqay astrayyay andyay atyay ayay osslay inyay ethay athwaypay ofyay umanhay existenceyay, andyay
ouldcay onlyyay ebay atyay easeyay inyay omesay eclusionsay ofyay ishay ownyay. Ereforethay, osay arfay
asyay ishay utiesday ouldway ermitpay, ehay odtray inyay ethay adowyshay y-pathsbay, andyay usthay
eptkay imselfhay implesay andyay ildlikechay; omingcay orthfay, enwhay occasionyay asway,
ithway ayay eshnessfray, andyay agrancefray, andyay ewyday uritypay ofyay oughtthay, ichwhay, asyay
anymay eoplepay aidsay, affectedyay emthay ikelay ethay eechspay ofyay anyay angelyay.

Uchsay asway ethay youngyay anmay omwhay ethay Everendray Mray. Ilsonway andyay ethay Overnorgay
adhay introducedyay osay openlyyay otay ethay ublicpay oticenay, iddingbay imhay eakspay, inyay
ethay earinghay ofyay allyay enmay, otay atthay ysterymay ofyay ayay oman’sway oulsay, osay acredsay
evenyay inyay itsyay ollutionpay. Ethay yingtray aturenay ofyay ishay ositionpay ovedray ethay
oodblay omfray ishay eekchay, andyay ademay ishay ipslay emuloustray.

eak“spay otay ethay omanway, ymay otherbray,” aidsay Mray. Ilsonway. it“ay isyay ofyay omentmay otay
erhay oulsay, andyay ereforethay, asyay ethay orshipfulway Overnorgay ayssay, omentousmay otay
inethay ownyay, inyay osewhay argechay ershay isyay. Exhortyay erhay otay onfesscay ethay uthtray!”

Ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday entbay ishay eadhay, inyay ilentsay ayerpray, asyay ityay
eemedsay, andyay enthay amecay orwardfay.

ester“hay Ynnepray,” aidsay ehay, eaninglay overyay ethay alconybay andyay ookinglay ownday
eadfastlystay intoyay erhay eyesyay, ou“thay earesthay atwhay isthay oodgay anmay ayssay, andyay
eestsay ethay accountabilityyay underyay ichwhay Iyay aborlay. Ifyay outhay eelestfay ityay otay ebay
orfay ythay oul’ssay eacepay, andyay atthay ythay earthlyyay unishmentpay illway erebythay ebay
ademay oremay effectualyay otay alvationsay, Iyay argechay eethay otay eakspay outyay ethay amenay
ofyay ythay ellow-sinnerfay andyay ellow-suffererfay! Ebay otnay ilentsay omfray anyyay
istakenmay itypay andyay endernesstay orfay imhay; orfay, elievebay emay, Esterhay, oughthay
ehay ereway otay epstay ownday omfray ayay ighhay aceplay, andyay andstay erethay esidebay eethay,
onyay ythay edestalpay ofyay ameshay, yetyay etterbay ereway ityay osay anthay otay idehay ayay uiltygay
earthay oughthray ifelay. Atwhay ancay ythay ilencesay oday orfay imhay, exceptyay ityay empttay
im—yeahay, ompelcay imhay, asyay ityay ere—toway addyay ypocrisyhay otay insay? Eavenhay athhay
antedgray eethay anyay openyay ignominyyay, atthay erebythay outhay ayestmay orkway outyay anyay
openyay iumphtray overyay ethay evilyay ithinway eethay, andyay ethay orrowsay ithoutway. Aketay
eedhay owhay outhay eniestday otay im—whohay, erchancepay, athhay otnay ethay ouragecay otay
aspgray ityay orfay imself—thehay itterbay, utbay olesomewhay, upcay atthay isyay ownay
esentedpray otay ythay ipslay!”

Ethay youngyay astor’spay oicevay asway emulouslytray eetsway, ichray, eepday, andyay
okenbray. Ethay eelingfay atthay ityay osay evidentlyyay anifestedmay, atherray anthay ethay
irectday urportpay ofyay ethay ordsway, ausedcay ityay otay ibratevay ithinway allyay eartshay,
andyay oughtbray ethay istenerslay intoyay oneyay accordyay ofyay ympathysay. Evenyay ethay oorpay
abybay, atyay Ester’shay osombay, asway affectedyay ybay ethay amesay influenceyay; orfay ityay
irectedday itsyay ithertohay acantvay azegay owardstay Mray. Immesdaleday, andyay eldhay upyay
itsyay ittlelay armsyay, ithway ayay alf-pleasedhay, alf-plaintivehay urmurmay. Osay
owerfulpay eemedsay ethay inister’smay appealyay, atthay ethay eoplepay ouldcay otnay
elievebay utbay atthay Esterhay Ynnepray ouldway eakspay outyay ethay uiltygay amenay; oryay
elseyay atthay ethay uiltygay oneyay imselfhay, inyay ateverwhay ighhay oryay owlylay aceplay ehay
oodstay, ouldway ebay awndray orthfay ybay anyay inwardyay andyay inevitableyay ecessitynay, andyay
ompelledcay otay ascendyay otay ethay affoldscay.

Esterhay ookshay erhay eadhay.

oman“way, ansgresstray otnay eyondbay ethay imitslay ofyay Eaven’shay ercymay!” iedcray ethay
Everendray Mray. Ilsonway, oremay arshlyhay anthay eforebay. at“thay ittlelay abebay athhay
eenbay iftedgay ithway ayay oicevay, otay econdsay andyay onfirmcay ethay ounselcay ichwhay outhay
asthay eardhay. Eakspay outyay ethay amenay! Atthay, andyay ythay epentanceray, aymay availyay otay
aketay ethay arletscay etterlay offyay ythay eastbray.”

ever“nay!” epliedray Esterhay Ynnepray, ookinglay, otnay atyay Mray. Ilsonway, utbay intoyay
ethay eepday andyay oubledtray eyesyay ofyay ethay youngeryay ergymanclay. it“ay isyay ootay eeplyday
andedbray. Yeyay annotcay aketay ityay offyay. Andyay ouldway atthay Iyay ightmay endureyay ishay
agonyyay, asyay ellway asyay inemay!”

eak“spay, omanway!” aidsay anotheryay oicevay, oldlycay andyay ernlystay, oceedingpray
omfray ethay owdcray aboutyay ethay affoldscay. eak“spay; andyay ivegay youryay ildchay ayay
atherfay!”

i“ay illway otnay eakspay!” answeredyay Esterhay, urningtay alepay asyay eathday, utbay
espondingray otay isthay oicevay, ichwhay eshay ootay urelysay ecognizedray. and“ay ymay
ildchay ustmay eeksay ayay eavenlyhay Atherfay; eshay allshay evernay owknay anyay earthlyyay
oneyay!”

e“shay illway otnay eakspay!” urmuredmay Mray. Immesdaleday, owhay, eaninglay overyay ethay
alconybay, ithway ishay andhay uponyay ishay earthay, adhay awaitedyay ethay esultray ofyay ishay
appealyay. Ehay ownay ewdray ackbay, ithway ayay onglay espirationray. ondrous“way engthstray
andyay enerositygay ofyay ayay oman’sway earthay! Eshay illway otnay eakspay!”

illustration[ay: e“shay asway edlay ackbay otay Isonpray”]

Iscerningday ethay impracticableyay atestay ofyay ethay oorpay ulprit’scay indmay, ethay
elderyay ergymanclay, owhay adhay arefullycay eparedpray imselfhay orfay ethay occasionyay,
addressedyay otay ethay ultitudemay ayay iscourseday onyay insay, inyay allyay itsyay anchesbray,
utbay ithway ontinualcay eferenceray otay ethay ignominiousyay etterlay. Osay orciblyfay
idday ehay elldway uponyay isthay ymbolsay, orfay ethay ourhay oryay oremay uringday ichwhay ishay
eriodspay ereway ollingray overyay ethay eople’spay eadshay, atthay ityay assumedyay ewnay
errorstay inyay eirthay imaginationyay, andyay eemedsay otay eriveday itsyay arletscay uehay
omfray ethay amesflay ofyay ethay infernalyay itpay. Esterhay Ynnepray, eanwhilemay, eptkay
erhay aceplay uponyay ethay edestalpay ofyay ameshay, ithway azedglay eyesyay, andyay anyay airyay ofyay
earyway indifferenceyay. Eshay adhay ornebay, atthay orningmay, allyay atthay aturenay ouldcay
endureyay; andyay asyay erhay emperamenttay asway otnay ofyay ethay orderyay atthay escapesyay omfray
ootay intenseyay ufferingsay ybay ayay oonsway, erhay iritspay ouldcay onlyyay eltershay itselfyay
eneathbay ayay onystay ustcray ofyay insensibilityyay, ilewhay ethay acultiesfay ofyay animalyay
ifelay emainedray entireyay. Inyay isthay atestay, ethay oicevay ofyay ethay eacherpray
underedthay emorselesslyray, utbay unavailinglyyay, uponyay erhay earsyay. Ethay infantyay,
uringday ethay atterlay ortionpay ofyay erhay ordealyay, iercedpay ethay airyay ithway itsyay
ailingsway andyay eamsscray; eshay ovestray otay ushhay ityay, echanicallymay, utbay eemedsay
arcelyscay otay ympathizesay ithway itsyay oubletray. Ithway ethay amesay ardhay emeanorday,
eshay asway edlay ackbay otay isonpray, andyay anishedvay omfray ethay ublicpay azegay ithinway
itsyay iron-clampedyay ortalpay. Ityay asway isperedwhay, ybay osethay owhay eeredpay afteryay
erhay, atthay ethay arletscay etterlay ewthray ayay uridlay eamglay alongyay ethay arkday
assage-waypay ofyay ethay interioryay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Ivyay.

                            Ethay Interviewyay.


Afteryay erhay eturnray otay ethay isonpray, Esterhay Ynnepray asway oundfay otay ebay inyay ayay
atestay ofyay ervousnay excitementyay atthay emandedday onstantcay atchfulnessway, estlay
eshay ouldshay erpetratepay iolencevay onyay erselfhay, oryay oday omesay alf-frenziedhay
ischiefmay otay ethay oorpay abebay. Asyay ightnay approachedyay, ityay ovingpray impossibleyay
otay uellqay erhay insubordinationyay ybay ebukeray oryay eatsthray ofyay unishmentpay,
Astermay Ackettbray, ethay ailerjay, oughtthay itfay otay introduceyay ayay ysicianphay. Ehay
escribedday imhay asyay ayay anmay ofyay illskay inyay allyay Istianchray odesmay ofyay ysicalphay
iencescay, andyay ikewiselay amiliarfay ithway ateverwhay ethay avagesay eoplepay ouldcay
eachtay, inyay espectray otay edicinalmay erbshay andyay ootsray atthay ewgray inyay ethay
orestfay. Otay aysay ethay uthtray, erethay asway uchmay eednay ofyay ofessionalpray
assistanceyay, otnay erelymay orfay Esterhay erselfhay, utbay illstay oremay urgentlyyay orfay
ethay ildchay; owhay, awingdray itsyay ustenancesay omfray ethay aternalmay osombay, eemedsay
otay avehay ankdray inyay ithway ityay allyay ethay urmoiltay, ethay anguishyay andyay espairday,
ichwhay ervadedpay ethay other’smay ystemsay. Ityay ownay ithedwray inyay onvulsionscay ofyay
ainpay, andyay asway ayay orciblefay ypetay, inyay itsyay ittlelay amefray, ofyay ethay oralmay agonyyay
ichwhay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay ornebay oughoutthray ethay ayday.

Oselyclay ollowingfay ethay ailerjay intoyay ethay ismalday apartmentyay appearedyay atthay
individualyay, ofyay ingularsay aspectyay, osewhay esencepray inyay ethay owdcray adhay eenbay
ofyay uchsay eepday interestyay otay ethay earerway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay. Ehay asway
odgedlay inyay ethay isonpray, otnay asyay uspectedsay ofyay anyyay offenceyay, utbay asyay ethay ostmay
onvenientcay andyay uitablesay odemay ofyay isposingday ofyay imhay, untilyay ethay
agistratesmay ouldshay avehay onferredcay ithway ethay Indianyay agamoressay espectingray
ishay ansomray. Ishay amenay asway announcedyay asyay Ogerray Illingworthchay. Ethay ailerjay,
afteryay usheringyay imhay intoyay ethay oomray, emainedray ayay omentmay, arvellingmay atyay ethay
omparativecay uietqay atthay ollowedfay ishay entranceyay; orfay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay
immediatelyyay ecomebay asyay illstay asyay eathday, althoughyay ethay ildchay ontinuedcay otay
oanmay.

ithee“pray, iendfray, eavelay emay aloneyay ithway ymay atientpay,” aidsay ethay
actitionerpray. ust“tray emay, oodgay ailerjay, youyay allshay ieflybray avehay eacepay inyay
youryay ousehay; andyay, Iyay omisepray youyay, Istressmay Ynnepray allshay ereafterhay ebay
oremay amenableyay otay ustjay authorityyay anthay youyay aymay avehay oundfay erhay
eretoforehay.”

ay“nay, ifyay youryay orshipway ancay accomplishyay atthay,” answeredyay Astermay Ackettbray,
i“ay allshay ownyay youyay orfay ayay anmay ofyay illskay indeedyay! Erilyvay, ethay omanway athhay
eenbay ikelay ayay ossessedpay oneyay; andyay erethay ackslay ittlelay, atthay Iyay ouldshay aketay
inyay andhay otay ivedray Atansay outyay ofyay erhay ithway ipesstray.”

Ethay angerstray adhay enteredyay ethay oomray ithway ethay aracteristicchay uietudeqay ofyay
ethay ofessionpray otay ichwhay ehay announcedyay imselfhay asyay elongingbay. Ornay idday ishay
emeanorday angechay, enwhay ethay ithdrawalway ofyay ethay ison-keeperpray eftlay imhay
acefay otay acefay ithway ethay omanway, osewhay absorbedyay oticenay ofyay imhay, inyay ethay
owdcray, adhay intimatedyay osay oseclay ayay elationray etweenbay imselfhay andyay erhay. Ishay
irstfay arecay asway ivengay otay ethay ildchay; osewhay iescray, indeedyay, asyay eshay aylay
ithingwray onyay ethay undle-bedtray, ademay ityay ofyay eremptorypay ecessitynay otay
ostponepay allyay otheryay usinessbay otay ethay asktay ofyay oothingsay erhay. Ehay examinedyay
ethay infantyay arefullycay, andyay enthay oceededpray otay unclaspyay ayay eathernlay asecay,
ichwhay ehay ooktay omfray eneathbay ishay essdray. Ityay appearedyay otay ontaincay edicalmay
eparationspray, oneyay ofyay ichwhay ehay ingledmay ithway ayay upcay ofyay aterway.

y“may oldyay udiesstay inyay alchemyyay,” observedyay ehay, and“ay ymay ojournsay, orfay aboveyay ayay
yearyay astpay, amongyay ayay eoplepay ellway ersedvay inyay ethay indlykay opertiespray ofyay
implessay, avehay ademay ayay etterbay ysicianphay ofyay emay anthay anymay atthay aimclay ethay
edicalmay egreeday. Erehay, omanway! Ethay ildchay isyay yours,—sheyay isyay onenay ofyay
ine,—neithermay illway eshay ecognizeray ymay oicevay oryay aspectyay asyay ayay ather’sfay.
Administeryay isthay aughtdray, ereforethay, ithway inethay ownyay andhay.”

Esterhay epelledray ethay offeredyay edicinemay, atyay ethay amesay imetay azinggay ithway
onglystray arkedmay apprehensionyay intoyay ishay acefay.

ouldst“way outhay avengeyay yselfthay onyay ethay innocentyay abebay?” isperedwhay eshay.

oolish“fay omanway!” espondedray ethay ysicianphay, alfhay oldlycay, alfhay
oothinglysay. at“whay ouldshay ailyay emay, otay armhay isthay isbegottenmay andyay
iserablemay abebay? Ethay edicinemay isyay otentpay orfay oodgay; andyay ereway ityay ymay
ild,—yeachay, inemay ownyay, asyay ellway asyay ine!—ithay ouldcay oday onay etterbay orfay
ityay.”

Asyay eshay illstay esitatedhay, eingbay, inyay actfay, inyay onay easonableray atestay ofyay
indmay, ehay ooktay ethay infantyay inyay ishay armsyay, andyay imselfhay administeredyay ethay
aughtdray. Ityay oonsay ovedpray itsyay efficacyyay, andyay edeemedray ethay eech’slay edgeplay.
Ethay oansmay ofyay ethay ittlelay atientpay ubsidedsay; itsyay onvulsivecay ossingstay
aduallygray easedcay; andyay, inyay ayay ewfay omentsmay, asyay isyay ethay ustomcay ofyay youngyay
ildrenchay afteryay eliefray omfray ainpay, ityay anksay intoyay ayay ofoundpray andyay ewyday
umberslay. Ethay ysicianphay, asyay ehay adhay ayay airfay ightray otay ebay ermedtay, extnay
estowedbay ishay attentionyay onyay ethay othermay. Ithway almcay andyay intentyay utinyscray ehay
eltfay erhay ulsepay, ookedlay intoyay erhay eyes,—ayay azegay atthay ademay erhay earthay
inkshray andyay uddershay, ecausebay osay amiliarfay, andyay yetyay osay angestray andyay
old,—andcay, inallyfay, atisfiedsay ithway ishay investigationyay, oceededpray otay
inglemay anotheryay aughtdray.

i“ay owknay otnay Ethelay ornay Epenthenay,” emarkedray ehay; ut“bay Iyay avehay earnedlay anymay
ewnay ecretssay inyay ethay ildernessway, andyay erehay isyay oneyay ofyay em,—athay eciperay atthay
anyay Indianyay aughttay emay, inyay equitalray ofyay omesay essonslay ofyay ymay ownyay, atthay ereway
asyay oldyay asyay Aracelsuspay. Inkdray ityay! Ityay aymay ebay esslay oothingsay anthay ayay inlesssay
onsciencecay. Atthay Iyay annotcay ivegay eethay. Utbay ityay illway almcay ethay ellsway andyay
eavinghay ofyay ythay assionpay, ikelay oilyay ownthray onyay ethay avesway ofyay ayay empestuoustay
easay.”

Ehay esentedpray ethay upcay otay Esterhay, owhay eceivedray ityay ithway ayay owslay, earnestyay
ooklay intoyay ishay acefay; otnay eciselypray ayay ooklay ofyay earfay, yetyay ullfay ofyay oubtday
andyay uestioningqay, asyay otay atwhay ishay urposespay ightmay ebay. Eshay ookedlay alsoyay atyay
erhay umberingslay ildchay.

i“ay avehay oughtthay ofyay eathday,” aidsay e,—“haveshay ishedway orfay it,—wouldyay evenyay
avehay ayedpray orfay ityay, ereway ityay itfay atthay uchsay asyay Iyay ouldshay aypray orfay
anythingyay. Yetyay ifyay eathday ebay inyay isthay upcay, Iyay idbay eethay inkthay againyay, ereyay
outhay eholdestbay emay uaffqay ityay. Eesay! Ityay isyay evenyay ownay atyay ymay ipslay.”

ink“dray, enthay,” epliedray ehay, illstay ithway ethay amesay oldcay omposurecay. ost“day
outhay owknay emay osay ittlelay, Esterhay Ynnepray? Areyay ymay urposespay ontway otay ebay osay
allowshay? Evenyay ifyay Iyay imagineyay ayay emeschay ofyay engeancevay, atwhay ouldcay Iyay oday
etterbay orfay ymay objectyay anthay otay etlay eethay ive,—thanlay otay ivegay eethay
edicinesmay againstyay allyay armhay andyay erilpay ofyay ife,—solay atthay isthay urningbay
ameshay aymay illstay azeblay uponyay ythay osombay?” Asyay ehay okespay, ehay aidlay ishay onglay
orefingerfay onyay ethay arletscay etterlay, ichwhay orthwithfay eemedsay otay orchscay
intoyay Ester’shay eastbray, asyay ifyay ityay adhay eenbay ed-hotray. Ehay oticednay erhay
involuntaryyay esturegay, andyay iledsmay. ive“lay, ereforethay, andyay earbay aboutyay ythay
oomday ithway eethay, inyay ethay eyesyay ofyay enmay andyay omen,—inway ethay eyesyay ofyay imhay omwhay
outhay idstday allcay ythay usband,—inhay ethay eyesyay ofyay yonderyay ildchay! Andyay, atthay
outhay ayestmay ivelay, aketay offyay isthay aughtdray.”

Ithoutway urtherfay expostulationyay oryay elayday, Esterhay Ynnepray aineddray ethay
upcay, andyay, atyay ethay otionmay ofyay ethay anmay ofyay illskay, eatedsay erselfhay onyay ethay edbay
erewhay ethay ildchay asway eepingslay; ilewhay ehay ewdray ethay onlyyay airchay ichwhay ethay
oomray affordedyay, andyay ooktay ishay ownyay eatsay esidebay erhay. Eshay ouldcay otnay utbay
embletray atyay esethay eparationspray; orfay eshay eltfay at—havingthay ownay oneday allyay
atthay umanityhay oryay inciplepray, oryay, ifyay osay ityay ereway, ayay efinedray ueltycray,
impelledyay imhay otay oday, orfay ethay eliefray ofyay ysicalphay uffering—hesay asway extnay
otay eattray ithway erhay asyay ethay anmay omwhay eshay adhay ostmay eeplyday andyay irreparablyyay
injuredyay.

ester“hay,” aidsay ehay, i“ay askyay otnay ereforewhay, ornay owhay, outhay asthay allenfay
intoyay ethay itpay, oryay aysay, atherray, outhay asthay ascendedyay otay ethay edestalpay ofyay
infamyyay, onyay ichwhay Iyay oundfay eethay. Ethay easonray isyay otnay arfay otay eeksay. Ityay asway
ymay ollyfay, andyay ythay eaknessway. I,—ayay anmay ofyay ought,—thethay ookwormbay ofyay
eatgray ibraries,—alay anmay alreadyyay inyay ecayday, avinghay ivengay ymay estbay yearsyay
otay eedfay ethay ungryhay eamdray ofyay owledge,—whatknay adhay Iyay otay oday ithway youthyay
andyay eautybay ikelay inethay ownyay! Isshapenmay omfray ymay irth-hourbay, owhay ouldcay Iyay
eludeday yselfmay ithway ethay ideayay atthay intellectualyay iftsgay ightmay eilvay
ysicalphay eformityday inyay ayay youngyay irl’sgay antasyfay! Enmay allcay emay iseway. Ifyay
agessay ereway everyay iseway inyay eirthay ownyay ehoofbay, Iyay ightmay avehay oreseenfay allyay
isthay. Iyay ightmay avehay ownknay atthay, asyay Iyay amecay outyay ofyay ethay astvay andyay ismalday
orestfay, andyay enteredyay isthay ettlementsay ofyay Istianchray enmay, ethay eryvay irstfay
objectyay otay eetmay ymay eyesyay ouldway ebay yselfthay, Esterhay Ynnepray, andingstay upyay, ayay
atuestay ofyay ignominyyay, eforebay ethay eoplepay. Aynay, omfray ethay omentmay enwhay eway
amecay ownday ethay oldyay urchchay epsstay ogethertay, ayay arriedmay airpay, Iyay ightmay avehay
eheldbay ethay ale-firebay ofyay atthay arletscay etterlay azingblay atyay ethay endyay ofyay ouryay
athpay!”

ou“thay owestknay,” aidsay Ester,—forhay, epressedday asyay eshay asway, eshay ouldcay otnay
endureyay isthay astlay uietqay abstay atyay ethay okentay ofyay erhay ame,—“thoushay owestknay
atthay Iyay asway ankfray ithway eethay. Iyay eltfay onay ovelay, ornay eignedfay anyyay.”

ue“tray,” epliedray ehay. it“ay asway ymay ollyfay! Iyay avehay aidsay ityay. Utbay, upyay otay atthay
epochyay ofyay ymay ifelay, Iyay adhay ivedlay inyay ainvay. Ethay orldway adhay eenbay osay
eerlesschay! Ymay earthay asway ayay abitationhay argelay enoughyay orfay anymay uestsgay, utbay
onelylay andyay illchay, andyay ithoutway ayay ouseholdhay irefay. Iyay ongedlay otay indlekay
oneyay! Ityay eemedsay otnay osay ildway ayay eam,—olddray asyay Iyay asway, andyay ombresay asyay Iyay
asway, andyay isshapenmay asyay Iyay as,—thatway ethay implesay issblay, ichwhay isyay
atteredscay arfay andyay ideway, orfay allyay ankindmay otay athergay upyay, ightmay yetyay ebay
inemay. Andyay osay, Esterhay, Iyay ewdray eethay intoyay ymay earthay, intoyay itsyay innermostyay
amberchay, andyay oughtsay otay armway eethay ybay ethay armthway ichwhay ythay esencepray ademay
erethay!”

i“ay avehay eatlygray ongedwray eethay,” urmuredmay Esterhay.

e“way avehay ongedwray eachyay otheryay,” answeredyay ehay. ine“may asway ethay irstfay ongwray,
enwhay Iyay etrayedbay ythay uddingbay youthyay intoyay ayay alsefay andyay unnaturalyay elationray
ithway ymay ecayday. Ereforethay, asyay ayay anmay owhay ashay otnay oughtthay andyay
ilosophizedphay inyay ainvay, Iyay eeksay onay engeancevay, otplay onay evilyay againstyay eethay.
Etweenbay eethay andyay emay ethay alescay angshay airlyfay alancedbay. Utbay, Esterhay, ethay
anmay iveslay owhay ashay ongedwray usyay othbay! Owhay isyay ehay?”

ask“ay emay otnay!” epliedray Esterhay Ynnepray, ookinglay irmlyfay intoyay ishay acefay.
at“thay outhay altshay evernay owknay!”

ever“nay, ayestsay outhay?” ejoinedray ehay, ithway ayay ilesmay ofyay arkday andyay
elf-relyingsay intelligenceyay. ever“nay owknay imhay! Elievebay emay, Esterhay, erethay
areyay ewfay ings,—whetherthay inyay ethay outwardyay orldway, oryay, otay ayay ertaincay epthday,
inyay ethay invisibleyay eresphay ofyay ought,—fewthay ingsthay iddenhay omfray ethay anmay
owhay evotesday imselfhay earnestlyyay andyay unreservedlyyay otay ethay olutionsay ofyay ayay
ysterymay. Outhay ayestmay overcay upyay ythay ecretsay omfray ethay yingpray ultitudemay.
Outhay ayestmay oncealcay ityay, ootay, omfray ethay inistersmay andyay agistratesmay, evenyay
asyay outhay idstday isthay ayday, enwhay eythay oughtsay otay enchwray ethay amenay outyay ofyay ythay
earthay, andyay ivegay eethay ayay artnerpay onyay ythay edestalpay. Utbay, asyay orfay emay, Iyay omecay
otay ethay inquestyay ithway otheryay ensessay anthay eythay ossesspay. Iyay allshay eeksay isthay
anmay, asyay Iyay avehay oughtsay uthtray inyay ooksbay; asyay Iyay avehay oughtsay oldgay inyay
alchemyyay. Erethay isyay ayay ympathysay atthay illway akemay emay onsciouscay ofyay imhay. Iyay
allshay eesay imhay embletray. Iyay allshay eelfay yselfmay uddershay, uddenlysay andyay
unawaresyay. Oonersay oryay aterlay, ehay ustmay eedsnay ebay inemay!”

Ethay eyesyay ofyay ethay inkledwray olarschay owedglay osay intenselyyay uponyay erhay, atthay
Esterhay Ynnepray aspedclay erhay andshay overyay erhay earthay, eadingdray estlay ehay
ouldshay eadray ethay ecretsay erethay atyay onceyay.

ou“thay iltway otnay evealray ishay amenay? Otnay ethay esslay ehay isyay inemay,” esumedray ehay,
ithway ayay ooklay ofyay onfidencecay, asyay ifyay estinyday ereway atyay oneyay ithway imhay. e“hay
earsbay onay etterlay ofyay infamyyay oughtwray intoyay ishay armentgay, asyay outhay ostday; utbay
Iyay allshay eadray ityay onyay ishay earthay. Yetyay earfay otnay orfay imhay! Inkthay otnay atthay Iyay
allshay interfereyay ithway Eaven’shay ownyay ethodmay ofyay etributionray, oryay, otay ymay ownyay
osslay, etraybay imhay otay ethay ipegray ofyay umanhay awlay. Eithernay oday outhay imagineyay
atthay Iyay allshay ontrivecay aughtyay againstyay ishay ifelay; onay, ornay againstyay ishay
amefay, ifyay, asyay Iyay udgejay, ehay ebay ayay anmay ofyay airfay eputeray. Etlay imhay ivelay! Etlay
imhay idehay imselfhay inyay outwardyay onorhay, ifyay ehay aymay! Otnay ethay esslay ehay allshay ebay
inemay!”

y“thay actsyay areyay ikelay ercymay,” aidsay Esterhay, ewilderedbay andyay appalledyay. ut“bay
ythay ordsway interpretyay eethay asyay ayay errortay!”

one“ay ingthay, outhay atthay astway ymay ifeway, Iyay ouldway enjoinyay uponyay eethay,”
ontinuedcay ethay olarschay. ou“thay asthay eptkay ethay ecretsay ofyay ythay aramourpay.
Eepkay, ikewiselay, inemay! Erethay areyay onenay inyay isthay andlay atthay owknay emay.
Eathebray otnay, otay anyyay umanhay oulsay, atthay outhay idstday everyay allcay emay usbandhay!
Erehay, onyay isthay ildway outskirtyay ofyay ethay earthyay, Iyay allshay itchpay ymay enttay; orfay,
elsewhereyay ayay andererway, andyay isolatedyay omfray umanhay interestsyay, Iyay indfay erehay ayay
omanway, ayay anmay, ayay ildchay, amongstyay omwhay andyay yselfmay erethay existyay ethay osestclay
igamentslay. Onay attermay etherwhay ofyay ovelay oryay atehay; onay attermay etherwhay ofyay
ightray oryay ongwray! Outhay andyay inethay, Esterhay Ynnepray, elongbay otay emay. Ymay omehay
isyay erewhay outhay artyay, andyay erewhay ehay isyay. Utbay etraybay emay otnay!”

illustration[ay: e“thay Eyesyay ofyay ethay inkledwray Olarschay owedglay”]

erefore“whay ostday outhay esireday ityay?” inquiredyay Esterhay, inkingshray, eshay
ardlyhay ewknay ywhay, omfray isthay ecretsay ondbay. y“whay otnay announceyay yselfthay
openlyyay, andyay astcay emay offyay atyay onceyay?”

it“ay aymay ebay,” ehay epliedray, ecause“bay Iyay illway otnay encounteryay ethay ishonorday
atthay esmirchesbay ethay usbandhay ofyay ayay aithlessfay omanway. Ityay aymay ebay orfay otheryay
easonsray. Enoughyay, ityay isyay ymay urposepay otay ivelay andyay ieday unknownyay. Etlay,
ereforethay, ythay usbandhay ebay otay ethay orldway asyay oneyay alreadyyay eadday, andyay ofyay
omwhay onay idingstay allshay everyay omecay. Ecognizeray emay otnay, ybay ordway, ybay ignsay,
ybay ooklay! Eathebray otnay ethay ecretsay, aboveyay allyay, otay ethay anmay outhay ottestway
ofyay. Ouldstshay outhay ailfay emay inyay isthay, ewarebay! Ishay amefay, ishay ositionpay, ishay
ifelay, illway ebay inyay ymay andshay. Ewarebay!”

i“ay illway eepkay ythay ecretsay, asyay Iyay avehay ishay,” aidsay Esterhay.

ear“sway ityay!” ejoinedray ehay.

Andyay eshay ooktay ethay oathyay.

and“ay ownay, Istressmay Ynnepray,” aidsay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, asyay ehay asway
ereafterhay otay ebay amednay, i“ay eavelay eethay aloneyay; aloneyay ithway ythay infantyay, andyay
ethay arletscay etterlay! Owhay isyay ityay, Esterhay? Othday ythay entencesay indbay eethay otay
earway ethay okentay inyay ythay eepslay? Artyay outhay otnay afraidyay ofyay ightmaresnay andyay
ideoushay eamsdray?”

y“whay ostday outhay ilesmay osay atyay emay?” inquiredyay Esterhay, oubledtray atyay ethay
expressionyay ofyay ishay eyesyay. art“ay outhay ikelay ethay Ackblay Anmay atthay auntshay ethay
orestfay oundray aboutyay usyay? Asthay outhay enticedyay emay intoyay ayay ondbay atthay illway
ovepray ethay uinray ofyay ymay oulsay?”

ot“nay ythay oulsay,” ehay answeredyay, ithway anotheryay ilesmay. o“nay, otnay inethay!”




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Vay.

                         Esterhay Atyay Erhay Eedlenay.


Esterhay Ynne’spray ermtay ofyay onfinementcay asway ownay atyay anyay endyay. Erhay ison-doorpray
asway ownthray openyay, andyay eshay amecay orthfay intoyay ethay unshinesay, ichwhay, allingfay
onyay allyay alikeyay, eemedsay, otay erhay icksay andyay orbidmay earthay, asyay ifyay eantmay orfay onay
otheryay urposepay anthay otay evealray ethay arletscay etterlay onyay erhay eastbray. Erhapspay
erethay asway ayay oremay ealray orturetay inyay erhay irstfay unattendedyay ootstepsfay omfray
ethay esholdthray ofyay ethay isonpray, anthay evenyay inyay ethay ocessionpray andyay ectaclespay
atthay avehay eenbay escribedday, erewhay eshay asway ademay ethay ommoncay infamyyay, atyay
ichwhay allyay ankindmay asway ummonedsay otay ointpay itsyay ingerfay. Enthay, eshay asway
upportedsay ybay anyay unnaturalyay ensiontay ofyay ethay ervesnay, andyay ybay allyay ethay
ombativecay energyyay ofyay erhay aracterchay, ichwhay enabledyay erhay otay onvertcay ethay
enescay intoyay ayay indkay ofyay uridlay iumphtray. Ityay asway, oreovermay, ayay eparatesay andyay
insulatedyay eventyay, otay occuryay utbay onceyay inyay erhay ifetimelay, andyay otay eetmay ichwhay,
ereforethay, ecklessray ofyay economyyay, eshay ightmay allcay upyay ethay italvay engthstray
atthay ouldway avehay ufficedsay orfay anymay uietqay yearsyay. Ethay eryvay awlay atthay
ondemnedcay er—ahay iantgay ofyay ernstay eaturesfay, utbay ithway igorvay otay upportsay,
asyay ellway asyay otay annihilateyay, inyay ishay ironyay arm—hadyay eldhay erhay upyay, oughthray
ethay erribletay ordealyay ofyay erhay ignominyyay. Utbay ownay, ithway isthay unattendedyay
alkway omfray erhay ison-doorpray, eganbay ethay ailyday ustomcay; andyay eshay ustmay eitheryay
ustainsay andyay arrycay ityay orwardfay ybay ethay ordinaryyay esourcesray ofyay erhay aturenay,
oryay inksay eneathbay ityay. Eshay ouldcay onay ongerlay orrowbay omfray ethay uturefay otay elphay
erhay oughthray ethay esentpray iefgray. O-morrowtay ouldway ingbray itsyay ownyay ialtray
ithway ityay; osay ouldway ethay extnay ayday, andyay osay ouldway ethay extnay; eachyay itsyay ownyay
ialtray, andyay yetyay ethay eryvay amesay atthay asway ownay osay unutterablyyay ievousgray otay
ebay ornebay. Ethay aysday ofyay ethay ar-offfay uturefay ouldway oiltay onwardyay, illstay ithway
ethay amesay urdenbay orfay erhay otay aketay upyay, andyay earbay alongyay ithway erhay, utbay evernay
otay ingflay ownday; orfay ethay accumulatingyay aysday, andyay addedyay yearsyay, ouldway ilepay
upyay eirthay iserymay uponyay ethay eaphay ofyay ameshay. Oughoutthray emthay allyay, ivinggay upyay
erhay individualityyay, eshay ouldway ecomebay ethay eneralgay ymbolsay atyay ichwhay ethay
eacherpray andyay oralistmay ightmay ointpay, andyay inyay ichwhay eythay ightmay ivifyvay andyay
embodyyay eirthay imagesyay ofyay oman’sway ailtyfray andyay infulsay assionpay. Usthay ethay
youngyay andyay urepay ouldway ebay aughttay otay ooklay atyay erhay, ithway ethay arletscay etterlay
amingflay onyay erhay east,—atbray erhay, ethay ildchay ofyay onorablehay arents,—atpay
erhay, ethay othermay ofyay ayay abebay, atthay ouldway ereafterhay ebay ayay oman,—atway erhay,
owhay adhay onceyay eenbay innocent,—asyay ethay igurefay, ethay odybay, ethay ealityray ofyay
insay. Andyay overyay erhay avegray, ethay infamyyay atthay eshay ustmay arrycay itherthay ouldway
ebay erhay onlyyay onumentmay.

Ityay aymay eemsay arvellousmay, atthay, ithway ethay orldway eforebay er,—kepthay ybay onay
estrictiveray auseclay ofyay erhay ondemnationcay ithinway ethay imitslay ofyay ethay
Uritanpay ettlementsay, osay emoteray andyay osay obscure,—freeyay otay eturnray otay erhay
irthplacebay, oryay otay anyyay otheryay Europeanyay andlay, andyay erethay idehay erhay
aracterchay andyay identityyay underyay ayay ewnay exterioryay, asyay ompletelycay asyay ifyay
emergingyay intoyay anotheryay atestay ofyay eing,—andbay avinghay alsoyay ethay assespay ofyay
ethay arkday, inscrutableyay orestfay openyay otay erhay, erewhay ethay ildnessway ofyay erhay
aturenay ightmay assimilateyay itselfyay ithway ayay eoplepay osewhay ustomscay andyay ifelay
ereway alienyay omfray ethay awlay atthay adhay ondemnedcay er,—ithay aymay eemsay
arvellousmay, atthay isthay omanway ouldshay illstay allcay atthay aceplay erhay omehay,
erewhay, andyay erewhay onlyyay, eshay ustmay eedsnay ebay ethay ypetay ofyay ameshay. Utbay erethay
isyay ayay atalityfay, ayay eelingfay osay irresistibleyay andyay inevitableyay atthay ityay ashay
ethay orcefay ofyay oomday, ichwhay almostyay invariablyyay ompelscay umanhay eingsbay otay
ingerlay aroundyay andyay aunthay, ost-likeghay, ethay otspay erewhay omesay eatgray andyay
arkedmay eventyay ashay ivengay ethay olorcay otay eirthay ifetimelay; andyay illstay ethay oremay
irresistiblyyay, ethay arkerday ethay ingetay atthay addenssay ityay. Erhay insay, erhay
ignominyyay, ereway ethay ootsray ichwhay eshay adhay uckstray intoyay ethay oilsay. Ityay asway asyay
ifyay ayay ewnay irthbay, ithway ongerstray assimilationsyay anthay ethay irstfay, adhay
onvertedcay ethay orest-landfay, illstay osay uncongenialyay otay everyyay otheryay ilgrimpay
andyay andererway, intoyay Esterhay Ynne’spray ildway andyay earydray, utbay ife-longlay
omehay. Allyay otheryay enesscay ofyay earth—evenyay atthay illagevay ofyay uralray Englandyay,
erewhay appyhay infancyyay andyay ainlessstay aidenhoodmay eemedsay yetyay otay ebay inyay erhay
other’smay eepingkay, ikelay armentsgay utpay offyay onglay ago—wereyay oreignfay otay erhay,
inyay omparisoncay. Ethay ainchay atthay oundbay erhay erehay asway ofyay ironyay inkslay, andyay
allinggay otay erhay inmostyay oulsay, utbay ouldcay evernay ebay okenbray.

Ityay ightmay ebay, oo,—doubtlesstay ityay asway osay, althoughyay eshay idhay ethay ecretsay
omfray erselfhay, andyay ewgray alepay eneverwhay ityay uggledstray outyay ofyay erhay earthay,
ikelay ayay erpentsay omfray itsyay ole,—ithay ightmay ebay atthay anotheryay eelingfay eptkay
erhay ithinway ethay enescay andyay athwaypay atthay adhay eenbay osay atalfay. Erethay eltdway,
erethay odetray ethay eetfay ofyay oneyay ithway omwhay eshay eemedday erselfhay onnectedcay inyay
ayay unionyay, atthay, unrecognizedyay onyay earthyay, ouldway ingbray emthay ogethertay eforebay
ethay arbay ofyay inalfay udgmentjay, andyay akemay atthay eirthay arriage-altarmay, orfay ayay
ointjay uturityfay ofyay endlessyay etributionray. Overyay andyay overyay againyay, ethay
emptertay ofyay oulssay adhay ustthray isthay ideayay uponyay Ester’shay ontemplationcay, andyay
aughedlay atyay ethay assionatepay andyay esperateday oyjay ithway ichwhay eshay eizedsay,
andyay enthay ovestray otay astcay ityay omfray erhay. Eshay arelybay ookedlay ethay ideayay inyay ethay
acefay, andyay astenedhay otay arbay ityay inyay itsyay ungeonday. Atwhay eshay ompelledcay
erselfhay otay elieve—whatbay, inallyfay, eshay easonedray uponyay, asyay erhay otivemay
orfay ontinuingcay ayay esidentray ofyay Ewnay England—wasyay alfhay ayay uthtray, andyay alfhay ayay
elf-delusionsay. Erehay, eshay aidsay otay erselfhay, adhay eenbay ethay enescay ofyay erhay
uiltgay, andyay erehay ouldshay ebay ethay enescay ofyay erhay earthlyyay unishmentpay; andyay osay,
erchancepay, ethay orturetay ofyay erhay ailyday ameshay ouldway atyay engthlay urgepay erhay
oulsay, andyay orkway outyay anotheryay uritypay anthay atthay ichwhay eshay adhay ostlay; oremay
aint-likesay, ecausebay ethay esultray ofyay artyrdommay.

illustration[ay: Ethay Onesomelay Ellingdway]

Esterhay Ynnepray, ereforethay, idday otnay eeflay. Onyay ethay outskirtsyay ofyay ethay owntay,
ithinway ethay ergevay ofyay ethay eninsulapay, utbay otnay inyay oseclay icinityvay otay anyyay
otheryay abitationhay, erethay asway ayay allsmay atchedthay ottagecay. Ityay adhay eenbay
uiltbay ybay anyay earlieryay ettlersay, andyay abandonedyay ecausebay ethay oilsay aboutyay ityay
asway ootay erilestay orfay ultivationcay, ilewhay itsyay omparativecay emotenessray utpay
ityay outyay ofyay ethay eresphay ofyay atthay ocialsay activityyay ichwhay alreadyyay arkedmay ethay
abitshay ofyay ethay emigrantsyay. Ityay oodstay onyay ethay oreshay, ookinglay acrossyay ayay asinbay
ofyay ethay easay atyay ethay orest-coveredfay illshay, owardstay ethay estway. Ayay umpclay ofyay
ubbyscray eestray, uchsay asyay aloneyay ewgray onyay ethay eninsulapay, idday otnay osay uchmay
oncealcay ethay ottagecay omfray iewvay, asyay eemsay otay enoteday atthay erehay asway omesay
objectyay ichwhay ouldway ainfay avehay eenbay, oryay atyay eastlay oughtyay otay ebay, oncealedcay.
Inyay isthay ittlelay, onesomelay ellingdway, ithway omesay enderslay eansmay atthay eshay
ossessedpay, andyay ybay ethay icenselay ofyay ethay agistratesmay, owhay illstay eptkay anyay
inquisitorialyay atchway overyay erhay, Esterhay establishedyay erselfhay, ithway erhay
infantyay ildchay. Ayay ysticmay adowshay ofyay uspicionsay immediatelyyay attachedyay itselfyay
otay ethay otspay. Ildrenchay, ootay youngyay otay omprehendcay ereforewhay isthay omanway
ouldshay ebay utshay outyay omfray ethay eresphay ofyay umanhay aritieschay, ouldway eepcray
ighnay enoughyay otay eholdbay erhay yingplay erhay eedlenay atyay ethay ottage-windowcay, oryay
andingstay inyay ethay oorwayday, oryay aboringlay inyay erhay ittlelay ardengay, oryay omingcay
orthfay alongyay ethay athwaypay atthay edlay ownwardtay; andyay, iscerningday ethay arletscay
etterlay onyay erhay eastbray, ouldway amperscay offyay ithway ayay angestray, ontagiouscay
earfay.

Onelylay asyay asway Ester’shay ituationsay, andyay ithoutway ayay iendfray onyay earthyay owhay
aredday otay owshay imselfhay, eshay, oweverhay, incurredyay onay iskray ofyay antway. Eshay
ossessedpay anyay artyay atthay ufficedsay, evenyay inyay ayay andlay atthay affordedyay
omparativelycay ittlelay opescay orfay itsyay exerciseyay, otay upplysay oodfay orfay erhay
ivingthray infantyay andyay erselfhay. Ityay asway ethay art—thenyay, asyay ownay, almostyay ethay
onlyyay oneyay ithinway ayay oman’sway asp—ofgray eedleworknay. Eshay orebay onyay erhay
eastbray, inyay ethay uriouslycay embroideredyay etterlay, ayay ecimenspay ofyay erhay
elicateday andyay imaginativeyay illskay, ofyay ichwhay ethay amesday ofyay ayay ourtcay ightmay
adlyglay avehay availedyay emselvesthay, otay addyay ethay icherray andyay oremay iritualspay
adornmentyay ofyay umanhay ingenuityyay otay eirthay abricsfay ofyay ilksay andyay oldgay. Erehay,
indeedyay, inyay ethay ablesay implicitysay atthay enerallygay aracterizedchay ethay
Uritanicpay odesmay ofyay essdray, erethay ightmay ebay anyay infrequentyay allcay orfay ethay
inerfay oductionspray ofyay erhay andiworkhay. Yetyay ethay astetay ofyay ethay ageyay,
emandingday ateverwhay asway elaborateyay inyay ompositionscay ofyay isthay indkay, idday otnay
ailfay otay extendyay itsyay influenceyay overyay ouryay ernstay ogenitorspray, owhay adhay astcay
ehindbay emthay osay anymay ashionsfay ichwhay ityay ightmay eemsay arderhay otay ispenseday
ithway. Ublicpay eremoniescay, uchsay asyay ordinationsyay, ethay installationyay ofyay
agistratesmay, andyay allyay atthay ouldcay ivegay ajestymay otay ethay ormsfay inyay ichwhay ayay
ewnay overnmentgay anifestedmay itselfyay otay ethay eoplepay, ereway, asyay ayay attermay ofyay
olicypay, arkedmay ybay ayay atelystay andyay ell-conductedway eremonialcay, andyay ayay
ombresay, utbay yetyay ayay udiedstay agnificencemay. Eepday uffsray, ainfullypay oughtwray
andsbay, andyay orgeouslygay embroideredyay ovesglay, ereway allyay eemedday ecessarynay otay
ethay officialyay atestay ofyay enmay assumingyay ethay einsray ofyay owerpay; andyay ereway
eadilyray allowedyay otay individualsyay ignifiedday ybay ankray oryay ealthway, evenyay ilewhay
umptuarysay awslay orbadefay esethay andyay imilarsay extravagancesyay otay ethay ebeianplay
orderyay. Inyay ethay arrayyay ofyay uneralsfay, oo,—whethertay orfay ethay apparelyay ofyay ethay
eadday odybay, oryay otay ypifytay, ybay anifoldmay emblematicyay evicesday ofyay ablesay othclay
andyay owysnay awnlay, ethay orrowsay ofyay ethay urvivors,—theresay asway ayay equentfray andyay
aracteristicchay emandday orfay uchsay aborlay asyay Esterhay Ynnepray ouldcay upplysay.
Aby-linen—forbay abiesbay enthay oreway obesray ofyay ate—affordedstay illstay
anotheryay ossibilitypay ofyay oiltay andyay emolumentyay.

Ybay egreesday, ornay eryvay owlyslay, erhay andiworkhay ecamebay atwhay ouldway ownay ebay
ermedtay ethay ashionfay. Etherwhay omfray ommiserationcay orfay ayay omanway ofyay osay
iserablemay ayay estinyday; oryay omfray ethay orbidmay uriositycay atthay ivesgay ayay
ictitiousfay aluevay evenyay otay ommoncay oryay orthlessway ingsthay; oryay ybay ateverwhay
otheryay intangibleyay ircumstancecay asway enthay, asyay ownay, ufficientsay otay estowbay,
onyay omesay ersonspay, atwhay othersyay ightmay eeksay inyay ainvay; oryay ecausebay Esterhay
eallyray illedfay ayay apgay ichwhay ustmay otherwiseyay avehay emainedray acantvay; ityay isyay
ertaincay atthay eshay adhay eadyray andyay airlyfay equitedray employmentyay orfay asyay anymay
ourshay asyay eshay awsay itfay otay occupyyay ithway erhay eedlenay. Anityvay, ityay aymay ebay,
osechay otay ortifymay itselfyay, ybay uttingpay onyay, orfay eremonialscay ofyay omppay andyay
atestay, ethay armentsgay atthay adhay eenbay oughtwray ybay erhay infulsay andshay. Erhay
eedleworknay asway eensay onyay ethay uffray ofyay ethay Overnorgay; ilitarymay enmay oreway ityay
onyay eirthay arfsscay, andyay ethay inistermay onyay ishay andbay; ityay eckedday ethay aby’sbay
ittlelay apcay; ityay asway utshay upyay, otay ebay ildewedmay andyay ouldermay awayyay, inyay ethay
offinscay ofyay ethay eadday. Utbay ityay isyay otnay ecordedray atthay, inyay ayay inglesay
instanceyay, erhay illskay asway alledcay inyay aidyay otay embroideryay ethay itewhay eilvay
ichwhay asway otay overcay ethay urepay ushesblay ofyay ayay idebray. Ethay exceptionyay
indicatedyay ethay ever-relentlessyay igorray ithway ichwhay ocietysay ownedfray uponyay
erhay insay.

Esterhay oughtsay otnay otay acquireyay anythingyay eyondbay ayay ubsistencesay, ofyay ethay
ainestplay andyay ostmay asceticyay escriptionday, orfay erselfhay, andyay ayay implesay
abundanceyay orfay erhay ildchay. Erhay ownyay essdray asway ofyay ethay oarsestcay aterialsmay
andyay ethay ostmay ombresay uehay; ithway onlyyay atthay oneyay ornament,—theyay arletscay
etter,—whichlay ityay asway erhay oomday otay earway. Ethay ild’schay attireyay, onyay ethay
otheryay andhay, asway istinguishedday ybay ayay ancifulfay, oryay, eway ightmay atherray aysay,
ayay antasticfay ingenuityyay, ichwhay ervedsay, indeedyay, otay eightenhay ethay airyyay
armchay atthay earlyyay eganbay otay evelopday itselfyay inyay ethay ittlelay irlgay, utbay ichwhay
appearedyay otay avehay alsoyay ayay eeperday eaningmay. Eway aymay eakspay urtherfay ofyay ityay
ereafterhay. Exceptyay orfay atthay allsmay expenditureyay inyay ethay ecorationday ofyay erhay
infantyay, Esterhay estowedbay allyay erhay uperfluoussay eansmay inyay aritychay, onyay
etcheswray esslay iserablemay anthay erselfhay, andyay owhay otnay unfrequentlyyay
insultedyay ethay andhay atthay edfay emthay. Uchmay ofyay ethay imetay, ichwhay eshay ightmay
eadilyray avehay appliedyay otay ethay etterbay effortsyay ofyay erhay artyay, eshay employedyay inyay
akingmay oarsecay armentsgay orfay ethay oorpay. Ityay isyay obablepray atthay erethay asway anyay
ideayay ofyay enancepay inyay isthay odemay ofyay occupationyay, andyay atthay eshay offeredyay upyay ayay
ealray acrificesay ofyay enjoymentyay, inyay evotingday osay anymay ourshay otay uchsay uderay
andiworkhay. Eshay adhay inyay erhay aturenay ayay ichray, oluptuousvay, Orientalyay
aracteristic,—achay astetay orfay ethay orgeouslygay eautifulbay, ichwhay, avesay inyay
ethay exquisiteyay oductionspray ofyay erhay eedlenay, oundfay othingnay elseyay, inyay allyay
ethay ossibilitiespay ofyay erhay ifelay, otay exerciseyay itselfyay uponyay. Omenway eriveday
ayay easureplay, incomprehensibleyay otay ethay otheryay exsay, omfray ethay elicateday oiltay
ofyay ethay eedlenay. Otay Esterhay Ynnepray ityay ightmay avehay eenbay ayay odemay ofyay
expressingyay, andyay ereforethay oothingsay, ethay assionpay ofyay erhay ifelay. Ikelay allyay
otheryay oysjay, eshay ejectedray ityay asyay insay. Isthay orbidmay eddlingmay ofyay onsciencecay
ithway anyay immaterialyay attermay etokenedbay, ityay isyay otay ebay earedfay, onay enuinegay
andyay eadfaststay enitencepay, utbay omethingsay oubtfulday, omethingsay atthay ightmay
ebay eeplyday ongwray, eneathbay.

Inyay isthay annermay, Esterhay Ynnepray amecay otay avehay ayay artpay otay erformpay inyay ethay
orldway. Ithway erhay ativenay energyyay ofyay aracterchay, andyay areray apacitycay, ityay
ouldcay otnay entirelyyay astcay erhay offyay, althoughyay ityay adhay etsay ayay arkmay uponyay erhay,
oremay intolerableyay otay ayay oman’sway earthay anthay atthay ichwhay andedbray ethay owbray
ofyay Aincay. Inyay allyay erhay intercourseyay ithway ocietysay, oweverhay, erethay asway
othingnay atthay ademay erhay eelfay asyay ifyay eshay elongedbay otay ityay. Everyyay esturegay,
everyyay ordway, andyay evenyay ethay ilencesay ofyay osethay ithway omwhay eshay amecay inyay
ontactcay, impliedyay, andyay oftenyay expressedyay, atthay eshay asway anishedbay, andyay asyay
uchmay aloneyay asyay ifyay eshay inhabitedyay anotheryay eresphay, oryay ommunicatedcay ithway
ethay ommoncay aturenay ybay otheryay organsyay andyay ensessay anthay ethay estray ofyay umanhay
indkay. Eshay oodstay apartyay omfray oralmay interestsyay, yetyay oseclay esidebay emthay,
ikelay ayay ostghay atthay evisitsray ethay amiliarfay iresidefay, andyay ancay onay ongerlay
akemay itselfyay eensay oryay eltfay; onay oremay ilesmay ithway ethay ouseholdhay oyjay, ornay
ournmay ithway ethay indredkay orrowsay; oryay, ouldshay ityay ucceedsay inyay anifestingmay
itsyay orbiddenfay ympathysay, awakeningyay onlyyay errortay andyay orriblehay epugnanceray.
Esethay emotionsyay, inyay actfay, andyay itsyay itterestbay ornscay esidesbay, eemedsay otay ebay
ethay olesay ortionpay atthay eshay etainedray inyay ethay universalyay earthay. Ityay asway otnay
anyay ageyay ofyay elicacyday; andyay erhay ositionpay, althoughyay eshay understoodyay ityay ellway,
andyay asway inyay ittlelay angerday ofyay orgettingfay ityay, asway oftenyay oughtbray eforebay
erhay ividvay elf-perceptionsay, ikelay ayay ewnay anguishyay, ybay ethay udestray ouchtay
uponyay ethay enderesttay otspay. Ethay oorpay, asyay eway avehay alreadyyay aidsay, omwhay eshay
oughtsay outyay otay ebay ethay objectsyay ofyay erhay ountybay, oftenyay eviledray ethay andhay
atthay asway etchedstray orthfay otay uccorsay emthay. Amesday ofyay elevatedyay ankray,
ikewiselay, osewhay oorsday eshay enteredyay inyay ethay ayway ofyay erhay occupationyay, ereway
accustomedyay otay istilday opsdray ofyay itternessbay intoyay erhay earthay; ometimessay
oughthray atthay alchemyyay ofyay uietqay alicemay, ybay ichwhay omenway ancay oncoctcay ayay
ubtlesay oisonpay omfray ordinaryyay iflestray; andyay ometimessay, alsoyay, ybay ayay oarsercay
expressionyay, atthay ellfay uponyay ethay ufferer’ssay efencelessday eastbray ikelay ayay
oughray owblay uponyay anyay ulceratedyay oundway. Esterhay adhay ooledschay erselfhay onglay
andyay ellway; eshay evernay espondedray otay esethay attacksyay, avesay ybay ayay ushflay ofyay
imsoncray atthay oseray irrepressiblyyay overyay erhay alepay eekchay, andyay againyay
ubsidedsay intoyay ethay epthsday ofyay erhay osombay. Eshay asway atient,—apay artyrmay,
indeed,—butyay eshay orborefay otay aypray orfay erhay enemiesyay; estlay, inyay itespay ofyay
erhay orgivingfay aspirationsyay, ethay ordsway ofyay ethay essingblay ouldshay ubbornlystay
isttway emselvesthay intoyay ayay ursecay.

Ontinuallycay, andyay inyay ayay ousandthay otheryay aysway, idday eshay eelfay ethay
innumerableyay obsthray ofyay anguishyay atthay adhay eenbay osay unninglycay ontrivedcay orfay
erhay ybay ethay undyingyay, ethay ever-activeyay entencesay ofyay ethay Uritanpay ibunaltray.
Ergymenclay ausedpay inyay ethay eetstray otay addressyay ordsway ofyay exhortationyay, atthay
oughtbray ayay owdcray, ithway itsyay ingledmay ingray andyay ownfray, aroundyay ethay oorpay,
infulsay omanway. Ifyay eshay enteredyay ayay urchchay, ustingtray otay areshay ethay Abbathsay
ilesmay ofyay ethay Universalyay Atherfay, ityay asway oftenyay erhay ishapmay otay indfay erselfhay
ethay exttay ofyay ethay iscourseday. Eshay ewgray otay avehay ayay eaddray ofyay ildrenchay; orfay
eythay adhay imbibedyay omfray eirthay arentspay ayay aguevay ideayay ofyay omethingsay orriblehay
inyay isthay earydray omanway, idingglay ilentlysay oughthray ethay owntay, ithway evernay
anyyay ompanioncay utbay oneyay onlyyay ildchay. Ereforethay, irstfay allowingyay erhay otay
asspay, eythay ursuedpay erhay atyay ayay istanceday ithway illshray iescray, andyay ethay
utteranceyay ofyay ayay ordway atthay adhay onay istinctday urportpay otay eirthay ownyay
indsmay, utbay asway onenay ethay esslay erribletay otay erhay, asyay oceedingpray omfray ipslay
atthay abbledbay ityay unconsciouslyyay. Ityay eemedsay otay argueyay osay ideway ayay iffusionday
ofyay erhay ameshay, atthay allyay aturenay ewknay ofyay ityay; ityay ouldcay avehay ausedcay erhay onay
eeperday angpay, adhay ethay eaveslay ofyay ethay eestray isperedwhay ethay arkday orystay
amongyay emselves,—hadthay ethay ummersay eezebray urmuredmay aboutyay it,—hadyay ethay
intryway astblay iekedshray ityay aloudyay! Anotheryay eculiarpay orturetay asway eltfay inyay
ethay azegay ofyay ayay ewnay eyeyay. Enwhay angersstray ookedlay uriouslycay atyay ethay arletscay
etter,—andlay onenay everyay ailedfay otay oday o,—theysay andedbray ityay afreshyay intoyay
Ester’shay oulsay; osay atthay, oftentimesyay, eshay ouldcay arcelyscay efrainray, yetyay
alwaysyay idday efrainray, omfray overingcay ethay ymbolsay ithway erhay andhay. Utbay enthay,
againyay, anyay accustomedyay eyeyay adhay ikewiselay itsyay ownyay anguishyay otay inflictyay. Itsyay
oolcay arestay ofyay amiliarityfay asway intolerableyay. Omfray irstfay otay astlay, inyay
ortshay, Esterhay Ynnepray adhay alwaysyay isthay eadfuldray agonyyay inyay eelingfay ayay umanhay
eyeyay uponyay ethay okentay; ethay otspay evernay ewgray allouscay; ityay eemedsay, onyay ethay
ontrarycay, otay owgray oremay ensitivesay ithway ailyday orturetay.

illustration[ay: Onelylay Ootstepsfay]

Utbay ometimessay, onceyay inyay anymay aysday, oryay erchancepay inyay anymay onthsmay, eshay
eltfay anyay eye—ayay umanhay eye—uponyay ethay ignominiousyay andbray, atthay eemedsay otay
ivegay ayay omentarymay eliefray, asyay ifyay alfhay ofyay erhay agonyyay ereway aredshay. Ethay extnay
instantyay, ackbay ityay allyay ushedray againyay, ithway illstay ayay eeperday obthray ofyay ainpay;
orfay, inyay atthay iefbray intervalyay, eshay adhay innedsay anewyay. Adhay Esterhay innedsay
aloneyay?

Erhay imaginationyay asway omewhatsay affectedyay, andyay, adhay eshay eenbay ofyay ayay oftersay
oralmay andyay intellectualyay ibrefay, ouldway avehay eenbay illstay oremay osay, ybay ethay
angestray andyay olitarysay anguishyay ofyay erhay ifelay. Alkingway otay andyay ofray, ithway
osethay onelylay ootstepsfay, inyay ethay ittlelay orldway ithway ichwhay eshay asway
outwardlyyay onnectedcay, ityay ownay andyay enthay appearedyay otay Ester,—ifhay
altogetheryay ancyfay, ityay asway everthelessnay ootay otentpay otay ebay esisted,—sheray
eltfay oryay anciedfay, enthay, atthay ethay arletscay etterlay adhay endowedyay erhay ithway ayay
ewnay ensesay. Eshay udderedshay otay elievebay, yetyay ouldcay otnay elphay elievingbay,
atthay ityay avegay erhay ayay ympatheticsay owledgeknay ofyay ethay iddenhay insay inyay otheryay
eartshay. Eshay asway error-strickentay ybay ethay evelationsray atthay ereway usthay
ademay. Atwhay ereway eythay? Ouldcay eythay ebay otheryay anthay ethay insidiousyay isperswhay
ofyay ethay adbay angelyay, owhay ouldway ainfay avehay ersuadedpay ethay ugglingstray omanway,
asyay yetyay onlyyay alfhay ishay ictimvay, atthay ethay outwardyay uisegay ofyay uritypay asway utbay
ayay ielay, andyay atthay, ifyay uthtray ereway everywhereyay otay ebay ownshay, ayay arletscay
etterlay ouldway azeblay orthfay onyay anymay ayay osombay esidesbay Esterhay Ynne’spray? Oryay,
ustmay eshay eceiveray osethay intimations—soyay obscureyay, yetyay osay istinct—asday
uthtray? Inyay allyay erhay iserablemay experienceyay, erethay asway othingnay elseyay osay
awfulyay andyay osay oathsomelay asyay isthay ensesay. Ityay erplexedpay, asyay ellway asyay ockedshay
erhay, ybay ethay irreverentyay inopportunenessyay ofyay ethay occasionsyay atthay oughtbray
ityay intoyay ividvay actionyay. Ometimessay ethay edray infamyyay uponyay erhay eastbray ouldway
ivegay ayay ympatheticsay obthray, asyay eshay assedpay earnay ayay enerablevay inistermay oryay
agistratemay, ethay odelmay ofyay ietypay andyay usticejay, otay omwhay atthay ageyay ofyay
antiqueyay everenceray ookedlay upyay, asyay otay ayay ortalmay anmay inyay ellowshipfay ithway
angelsyay. at“whay evilyay ingthay isyay atyay andhay?” ouldway Esterhay aysay otay erselfhay.
Iftinglay erhay eluctantray eyesyay, erethay ouldway ebay othingnay umanhay ithinway ethay
opescay ofyay iewvay, avesay ethay ormfay ofyay isthay earthlyyay aintsay! Againyay, ayay ysticmay
isterhoodsay ouldway ontumaciouslycay assertyay itselfyay, asyay eshay etmay ethay
anctifiedsay ownfray ofyay omesay atronmay, owhay, accordingyay otay ethay umorray ofyay allyay
onguestay, adhay eptkay oldcay owsnay ithinway erhay osombay oughoutthray ifelay. Atthay
unsunnedyay owsnay inyay ethay atron’smay osombay, andyay ethay urningbay ameshay onyay Esterhay
Ynne’s,—whatpray adhay ethay otway inyay ommoncay? Oryay, onceyay oremay, ethay electricyay
illthray ouldway ivegay erhay arning,—“beholdway, Esterhay, erehay isyay ayay
ompanion!”—andcay, ookinglay upyay, eshay ouldway etectday ethay eyesyay ofyay ayay youngyay
aidenmay ancingglay atyay ethay arletscay etterlay, ylyshay andyay asideyay, andyay uicklyqay
avertedyay ithway ayay aintfay, illchay imsoncray inyay erhay eekschay; asyay ifyay erhay uritypay
ereway omewhatsay ulliedsay ybay atthay omentarymay anceglay. Oyay Iendfay, osewhay
alismantay asway atthay atalfay ymbolsay, ouldstway outhay eavelay othingnay, etherwhay inyay
youthyay oryay ageyay, orfay isthay oorpay innersay otay evere?—suchray osslay ofyay aithfay isyay
everyay oneyay ofyay ethay addestsay esultsray ofyay insay. Ebay ityay acceptedyay asyay ayay oofpray atthay
allyay asway otnay orruptcay inyay isthay oorpay ictimvay ofyay erhay ownyay ailtyfray, andyay an’smay
ardhay awlay, atthay Esterhay Ynnepray yetyay uggledstray otay elievebay atthay onay
ellow-mortalfay asway uiltygay ikelay erselfhay.

Ethay ulgarvay, owhay, inyay osethay earydray oldyay imestay, ereway alwaysyay ontributingcay ayay
otesquegray orrorhay otay atwhay interestedyay eirthay imaginationsyay, adhay ayay orystay
aboutyay ethay arletscay etterlay ichwhay eway ightmay eadilyray orkway upyay intoyay ayay
errifictay egendlay. Eythay averredyay, atthay ethay ymbolsay asway otnay eremay arletscay
othclay, ingedtay inyay anyay earthlyyay ye-potday, utbay asway ed-hotray ithway infernalyay
irefay, andyay ouldcay ebay eensay owingglay allyay alightyay, eneverwhay Esterhay Ynnepray
alkedway abroadyay inyay ethay ight-timenay. Andyay eway ustmay eedsnay aysay, ityay earedsay
Ester’shay osombay osay eeplyday, atthay erhapspay erethay asway oremay uthtray inyay ethay
umorray anthay ouryay odernmay incredulityyay aymay ebay inclinedyay otay admityay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Ivay.

                                Earlpay.


illustration[ay]

Eway avehay asyay yetyay ardlyhay okenspay ofyay ethay infantyay; atthay ittlelay eaturecray,
osewhay innocentyay ifelay adhay ungspray, ybay ethay inscrutableyay ecreeday ofyay
Ovidencepray, ayay ovelylay andyay immortalyay owerflay, outyay ofyay ethay ankray uxuriancelay
ofyay ayay uiltygay assionpay. Owhay angestray ityay eemedsay otay ethay adsay omanway, asyay eshay
atchedway ethay owthgray, andyay ethay eautybay atthay ecamebay everyyay ayday oremay
illiantbray, andyay ethay intelligenceyay atthay ewthray itsyay uiveringqay unshinesay overyay
ethay inytay eaturesfay ofyay isthay ildchay! Erhay Earl!—forpay osay adhay Esterhay alledcay
erhay; otnay asyay ayay amenay expressiveyay ofyay erhay aspectyay, ichwhay adhay othingnay ofyay ethay
almcay, itewhay, unimpassionedyay ustrelay atthay ouldway ebay indicatedyay ybay ethay
omparisoncay. Utbay eshay amednay ethay infantyay earl“pay,” asyay eingbay ofyay eatgray
ice,—purchasedpray ithway allyay eshay ad,—herhay other’smay onlyyay easuretray! Owhay
angestray, indeedyay! Anmay adhay arkedmay isthay oman’sway insay ybay ayay arletscay etterlay,
ichwhay adhay uchsay otentpay andyay isastrousday efficacyyay atthay onay umanhay ympathysay
ouldcay eachray erhay, avesay ityay ereway infulsay ikelay erselfhay. Odgay, asyay ayay irectday
onsequencecay ofyay ethay insay ichwhay anmay usthay unishedpay, adhay ivengay erhay ayay ovelylay
ildchay, osewhay aceplay asway onyay atthay amesay ishonoredday osombay, otay onnectcay erhay
arentpay oreverfay ithway ethay aceray andyay escentday ofyay ortalsmay, andyay otay ebay inallyfay
ayay essedblay oulsay inyay eavenhay! Yetyay esethay oughtsthay affectedyay Esterhay Ynnepray
esslay ithway opehay anthay apprehensionyay. Eshay ewknay atthay erhay eedday adhay eenbay
evilyay; eshay ouldcay avehay onay aithfay, ereforethay, atthay itsyay esultray ouldway ebay
oodgay. Ayday afteryay ayday, eshay ookedlay earfullyfay intoyay ethay ild’schay expandingyay
aturenay, everyay eadingdray otay etectday omesay arkday andyay ildway eculiaritypay, atthay
ouldshay orrespondcay ithway ethay uiltinessgay otay ichwhay eshay owedyay erhay eingbay.

Ertainlycay, erethay asway onay ysicalphay efectday. Ybay itsyay erfectpay apeshay, itsyay
igorvay, andyay itsyay aturalnay exterityday inyay ethay useyay ofyay allyay itsyay untriedyay imbslay,
ethay infantyay asway orthyway otay avehay eenbay oughtbray orthfay inyay Edenyay; orthyway otay
avehay eenbay eftlay erethay, otay ebay ethay aythingplay ofyay ethay angelsyay, afteryay ethay
orld’sway irstfay arentspay ereway ivendray outyay. Ethay ildchay adhay ayay ativenay acegray
ichwhay oesday otnay invariablyyay oexistcay ithway aultlessfay eautybay; itsyay attireyay,
oweverhay implesay, alwaysyay impressedyay ethay eholderbay asyay ifyay ityay ereway ethay eryvay
arbgay atthay eciselypray ecamebay ityay estbay. Utbay ittlelay Earlpay asway otnay adclay inyay
usticray eedsway. Erhay othermay, ithway ayay orbidmay urposepay atthay aymay ebay etterbay
understoodyay ereafterhay, adhay oughtbay ethay ichestray issuestay atthay ouldcay ebay
ocuredpray, andyay allowedyay erhay imaginativeyay acultyfay itsyay ullfay ayplay inyay ethay
arrangementyay andyay ecorationday ofyay ethay essesdray ichwhay ethay ildchay oreway, eforebay
ethay ublicpay eyeyay. Osay agnificentmay asway ethay allsmay igurefay, enwhay usthay
arrayedyay, andyay uchsay asway ethay endorsplay ofyay Earl’spay ownyay operpray eautybay,
iningshay oughthray ethay orgeousgay obesray ichwhay ightmay avehay extinguishedyay ayay
alerpay ovelinesslay, atthay erethay asway anyay absoluteyay irclecay ofyay adianceray aroundyay
erhay, onyay ethay arksomeday ottagecay oorflay. Andyay yetyay ayay ussetray owngay, orntay andyay
oiledsay ithway ethay ild’schay uderay ayplay, ademay ayay icturepay ofyay erhay ustjay asyay
erfectpay. Earl’spay aspectyay asway imbuedyay ithway ayay ellspay ofyay infiniteyay arietyvay;
inyay isthay oneyay ildchay erethay ereway anymay ildrenchay, omprehendingcay ethay ullfay
opescay etweenbay ethay ild-flowerway ettinesspray ofyay ayay easant-babypay, andyay ethay
omppay, inyay ittlelay, ofyay anyay infantyay incesspray. Oughoutthray allyay, oweverhay, erethay
asway ayay aittray ofyay assionpay, ayay ertaincay epthday ofyay uehay, ichwhay eshay evernay ostlay;
andyay ifyay, inyay anyyay ofyay erhay angeschay, eshay adhay owngray ainterfay oryay alerpay, eshay
ouldway avehay easedcay otay ebay erself,—ithay ouldway avehay eenbay onay ongerlay Earlpay!

Isthay outwardyay utabilitymay indicatedyay, andyay idday otnay oremay anthay airlyfay
expressyay, ethay ariousvay opertiespray ofyay erhay inneryay ifelay. Erhay aturenay appearedyay
otay ossesspay epthday, ootay, asyay ellway asyay arietyvay; ut—orbay elseyay Ester’shay earsfay
eceivedday er—ithay ackedlay eferenceray andyay adaptationyay otay ethay orldway intoyay
ichwhay eshay asway ornbay. Ethay ildchay ouldcay otnay ebay ademay amenableyay otay ulesray. Inyay
ivinggay erhay existenceyay, ayay eatgray awlay adhay eenbay okenbray; andyay ethay esultray asway
ayay eingbay osewhay elementsyay ereway erhapspay eautifulbay andyay illiantbray, utbay allyay
inyay isorderday; oryay ithway anyay orderyay eculiarpay otay emselvesthay, amidstyay ichwhay ethay
ointpay ofyay arietyvay andyay arrangementyay asway ifficultday oryay impossibleyay otay ebay
iscoveredday. Esterhay ouldcay onlyyay accountyay orfay ethay ild’schay aracter—andchay
evenyay enthay ostmay aguelyvay andyay imperfectly—byyay ecallingray atwhay eshay erselfhay
adhay eenbay, uringday atthay omentousmay eriodpay ilewhay Earlpay asway imbibingyay erhay
oulsay omfray ethay iritualspay orldway, andyay erhay odilybay amefray omfray itsyay aterialmay
ofyay earthyay. Ethay other’smay impassionedyay atestay adhay eenbay ethay ediummay oughthray
ichwhay ereway ansmittedtray otay ethay unbornyay infantyay ethay aysray ofyay itsyay oralmay
ifelay; andyay, oweverhay itewhay andyay earclay originallyyay, eythay adhay akentay ethay eepday
ainsstay ofyay imsoncray andyay oldgay, ethay ieryfay ustrelay, ethay ackblay adowshay, andyay
ethay untemperedyay ightlay ofyay ethay interveningyay ubstancesay. Aboveyay allyay, ethay
arfareway ofyay Ester’shay iritspay, atyay atthay epochyay, asway erpetuatedpay inyay Earlpay.
Eshay ouldcay ecognizeray erhay ildway, esperateday, efiantday oodmay, ethay ightinessflay
ofyay erhay empertay, andyay evenyay omesay ofyay ethay eryvay oud-shapesclay ofyay oomglay andyay
espondencyday atthay adhay oodedbray inyay erhay earthay. Eythay ereway ownay illuminatedyay
ybay ethay orningmay adianceray ofyay ayay youngyay ild’schay ispositionday, utbay aterlay inyay
ethay ayday ofyay earthlyyay existenceyay ightmay ebay olificpray ofyay ethay ormstay andyay
irlwindwhay.

Ethay isciplineday ofyay ethay amilyfay, inyay osethay aysday, asway ofyay ayay arfay oremay igidray
indkay anthay ownay. Ethay ownfray, ethay arshhay ebukeray, ethay equentfray applicationyay
ofyay ethay odray, enjoinedyay ybay Ipturalscray authorityyay, ereway usedyay, otnay erelymay inyay
ethay ayway ofyay unishmentpay orfay actualyay offencesyay, utbay asyay ayay olesomewhay egimenray
orfay ethay owthgray andyay omotionpray ofyay allyay ildishchay irtuesvay. Esterhay Ynnepray,
everthelessnay, ethay onelylay othermay ofyay isthay oneyay ildchay, anray ittlelay iskray ofyay
erringyay onyay ethay idesay ofyay undueyay everitysay. Indfulmay, oweverhay, ofyay erhay ownyay
errorsyay andyay isfortunesmay, eshay earlyyay oughtsay otay imposeyay ayay endertay, utbay
ictstray ontrolcay overyay ethay infantyay immortalityyay atthay asway ommittedcay otay erhay
argechay. Utbay ethay asktay asway eyondbay erhay illskay. Afteryay estingtay othbay ilessmay
andyay ownsfray, andyay ovingpray atthay eithernay odemay ofyay eatmenttray ossessedpay anyyay
alculablecay influenceyay, Esterhay asway ultimatelyyay ompelledcay otay andstay asideyay,
andyay ermitpay ethay ildchay otay ebay ayedsway ybay erhay ownyay impulsesyay. Ysicalphay
ompulsioncay oryay estraintray asway effectualyay, ofyay oursecay, ilewhay ityay astedlay. Asyay
otay anyyay otheryay indkay ofyay isciplineday, etherwhay addressedyay otay erhay indmay oryay
earthay, ittlelay Earlpay ightmay oryay ightmay otnay ebay ithinway itsyay eachray, inyay
accordanceyay ithway ethay apricecay atthay uledray ethay omentmay. Erhay othermay, ilewhay
Earlpay asway yetyay anyay infantyay, ewgray acquaintedyay ithway ayay ertaincay eculiarpay ooklay,
atthay arnedway erhay enwhay ityay ouldway ebay aborlay ownthray awayyay otay insistyay,
ersuadepay, oryay eadplay. Ityay asway ayay ooklay osay intelligentyay, yetyay inexplicableyay,
osay erversepay, ometimessay osay aliciousmay, utbay enerallygay accompaniedyay ybay ayay
ildway owflay ofyay iritsspay, atthay Esterhay ouldcay otnay elphay uestioningqay, atyay uchsay
omentsmay, etherwhay Earlpay ereway ayay umanhay ildchay. Eshay eemedsay atherray anyay airyyay
itespray, ichwhay, afteryay ayingplay itsyay antasticfay ortsspay orfay ayay ittlelay ilewhay
uponyay ethay ottagecay oorflay, ouldway itflay awayyay ithway ayay ockingmay ilesmay. Eneverwhay
atthay ooklay appearedyay inyay erhay ildway, ightbray, eeplyday ackblay eyesyay, ityay investedyay
erhay ithway ayay angestray emotenessray andyay intangibilityyay; ityay asway asyay ifyay eshay ereway
overinghay inyay ethay airyay andyay ightmay anishvay, ikelay ayay immeringglay ightlay, atthay
omescay eway owknay otnay encewhay, andyay oesgay eway owknay otnay itherwhay. Eholdingbay ityay,
Esterhay asway onstrainedcay otay ushray owardstay ethay ild,—tochay ursuepay ethay
ittlelay elfyay inyay ethay ightflay ichwhay eshay invariablyyay egan,—tobay atchsnay erhay otay
erhay osombay, ithway ayay oseclay essurepray andyay earnestyay isses,—notkay osay uchmay omfray
overflowingyay ovelay, asyay otay assureyay erselfhay atthay Earlpay asway eshflay andyay oodblay,
andyay otnay utterlyyay elusiveday. Utbay Earl’spay aughlay, enwhay eshay asway aughtcay,
oughthay ullfay ofyay errimentmay andyay usicmay, ademay erhay othermay oremay oubtfulday anthay
eforebay.

Eart-smittenhay atyay isthay ewilderingbay andyay afflingbay ellspay, atthay osay oftenyay
amecay etweenbay erselfhay andyay erhay olesay easuretray, omwhay eshay adhay oughtbay osay
earday, andyay owhay asway allyay erhay orldway, Esterhay ometimessay urstbay intoyay
assionatepay earstay. Enthay, erhaps,—forpay erethay asway onay oreseeingfay owhay ityay
ightmay affectyay er,—pearlhay ouldway ownfray, andyay enchclay erhay ittlelay istfay, andyay
ardenhay erhay allsmay eaturesfay intoyay ayay ernstay, unsympathizingyay ooklay ofyay
iscontentday. Otnay eldomsay, eshay ouldway aughlay anewyay, andyay ouderlay anthay eforebay,
ikelay ayay ingthay incapableyay andyay unintelligentyay ofyay umanhay orrowsay. Or—butyay isthay
oremay arelyray appened—shehay ouldway ebay onvulsedcay ithway ayay ageray ofyay iefgray, andyay
obsay outyay erhay ovelay orfay erhay othermay, inyay okenbray ordsway, andyay eemsay intentyay onyay
ovingpray atthay eshay adhay ayay earthay, ybay eakingbray ityay. Yetyay Esterhay asway ardlyhay
