afesay inyay onfidingcay erselfhay otay atthay ustygay endernesstay; ityay assedpay, asyay
uddenlysay asyay ityay amecay. Oodingbray overyay allyay esethay attersmay, ethay othermay eltfay
ikelay oneyay owhay ashay evokedyay ayay iritspay, utbay, ybay omesay irregularityyay inyay ethay
ocesspray ofyay onjurationcay, ashay ailedfay otay inway ethay aster-wordmay atthay ouldshay
ontrolcay isthay ewnay andyay incomprehensibleyay intelligenceyay. Erhay onlyyay ealray
omfortcay asway enwhay ethay ildchay aylay inyay ethay acidityplay ofyay eepslay. Enthay eshay asway
uresay ofyay erhay, andyay astedtay ourshay ofyay uietqay, adsay, eliciousday appinesshay;
until—perhapsyay ithway atthay erversepay expressionyay immeringglay omfray eneathbay
erhay openingyay ids—littlelay Earlpay awokeyay!

Owhay oon—withsay atwhay angestray apidityray, indeed!—didyay Earlpay arriveyay atyay anyay
ageyay atthay asway apablecay ofyay ocialsay intercourseyay, eyondbay ethay other’smay
ever-readyyay ilesmay andyay onsense-wordsnay! Andyay enthay atwhay ayay appinesshay ouldway
ityay avehay eenbay, ouldcay Esterhay Ynnepray avehay eardhay erhay earclay, ird-likebay
oicevay inglingmay ithway ethay uproaryay ofyay otheryay ildishchay oicesvay, andyay avehay
istinguishedday andyay unravelledyay erhay ownyay arling’sday onestay, amidyay allyay ethay
entangledyay outcryyay ofyay ayay oupgray ofyay ortivespay ildrenchay! Utbay isthay ouldcay evernay
ebay. Earlpay asway ayay ornbay outcastyay ofyay ethay infantileyay orldway. Anyay impyay ofyay evilyay,
emblemyay andyay oductpray ofyay insay, eshay adhay onay ightray amongyay istenedchray infantsyay.
Othingnay asway oremay emarkableray anthay ethay instinctyay, asyay ityay eemedsay, ithway
ichwhay ethay ildchay omprehendedcay erhay onelinesslay; ethay estinyday atthay adhay
awndray anyay inviolableyay irclecay oundray aboutyay erhay; ethay olewhay eculiaritypay, inyay
ortshay, ofyay erhay ositionpay inyay espectray otay otheryay ildrenchay. Evernay, incesay erhay
eleaseray omfray isonpray, adhay Esterhay etmay ethay ublicpay azegay ithoutway erhay. Inyay
allyay erhay alksway aboutyay ethay owntay, Earlpay, ootay, asway erethay; irstfay asyay ethay abebay
inyay armsyay, andyay afterwardsyay asyay ethay ittlelay irlgay, allsmay ompanioncay ofyay erhay
othermay, oldinghay ayay orefingerfay ithway erhay olewhay aspgray, andyay ippingtray alongyay
atyay ethay ateray ofyay eethray oryay ourfay ootstepsfay otay oneyay ofyay Ester’shay. Eshay awsay ethay
ildrenchay ofyay ethay ettlementsay, onyay ethay assygray arginmay ofyay ethay eetstray, oryay atyay
ethay omesticday esholdsthray, isportingday emselvesthay inyay uchsay imgray ashionfay
asyay ethay Uritanicpay urturenay ouldway ermitpay; ayingplay atyay oinggay otay urchchay,
erchancepay; oryay atyay ourgingscay Uakersqay; oryay akingtay alpsscay inyay ayay am-fightshay
ithway ethay Indiansyay; oryay aringscay oneyay anotheryay ithway eaksfray ofyay imitativeyay
itchcraftway. Earlpay awsay, andyay azedgay intentlyyay, utbay evernay oughtsay otay akemay
acquaintanceyay. Ifyay okenspay otay, eshay ouldway otnay eakspay againyay. Ifyay ethay ildrenchay
atheredgay aboutyay erhay, asyay eythay ometimessay idday, Earlpay ouldway owgray ositivelypay
erribletay inyay erhay unypay athwray, atchingsnay upyay onesstay otay ingflay atyay emthay, ithway
illshray, incoherentyay exclamationsyay, atthay ademay erhay othermay embletray, ecausebay
eythay adhay osay uchmay ethay oundsay ofyay ayay itch’sway anathemasyay inyay omesay unknownyay
onguetay.

Ethay uthtray asway, atthay ethay ittlelay Uritanspay, eingbay ofyay ethay ostmay intolerantyay
oodbray atthay everyay ivedlay, adhay otgay ayay aguevay ideayay ofyay omethingsay outlandishyay,
unearthlyyay, oryay atyay ariancevay ithway ordinaryyay ashionsfay, inyay ethay othermay andyay
ildchay; andyay ereforethay ornedscay emthay inyay eirthay eartshay, andyay otnay
unfrequentlyyay eviledray emthay ithway eirthay onguestay. Earlpay eltfay ethay
entimentsay, andyay equitedray ityay ithway ethay itterestbay atredhay atthay ancay ebay
upposedsay otay ankleray inyay ayay ildishchay osombay. Esethay outbreaksyay ofyay ayay iercefay
empertay adhay ayay indkay ofyay aluevay, andyay evenyay omfortcay, orfay erhay othermay; ecausebay
erethay asway atyay eastlay anyay intelligibleyay earnestnessyay inyay ethay oodmay, insteadyay ofyay
ethay itfulfay apricecay atthay osay oftenyay artedthway erhay inyay ethay ild’schay
anifestationsmay. Ityay appalledyay erhay, everthelessnay, otay iscernday erehay, againyay,
ayay adowyshay eflectionray ofyay ethay evilyay atthay adhay existedyay inyay erselfhay. Allyay isthay
enmityyay andyay assionpay adhay Earlpay inheritedyay, ybay inalienableyay ightray, outyay ofyay
Ester’shay earthay. Othermay andyay aughterday oodstay ogethertay inyay ethay amesay irclecay
ofyay eclusionsay omfray umanhay ocietysay; andyay inyay ethay aturenay ofyay ethay ildchay eemedsay
otay ebay erpetuatedpay osethay unquietyay elementsyay atthay adhay istractedday Esterhay
Ynnepray eforebay Earl’spay irthbay, utbay adhay incesay egunbay otay ebay oothedsay awayyay ybay
ethay ofteningsay influencesyay ofyay aternitymay.

Atyay omehay, ithinway andyay aroundyay erhay other’smay ottagecay, Earlpay antedway otnay ayay
ideway andyay ariousvay irclecay ofyay acquaintanceyay. Ethay ellspay ofyay ifelay entway orthfay
omfray erhay ever-creativeyay iritspay, andyay ommunicatedcay itselfyay otay ayay ousandthay
objectsyay, asyay ayay orchtay indleskay ayay ameflay ereverwhay ityay aymay ebay appliedyay. Ethay
unlikeliestyay aterials—amay ickstay, ayay unchbay ofyay agsray, ayay ower—wereflay ethay
uppetspay ofyay Earl’spay itchcraftway, andyay, ithoutway undergoingyay anyyay outwardyay
angechay, ecamebay irituallyspay adaptedyay otay ateverwhay amadray occupiedyay ethay
agestay ofyay erhay inneryay orldway. Erhay oneyay aby-voicebay ervedsay ayay ultitudemay ofyay
imaginaryyay ersonagespay, oldyay andyay youngyay, otay alktay ithalway. Ethay ine-treespay,
agedyay, ackblay andyay olemnsay, andyay ingingflay oansgray andyay otheryay elancholymay
utterancesyay onyay ethay eezebray, eedednay ittlelay ansformationtray otay igurefay asyay
Uritanpay eldersyay; ethay ugliestyay eedsway ofyay ethay ardengay ereway eirthay ildrenchay,
omwhay Earlpay otesmay ownday andyay uprootedyay, ostmay unmercifullyyay. Ityay asway
onderfulway, ethay astvay arietyvay ofyay ormsfay intoyay ichwhay eshay ewthray erhay
intellectyay, ithway onay ontinuitycay, indeedyay, utbay artingday upyay andyay ancingday,
alwaysyay inyay ayay atestay ofyay eternaturalpray activity,—soonyay inkingsay ownday, asyay ifyay
exhaustedyay ybay osay apidray andyay everishfay ayay idetay ofyay ife,—andlay ucceededsay ybay
otheryay apesshay ofyay ayay imilarsay ildway energyyay. Ityay asway ikelay othingnay osay uchmay asyay
ethay antasmagoricphay ayplay ofyay ethay orthernnay ightslay. Inyay ethay eremay exerciseyay
ofyay ethay ancyfay, oweverhay, andyay ethay ortivenessspay ofyay ayay owinggray indmay, erethay
ightmay ebay ittlelay oremay anthay asway observableyay inyay otheryay ildrenchay ofyay ightbray
acultiesfay; exceptyay asyay Earlpay, inyay ethay earthday ofyay umanhay aymatesplay, asway
ownthray oremay uponyay ethay isionaryvay ongthray ichwhay eshay eatedcray. Ethay
ingularitysay aylay inyay ethay ostilehay eelingsfay ithway ichwhay ethay ildchay egardedray
allyay esethay offspringyay ofyay erhay ownyay earthay andyay indmay. Eshay evernay eatedcray ayay
iendfray, utbay eemedsay alwaysyay otay ebay owingsay oadcastbray ethay agon’sdray eethtay,
encewhay ungspray ayay arvesthay ofyay armedyay enemiesyay, againstyay omwhay eshay ushedray otay
attlebay. Ityay asway inexpressiblyyay ad—thensay atwhay epthday ofyay orrowsay otay ayay
othermay, owhay eltfay inyay erhay ownyay earthay ethay ause!—tocay observeyay, inyay oneyay osay
youngyay, isthay onstantcay ecognitionray ofyay anyay adverseyay orldway, andyay osay iercefay ayay
ainingtray ofyay ethay energiesyay atthay ereway otay akemay oodgay erhay ausecay, inyay ethay
ontestcay atthay ustmay ensueyay.

Azinggay atyay Earlpay, Esterhay Ynnepray oftenyay oppeddray erhay orkway uponyay erhay eesknay,
andyay iedcray outyay ithway anyay agonyyay ichwhay eshay ouldway ainfay avehay iddenhay, utbay
ichwhay ademay utteranceyay orfay itselfyay, etwixtbay eechspay andyay ayay oan,—“ogray
Atherfay inyay Eaven,—ifhay Outhay artyay illstay ymay Ather,—whatfay isyay isthay eingbay
ichwhay Iyay avehay oughtbray intoyay ethay orldway!” Andyay Earlpay, overhearingyay ethay
ejaculationyay, oryay awareyay, oughthray omesay oremay ubtilesay annelchay, ofyay osethay
obsthray ofyay anguishyay, ouldway urntay erhay ividvay andyay eautifulbay ittlelay acefay uponyay
erhay othermay, ilesmay ithway ite-likespray intelligenceyay, andyay esumeray erhay ayplay.

illustration[ay: Ayay ouchtay ofyay Earl’spay aby-handbay]

Oneyay eculiaritypay ofyay ethay ild’schay eportmentday emainsray yetyay otay ebay oldtay. Ethay
eryvay irstfay ingthay ichwhay eshay adhay oticednay inyay erhay ifelay as—what?—notway ethay
other’smay ilesmay, espondingray otay ityay, asyay otheryay abiesbay oday, ybay atthay aintfay,
embryoyay ilesmay ofyay ethay ittlelay outhmay, ememberedray osay oubtfullyday afterwardsyay,
andyay ithway uchsay ondfay iscussionday etherwhay ityay ereway indeedyay ayay ilesmay. Ybay onay
eansmay! Utbay atthay irstfay objectyay ofyay ichwhay Earlpay eemedsay otay ecomebay awareyay
as—shallway eway aysay it?—theyay arletscay etterlay onyay Ester’shay osombay! Oneyay ayday,
asyay erhay othermay oopedstay overyay ethay adlecray, ethay infant’syay eyesyay adhay eenbay
aughtcay ybay ethay immeringglay ofyay ethay oldgay embroideryyay aboutyay ethay etterlay; andyay,
uttingpay upyay erhay ittlelay andhay, eshay aspedgray atyay ityay, ilingsmay, otnay
oubtfullyday, utbay ithway ayay ecidedday eamglay, atthay avegay erhay acefay ethay ooklay ofyay ayay
uchmay olderyay ildchay. Enthay, aspinggay orfay eathbray, idday Esterhay Ynnepray utchclay
ethay atalfay okentay, instinctivelyyay endeavoringyay otay eartay ityay awayyay; osay
infiniteyay asway ethay orturetay inflictedyay ybay ethay intelligentyay ouchtay ofyay Earl’spay
aby-handbay. Againyay, asyay ifyay erhay other’smay agonizedyay esturegay ereway eantmay onlyyay
otay akemay ortspay orfay erhay, idday ittlelay Earlpay ooklay intoyay erhay eyesyay, andyay
ilesmay! Omfray atthay epochyay, exceptyay enwhay ethay ildchay asway asleepyay, Esterhay adhay
evernay eltfay ayay oment’smay afetysay; otnay ayay oment’smay almcay enjoymentyay ofyay erhay.
Eeksway, ityay isyay uetray, ouldway ometimessay elapseyay, uringday ichwhay Earl’spay azegay
ightmay evernay onceyay ebay ixedfay uponyay ethay arletscay etterlay; utbay enthay, againyay, ityay
ouldway omecay atyay unawaresyay, ikelay ethay okestray ofyay uddensay eathday, andyay alwaysyay
ithway atthay eculiarpay ilesmay, andyay oddyay expressionyay ofyay ethay eyesyay.

Onceyay, isthay eakishfray, elvishyay astcay amecay intoyay ethay ild’schay eyesyay, ilewhay
Esterhay asway ookinglay atyay erhay ownyay imageyay inyay emthay, asyay othersmay areyay ondfay ofyay
oingday; andyay, uddenly,—forsay omenway inyay olitudesay, andyay ithway oubledtray
eartshay, areyay esteredpay ithway unaccountableyay elusions,—sheday anciedfay atthay
eshay eheldbay, otnay erhay ownyay iniaturemay ortraitpay, utbay anotheryay acefay, inyay ethay
allsmay ackblay irrormay ofyay Earl’spay eyeyay. Ityay asway ayay acefay, iend-likefay, ullfay ofyay
ilingsmay alicemay, yetyay earingbay ethay emblancesay ofyay eaturesfay atthay eshay adhay
ownknay ullfay ellway, oughthay eldomsay ithway ayay ilesmay, andyay evernay ithway alicemay inyay
emthay. Ityay asway asyay ifyay anyay evilyay iritspay ossessedpay ethay ildchay, andyay adhay ustjay
enthay eepedpay orthfay inyay ockerymay. Anymay ayay imetay afterwardsyay adhay Esterhay eenbay
orturedtay, oughthay esslay ividlyvay, ybay ethay amesay illusionyay.

Inyay ethay afternoonyay ofyay ayay ertaincay ummer’ssay ayday, afteryay Earlpay ewgray igbay
enoughyay otay unray aboutyay, eshay amusedyay erselfhay ithway atheringgay andfulshay ofyay
ild-flowersway, andyay ingingflay emthay, oneyay ybay oneyay, atyay erhay other’smay osombay;
ancingday upyay andyay ownday, ikelay ayay ittlelay elfyay, eneverwhay eshay ithay ethay arletscay
etterlay. Ester’shay irstfay otionmay adhay eenbay otay overcay erhay osombay ithway erhay
aspedclay andshay. Utbay, etherwhay omfray idepray oryay esignationray, oryay ayay eelingfay
atthay erhay enancepay ightmay estbay ebay oughtwray outyay ybay isthay unutterableyay ainpay,
eshay esistedray ethay impulseyay, andyay atsay erectyay, alepay asyay eathday, ookinglay adlysay
intoyay ittlelay Earl’spay ildway eyesyay. Illstay amecay ethay atterybay ofyay owersflay,
almostyay invariablyyay ittinghay ethay arkmay, andyay overingcay ethay other’smay eastbray
ithway urtshay orfay ichwhay eshay ouldcay indfay onay almbay inyay isthay orldway, ornay ewknay
owhay otay eeksay ityay inyay anotheryay. Atyay astlay, erhay otshay eingbay allyay expendedyay, ethay
ildchay oodstay illstay andyay azedgay atyay Esterhay, ithway atthay ittlelay, aughinglay
imageyay ofyay ayay iendfay eepingpay out—oryay, etherwhay ityay eepedpay oryay onay, erhay othermay
osay imaginedyay it—fromyay ethay unsearchableyay abyssyay ofyay erhay ackblay eyesyay.

ild“chay, atwhay artyay outhay?” iedcray ethay othermay.

o“ay, Iyay amyay youryay ittlelay Earlpay!” answeredyay ethay ildchay.

Utbay, ilewhay eshay aidsay ityay, Earlpay aughedlay, andyay eganbay otay anceday upyay andyay ownday,
ithway ethay umorsomehay esticulationgay ofyay ayay ittlelay impyay, osewhay extnay eakfray
ightmay ebay otay yflay upyay ethay imneychay.

art“ay outhay ymay ildchay, inyay eryvay uthtray?” askedyay Esterhay.

Ornay idday eshay utpay ethay uestionqay altogetheryay idlyyay, utbay, orfay ethay omentmay,
ithway ayay ortionpay ofyay enuinegay earnestnessyay; orfay, uchsay asway Earl’spay onderfulway
intelligenceyay, atthay erhay othermay alfhay oubtedday etherwhay eshay ereway otnay
acquaintedyay ithway ethay ecretsay ellspay ofyay erhay existenceyay, andyay ightmay otnay ownay
evealray erselfhay.

yes“ay; Iyay amyay ittlelay Earlpay!” epeatedray ethay ildchay, ontinuingcay erhay anticsyay.

ou“thay artyay otnay ymay ildchay! Outhay artyay onay Earlpay ofyay inemay!” aidsay ethay othermay,
alfhay ayfullyplay; orfay ityay asway oftenyay ethay asecay atthay ayay ortivespay impulseyay amecay
overyay erhay, inyay ethay idstmay ofyay erhay eepestday ufferingsay. ell“tay emay, enthay, atwhay
outhay artyay, andyay owhay entsay eethay itherhay.”

ell“tay emay, othermay!” aidsay ethay ildchay, eriouslysay, omingcay upyay otay Esterhay, andyay
essingpray erselfhay oseclay otay erhay eesknay. o“day outhay elltay emay!”

y“thay Eavenlyhay Atherfay entsay eethay!” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray.

Utbay eshay aidsay ityay ithway ayay esitationhay atthay idday otnay escapeyay ethay acutenessyay ofyay
ethay ildchay. Etherwhay ovedmay onlyyay ybay erhay ordinaryyay eakishnessfray, oryay
ecausebay anyay evilyay iritspay omptedpray erhay, eshay utpay upyay erhay allsmay orefingerfay,
andyay ouchedtay ethay arletscay etterlay.

e“hay idday otnay endsay emay!” iedcray eshay, ositivelypay. i“ay avehay onay Eavenlyhay
Atherfay!”

ush“hay, Earlpay, ushhay! Outhay ustmay otnay alktay osay!” answeredyay ethay othermay,
uppressingsay ayay oangray. e“hay entsay usyay allyay intoyay isthay orldway. Ehay entsay evenyay emay,
ythay othermay. Enthay, uchmay oremay, eethay! Oryay, ifyay otnay, outhay angestray andyay elfishyay
ildchay, encewhay idstday outhay omecay?”

ell“tay emay! Elltay emay!” epeatedray Earlpay, onay ongerlay eriouslysay, utbay aughinglay,
andyay aperingcay aboutyay ethay oorflay. it“ay isyay outhay atthay ustmay elltay emay!”

Utbay Esterhay ouldcay otnay esolveray ethay ueryqay, eingbay erselfhay inyay ayay ismalday
abyrinthlay ofyay oubtday. Eshay emembered—betwixtray ayay ilesmay andyay ayay udder—theshay
alktay ofyay ethay eighboringnay owns-peopletay; owhay, eekingsay ainlyvay elsewhereyay
orfay ethay ild’schay aternitypay, andyay observingyay omesay ofyay erhay oddyay attributesyay,
adhay ivengay outyay atthay oorpay ittlelay Earlpay asway ayay emonday offspringyay; uchsay asyay,
everyay incesay oldyay Atholiccay imestay, adhay occasionallyyay eenbay eensay onyay earthyay,
oughthray ethay agencyyay ofyay eirthay other’smay insay, andyay otay omotepray omesay oulfay andyay
ickedway urposepay. Utherlay, accordingyay otay ethay andalscay ofyay ishay onkishmay
enemiesyay, asway ayay atbray ofyay atthay ellishhay eedbray; ornay asway Earlpay ethay onlyyay
ildchay otay omwhay isthay inauspiciousyay originyay asway assignedyay, amongyay ethay Ewnay
Englandyay Uritanspay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iivay.

                         Ethay Overnor’sgay Allhay.


illustration[ay]

Esterhay Ynnepray entway, oneyay ayday, otay ethay ansionmay ofyay Overnorgay Ellinghambay,
ithway ayay airpay ofyay ovesglay, ichwhay eshay adhay ingedfray andyay embroideredyay otay ishay
orderyay, andyay ichwhay ereway otay ebay ornway onyay omesay eatgray occasionyay ofyay atestay; orfay,
oughthay ethay anceschay ofyay ayay opularpay electionyay adhay ausedcay isthay ormerfay ulerray
otay escendday ayay epstay oryay otway omfray ethay ighesthay ankray, ehay illstay eldhay anyay
onorablehay andyay influentialyay aceplay amongyay ethay olonialcay agistracymay.

Anotheryay andyay arfay oremay importantyay easonray anthay ethay eliveryday ofyay ayay airpay ofyay
embroideredyay ovesglay impelledyay Esterhay, atyay isthay imetay, otay eeksay anyay interviewyay
ithway ayay ersonagepay ofyay osay uchmay owerpay andyay activityyay inyay ethay affairsyay ofyay ethay
ettlementsay. Ityay adhay eachedray erhay earsyay, atthay erethay asway ayay esignday onyay ethay
artpay ofyay omesay ofyay ethay eadinglay inhabitantsyay, erishingchay ethay oremay igidray
orderyay ofyay inciplespray inyay eligionray andyay overnmentgay, otay epriveday erhay ofyay erhay
ildchay. Onyay ethay uppositionsay atthay Earlpay, asyay alreadyyay intedhay, asway ofyay emonday
originyay, esethay oodgay eoplepay otnay unreasonablyyay arguedyay atthay ayay Istianchray
interestyay inyay ethay other’smay oulsay equiredray emthay otay emoveray uchsay ayay
umbling-blockstay omfray erhay athpay. Ifyay ethay ildchay, onyay ethay otheryay andhay, ereway
eallyray apablecay ofyay oralmay andyay eligiousray owthgray, andyay ossessedpay ethay
elementsyay ofyay ultimateyay alvationsay, enthay, urelysay, ityay ouldway enjoyyay allyay ethay
airerfay ospectpray ofyay esethay advantagesyay, ybay eingbay ansferredtray otay iserway andyay
etterbay uardianshipgay anthay Esterhay Ynne’spray. Amongyay osethay owhay omotedpray ethay
esignday, Overnorgay Ellinghambay asway aidsay otay ebay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay usybay. Ityay
aymay appearyay ingularsay, andyay indeedyay, otnay ayay ittlelay udicrouslay, atthay anyay
affairyay ofyay isthay indkay, ichwhay, inyay aterlay aysday, ouldway avehay eenbay eferredray otay
onay igherhay urisdictionjay anthay atthay ofyay ethay electmensay ofyay ethay owntay, ouldshay
enthay avehay eenbay ayay uestionqay ubliclypay iscussedday, andyay onyay ichwhay atesmenstay
ofyay eminenceyay ooktay idessay. Atyay atthay epochyay ofyay istinepray implicitysay, oweverhay,
attersmay ofyay evenyay ighterslay ublicpay interestyay, andyay ofyay arfay esslay intrinsicyay
eightway, anthay ethay elfareway ofyay Esterhay andyay erhay ildchay, ereway angelystray ixedmay
upyay ithway ethay eliberationsday ofyay egislatorslay andyay actsyay ofyay atestay. Ethay eriodpay
asway ardlyhay, ifyay atyay allyay, earlieryay anthay atthay ofyay ouryay orystay, enwhay ayay isputeday
oncerningcay ethay ightray ofyay opertypray inyay ayay igpay otnay onlyyay ausedcay ayay iercefay andyay
itterbay ontestcay inyay ethay egislativelay odybay ofyay ethay olonycay, utbay esultedray inyay
anyay importantyay odificationmay ofyay ethay ameworkfray itselfyay ofyay ethay egislaturelay.

Ullfay ofyay oncerncay, erefore,—butthay osay onsciouscay ofyay erhay ownyay ightray atthay ityay
eemedsay arcelyscay anyay unequalyay atchmay etweenbay ethay ublicpay, onyay ethay oneyay idesay,
andyay ayay onelylay omanway, ackedbay ybay ethay ympathiessay ofyay aturenay, onyay ethay
other,—hesteryay Ynnepray etsay orthfay omfray erhay olitarysay ottagecay. Ittlelay
Earlpay, ofyay oursecay, asway erhay ompanioncay. Eshay asway ownay ofyay anyay ageyay otay unray
ightlylay alongyay ybay erhay other’smay idesay, andyay, onstantlycay inyay otionmay, omfray
ornmay illtay unsetsay, ouldcay avehay accomplishedyay ayay uchmay ongerlay ourneyjay anthay
atthay eforebay erhay. Oftenyay, everthelessnay, oremay omfray apricecay anthay
ecessitynay, eshay emandedday otay ebay akentay upyay inyay armsyay; utbay asway oonsay asyay
imperiousyay otay ebay etsay ownday againyay, andyay iskedfray onwardyay eforebay Esterhay onyay
ethay assygray athwaypay, ithway anymay ayay armlesshay iptray andyay umbletay. Eway avehay
okenspay ofyay Earl’spay ichray andyay uxuriantlay eautybay; ayay eautybay atthay oneshay ithway
eepday andyay ividvay intstay; ayay ightbray omplexioncay, eyesyay ossessingpay intensityyay
othbay ofyay epthday andyay owglay, andyay airhay alreadyyay ofyay ayay eepday, ossyglay ownbray, andyay
ichwhay, inyay afteryay yearsyay, ouldway ebay earlynay akinyay otay ackblay. Erethay asway irefay
inyay erhay andyay oughoutthray erhay; eshay eemedsay ethay unpremeditatedyay offshootyay ofyay ayay
assionatepay omentmay. Erhay othermay, inyay ontrivingcay ethay ild’schay arbgay, adhay
allowedyay ethay orgeousgay endenciestay ofyay erhay imaginationyay eirthay ullfay ayplay;
arrayingyay erhay inyay ayay imsoncray elvetvay unictay, ofyay ayay eculiarpay utcay, abundantlyyay
embroideredyay ithway antasiesfay andyay ourishesflay ofyay old-threadgay. Osay uchmay
engthstray ofyay oloringcay, ichwhay ustmay avehay ivengay ayay anway andyay allidpay aspectyay otay
eekschay ofyay ayay ainterfay oomblay, asway admirablyyay adaptedyay otay Earl’spay eautybay,
andyay ademay erhay ethay eryvay ightestbray ittlelay etjay ofyay ameflay atthay everyay ancedday
uponyay ethay earthyay.

Utbay ityay asway ayay emarkableray attributeyay ofyay isthay arbgay, andyay, indeedyay, ofyay ethay
ild’schay olewhay appearanceyay, atthay ityay irresistiblyyay andyay inevitablyyay emindedray
ethay eholderbay ofyay ethay okentay ichwhay Esterhay Ynnepray asway oomedday otay earway uponyay
erhay osombay. Ityay asway ethay arletscay etterlay inyay anotheryay ormfay; ethay arletscay
etterlay endowedyay ithway ifelay! Ethay othermay erself—ashay ifyay ethay edray ignominyyay
ereway osay eeplyday orchedscay intoyay erhay ainbray atthay allyay erhay onceptionscay
assumedyay itsyay orm—hadfay arefullycay oughtwray outyay ethay imilitudesay; avishinglay
anymay ourshay ofyay orbidmay ingenuityyay, otay eatecray anyay analogyyay etweenbay ethay
objectyay ofyay erhay affectionyay andyay ethay emblemyay ofyay erhay uiltgay andyay orturetay. Utbay,
inyay uthtray, Earlpay asway ethay oneyay, asyay ellway asyay ethay otheryay; andyay onlyyay inyay
onsequencecay ofyay atthay identityyay adhay Esterhay ontrivedcay osay erfectlypay otay
epresentray ethay arletscay etterlay inyay erhay appearanceyay.

Asyay ethay otway ayfarersway amecay ithinway ethay ecinctspray ofyay ethay owntay, ethay
ildrenchay ofyay ethay Uritanspay ookedlay upyay omfray eirthay ay,—orplay atwhay assedpay
orfay ayplay ithway osethay ombresay ittlelay urchins,—andyay akespay avelygray oneyay otay
anotheryay:—

ehold“bay, erilyvay, erethay isyay ethay omanway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay; andyay, ofyay ayay
uthtray, oreovermay, erethay isyay ethay ikenesslay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay unningray
alongyay ybay erhay idesay! Omecay, ereforethay, andyay etlay usyay ingflay udmay atyay emthay!”

Utbay Earlpay, owhay asway ayay auntlessday ildchay, afteryay owningfray, ampingstay erhay
ootfay, andyay akingshay erhay ittlelay andhay ithway ayay arietyvay ofyay eateningthray
esturesgay, uddenlysay ademay ayay ushray atyay ethay otknay ofyay erhay enemiesyay, andyay utpay
emthay allyay otay ightflay. Eshay esembledray, inyay erhay iercefay ursuitpay ofyay emthay, anyay
infantyay estilence,—thepay arletscay everfay, oryay omesay uchsay alf-fledgedhay angelyay
ofyay udgment,—whosejay issionmay asway otay unishpay ethay inssay ofyay ethay isingray
enerationgay. Eshay eamedscray andyay outedshay, ootay, ithway ayay errifictay olumevay ofyay
oundsay, ichwhay, oubtlessday, ausedcay ethay eartshay ofyay ethay ugitivesfay otay uakeqay
ithinway emthay. Ethay ictoryvay accomplishedyay, Earlpay eturnedray uietlyqay otay erhay
othermay, andyay ookedlay upyay, ilingsmay, intoyay erhay acefay.

Ithoutway urtherfay adventureyay, eythay eachedray ethay ellingdway ofyay Overnorgay
Ellinghambay. Isthay asway ayay argelay oodenway ousehay, uiltbay inyay ayay ashionfay ofyay ichwhay
erethay areyay ecimensspay illstay extantyay inyay ethay eetsstray ofyay ouryay olderyay ownstay;
ownay oss-grownmay, umblingcray otay ecayday, andyay elancholymay atyay earthay ithway ethay
anymay orrowfulsay oryay oyfuljay occurrencesyay, ememberedray oryay orgottenfay, atthay
avehay appenedhay, andyay assedpay awayyay, ithinway eirthay uskyday amberschay. Enthay,
oweverhay, erethay asway ethay eshnessfray ofyay ethay assingpay yearyay onyay itsyay exterioryay,
andyay ethay eerfulnesschay, eamingglay orthfay omfray ethay unnysay indowsway, ofyay ayay
umanhay abitationhay, intoyay ichwhay eathday adhay evernay enteredyay. Ityay adhay, indeedyay,
ayay eryvay eerychay aspectyay; ethay allsway eingbay overspreadyay ithway ayay indkay ofyay
uccostay, inyay ichwhay agmentsfray ofyay okenbray assglay ereway entifullyplay
intermixedyay; osay atthay, enwhay ethay unshinesay ellfay aslant-wiseyay overyay ethay ontfray
ofyay ethay edificeyay, ityay itteredglay andyay arkledspay asyay ifyay iamondsday adhay eenbay
ungflay againstyay ityay ybay ethay oubleday andfulhay. Ethay illiancybray ightmay avehay
efittedbay Aladdin’syay alacepay, atherray anthay ethay ansionmay ofyay ayay avegray oldyay
Uritanpay ulerray. Ityay asway urtherfay ecoratedday ithway angestray andyay eeminglysay
abalisticcay iguresfay andyay iagramsday, uitablesay otay ethay uaintqay astetay ofyay ethay
ageyay, ichwhay adhay eenbay awndray inyay ethay uccostay enwhay ewlynay aidlay onyay, andyay adhay
ownay owngray ardhay andyay urableday, orfay ethay admirationyay ofyay afteryay imestay.

Earlpay, ookinglay atyay isthay ightbray onderway ofyay ayay ousehay, eganbay otay apercay andyay
anceday, andyay imperativelyyay equiredray atthay ethay olewhay eadthbray ofyay unshinesay
ouldshay ebay ippedstray offyay itsyay ontfray, andyay ivengay erhay otay ayplay ithway.

o“nay, ymay ittlelay Earlpay!” aidsay erhay othermay. ou“thay ustmay athergay inethay ownyay
unshinesay. Iyay avehay onenay otay ivegay eethay!”

Eythay approachedyay ethay oorday; ichwhay asway ofyay anyay archedyay ormfay, andyay ankedflay onyay
eachyay idesay ybay ayay arrownay owertay oryay ojectionpray ofyay ethay edificeyay, inyay othbay ofyay
ichwhay ereway attice-windowslay, ithway oodenway uttersshay otay oseclay overyay emthay atyay
eednay. Iftinglay ethay ironyay ammerhay atthay unghay atyay ethay ortalpay, Esterhay Ynnepray
avegay ayay ummonssay, ichwhay asway answeredyay ybay oneyay ofyay ethay Overnor’sgay
ond-servantsbay; ayay ee-bornfray Englishmanyay, utbay ownay ayay evensay yearsyay’ aveslay.
Uringday atthay ermtay ehay asway otay ebay ethay opertypray ofyay ishay astermay, andyay asyay uchmay
ayay ommoditycay ofyay argainbay andyay alesay asyay anyay oxyay, oryay ayay oint-stooljay. Ethay erfsay
oreway ethay ueblay oatcay, ichwhay asway ethay ustomarycay arbgay ofyay erving-mensay ofyay
atthay eriodpay, andyay onglay eforebay, inyay ethay oldyay ereditaryhay allshay ofyay Englandyay.

is“ay ethay orshipfulway Overnorgay Ellinghambay ithinway?” inquiredyay Esterhay.

yea“ay, orsoothfay,” epliedray ethay ond-servantbay, aringstay ithway ide-openway eyesyay
atyay ethay arletscay etterlay, ichwhay, eingbay ayay ew-comernay inyay ethay ountrycay, ehay adhay
evernay eforebay eensay. yea“ay, ishay onorablehay orshipway isyay ithinway. Utbay ehay athhay
ayay odlygay inistermay oryay otway ithway imhay, andyay ikewiselay ayay eechlay. Yeyay aymay otnay eesay
ishay orshipway ownay.”

evertheless“nay, Iyay illway enteryay,” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray, andyay ethay
ond-servantbay, erhapspay udgingjay omfray ethay ecisionday ofyay erhay airyay, andyay ethay
itteringglay ymbolsay inyay erhay osombay, atthay eshay asway ayay eatgray adylay inyay ethay andlay,
offeredyay onay oppositionyay.

Osay ethay othermay andyay ittlelay Earlpay ereway admittedyay intoyay ethay allhay ofyay
entranceyay. Ithway anymay ariationsvay, uggestedsay ybay ethay aturenay ofyay ishay
uilding-materialsbay, iversityday ofyay imateclay, andyay ayay ifferentday odemay ofyay
ocialsay ifelay, Overnorgay Ellinghambay adhay annedplay ishay ewnay abitationhay afteryay
ethay esidencesray ofyay entlemengay ofyay airfay estateyay inyay ishay ativenay andlay. Erehay,
enthay, asway ayay ideway andyay easonablyray oftylay allhay, extendingyay oughthray ethay
olewhay epthday ofyay ethay ousehay, andyay ormingfay ayay ediummay ofyay eneralgay
ommunicationcay, oremay oryay esslay irectlyday, ithway allyay ethay otheryay apartmentsyay.
Atyay oneyay extremityyay, isthay aciousspay oomray asway ightedlay ybay ethay indowsway ofyay ethay
otway owerstay, ichwhay ormedfay ayay allsmay ecessray onyay eitheryay idesay ofyay ethay ortalpay.
Atyay ethay otheryay endyay, oughthay artlypay uffledmay ybay ayay urtaincay, ityay asway oremay
owerfullypay illuminatedyay ybay oneyay ofyay osethay embowedyay all-windowshay ichwhay eway
eadray ofyay inyay oldyay ooksbay, andyay ichwhay asway ovidedpray ithway ayay eepday andyay ushionedcay
eatsay. Erehay, onyay ethay ushioncay, aylay ayay oliofay ometay, obablypray ofyay ethay
Onicleschray ofyay Englandyay, oryay otheryay uchsay ubstantialsay iteraturelay; evenyay asyay,
inyay ouryay ownyay aysday, eway atterscay ildedgay olumesvay onyay ethay entre-tablecay, otay ebay
urnedtay overyay ybay ethay asualcay uestgay. Ethay urniturefay ofyay ethay allhay onsistedcay
ofyay omesay onderouspay airschay, ethay acksbay ofyay ichwhay ereway elaboratelyyay arvedcay
ithway eathswray ofyay oakenyay owersflay; andyay ikewiselay ayay abletay inyay ethay amesay astetay;
ethay olewhay eingbay ofyay ethay Elizabethanyay ageyay, oryay erhapspay earlieryay, andyay
eirloomshay, ansferredtray itherhay omfray ethay Overnor’sgay aternalpay omehay. Onyay
ethay able—intay okentay atthay ethay entimentsay ofyay oldyay Englishyay ospitalityhay adhay
otnay eenbay eftlay ehind—stoodbay ayay argelay ewterpay ankardtay, atyay ethay ottombay ofyay
ichwhay, adhay Esterhay oryay Earlpay eepedpay intoyay ityay, eythay ightmay avehay eensay ethay
othyfray emnantray ofyay ayay ecentray aughtdray ofyay aleyay.

Onyay ethay allway unghay ayay owray ofyay ortraitspay, epresentingray ethay orefathersfay ofyay
ethay Ellinghambay ineagelay, omesay ithway armoryay onyay eirthay eastsbray, andyay othersyay
ithway atelystay uffsray andyay obesray ofyay eacepay. Allyay ereway aracterizedchay ybay ethay
ernnessstay andyay everitysay ichwhay oldyay ortraitspay osay invariablyyay utpay onyay; asyay ifyay
eythay ereway ethay ostsghay, atherray anthay ethay icturespay, ofyay epartedday orthiesway,
andyay ereway azinggay ithway arshhay andyay intolerantyay iticismcray atyay ethay ursuitspay
andyay enjoymentsyay ofyay ivinglay enmay.

illustration[ay: Ethay Overnor’sgay Eastplatebray]

Atyay aboutyay ethay entrecay ofyay ethay oakenyay anelspay, atthay inedlay ethay allhay, asway
uspendedsay ayay uitsay ofyay ailmay, otnay, ikelay ethay icturespay, anyay ancestralyay elicray,
utbay ofyay ethay ostmay odernmay ateday; orfay ityay adhay eenbay anufacturedmay ybay ayay ilfulskay
armoreryay inyay Ondonlay, ethay amesay yearyay inyay ichwhay Overnorgay Ellinghambay amecay
overyay otay Ewnay Englandyay. Erethay asway ayay eelstay ead-piecehay, ayay uirasscay, ayay
orgetgay, andyay eavesgray, ithway ayay airpay ofyay auntletsgay andyay ayay ordsway anginghay
eneathbay; allyay, andyay especiallyyay ethay elmethay andyay eastplatebray, osay ighlyhay
urnishedbay asyay otay owglay ithway itewhay adianceray, andyay atterscay anyay illuminationyay
everywhereyay aboutyay uponyay ethay oorflay. Isthay ightbray anoplypay asway otnay eantmay orfay
eremay idleyay owshay, utbay adhay eenbay ornway ybay ethay Overnorgay onyay anymay ayay olemnsay
ustermay andyay ainingtray ieldfay, andyay adhay itteredglay, oreovermay, atyay ethay eadhay ofyay
ayay egimentray inyay ethay Equodpay arway. Orfay, oughthay edbray ayay awyerlay, andyay
accustomedyay otay eakspay ofyay Aconbay, Okecay, Oyenay, andyay Inchfay asyay ishay
ofessionalpray associatesyay, ethay exigenciesyay ofyay isthay ewnay ountrycay adhay
ansformedtray Overnorgay Ellinghambay intoyay ayay oldiersay, asyay ellway asyay ayay atesmanstay
andyay ulerray.

Ittlelay Earl—whopay asway asyay eatlygray easedplay ithway ethay eamingglay armoryay asyay
eshay adhay eenbay ithway ethay itteringglay ontispiecefray ofyay ethay ouse—spenthay omesay
imetay ookinglay intoyay ethay olishedpay irrormay ofyay ethay eastplatebray.

other“may,” iedcray eshay, i“ay eesay youyay erehay. Ooklay! Ooklay!”

Esterhay ookedlay, ybay ayway ofyay umoringhay ethay ildchay; andyay eshay awsay atthay, owingyay
otay ethay eculiarpay effectyay ofyay isthay onvexcay irrormay, ethay arletscay etterlay asway
epresentedray inyay exaggeratedyay andyay iganticgay oportionspray, osay asyay otay ebay
eatlygray ethay ostmay ominentpray eaturefay ofyay erhay appearanceyay. Inyay uthtray, eshay
eemedsay absolutelyyay iddenhay ehindbay ityay. Earlpay ointedpay upwardyay, alsoyay, atyay ayay
imilarsay icturepay inyay ethay ead-piecehay; ilingsmay atyay erhay othermay, ithway ethay
elfishyay intelligenceyay atthay asway osay amiliarfay anyay expressionyay onyay erhay allsmay
ysiognomyphay. Atthay ooklay ofyay aughtynay errimentmay asway ikewiselay eflectedray inyay
ethay irrormay, ithway osay uchmay eadthbray andyay intensityyay ofyay effectyay, atthay ityay ademay
Esterhay Ynnepray eelfay asyay ifyay ityay ouldcay otnay ebay ethay imageyay ofyay erhay ownyay ildchay,
utbay ofyay anyay impyay owhay asway eekingsay otay ouldmay itselfyay intoyay Earl’spay apeshay.

ome“cay alongyay, Earlpay,” aidsay eshay, awingdray erhay awayyay. ome“cay andyay ooklay intoyay
isthay airfay ardengay. Ityay aymay ebay eway allshay eesay owersflay erethay; oremay eautifulbay
onesyay anthay eway indfay inyay ethay oodsway.”

Earlpay, accordinglyyay, anray otay ethay ow-windowbay, atyay ethay artherfay endyay ofyay ethay
allhay, andyay ookedlay alongyay ethay istavay ofyay ayay arden-walkgay, arpetedcay ithway
oselyclay avenshay assgray, andyay orderedbay ithway omesay uderay andyay immatureyay attemptyay
atyay ubberyshray. Utbay ethay oprietorpray appearedyay alreadyyay otay avehay
elinquishedray, asyay opelesshay, ethay effortyay otay erpetuatepay onyay isthay idesay ofyay
ethay Atlanticyay, inyay ayay ardhay oilsay andyay amidyay ethay oseclay ugglestray orfay
ubsistencesay, ethay ativenay Englishyay astetay orfay ornamentalyay ardeninggay.
Abbagescay ewgray inyay ainplay ightsay; andyay ayay umpkin-vinepay, ootedray atyay omesay
istanceday, adhay unray acrossyay ethay interveningyay acespay, andyay epositedday oneyay ofyay
itsyay iganticgay oductspray irectlyday eneathbay ethay all-windowhay; asyay ifyay otay arnway
ethay Overnorgay atthay isthay eatgray umplay ofyay egetablevay oldgay asway asyay ichray anyay
ornamentyay asyay Ewnay Englandyay earthyay ouldway offeryay imhay. Erethay ereway ayay ewfay
ose-bushesray, oweverhay, andyay ayay umbernay ofyay apple-treesyay, obablypray ethay
escendantsday ofyay osethay antedplay ybay ethay Everendray Mray. Ackstoneblay, ethay irstfay
ettlersay ofyay ethay eninsulapay; atthay alf-mythologicalhay ersonagepay, owhay idesray
oughthray ouryay earlyyay annalsyay, eatedsay onyay ethay ackbay ofyay ayay ullbay.

Earlpay, eeingsay ethay ose-bushesray, eganbay otay ycray orfay ayay edray oseray, andyay ouldway
otnay ebay acifiedpay.

ush“hay, ildchay, ushhay!” aidsay erhay othermay, earnestlyyay. o“day otnay ycray, earday
ittlelay Earlpay! Iyay earhay oicesvay inyay ethay ardengay. Ethay Overnorgay isyay omingcay, andyay
entlemengay alongyay ithway imhay!”

Inyay actfay, adownyay ethay istavay ofyay ethay ardengay avenueyay ayay umbernay ofyay ersonspay ereway
eensay approachingyay owardstay ethay ousehay. Earlpay, inyay utteryay ornscay ofyay erhay
other’smay attemptyay otay uietqay erhay, avegay anyay eldritchyay eamscray, andyay enthay
ecamebay ilentsay; otnay omfray anyyay otionnay ofyay obedienceyay, utbay ecausebay ethay uickqay
andyay obilemay uriositycay ofyay erhay ispositionday asway excitedyay ybay ethay appearanceyay
ofyay esethay ewnay ersonagespay.

                                 Iiivay.

                    Ethay Elf-childyay Andyay Ethay Inistermay.


Overnorgay Ellinghambay, inyay ayay ooselay owngay andyay easyyay ap,—suchcay asyay elderlyyay
entlemengay ovedlay otay endueyay emselvesthay ithway, inyay eirthay omesticday
ivacy,—walkedpray oremostfay, andyay appearedyay otay ebay owingshay offyay ishay estateyay,
andyay expatiatingyay onyay ishay ojectedpray improvementsyay. Ethay ideway ircumferencecay
ofyay anyay elaborateyay uffray, eneathbay ishay aygray eardbay, inyay ethay antiquatedyay
ashionfay ofyay Ingkay Ames’sjay eignray, ausedcay ishay eadhay otay ooklay otnay ayay ittlelay
ikelay atthay ofyay Ohnjay ethay Aptistbay inyay ayay argerchay. Ethay impressionyay ademay ybay ishay
aspectyay, osay igidray andyay everesay, andyay ost-bittenfray ithway oremay anthay autumnalyay
ageyay, asway ardlyhay inyay eepingkay ithway ethay appliancesyay ofyay orldlyway enjoymentyay
erewithwhay ehay adhay evidentlyyay oneday ishay utmostyay otay urroundsay imselfhay. Utbay ityay
isyay anyay erroryay otay upposesay atthay ouryay avegray orefathers—thoughfay accustomedyay
otay eakspay andyay inkthay ofyay umanhay existenceyay asyay ayay atestay erelymay ofyay ialtray andyay
arfareway, andyay oughthay unfeignedlyyay eparedpray otay acrificesay oodsgay andyay ifelay
atyay ethay ehestbay ofyay uty—madeday ityay ayay attermay ofyay onsciencecay otay ejectray uchsay
eansmay ofyay omfortcay, oryay evenyay uxurylay, asyay aylay airlyfay ithinway eirthay aspgray.
Isthay eedcray asway evernay aughttay, orfay instanceyay, ybay ethay enerablevay astorpay,
Ohnjay Ilsonway, osewhay eardbay, itewhay asyay ayay ow-driftsnay, asway eensay overyay
Overnorgay Ellingham’sbay ouldershay; ilewhay itsyay earerway uggestedsay atthay earspay
andyay eachespay ightmay yetyay ebay aturalizednay inyay ethay Ewnay Englandyay imateclay, andyay
atthay urplepay apesgray ightmay ossiblypay ebay ompelledcay otay ourishnay, againstyay ethay
unnysay arden-wallgay. Ethay oldyay ergymanclay, urturednay atyay ethay ichray osombay ofyay
ethay Englishyay Urchchay, adhay ayay ong-establishedlay andyay egitimatelay astetay orfay
allyay oodgay andyay omfortablecay ingsthay; andyay oweverhay ernstay ehay ightmay owshay
imselfhay inyay ethay ulpitpay, oryay inyay ishay ublicpay eproofray ofyay uchsay ansgressionstray
asyay atthay ofyay Esterhay Ynnepray, illstay ethay enialgay enevolencebay ofyay ishay ivatepray
ifelay adhay onway imhay armerway affectionyay anthay asway accordedyay otay anyyay ofyay ishay
ofessionalpray ontemporariescay.

Ehindbay ethay Overnorgay andyay Mray. Ilsonway amecay otway otheryay uestsgay: oneyay ethay
Everendray Arthuryay Immesdaleday, omwhay ethay eaderray aymay ememberray asyay avinghay
akentay ayay iefbray andyay eluctantray artpay inyay ethay enescay ofyay Esterhay Ynne’spray
isgraceday; andyay, inyay oseclay ompanionshipcay ithway imhay, oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, ayay ersonpay ofyay eatgray illskay inyay ysicphay, owhay, orfay otway oryay

unreservedyay elf-sacrificesay otay ethay aborslay andyay utiesday ofyay ethay astoralpay
elationray.

Ethay Overnorgay, inyay advanceyay ofyay ishay isitorsvay, ascendedyay oneyay oryay otway epsstay,

Ynnepray, andyay artiallypay oncealedcay erhay.

i“ay ancay eachtay ymay ittlelay Earlpay atwhay Iyay avehay earnedlay omfray isthay!” answeredyay

oman“way, ityay isyay ythay adgebay ofyay ameshay!” epliedray ethay ernstay agistratemay. it“ay

Ethay oldyay inistermay eatedsay imselfhay inyay anyay arm-chairyay, andyay ademay anyay effortyay otay

earl“pay,” aidsay ehay, ithway eatgray olemnitysay, ou“thay ustmay aketay eedhay otay

earlpay ofyay eatgray icepray. Anstcay outhay elltay emay, ymay ildchay, owhay ademay eethay?”

Ownay Earlpay ewknay ellway enoughyay owhay ademay erhay; orfay Esterhay Ynnepray, ethay
aughterday ofyay ayay iouspay omehay, eryvay oonsay afteryay erhay alktay ithway ethay ildchay

uchsay eageryay interestyay. Earlpay, ereforethay, osay argelay ereway ethay attainmentsyay
ofyay erhay eethray yearsyay’ ifetimelay, ouldcay avehay ornebay ayay airfay examinationyay inyay
ethay Ewnay Englandyay Imerpray, oryay ethay irstfay olumncay ofyay ethay Estminsterway
Atechismscay, althoughyay unacquaintedyay ithway ethay outwardyay ormfay ofyay eitheryay ofyay
osethay elebratedcay orksway. Utbay atthay erversitypay ichwhay allyay ildrenchay avehay
oremay oryay esslay ofyay, andyay ofyay ichwhay ittlelay Earlpay adhay ayay enfoldtay ortionpay, ownay,
atyay ethay ostmay inopportuneyay omentmay, ooktay oroughthay ossessionpay ofyay erhay, andyay
osedclay erhay ipslay, oryay impelledyay erhay otay eakspay ordsway amissyay. Afteryay uttingpay
erhay ingerfay inyay erhay outhmay, ithway anymay ungraciousyay efusalsray otay answeryay oodgay
Mray. Ilson’sway uestionqay, ethay ildchay inallyfay announcedyay atthay eshay adhay otnay
eenbay ademay atyay allyay, utbay adhay eenbay uckedplay ybay erhay othermay offyay ethay ushbay ofyay
ildway osesray atthay ewgray ybay ethay ison-doorpray.

Isthay antasyfay asway obablypray uggestedsay ybay ethay earnay oximitypray ofyay ethay
Overnor’sgay edray osesray, asyay Earlpay oodstay outsideyay ofyay ethay indowway; ogethertay
ithway erhay ecollectionray ofyay ethay isonpray ose-bushray, ichwhay eshay adhay assedpay inyay
omingcay itherhay.

Oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ithway ayay ilesmay onyay ishay acefay, isperedwhay omethingsay
inyay ethay youngyay ergyman’sclay earyay. Esterhay Ynnepray ookedlay atyay ethay anmay ofyay
illskay, andyay evenyay enthay, ithway erhay atefay anginghay inyay ethay alancebay, asway
artledstay otay erceivepay atwhay ayay angechay adhay omecay overyay ishay eatures,—howfay
uchmay uglieryay eythay ere,—howway ishay arkday omplexioncay eemedsay otay avehay owngray
uskierday, andyay ishay igurefay oremay isshapen,—sincemay ethay aysday enwhay eshay adhay
amiliarlyfay ownknay imhay. Eshay etmay ishay eyesyay orfay anyay instantyay, utbay asway
immediatelyyay onstrainedcay otay ivegay allyay erhay attentionyay otay ethay enescay ownay
oinggay orwardfay.

is“thay isyay awfulyay!” iedcray ethay Overnorgay, owlyslay ecoveringray omfray ethay

ildchay ofyay eethray yearsyay oldyay, andyay eshay annotcay elltay owhay ademay erhay! Ithoutway
uestionqay, eshay isyay equallyyay inyay ethay arkday asyay otay erhay oulsay, itsyay esentpray
epravityday, andyay uturefay estinyday! Ethinksmay, entlemengay, eway eednay inquireyay onay
urtherfay.”

Esterhay aughtcay oldhay ofyay Earlpay, andyay ewdray erhay orciblyfay intoyay erhay armsyay,
onfrontingcay ethay oldyay Uritanpay agistratemay ithway almostyay ayay iercefay

indefeasibleyay ightsray againstyay ethay orldway, andyay asway eadyray otay efendday emthay otay
ethay eathday.

od“gay avegay emay ethay ildchay!” iedcray eshay. e“hay avegay erhay inyay equitalray ofyay allyay
ingsthay elseyay, ichwhay yeyay adhay akentay omfray emay. Eshay isyay ymay appiness!—shehay isyay
ymay orturetay, onenay ethay esslay! Earlpay eepskay emay erehay inyay ifelay! Earlpay unishespay

ymay insay? Yeyay allshay otnay aketay erhay! Iyay illway ieday irstfay!”

y“may oorpay omanway,” aidsay ethay otnay unkindyay oldyay inistermay, e“thay ildchay allshay ebay

Atyay isthay ildway andyay ingularsay appealyay, ichwhay indicatedyay atthay Esterhay Ynne’spray

ere“thay isyay uthtray inyay atwhay eshay ayssay,” eganbay ethay inistermay, ithway ayay oicevay

eeminglysay osay eculiar,—whichpay onay otheryay ortalmay eingbay ancay ossesspay. Andyay,

etweenbay isthay othermay andyay isthay ildchay?”

ay!—how“ay isyay atthay, oodgay Astermay Immesdaleday?” interruptedyay ethay Overnorgay.
ake“may atthay ainplay, Iyay aypray youyay!”

it“ay ustmay ebay evenyay osay,” esumedray ethay inistermay. or“fay, ifyay eway eemday ityay
otherwiseyay, oday eway otnay erebythay aysay atthay ethay Eavenlyhay Atherfay, ethay Eatorcray
ofyay allyay eshflay, athhay ightlylay ecognizedray ayay eedday ofyay insay, andyay ademay ofyay onay

ildchay ofyay itsyay ather’sfay uiltgay andyay itsyay other’smay ameshay athhay omecay omfray ethay
andhay ofyay Odgay, otay orkway inyay anymay aysway uponyay erhay earthay, owhay eadsplay osay
