Ityay asway eantmay orfay ayay essingblay; orfay ethay oneyay essingblay ofyay erhay ifelay! Ityay asway
eantmay, oubtlessday, asyay ethay othermay erselfhay athhay oldtay usyay, orfay ayay
etributionray ootay; ayay orturetay otay ebay eltfay atyay anymay anyay unthought-ofyay omentmay;
ayay angpay, ayay ingstay, anyay ever-recurringyay agonyyay, inyay ethay idstmay ofyay ayay oubledtray
oyjay! Athhay eshay otnay expressedyay isthay oughtthay inyay ethay arbgay ofyay ethay oorpay
ildchay, osay orciblyfay emindingray usyay ofyay atthay edray ymbolsay ichwhay earssay erhay
osombay?”

ell“way aidsay, againyay!” iedcray oodgay Mray. Ilsonway. i“ay earedfay ethay omanway adhay onay
etterbay oughtthay anthay otay akemay ayay ountebankmay ofyay erhay ildchay!”

o“ay, otnay o!—notsay osay!” ontinuedcay Mray. Immesdaleday. e“shay ecognizesray,
elievebay emay, ethay olemnsay iraclemay ichwhay Odgay athhay oughtwray, inyay ethay
existenceyay ofyay atthay ildchay. Andyay aymay eshay eelfay, oo,—whattay, ethinksmay, isyay
ethay eryvay uth,—thattray isthay oonbay asway eantmay, aboveyay allyay ingsthay elseyay, otay
eepkay ethay other’smay oulsay aliveyay, andyay otay eservepray erhay omfray ackerblay epthsday
ofyay insay intoyay ichwhay Atansay ightmay elseyay avehay oughtsay otay ungeplay erhay!
Ereforethay ityay isyay oodgay orfay isthay oorpay, infulsay omanway atthay eshay athhay anyay
infantyay immortalityyay, ayay eingbay apablecay ofyay eternalyay oyjay oryay orrowsay,
onfidedcay otay erhay are,—tocay ebay ainedtray upyay ybay erhay otay ighteousness,—toray
emindray erhay, atyay everyyay omentmay, ofyay erhay all,—butfay yetyay otay eachtay erhay, asyay ityay
ereway ybay ethay Eator’scray acredsay edgeplay, atthay, ifyay eshay ingbray ethay ildchay otay
eavenhay, ethay ildchay alsoyay illway ingbray itsyay arentpay itherthay! Ereinhay isyay ethay
infulsay othermay appierhay anthay ethay infulsay atherfay. Orfay Esterhay Ynne’spray
akesay, enthay, andyay onay esslay orfay ethay oorpay ild’schay akesay, etlay usyay eavelay emthay
asyay Ovidencepray athhay eensay itfay otay aceplay emthay!”

you“ay eakspay, ymay iendfray, ithway ayay angestray earnestnessyay,” aidsay oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, ilingsmay atyay imhay.

and“ay erethay isyay ayay eightyway importyay inyay atwhay ymay youngyay otherbray athhay okenspay,”
addedyay ethay Everendray Mray. Ilsonway. at“whay aysay youyay, orshipfulway Astermay
Ellinghambay? Athhay ehay otnay eadedplay ellway orfay ethay oorpay omanway?”

indeed“ay athhay ehay,” answeredyay ethay agistratemay, and“ay athhay adducedyay uchsay
argumentsyay, atthay eway illway evenyay eavelay ethay attermay asyay ityay ownay andsstay; osay
onglay, atyay eastlay, asyay erethay allshay ebay onay urtherfay andalscay inyay ethay omanway.
Arecay ustmay ebay adhay, everthelessnay, otay utpay ethay ildchay otay ueday andyay atedstay
examinationyay inyay ethay atechismcay, atyay ythay andshay oryay Astermay Immesdale’sday.
Oreovermay, atyay ayay operpray easonsay, ethay ithing-mentay ustmay aketay eedhay atthay eshay
ogay othbay otay oolschay andyay otay eetingmay.”

Ethay youngyay inistermay, onyay easingcay otay eakspay, adhay ithdrawnway ayay ewfay epsstay
omfray ethay oupgray, andyay oodstay ithway ishay acefay artiallypay oncealedcay inyay ethay
eavyhay oldsfay ofyay ethay indow-curtainway; ilewhay ethay adowshay ofyay ishay igurefay,
ichwhay ethay unlightsay astcay uponyay ethay oorflay, asway emuloustray ithway ethay
ehemencevay ofyay ishay appealyay. Earlpay, atthay ildway andyay ightyflay ittlelay elfyay,
olestay oftlysay owardstay imhay, andyay akingtay ishay andhay inyay ethay aspgray ofyay othbay erhay
ownyay, aidlay erhay eekchay againstyay ityay; ayay aresscay osay endertay, andyay ithalway osay
unobtrusiveyay, atthay erhay othermay, owhay asway ookinglay onyay, askedyay erself,—“ishay
atthay ymay Earlpay?” Yetyay eshay ewknay atthay erethay asway ovelay inyay ethay ild’schay earthay,
althoughyay ityay ostlymay evealedray itselfyay inyay assionpay, andyay ardlyhay icetway inyay erhay
ifetimelay adhay eenbay oftenedsay ybay uchsay entlenessgay asyay ownay. Ethay
inister,—formay, avesay ethay ong-soughtlay egardsray ofyay omanway, othingnay isyay
eetersway anthay esethay arksmay ofyay ildishchay eferencepray, accordedyay
ontaneouslyspay ybay ayay iritualspay instinctyay, andyay ereforethay eemingsay otay implyyay
inyay usyay omethingsay ulytray orthyway otay ebay oved,—thelay inistermay ookedlay oundray,
aidlay ishay andhay onyay ethay ild’schay eadhay, esitatedhay anyay instantyay, andyay enthay
issedkay erhay owbray. Ittlelay Earl’spay unwontedyay oodmay ofyay entimentsay astedlay onay
ongerlay; eshay aughedlay, andyay entway aperingcay ownday ethay allhay, osay airilyyay, atthay
oldyay Mray. Ilsonway aisedray ayay uestionqay etherwhay evenyay erhay iptoestay ouchedtay ethay
oorflay.

e“thay ittlelay aggagebay athhay itchcraftway inyay erhay, Iyay ofesspray,” aidsay ehay otay Mray.
Immesdaleday. e“shay eedsnay onay oldyay oman’sway oomstickbray otay yflay ithalway!”

a“ay angestray ildchay!” emarkedray oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay. it“ay isyay easyyay otay
eesay ethay other’smay artpay inyay erhay. Ouldway ityay ebay eyondbay ayay ilosopher’sphay
esearchray, inkthay yeyay, entlemengay, otay analyzeyay atthay ild’schay aturenay, andyay,
omfray itsyay akemay andyay ouldmay, otay ivegay ayay ewdshray uessgay atyay ethay atherfay?”

ay“nay; ityay ouldway ebay infulsay, inyay uchsay ayay uestionqay, otay ollowfay ethay ewclay ofyay
ofanepray ilosophyphay,” aidsay Mray. Ilsonway. etter“bay otay astfay andyay aypray uponyay
ityay; andyay illstay etterbay, ityay aymay ebay, otay eavelay ethay ysterymay asyay eway indfay ityay,
unlessyay Ovidencepray evealray ityay ofyay itsyay ownyay accordyay. Erebythay, everyyay oodgay
Istianchray anmay athhay ayay itletay otay owshay ayay ather’sfay indnesskay owardstay ethay
oorpay, esertedday abebay.”

Ethay affairyay eingbay osay atisfactorilysay oncludedcay, Esterhay Ynnepray, ithway
Earlpay, epartedday omfray ethay ousehay. Asyay eythay escendedday ethay epsstay, ityay isyay
averredyay atthay ethay atticelay ofyay ayay amber-windowchay asway ownthray openyay, andyay
orthfay intoyay ethay unnysay ayday asway ustthray ethay acefay ofyay Istressmay Ibbinshay,
Overnorgay Ellingham’sbay itter-temperedbay istersay, andyay ethay amesay owhay, ayay ewfay
yearsyay aterlay, asway executedyay asyay ayay itchway.

ist“hay, isthay!” aidsay eshay, ilewhay erhay ill-omenedyay ysiognomyphay eemedsay otay
astcay ayay adowshay overyay ethay eerfulchay ewnessnay ofyay ethay ousehay. ilt“way outhay ogay
ithway usyay o-nighttay? Erethay illway ebay ayay errymay ompanycay inyay ethay orestfay; andyay Iyay
ellnighway omisedpray ethay Ackblay Anmay atthay omelycay Esterhay Ynnepray ouldshay akemay
oneyay.”

ake“may ymay excuseyay otay imhay, osay easeplay youyay!” answeredyay Esterhay, ithway ayay
iumphanttray ilesmay. i“ay ustmay arrytay atyay omehay, andyay eepkay atchway overyay ymay ittlelay
Earlpay. Adhay eythay akentay erhay omfray emay, Iyay ouldway illinglyway avehay onegay ithway
eethay intoyay ethay orestfay, andyay ignedsay ymay amenay inyay ethay Ackblay An’smay ookbay ootay,
andyay atthay ithway inemay ownyay oodblay!”

e“way allshay avehay eethay erethay anonyay!” aidsay ethay itch-ladyway, owningfray, asyay eshay
ewdray ackbay erhay eadhay.

Utbay ere—ifhay eway upposesay isthay interviewyay etwixtbay Istressmay Ibbinshay andyay
Esterhay Ynnepray otay ebay authenticyay, andyay otnay ayay arable—waspay alreadyyay anyay
illustrationyay ofyay ethay youngyay inister’smay argumentyay againstyay underingsay ethay
elationray ofyay ayay allenfay othermay otay ethay offspringyay ofyay erhay ailtyfray. Evenyay usthay
earlyyay adhay ethay ildchay avedsay erhay omfray Atan’ssay aresnay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Ixyay.

                              Ethay Eechlay.


Underyay ethay appellationyay ofyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ethay eaderray illway
ememberray, asway iddenhay anotheryay amenay, ichwhay itsyay ormerfay earerway adhay
esolvedray ouldshay evernay oremay ebay okenspay. Ityay ashay eenbay elatedray, owhay, inyay ethay
owdcray atthay itnessedway Esterhay Ynne’spray ignominiousyay exposureyay, oodstay ayay
anmay, elderlyyay, avel-worntray, owhay, ustjay emergingyay omfray ethay erilouspay
ildernessway, eheldbay ethay omanway, inyay omwhay ehay opedhay otay indfay embodiedyay ethay
armthway andyay eerfulnesschay ofyay omehay, etsay upyay asyay ayay ypetay ofyay insay eforebay ethay
eoplepay. Erhay atronlymay amefay asway oddentray underyay allyay en’smay eetfay. Infamyyay asway
abblingbay aroundyay erhay inyay ethay ublicpay arket-placemay. Orfay erhay indredkay,
ouldshay ethay idingstay everyay eachray emthay, andyay orfay ethay ompanionscay ofyay erhay
unspottedyay ifelay, erethay emainedray othingnay utbay ethay ontagioncay ofyay erhay
ishonorday; ichwhay ouldway otnay ailfay otay ebay istributedday inyay ictstray accordanceyay
andyay oportionpray ithway ethay intimacyyay andyay acrednesssay ofyay eirthay eviouspray
elationshipray. Enthay y—sincewhay ethay oicechay asway ithway imself—shouldhay ethay
individualyay, osewhay onnectioncay ithway ethay allenfay omanway adhay eenbay ethay ostmay
intimateyay andyay acredsay ofyay emthay allyay, omecay orwardfay otay indicatevay ishay aimclay
otay anyay inheritanceyay osay ittlelay esirableday? Ehay esolvedray otnay otay ebay illoriedpay
esidebay erhay onyay erhay edestalpay ofyay ameshay. Unknownyay otay allyay utbay Esterhay Ynnepray,
andyay ossessingpay ethay ocklay andyay eykay ofyay erhay ilencesay, ehay osechay otay ithdrawway
ishay amenay omfray ethay ollray ofyay ankindmay, andyay, asyay egardedray ishay ormerfay iestay
andyay interestsyay, otay anishvay outyay ofyay ifelay asyay ompletelycay asyay ifyay ehay indeedyay aylay
atyay ethay ottombay ofyay ethay oceanyay, itherwhay umorray adhay onglay agoyay onsignedcay imhay.
Isthay urposepay onceyay effectedyay, ewnay interestsyay ouldway immediatelyyay ingspray upyay,
andyay ikewiselay ayay ewnay urposepay; arkday, ityay isyay uetray, ifyay otnay uiltygay, utbay ofyay
orcefay enoughyay otay engageyay ethay ullfay engthstray ofyay ishay acultiesfay.

Inyay ursuancepay ofyay isthay esolveray, ehay ooktay upyay ishay esidenceray inyay ethay Uritanpay
owntay, asyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ithoutway otheryay introductionyay anthay ethay
earninglay andyay intelligenceyay ofyay ichwhay ehay ossessedpay oremay anthay ayay ommoncay
easuremay. Asyay ishay udiesstay, atyay ayay eviouspray eriodpay ofyay ishay ifelay, adhay ademay
imhay extensivelyyay acquaintedyay ithway ethay edicalmay iencescay ofyay ethay ayday, ityay asway
asyay ayay ysicianphay atthay ehay esentedpray imselfhay, andyay asyay uchsay asway ordiallycay
eceivedray. Ilfulskay enmay, ofyay ethay edicalmay andyay irurgicalchay ofessionpray, ereway
ofyay areray occurrenceyay inyay ethay olonycay. Eythay eldomsay, ityay ouldway appearyay,
artookpay ofyay ethay eligiousray ealzay atthay oughtbray otheryay emigrantsyay acrossyay ethay
Atlanticyay. Inyay eirthay esearchesray intoyay ethay umanhay amefray, ityay aymay ebay atthay ethay
igherhay andyay oremay ubtilesay acultiesfay ofyay uchsay enmay ereway aterializedmay, andyay
atthay eythay ostlay ethay iritualspay iewvay ofyay existenceyay amidyay ethay intricaciesyay ofyay
atthay ondrousway echanismmay, ichwhay eemedsay otay involveyay artyay enoughyay otay
omprisecay allyay ofyay ifelay ithinway itselfyay. Atyay allyay eventsyay, ethay ealthhay ofyay ethay
oodgay owntay ofyay Ostonbay, osay arfay asyay edicinemay adhay aughtyay otay oday ithway ityay, adhay
ithertohay ainlay inyay ethay uardianshipgay ofyay anyay agedyay eaconday andyay apothecaryyay,
osewhay ietypay andyay odlygay eportmentday ereway ongerstray estimonialstay inyay ishay
avorfay anthay anyyay atthay ehay ouldcay avehay oducedpray inyay ethay apeshay ofyay ayay iplomaday.
Ethay onlyyay urgeonsay asway oneyay owhay ombinedcay ethay occasionalyay exerciseyay ofyay atthay
oblenay artyay ithway ethay ailyday andyay abitualhay ourishflay ofyay ayay azorray. Otay uchsay ayay
ofessionalpray odybay Ogerray Illingworthchay asway ayay illiantbray acquisitionyay. Ehay
oonsay anifestedmay ishay amiliarityfay ithway ethay onderouspay andyay imposingyay
achinerymay ofyay antiqueyay ysicphay; inyay ichwhay everyyay emedyray ontainedcay ayay
ultitudemay ofyay ar-fetchedfay andyay eterogeneoushay ingredientsyay, asyay elaboratelyyay
ompoundedcay asyay ifyay ethay oposedpray esultray adhay eenbay ethay Elixiryay ofyay Ifelay. Inyay
ishay Indianyay aptivitycay, oreovermay, ehay adhay ainedgay uchmay owledgeknay ofyay ethay
opertiespray ofyay ativenay erbshay andyay ootsray; ornay idday ehay oncealcay omfray ishay
atientspay, atthay esethay implesay edicinesmay, Ature’snay oonbay otay ethay untutoredyay
avagesay, adhay uiteqay asyay argelay ayay areshay ofyay ishay ownyay onfidencecay asyay ethay
Europeanyay armacopœiaphay, ichwhay osay anymay earnedlay octorsday adhay entspay
enturiescay inyay elaboratingyay.

Isthay earnedlay angerstray asway exemplaryyay, asyay egardedray, atyay eastlay, ethay
outwardyay ormsfay ofyay ayay eligiousray ifelay, andyay, earlyyay afteryay ishay arrivalyay, adhay
osenchay orfay ishay iritualspay uidegay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday. Ethay youngyay
ivineday, osewhay olar-likeschay enownray illstay ivedlay inyay Oxfordyay, asway
onsideredcay ybay ishay oremay erventfay admirersyay asyay ittlelay esslay anthay ayay
eaven-ordainedhay apostleyay, estinedday, ouldshay ehay ivelay andyay aborlay orfay ethay
ordinaryyay ermtay ofyay ifelay, otay oday asyay eatgray eedsday orfay ethay ownay eeblefay Ewnay
Englandyay Urchchay, asyay ethay earlyyay Athersfay adhay achievedyay orfay ethay infancyyay ofyay
ethay Istianchray aithfay. Aboutyay isthay eriodpay, oweverhay, ethay ealthhay ofyay Mray.
Immesdaleday adhay evidentlyyay egunbay otay ailfay. Ybay osethay estbay acquaintedyay ithway
ishay abitshay, ethay alenesspay ofyay ethay youngyay inister’smay eekchay asway accountedyay
orfay ybay ishay ootay earnestyay evotionday otay udystay, ishay upulousscray ulfilmentfay ofyay
arochialpay utyday, andyay, oremay anthay allyay, ybay ethay astsfay andyay igilsvay ofyay ichwhay
ehay ademay ayay equentfray acticepray, inyay orderyay otay eepkay ethay ossnessgray ofyay isthay
earthlyyay atestay omfray oggingclay andyay obscuringyay ishay iritualspay amplay. Omesay
eclaredday, atthay, ifyay Mray. Immesdaleday ereway eallyray oinggay otay ieday, ityay asway
ausecay enoughyay, atthay ethay orldway asway otnay orthyway otay ebay anyyay ongerlay oddentray
ybay ishay eetfay. Ehay imselfhay, onyay ethay otheryay andhay, ithway aracteristicchay
umilityhay, avowedyay ishay eliefbay, atthay, ifyay Ovidencepray ouldshay eesay itfay otay
emoveray imhay, ityay ouldway ebay ecausebay ofyay ishay ownyay unworthinessyay otay erformpay itsyay
umblesthay issionmay erehay onyay earthyay. Ithway allyay isthay ifferenceday ofyay opinionyay asyay
otay ethay ausecay ofyay ishay eclineday, erethay ouldcay ebay onay uestionqay ofyay ethay actfay.
Ishay ormfay ewgray emaciatedyay; ishay oicevay, oughthay illstay ichray andyay eetsway, adhay ayay
ertaincay elancholymay ophecypray ofyay ecayday inyay ityay; ehay asway oftenyay observedyay, onyay
anyyay ightslay alarmyay oryay otheryay uddensay accidentyay, otay utpay ishay andhay overyay ishay
earthay, ithway irstfay ayay ushflay andyay enthay ayay alenesspay, indicativeyay ofyay ainpay.

Uchsay asway ethay youngyay ergyman’sclay onditioncay, andyay osay imminentyay ethay ospectpray
atthay ishay awningday ightlay ouldway ebay extinguishedyay, allyay untimelyyay, enwhay Ogerray
Illingworthchay ademay ishay adventyay otay ethay owntay. Ishay irstfay entryyay onyay ethay
enescay, ewfay eoplepay ouldcay elltay encewhay, oppingdray ownday, asyay ityay ereway, outyay ofyay
ethay yskay, oryay artingstay omfray ethay ethernay earthyay, adhay anyay aspectyay ofyay ysterymay,
ichwhay asway easilyyay eightenedhay otay ethay iraculousmay. Ehay asway ownay ownknay otay ebay
ayay anmay ofyay illskay; ityay asway observedyay atthay ehay atheredgay erbshay, andyay ethay
ossomsblay ofyay ild-flowersway, andyay ugday upyay ootsray, andyay uckedplay offyay igstway omfray
ethay orest-treesfay, ikelay oneyay acquaintedyay ithway iddenhay irtuesvay inyay atwhay asway
aluelessvay otay ommoncay eyesyay. Ehay asway eardhay otay eakspay ofyay Irsay Enelmkay Igbyday,
andyay otheryay amousfay en,—whosemay ientificscay attainmentsyay ereway esteemedyay
ardlyhay esslay anthay upernatural,—assay avinghay eenbay ishay orrespondentscay oryay
associatesyay. Ywhay, ithway uchsay ankray inyay ethay earnedlay orldway, adhay ehay omecay
itherhay? Atwhay ouldcay ehay, osewhay eresphay asway inyay eatgray itiescay, ebay eekingsay inyay
ethay ildernessway? Inyay answeryay otay isthay ueryqay, ayay umorray ainedgay ound,—andgray,
oweverhay absurdyay, asway entertainedyay ybay omesay eryvay ensiblesay eople,—thatpay
Eavenhay adhay oughtwray anyay absoluteyay iraclemay, ybay ansportingtray anyay eminentyay
Octorday ofyay Ysicphay, omfray ayay Ermangay universityyay, odilybay oughthray ethay airyay,
andyay ettingsay imhay ownday atyay ethay oorday ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday udystay!
Individualsyay ofyay iserway aithfay, indeedyay, owhay ewknay atthay Eavenhay omotespray itsyay
urposespay ithoutway aimingyay atyay ethay age-effectstay ofyay atwhay isyay alledcay
iraculousmay interpositionyay, ereway inclinedyay otay eesay ayay ovidentialpray andhay inyay
Ogerray Illingworth’schay osay opportuneyay arrivalyay.

Isthay ideayay asway ountenancedcay ybay ethay ongstray interestyay ichwhay ethay ysicianphay
everyay anifestedmay inyay ethay youngyay ergymanclay; ehay attachedyay imselfhay otay imhay asyay
ayay arishionerpay, andyay oughtsay otay inway ayay iendlyfray egardray andyay onfidencecay omfray
ishay aturallynay eservedray ensibilitysay. Ehay expressedyay eatgray alarmyay atyay ishay
astor’spay atestay ofyay ealthhay, utbay asway anxiousyay otay attemptyay ethay urecay, andyay, ifyay
earlyyay undertakenyay, eemedsay otnay espondentday ofyay ayay avorablefay esultray. Ethay
eldersyay, ethay eaconsday, ethay otherlymay amesday, andyay ethay youngyay andyay airfay
aidensmay, ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday ockflay, ereway alikeyay importunateyay atthay ehay
ouldshay akemay ialtray ofyay ethay ysician’sphay anklyfray offeredyay illskay. Mray.
Immesdaleday entlygay epelledray eirthay entreatiesyay.

i“ay eednay onay edicinemay,” aidsay ehay.

Utbay owhay ouldcay ethay youngyay inistermay aysay osay, enwhay, ithway everyyay uccessivesay
Abbathsay, ishay eekchay asway alerpay andyay innerthay, andyay ishay oicevay oremay emuloustray
anthay efore,—whenbay ityay adhay ownay ecomebay ayay onstantcay abithay, atherray anthay ayay
asualcay esturegay, otay esspray ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay? Asway ehay earyway ofyay ishay
aborslay? Idday ehay ishway otay ieday? Esethay uestionsqay ereway olemnlysay opoundedpray
otay Mray. Immesdaleday ybay ethay elderyay inistersmay ofyay Ostonbay andyay ethay eaconsday ofyay
ishay urchchay, owhay, otay useyay eirthay ownyay asephray, ealt“day ithway imhay” onyay ethay insay
ofyay ejectingray ethay aidyay ichwhay Ovidencepray osay anifestlymay eldhay outyay. Ehay
istenedlay inyay ilencesay, andyay inallyfay omisedpray otay onfercay ithway ethay
ysicianphay.

ere“way ityay Od’sgay illway,” aidsay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, enwhay, inyay
ulfilmentfay ofyay isthay edgeplay, ehay equestedray oldyay Ogerray Illingworth’schay
ofessionalpray adviceyay, i“ay ouldcay ebay ellway ontentcay, atthay ymay aborslay, andyay ymay
orrowssay, andyay ymay inssay, andyay ymay ainspay, ouldshay ortlyshay endyay ithway emay, andyay
atwhay isyay earthlyyay ofyay emthay ebay uriedbay inyay ymay avegray, andyay ethay iritualspay ogay
ithway emay otay ymay eternalyay atestay, atherray anthay atthay youyay ouldshay utpay youryay
illskay otay ethay oofpray inyay ymay ehalfbay.”

ah“ay,” epliedray Ogerray Illingworthchay, ithway atthay uietnessqay ichwhay, etherwhay
imposedyay oryay aturalnay, arkedmay allyay ishay eportmentday, it“ay isyay usthay atthay ayay
youngyay ergymanclay isyay aptyay otay eakspay. Youthfulyay enmay, otnay avinghay akentay ayay eepday
ootray, ivegay upyay eirthay oldhay ofyay ifelay osay easilyyay! Andyay aintlysay enmay, owhay alkway
ithway Odgay onyay earthyay, ouldway ainfay ebay awayyay, otay alkway ithway imhay onyay ethay oldengay
avementspay ofyay ethay Ewnay Erusalemjay.”

ay“nay,” ejoinedray ethay youngyay inistermay, uttingpay ishay andhay otay ishay earthay,
ithway ayay ushflay ofyay ainpay ittingflay overyay ishay owbray, ere“way Iyay orthierway otay alkway
erethay, Iyay ouldcay ebay etterbay ontentcay otay oiltay erehay.”

ood“gay enmay everyay interpretyay emselvesthay ootay eanlymay,” aidsay ethay ysicianphay.

illustration[ay: Ethay Inistermay andyay Eechlay]

Inyay isthay annermay, ethay ysteriousmay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay ecamebay ethay
edicalmay adviseryay ofyay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday. Asyay otnay onlyyay ethay
iseaseday interestedyay ethay ysicianphay, utbay ehay asway onglystray ovedmay otay ooklay
intoyay ethay aracterchay andyay ualitiesqay ofyay ethay atientpay, esethay otway enmay, osay
ifferentday inyay ageyay, amecay aduallygray otay endspay uchmay imetay ogethertay. Orfay ethay
akesay ofyay ethay inister’smay ealthhay, andyay otay enableyay ethay eechlay otay athergay
antsplay ithway ealinghay almbay inyay emthay, eythay ooktay onglay alksway onyay ethay
ea-shoresay, oryay inyay ethay orestfay; inglingmay ariousvay alktay ithway ethay ashplay andyay
urmurmay ofyay ethay avesway, andyay ethay olemnsay ind-anthemway amongyay ethay ee-topstray.
Oftenyay, ikewiselay, oneyay asway ethay uestgay ofyay ethay otheryay, inyay ishay aceplay ofyay
udystay andyay etirementray. Erethay asway ayay ascinationfay orfay ethay inistermay inyay ethay
ompanycay ofyay ethay anmay ofyay iencescay, inyay omwhay ehay ecognizedray anyay intellectualyay
ultivationcay ofyay onay oderatemay epthday oryay opescay; ogethertay ithway ayay angeray andyay
eedomfray ofyay ideasyay, atthay ehay ouldway avehay ainlyvay ookedlay orfay amongyay ethay
embersmay ofyay ishay ownyay ofessionpray. Inyay uthtray, ehay asway artledstay, ifyay otnay
ockedshay, otay indfay isthay attributeyay inyay ethay ysicianphay. Mray. Immesdaleday asway ayay
uetray iestpray, ayay uetray eligionistray, ithway ethay everentialray entimentsay
argelylay evelopedday, andyay anyay orderyay ofyay indmay atthay impelledyay itselfyay
owerfullypay alongyay ethay acktray ofyay ayay eedcray, andyay oreway itsyay assagepay
ontinuallycay eeperday ithway ethay apselay ofyay imetay. Inyay onay atestay ofyay ocietysay
ouldway ehay avehay eenbay atwhay isyay alledcay ayay anmay ofyay iberallay iewsvay; ityay ouldway
alwaysyay ebay essentialyay otay ishay eacepay otay eelfay ethay essurepray ofyay ayay aithfay aboutyay
imhay, upportingsay, ilewhay ityay onfinedcay imhay ithinway itsyay ironyay ameworkfray. Otnay
ethay esslay, oweverhay, oughthay ithway ayay emuloustray enjoymentyay, idday ehay eelfay ethay
occasionalyay eliefray ofyay ookinglay atyay ethay universeyay oughthray ethay ediummay ofyay
anotheryay indkay ofyay intellectyay anthay osethay ithway ichwhay ehay abituallyhay eldhay
onversecay. Ityay asway asyay ifyay ayay indowway ereway ownthray openyay, admittingyay ayay eerfray
atmosphereyay intoyay ethay oseclay andyay ifledstay udystay, erewhay ishay ifelay asway
astingway itselfyay awayyay, amidyay amplightlay, oryay obstructedyay ay-beamsday, andyay ethay
ustymay agrancefray, ebay ityay ensualsay oryay oralmay, atthay exhalesyay omfray ooksbay. Utbay
ethay airyay asway ootay eshfray andyay illchay otay ebay onglay eathedbray ithway omfortcay. Osay
ethay inistermay, andyay ethay ysicianphay ithway imhay, ithdrewway againyay ithinway ethay
imitslay ofyay atwhay eirthay urchchay efinedday asyay orthodoxyay.

Usthay Ogerray Illingworthchay utinizedscray ishay atientpay arefullycay, othbay asyay ehay
awsay imhay inyay ishay ordinaryyay ifelay, eepingkay anyay accustomedyay athwaypay inyay ethay
angeray ofyay oughtsthay amiliarfay otay imhay, andyay asyay ehay appearedyay enwhay ownthray
amidstyay otheryay oralmay eneryscay, ethay oveltynay ofyay ichwhay ightmay allcay outyay
omethingsay ewnay otay ethay urfacesay ofyay ishay aracterchay. Ehay eemedday ityay essentialyay,
ityay ouldway eemsay, otay owknay ethay anmay, eforebay attemptingyay otay oday imhay oodgay.
Ereverwhay erethay isyay ayay earthay andyay anyay intellectyay, ethay iseasesday ofyay ethay
ysicalphay amefray areyay ingedtay ithway ethay eculiaritiespay ofyay esethay. Inyay Arthuryay
Immesdaleday, oughtthay andyay imaginationyay ereway osay activeyay, andyay ensibilitysay osay
intenseyay, atthay ethay odilybay infirmityyay ouldway ebay ikelylay otay avehay itsyay
oundworkgray erethay. Osay Ogerray Illingworth—thechay anmay ofyay illskay, ethay indkay
andyay iendlyfray ysician—strovephay otay ogay eepday intoyay ishay atient’spay osombay,
elvingday amongyay ishay inciplespray, yingpray intoyay ishay ecollectionsray, andyay
obingpray everythingyay ithway ayay autiouscay ouchtay, ikelay ayay easure-seekertray inyay ayay
arkday averncay. Ewfay ecretssay ancay escapeyay anyay investigatoryay, owhay ashay
opportunityyay andyay icenselay otay undertakeyay uchsay ayay uestqay, andyay illskay otay ollowfay
ityay upyay. Ayay anmay urdenedbay ithway ayay ecretsay ouldshay especiallyyay avoidyay ethay
intimacyyay ofyay ishay ysicianphay. Ifyay ethay atterlay ossesspay ativenay agacitysay, andyay
ayay amelessnay omethingsay ore,—letmay usyay allcay ityay intuitionyay; ifyay ehay owshay onay
intrusiveyay egotismyay, ornay isagreeablyday ominentpray aracteristicschay ofyay ishay
ownyay; ifyay ehay avehay ethay owerpay, ichwhay ustmay ebay ornbay ithway imhay, otay ingbray ishay
indmay intoyay uchsay affinityyay ithway ishay atient’spay, atthay isthay astlay allshay
unawaresyay avehay okenspay atwhay ehay imaginesyay imselfhay onlyyay otay avehay oughtthay; ifyay
uchsay evelationsray ebay eceivedray ithoutway umulttay, andyay acknowledgedyay otnay osay
oftenyay ybay anyay utteredyay ympathysay asyay ybay ilencesay, anyay inarticulateyay eathbray,
andyay erehay andyay erethay ayay ordway, otay indicateyay atthay allyay isyay understoodyay; ifyay otay
esethay ualificationsqay ofyay ayay onfidantcay ebay oinedjay ethay advantagesyay affordedyay
ybay ishay ecognizedray aracterchay asyay ayay ysician;—thenphay, atyay omesay inevitableyay
omentmay, illway ethay oulsay ofyay ethay ufferersay ebay issolvedday, andyay owflay orthfay inyay
ayay arkday, utbay ansparenttray eamstray, ingingbray allyay itsyay ysteriesmay intoyay ethay
aylightday.

Ogerray Illingworthchay ossessedpay allyay, oryay ostmay, ofyay ethay attributesyay aboveyay
enumeratedyay. Everthelessnay, imetay entway onyay; ayay indkay ofyay intimacyyay, asyay eway avehay
aidsay, ewgray upyay etweenbay esethay otway ultivatedcay indsmay, ichwhay adhay asyay ideway ayay
ieldfay asyay ethay olewhay eresphay ofyay umanhay oughtthay andyay udystay, otay eetmay uponyay;
eythay iscussedday everyyay opictay ofyay ethicsyay andyay eligionray, ofyay ublicpay affairsyay
andyay ivatepray aracterchay; eythay alkedtay uchmay, onyay othbay idessay, ofyay attersmay
atthay eemedsay ersonalpay otay emselvesthay; andyay yetyay onay ecretsay, uchsay asyay ethay
ysicianphay anciedfay ustmay existyay erethay, everyay olestay outyay ofyay ethay inister’smay
onsciousnesscay intoyay ishay ompanion’scay earyay. Ethay atterlay adhay ishay uspicionssay,
indeedyay, atthay evenyay ethay aturenay ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday odilybay iseaseday adhay
evernay airlyfay eenbay evealedray otay imhay. Ityay asway ayay angestray eserveray!

Afteryay ayay imetay, atyay ayay inthay omfray Ogerray Illingworthchay, ethay iendsfray ofyay Mray.
Immesdaleday effectedyay anyay arrangementyay ybay ichwhay ethay otway ereway odgedlay inyay ethay
amesay ousehay; osay atthay everyyay ebbyay andyay owflay ofyay ethay inister’smay ife-tidelay
ightmay asspay underyay ethay eyeyay ofyay ishay anxiousyay andyay attachedyay ysicianphay. Erethay
asway uchmay oyjay oughoutthray ethay owntay, enwhay isthay eatlygray esirableday objectyay
asway attainedyay. Ityay asway eldhay otay ebay ethay estbay ossiblepay easuremay orfay ethay
youngyay ergyman’sclay elfareway; unlessyay, indeedyay, asyay oftenyay urgedyay ybay uchsay asyay
eltfay authorizedyay otay oday osay, ehay adhay electedsay omesay oneyay ofyay ethay anymay
oomingblay amselsday, irituallyspay evotedday otay imhay, otay ecomebay ishay evotedday
ifeway. Isthay atterlay epstay, oweverhay, erethay asway onay esentpray ospectpray atthay
Arthuryay Immesdaleday ouldway ebay evailedpray uponyay otay aketay; ehay ejectedray allyay
uggestionssay ofyay ethay indkay, asyay ifyay iestlypray elibacycay ereway oneyay ofyay ishay
articlesyay ofyay urch-disciplinechay. Oomedday ybay ishay ownyay oicechay, ereforethay, asyay
Mray. Immesdaleday osay evidentlyyay asway, otay eatyay ishay unsavoryyay orselmay alwaysyay atyay
another’syay oardbay, andyay endureyay ethay ife-longlay illchay ichwhay ustmay ebay ishay otlay
owhay eekssay otay armway imselfhay onlyyay atyay another’syay iresidefay, ityay ulytray eemedsay
atthay isthay agacioussay, experiencedyay, enevolentbay oldyay ysicianphay, ithway ishay
oncordcay ofyay aternalpay andyay everentialray ovelay orfay ethay youngyay astorpay, asway ethay
eryvay anmay, ofyay allyay ankindmay, otay ebay onstantlycay ithinway eachray ofyay ishay oicevay.

Ethay ewnay abodeyay ofyay ethay otway iendsfray asway ithway ayay iouspay idowway, ofyay oodgay
ocialsay ankray, owhay eltdway inyay ayay ousehay overingcay ettypray earlynay ethay itesay onyay
ichwhay ethay enerablevay ucturestray ofyay Ing’skay Apelchay ashay incesay eenbay uiltbay.
Ityay adhay ethay aveyardgray, originallyyay Isaacyay Ohnson’sjay ome-fieldhay, onyay oneyay
idesay, andyay osay asway ellway adaptedyay otay allcay upyay erioussay eflectionsray, uitedsay
otay eirthay espectiveray employmentsyay, inyay othbay inistermay andyay anmay ofyay ysicphay.
Ethay otherlymay arecay ofyay ethay oodgay idowway assignedyay otay Mray. Immesdaleday ayay ontfray
apartmentyay, ithway ayay unnysay exposureyay, andyay eavyhay indow-curtainsway, otay eatecray
ayay oontidenay adowshay, enwhay esirableday. Ethay allsway ereway unghay oundray ithway
apestrytay, aidsay otay ebay omfray ethay Obelingay oomslay, andyay, atyay allyay eventsyay,
epresentingray ethay Ipturalscray orystay ofyay Avidday andyay Athshebabay, andyay Athannay
ethay Ophetpray, inyay olorscay illstay unfadedyay, utbay ichwhay ademay ethay airfay omanway
ofyay ethay enescay almostyay asyay imlygray icturesquepay asyay ethay oe-denouncingway eersay.
Erehay ethay alepay ergymanclay iledpay upyay ishay ibrarylay, ichray ithway
archment-boundpay oliosfay ofyay ethay Athersfay, andyay ethay orelay ofyay Abbisray, andyay
onkishmay eruditionyay, ofyay ichwhay ethay Otestantpray ivinesday, evenyay ilewhay eythay
ilifiedvay andyay ecriedday atthay assclay ofyay iterswray, ereway yetyay onstrainedcay oftenyay
otay availyay emselvesthay. Onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay ousehay oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay arrangedyay ishay udystay andyay aboratorylay; otnay uchsay asyay ayay odernmay
anmay ofyay iencescay ouldway eckonray evenyay olerablytay ompletecay, utbay ovidedpray ithway
ayay istillingday apparatusyay, andyay ethay eansmay ofyay ompoundingcay ugsdray andyay
emicalschay, ichwhay ethay actisedpray alchemistyay ewknay ellway owhay otay urntay otay
urposepay. Ithway uchsay ommodiousnesscay ofyay ituationsay, esethay otway earnedlay
ersonspay atsay emselvesthay ownday, eachyay inyay ishay ownyay omainday, yetyay amiliarlyfay
assingpay omfray oneyay apartmentyay otay ethay otheryay, andyay estowingbay ayay utualmay andyay
otnay incuriousyay inspectionyay intoyay oneyay another’syay usinessbay.

Andyay ethay Everendray Arthuryay Immesdale’sday estbay iscerningday iendsfray, asyay eway
avehay intimatedyay, eryvay easonablyray imaginedyay atthay ethay andhay ofyay Ovidencepray
adhay oneday allyay isthay, orfay ethay urpose—besoughtpay inyay osay anymay ublicpay, andyay
omesticday, andyay ecretsay ayers—ofpray estoringray ethay youngyay inistermay otay
ealthhay. Ut—itbay ustmay ownay ebay aid—anothersay ortionpay ofyay ethay ommunitycay adhay
atterlylay egunbay otay aketay itsyay ownyay iewvay ofyay ethay elationray etwixtbay Mray.
Immesdaleday andyay ethay ysteriousmay oldyay ysicianphay. Enwhay anyay uninstructedyay
ultitudemay attemptsyay otay eesay ithway itsyay eyesyay, ityay isyay exceedinglyyay aptyay otay ebay
eceivedday. Enwhay, oweverhay, ityay ormsfay itsyay udgmentjay, asyay ityay usuallyyay oesday, onyay
ethay intuitionsyay ofyay itsyay eatgray andyay armway earthay, ethay onclusionscay usthay
attainedyay areyay oftenyay osay ofoundpray andyay osay unerringyay, asyay otay ossesspay ethay
aracterchay ofyay uthstray upernaturallysay evealedray. Ethay eoplepay, inyay ethay asecay
ofyay ichwhay eway eakspay, ouldcay ustifyjay itsyay ejudicepray againstyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay ybay onay actfay oryay argumentyay orthyway ofyay erioussay efutationray.
Erethay asway anyay agedyay andicraftsmanhay, ityay isyay uetray, owhay adhay eenbay ayay itizencay
ofyay Ondonlay atyay ethay eriodpay ofyay Irsay Omasthay Overbury’syay urdermay, ownay omesay
irtythay yearsyay agoneyay; ehay estifiedtay otay avinghay eensay ethay ysicianphay, underyay
omesay otheryay amenay, ichwhay ethay arratornay ofyay ethay orystay adhay ownay orgottenfay, inyay
ompanycay ithway Octorday Ormanfay, ethay amousfay oldyay onjurercay, owhay asway
implicatedyay inyay ethay affairyay ofyay Overburyyay. Otway oryay eethray individualsyay intedhay,
atthay ethay anmay ofyay illskay, uringday ishay Indianyay aptivitycay, adhay enlargedyay ishay
edicalmay attainmentsyay ybay oiningjay inyay ethay incantationsyay ofyay ethay avagesay
iestspray; owhay ereway universallyyay acknowledgedyay otay ebay owerfulpay enchantersyay,
oftenyay erformingpay eeminglysay iraculousmay urescay ybay eirthay illskay inyay ethay
ackblay artyay. Ayay argelay umber—andnay anymay ofyay esethay ereway ersonspay ofyay uchsay
obersay ensesay andyay acticalpray observationyay atthay eirthay opinionsyay ouldway avehay
eenbay aluablevay, inyay otheryay atters—affirmedmay atthay Ogerray Illingworth’schay
aspectyay adhay undergoneyay ayay emarkableray angechay ilewhay ehay adhay eltdway inyay owntay,
andyay especiallyyay incesay ishay abodeyay ithway Mray. Immesdaleday. Atyay irstfay, ishay
expressionyay adhay eenbay almcay, editativemay, olar-likeschay. Ownay, erethay asway
omethingsay uglyyay andyay evilyay inyay ishay acefay, ichwhay eythay adhay otnay eviouslypray
oticednay, andyay ichwhay ewgray illstay ethay oremay obviousyay otay ightsay, ethay ofteneryay
eythay ookedlay uponyay imhay. Accordingyay otay ethay ulgarvay ideayay, ethay irefay inyay ishay
aboratorylay adhay eenbay oughtbray omfray ethay owerlay egionsray, andyay asway edfay ithway
infernalyay uelfay; andyay osay, asyay ightmay ebay expectedyay, ishay isagevay asway ettinggay
ootysay ithway ethay okesmay.

Otay umsay upyay ethay attermay, ityay ewgray otay ebay ayay idelyway iffusedday opinionyay, atthay
ethay Everendray Arthuryay Immesdaleday, ikelay anymay otheryay ersonagespay ofyay especialyay
anctitysay, inyay allyay agesyay ofyay ethay Istianchray orldway, asway auntedhay eitheryay ybay
Atansay imselfhay, oryay Atan’ssay emissaryyay, inyay ethay uisegay ofyay oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay. Isthay iabolicalday agentyay adhay ethay Ivineday ermissionpay, orfay ayay
easonsay, otay urrowbay intoyay ethay ergyman’sclay intimacyyay, andyay otplay againstyay ishay
oulsay. Onay ensiblesay anmay, ityay asway onfessedcay, ouldcay oubtday onyay ichwhay idesay ethay
ictoryvay ouldway urntay. Ethay eoplepay ookedlay, ithway anyay unshakenyay opehay, otay eesay
ethay inistermay omecay orthfay outyay ofyay ethay onflictcay, ansfiguredtray ithway ethay
oryglay ichwhay ehay ouldway unquestionablyyay inway. Eanwhilemay, everthelessnay, ityay
asway adsay otay inkthay ofyay ethay erchancepay ortalmay agonyyay oughthray ichwhay ehay ustmay
ugglestray owardstay ishay iumphtray.

Alasyay! otay udgejay omfray ethay oomglay andyay errortay inyay ethay epthsday ofyay ethay oorpay
inister’smay eyesyay, ethay attlebay asway ayay oresay oneyay andyay ethay ictoryvay anythingyay
utbay ecuresay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Xay.

                      Ethay Eechlay Andyay Ishay Atientpay.


Oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, oughoutthray ifelay, adhay eenbay almcay inyay
emperamenttay, indlykay, oughthay otnay ofyay armway affectionsyay, utbay everyay, andyay inyay
allyay ishay elationsray ithway ethay orldway, ayay urepay andyay uprightyay anmay. Ehay adhay egunbay
anyay investigationyay, asyay ehay imaginedyay, ithway ethay everesay andyay equalyay integrityyay
ofyay ayay udgejay, esirousday onlyyay ofyay uthtray, evenyay asyay ifyay ethay uestionqay involvedyay
onay oremay anthay ethay air-drawnyay ineslay andyay iguresfay ofyay ayay eometricalgay oblempray,
insteadyay ofyay umanhay assionspay, andyay ongswray inflictedyay onyay imselfhay. Utbay, asyay ehay
oceededpray, ayay erribletay ascinationfay, ayay indkay ofyay iercefay, oughthay illstay
almcay, ecessitynay, eizedsay ethay oldyay anmay ithinway itsyay ipegray, andyay evernay etsay
imhay eefray againyay, untilyay ehay adhay oneday allyay itsyay iddingbay. Ehay ownay ugday intoyay ethay
oorpay ergyman’sclay earthay, ikelay ayay inermay earchingsay orfay oldgay; oryay, atherray,
ikelay ayay extonsay elvingday intoyay ayay avegray, ossiblypay inyay uestqay ofyay ayay eweljay atthay
adhay eenbay uriedbay onyay ethay eadday an’smay osombay, utbay ikelylay otay indfay othingnay
avesay ortalitymay andyay orruptioncay. Alasyay orfay ishay ownyay oulsay, ifyay esethay ereway
atwhay ehay oughtsay!

Ometimessay, ayay ightlay immeredglay outyay ofyay ethay ysician’sphay eyesyay, urningbay ueblay
andyay ominousyay, ikelay ethay eflectionray ofyay ayay urnacefay, oryay, etlay usyay aysay, ikelay
oneyay ofyay osethay eamsglay ofyay astlyghay irefay atthay artedday omfray Unyan’sbay awfulyay
oorwayday inyay ethay illsidehay, andyay uiveredqay onyay ethay ilgrim’spay acefay. Ethay oilsay
erewhay isthay arkday inermay asway orkingway adhay erchancepay ownshay indicationsyay atthay
encouragedyay imhay.

is“thay anmay,” aidsay ehay, atyay oneyay uchsay omentmay, otay imselfhay, ure“pay asyay eythay
eemday im,—allhay iritualspay asyay ehay eems,—hathsay inheritedyay ayay ongstray animalyay
aturenay omfray ishay atherfay oryay ishay othermay. Etlay usyay igday ayay ittlelay urtherfay inyay
ethay irectionday ofyay isthay einvay!”

Enthay, afteryay onglay earchsay intoyay ethay inister’smay imday interioryay, andyay urningtay
overyay anymay eciouspray aterialsmay, inyay ethay apeshay ofyay ighhay aspirationsyay orfay ethay
elfareway ofyay ishay aceray, armway ovelay ofyay oulssay, urepay entimentssay, aturalnay
ietypay, engthenedstray ybay oughtthay andyay udystay, andyay illuminatedyay ybay
evelation,—allray ofyay ichwhay invaluableyay oldgay asway erhapspay onay etterbay anthay
ubbishray otay ethay eeker,—hesay ouldway urntay ackbay, iscouragedday, andyay eginbay ishay
uestqay owardstay anotheryay ointpay. Ehay opedgray alongyay asyay ealthilystay, ithway asyay
autiouscay ayay eadtray, andyay asyay aryway anyay outlookyay, asyay ayay iefthay enteringyay ayay
amberchay erewhay ayay anmay ieslay onlyyay alfhay asleep,—oryay, ityay aymay ebay, oadbray
awake,—withyay urposepay otay ealstay ethay eryvay easuretray ichwhay isthay anmay uardsgay
asyay ethay appleyay ofyay ishay eyeyay. Inyay itespay ofyay ishay emeditatedpray arefulnesscay, ethay
oorflay ouldway ownay andyay enthay eakcray; ishay armentsgay ouldway ustleray; ethay adowshay
ofyay ishay esencepray, inyay ayay orbiddenfay oximitypray, ouldway ebay ownthray acrossyay ishay
ictimvay. Inyay otheryay ordsway, Mray. Immesdaleday, osewhay ensibilitysay ofyay ervenay
oftenyay oducedpray ethay effectyay ofyay iritualspay intuitionyay, ouldway ecomebay aguelyvay
awareyay atthay omethingsay inimicalyay otay ishay eacepay adhay ustthray itselfyay intoyay
elationray ithway imhay. Utbay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ootay, adhay erceptionspay
atthay ereway almostyay intuitiveyay; andyay enwhay ethay inistermay ewthray ishay artledstay
eyesyay owardstay imhay, erethay ethay ysicianphay atsay; ishay indkay, atchfulway,
ympathizingsay, utbay evernay intrusiveyay iendfray.

Yetyay Mray. Immesdaleday ouldway erhapspay avehay eensay isthay individual’syay aracterchay
oremay erfectlypay, ifyay ayay ertaincay orbidnessmay, otay ichwhay icksay eartshay areyay
iablelay, adhay otnay enderedray imhay uspicioussay ofyay allyay ankindmay. Ustingtray onay
anmay asyay ishay iendfray, ehay ouldcay otnay ecognizeray ishay enemyyay enwhay ethay atterlay
actuallyyay appearedyay. Ehay ereforethay illstay eptkay upyay ayay amiliarfay intercourseyay
ithway imhay, ailyday eceivingray ethay oldyay ysicianphay inyay ishay udystay; oryay isitingvay
ethay aboratorylay, andyay, orfay ecreation’sray akesay, atchingway ethay ocessespray ybay
ichwhay eedsway ereway onvertedcay intoyay ugsdray ofyay otencypay.

Oneyay ayday, eaninglay ishay oreheadfay onyay ishay andhay, andyay ishay elbowyay onyay ethay illsay
ofyay ethay openyay indowway, atthay ookedlay owardstay ethay aveyardgray, ehay alkedtay ithway
Ogerray Illingworthchay, ilewhay ethay oldyay anmay asway examiningyay ayay undlebay ofyay
unsightlyyay antsplay.

ere“whay,” askedyay ehay, ithway ayay ooklay askanceyay atyay em,—forthay ityay asway ethay
ergyman’sclay eculiaritypay atthay ehay eldomsay, owadaysnay, ookedlay aightforthstray
atyay anyyay objectyay, etherwhay umanhay oryay inanimate,—“whereyay, ymay indkay octorday,
idday youyay athergay osethay erbshay, ithway uchsay ayay arkday, abbyflay eaflay?”

even“ay inyay ethay aveyardgray erehay atyay andhay,” answeredyay ethay ysicianphay,
ontinuingcay ishay employmentyay. ey“thay areyay ewnay otay emay. Iyay oundfay emthay owinggray
onyay ayay avegray, ichwhay orebay onay ombstonetay, ornay otheryay emorialmay ofyay ethay eadday
anmay, avesay esethay uglyyay eedsway, atthay avehay akentay uponyay emselvesthay otay eepkay
imhay inyay emembranceray. Eythay ewgray outyay ofyay ishay earthay, andyay ypifytay, ityay aymay ebay,
omesay ideoushay ecretsay atthay asway uriedbay ithway imhay, andyay ichwhay ehay adhay oneday
etterbay otay onfesscay uringday ishay ifetimelay.”

erchance“pay,” aidsay Mray. Immesdaleday, e“hay earnestlyyay esiredday ityay, utbay ouldcay
otnay.”

and“ay ereforewhay?” ejoinedray ethay ysicianphay. erefore“whay otnay; incesay allyay ethay
owerspay ofyay aturenay allcay osay earnestlyyay orfay ethay onfessioncay ofyay insay, atthay
esethay ackblay eedsway avehay ungspray upyay outyay ofyay ayay uriedbay earthay, otay akemay
anifestmay anyay unspokenyay imecray?”

at“thay, oodgay Irsay, isyay utbay ayay antasyfay ofyay yoursyay,” epliedray ethay inistermay.
ere“thay ancay ebay, ifyay Iyay orebodefay arightyay, onay owerpay, ortshay ofyay ethay Ivineday
ercymay, otay iscloseday, etherwhay ybay utteredyay ordsway, oryay ybay ypetay oryay emblemyay,
ethay ecretssay atthay aymay ebay uriedbay ithway ayay umanhay earthay. Ethay earthay, akingmay
itselfyay uiltygay ofyay uchsay ecretssay, ustmay erforcepay oldhay emthay, untilyay ethay ayday
enwhay allyay iddenhay ingsthay allshay ebay evealedray. Ornay avehay Iyay osay eadray oryay
interpretedyay Olyhay Itwray, asyay otay understandyay atthay ethay isclosureday ofyay umanhay
oughtsthay andyay eedsday, enthay otay ebay ademay, isyay intendedyay asyay ayay artpay ofyay ethay
etributionray. Atthay, urelysay, ereway ayay allowshay iewvay ofyay ityay. Onay; esethay
evelationsray, unlessyay Iyay eatlygray erryay, areyay eantmay erelymay otay omotepray ethay
intellectualyay atisfactionsay ofyay allyay intelligentyay eingsbay, owhay illway andstay
aitingway, onyay atthay ayday, otay eesay ethay arkday oblempray ofyay isthay ifelay ademay ainplay.
Ayay owledgeknay ofyay en’smay eartshay illway ebay eedfulnay otay ethay ompletestcay olutionsay
ofyay atthay oblempray. Andyay Iyay onceivecay, oreovermay, atthay ethay eartshay oldinghay
uchsay iserablemay ecretssay asyay youyay eakspay ofyay illway yieldyay emthay upyay, atyay atthay
astlay ayday, otnay ithway eluctanceray, utbay ithway ayay oyjay unutterableyay.”

en“thay ywhay otnay evealray emthay erehay?” askedyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ancingglay
uietlyqay asideyay atyay ethay inistermay. y“whay ouldshay otnay ethay uiltygay onesyay oonersay
availyay emselvesthay ofyay isthay unutterableyay olacesay?”

ey“thay ostlymay oday,” aidsay ethay ergymanclay, ipinggray ardhay atyay ishay eastbray asyay ifyay
afflictedyay ithway anyay importunateyay obthray ofyay ainpay. any“may, anymay ayay oorpay oulsay
athhay ivengay itsyay onfidencecay otay emay, otnay onlyyay onyay ethay eath-bedday, utbay ilewhay
ongstray inyay ifelay, andyay airfay inyay eputationray. Andyay everyay, afteryay uchsay anyay
outpouringyay, Oyay, atwhay ayay eliefray avehay Iyay itnessedway inyay osethay infulsay
ethrenbray! evenyay asyay inyay oneyay owhay atyay astlay awsdray eefray airyay, afteryay onglay
iflingstay ithway ishay ownyay ollutedpay eathbray. Owhay ancay ityay ebay otherwiseyay? Ywhay
ouldshay ayay etchedwray anmay, uiltygay, eway illway aysay, ofyay urdermay, eferpray otay eepkay
ethay eadday orpsecay uriedbay inyay ishay ownyay earthay, atherray anthay ingflay ityay orthfay atyay
onceyay, andyay etlay ethay universeyay aketay arecay ofyay ityay!”

yet“ay omesay enmay urybay eirthay ecretssay usthay,” observedyay ethay almcay ysicianphay.

ue“tray; erethay areyay uchsay enmay,” answeredyay Mray. Immesdaleday. ut“bay, otnay otay
uggestsay oremay obviousyay easonsray, ityay aymay ebay atthay eythay areyay eptkay ilentsay ybay
ethay eryvay onstitutioncay ofyay eirthay aturenay. Or,—canyay eway otnay upposesay
it?—guiltyyay asyay eythay aymay ebay, etainingray, everthelessnay, ayay ealzay orfay Od’sgay
oryglay andyay an’smay elfareway, eythay inkshray omfray isplayingday emselvesthay ackblay
andyay ilthyfay inyay ethay iewvay ofyay enmay; ecausebay, enceforwardthay, onay oodgay ancay ebay
achievedyay ybay emthay; onay evilyay ofyay ethay astpay ebay edeemedray ybay etterbay ervicesay.
Osay, otay eirthay ownyay unutterableyay ormenttay, eythay ogay aboutyay amongyay eirthay
ellow-creaturesfay, ookinglay urepay asyay ew-fallennay owsnay ilewhay eirthay eartshay
areyay allyay eckledspay andyay ottedspay ithway iniquityyay ofyay ichwhay eythay annotcay idray
emselvesthay.”

ese“thay enmay eceiveday emselvesthay,” aidsay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ithway
omewhatsay oremay emphasisyay anthay usualyay, andyay akingmay ayay ightslay esturegay ithway
ishay orefingerfay. ey“thay earfay otay aketay upyay ethay ameshay atthay ightfullyray
elongsbay otay emthay. Eirthay ovelay orfay anmay, eirthay ealzay orfay Od’sgay
ervice,—thesesay olyhay impulsesyay aymay oryay aymay otnay oexistcay inyay eirthay eartshay
ithway ethay evilyay inmatesyay otay ichwhay eirthay uiltgay ashay unbarredyay ethay oorday, andyay
ichwhay ustmay eedsnay opagatepray ayay ellishhay eedbray ithinway emthay. Utbay, ifyay eythay
eeksay otay orifyglay Odgay, etlay emthay otnay iftlay eavenwardhay eirthay uncleanyay andshay!
Ifyay eythay ouldway ervesay eirthay ellow-menfay, etlay emthay oday ityay ybay akingmay
anifestmay ethay owerpay andyay ealityray ofyay onsciencecay, inyay onstrainingcay emthay otay
enitentialpay elf-abasementsay! Ouldstway outhay avehay emay otay elievebay, Oyay iseway
andyay iouspay iendfray, atthay ayay alsefay owshay ancay ebay etter—canbay ebay oremay orfay
Od’sgay oryglay, oryay an’smay elfare—thanway Od’sgay ownyay uthtray? Usttray emay, uchsay
enmay eceiveday emselvesthay!”

it“ay aymay ebay osay,” aidsay ethay youngyay ergymanclay, indifferentlyyay, asyay aivingway ayay
iscussionday atthay ehay onsideredcay irrelevantyay oryay unseasonableyay. Ehay adhay ayay
eadyray acultyfay, indeedyay, ofyay escapingyay omfray anyyay opictay atthay agitatedyay ishay
ootay ensitivesay andyay ervousnay emperament.—“buttay, ownay, Iyay ouldway askyay ofyay ymay
ell-skilledway ysicianphay, etherwhay, inyay oodgay oothsay, ehay eemsday emay otay avehay
ofitedpray ybay ishay indlykay arecay ofyay isthay eakway amefray ofyay inemay?”

Eforebay Ogerray Illingworthchay ouldcay answeryay, eythay eardhay ethay earclay, ildway
aughterlay ofyay ayay youngyay ild’schay oicevay, oceedingpray omfray ethay adjacentyay
urial-groundbay. Ookinglay instinctivelyyay omfray ethay openyay indow,—forway ityay asway
ummer-time,—thesay inistermay eheldbay Esterhay Ynnepray andyay ittlelay Earlpay
assingpay alongyay ethay ootpathfay atthay aversedtray ethay enclosureyay. Earlpay ookedlay
asyay eautifulbay asyay ethay ayday, utbay asway inyay oneyay ofyay osethay oodsmay ofyay erversepay
errimentmay ichwhay, eneverwhay eythay occurredyay, eemedsay otay emoveray erhay entirelyyay
outyay ofyay ethay eresphay ofyay ympathysay oryay umanhay ontactcay. Eshay ownay ippedskay
irreverentlyyay omfray oneyay avegray otay anotheryay; untilyay, omingcay otay ethay oadbray,
atflay, armorialyay ombstonetay ofyay ayay epartedday orthy,—perhapsway ofyay Isaacyay
Ohnsonjay imself,—shehay eganbay otay anceday uponyay ityay. Inyay eplyray otay erhay other’smay
ommandcay andyay entreatyyay atthay eshay ouldway ehavebay oremay ecorouslyday, ittlelay
Earlpay ausedpay otay athergay ethay icklypray urrsbay omfray ayay alltay urdockbay ichwhay
ewgray esidebay ethay ombtay. Akingtay ayay andfulhay ofyay esethay, eshay arrangedyay emthay
alongyay ethay ineslay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay atthay ecoratedday ethay aternalmay
osombay, otay ichwhay ethay urrsbay, asyay eirthay aturenay asway, enaciouslytay adheredyay.
Esterhay idday otnay uckplay emthay offyay.

Ogerray Illingworthchay adhay ybay isthay imetay approachedyay ethay indowway, andyay iledsmay
imlygray ownday.

ere“thay isyay onay awlay, ornay everenceray orfay authorityyay, onay egardray orfay umanhay
ordinancesyay oryay opinionsyay, ightray oryay ongwray, ixedmay upyay ithway atthay ild’schay
ompositioncay,” emarkedray ehay, asyay uchmay otay imselfhay asyay otay ishay ompanioncay. i“ay
awsay erhay, ethay otheryay ayday, espatterbay ethay Overnorgay imselfhay ithway aterway, atyay
ethay attle-troughcay inyay Ingspray Anelay. Atwhay, inyay Eaven’shay amenay, isyay eshay? Isyay
ethay impyay altogetheryay evilyay? Athhay eshay affectionsyay? Athhay eshay anyyay
iscoverableday inciplepray ofyay eingbay?”

one“nay, avesay ethay eedomfray ofyay ayay okenbray awlay,” answeredyay Mray. Immesdaleday, inyay
ayay uietqay ayway, asyay ifyay ehay adhay eenbay iscussingday ethay ointpay ithinway imselfhay.
ether“whay apablecay ofyay oodgay, Iyay owknay otnay.”

Ethay ildchay obablypray overheardyay eirthay oicesvay; orfay, ookinglay upyay otay ethay
indowway, ithway ayay ightbray, utbay aughtynay ilesmay ofyay irthmay andyay intelligenceyay,
eshay ewthray oneyay ofyay ethay icklypray urrsbay atyay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday. Ethay
ensitivesay ergymanclay unkshray, ithway ervousnay eaddray, omfray ethay ightlay
issilemay. Etectingday ishay emotionyay, Earlpay appedclay erhay ittlelay andshay, inyay ethay
ostmay extravagantyay ecstasyyay. Esterhay Ynnepray, ikewiselay, adhay involuntarilyyay
ookedlay upyay; andyay allyay esethay ourfay ersonspay, oldyay andyay youngyay, egardedray oneyay
anotheryay inyay ilencesay, illtay ethay ildchay aughedlay aloudyay, andyay outed,—“comeshay
awayyay, othermay! Omecay awayyay, oryay yonderyay oldyay Ackblay Anmay illway atchcay youyay! Ehay
athhay otgay oldhay ofyay ethay inistermay alreadyyay. Omecay awayyay, othermay, oryay ehay illway
atchcay youyay! Utbay ehay annotcay atchcay ittlelay Earlpay!”

Osay eshay ewdray erhay othermay awayyay, ippingskay, ancingday, andyay iskingfray
antasticallyfay, amongyay ethay illockshay ofyay ethay eadday eoplepay, ikelay ayay eaturecray
atthay adhay othingnay inyay ommoncay ithway ayay ygonebay andyay uriedbay enerationgay, ornay
ownedyay erselfhay akinyay otay ityay. Ityay asway asyay ifyay eshay adhay eenbay ademay afreshyay, outyay
ofyay ewnay elementsyay, andyay ustmay erforcepay ebay ermittedpay otay ivelay erhay ownyay ifelay,
andyay ebay ayay awlay untoyay erselfhay, ithoutway erhay eccentricitiesyay eingbay eckonedray
otay erhay orfay ayay imecray.

ere“thay oesgay ayay omanway,” esumedray Ogerray Illingworthchay, afteryay ayay ausepay,
o“whay, ebay erhay emeritsday atwhay eythay aymay, athhay onenay ofyay atthay ysterymay ofyay
iddenhay infulnesssay ichwhay youyay eemday osay ievousgray otay ebay ornebay. Isyay Esterhay
Ynnepray ethay esslay iserablemay, inkthay youyay, orfay atthay arletscay etterlay onyay erhay
eastbray?”

i“ay oday erilyvay elievebay ityay,” answeredyay ethay ergymanclay. evertheless“nay, Iyay
annotcay answeryay orfay erhay. Erethay asway ayay ooklay ofyay ainpay inyay erhay acefay, ichwhay Iyay
ouldway adlyglay avehay eenbay aredspay ethay ightsay ofyay. Utbay illstay, ethinksmay, ityay
ustmay eedsnay ebay etterbay orfay ethay ufferersay otay ebay eefray otay owshay ishay ainpay, asyay
isthay oorpay omanway Esterhay isyay, anthay otay overcay ityay allyay upyay inyay ishay earthay.”

Erethay asway anotheryay ausepay; andyay ethay ysicianphay eganbay anewyay otay examineyay andyay
arrangeyay ethay antsplay ichwhay ehay adhay atheredgay.

you“ay inquiredyay ofyay emay, ayay ittlelay imetay agoneyay,” aidsay ehay, atyay engthlay, y“may
udgmentjay asyay ouchingtay youryay ealthhay.”

i“ay idday,” answeredyay ethay ergymanclay, and“ay ouldway adlyglay earnlay ityay. Eakspay
anklyfray, Iyay aypray youyay, ebay ityay orfay ifelay oryay eathday.”

eely“fray, enthay, andyay ainlyplay,” aidsay ethay ysicianphay, illstay usybay ithway ishay
antsplay, utbay eepingkay ayay aryway eyeyay onyay Mray. Immesdaleday, e“thay isorderday isyay ayay
angestray oneyay; otnay osay uchmay inyay itselfyay, ornay asyay outwardlyyay anifested,—inmay
osay arfay, atyay eastlay, asyay ethay ymptomssay avehay eenbay aidlay openyay otay ymay
observationyay. Ookinglay ailyday atyay youyay, ymay oodgay Irsay, andyay atchingway ethay
okenstay ofyay youryay aspectyay, ownay orfay onthsmay onegay ybay, Iyay ouldshay eemday youyay ayay anmay
oresay icksay, ityay aymay ebay, yetyay otnay osay icksay utbay atthay anyay instructedyay andyay
atchfulway ysicianphay ightmay ellway opehay otay urecay youyay. Ut—ibay owknay otnay atwhay
otay ay—thesay iseaseday isyay atwhay Iyay eemsay otay owknay, yetyay owknay ityay otnay.”

you“ay eakspay inyay iddlesray, earnedlay Irsay,” aidsay ethay alepay inistermay, ancingglay
asideyay outyay ofyay ethay indowway.

en“thay, otay eakspay oremay ainlyplay,” ontinuedcay ethay ysicianphay, and“ay Iyay avecray
ardonpay, Ir,—shouldsay ityay eemsay otay equireray ardon,—forpay isthay eedfulnay
ainnessplay ofyay ymay eechspay. Etlay emay ask,—asyay youryay iend,—asfray oneyay avinghay
argechay, underyay Ovidencepray, ofyay youryay ifelay andyay ysicalphay ell-being,—hathway
allyay ethay operationyay ofyay isthay isorderday eenbay airlyfay aidlay openyay andyay ecountedray
otay emay?”

ow“hay ancay youyay uestionqay ityay?” askedyay ethay inistermay. urely“say, ityay ereway
ild’schay ayplay, otay allcay inyay ayay ysicianphay, andyay enthay idehay ethay oresay!”

you“ay ouldway elltay emay, enthay, atthay Iyay owknay allyay?” aidsay Ogerray Illingworthchay,
eliberatelyday, andyay ixingfay anyay eyeyay, ightbray ithway intenseyay andyay oncentratedcay
intelligenceyay, onyay ethay inister’smay acefay. e“bay ityay osay! Utbay, againyay! Ehay otay
omwhay onlyyay ethay outwardyay andyay ysicalphay evilyay isyay aidlay openyay, owethknay,
oftentimesyay, utbay alfhay ethay evilyay ichwhay ehay isyay alledcay uponyay otay urecay. Ayay
odilybay iseaseday, ichwhay eway ooklay uponyay asyay olewhay andyay entireyay ithinway itselfyay,
aymay, afteryay allyay, ebay utbay ayay ymptomsay ofyay omesay ailmentyay inyay ethay iritualspay
artpay. Youryay ardonpay, onceyay againyay, oodgay Irsay, ifyay ymay eechspay ivegay ethay adowshay
ofyay offenceyay. Youyay, Irsay, ofyay allyay enmay omwhay Iyay avehay ownknay, areyay ehay osewhay odybay
isyay ethay osestclay onjoinedcay, andyay imbuedyay, andyay identifiedyay, osay otay eakspay,
ithway ethay iritspay ereofwhay ityay isyay ethay instrumentyay.”

en“thay Iyay eednay askyay onay urtherfay,” aidsay ethay ergymanclay, omewhatsay astilyhay
isingray omfray ishay airchay. you“ay ealday otnay, Iyay aketay ityay, inyay edicinemay orfay ethay
oulsay!”

us“thay, ayay icknesssay,” ontinuedcay Ogerray Illingworthchay, oinggay onyay, inyay anyay
unalteredyay onetay, ithoutway eedinghay ethay interruption,—butyay andingstay upyay,
andyay onfrontingcay ethay emaciatedyay andyay ite-cheekedwhay inistermay, ithway ishay
owlay, arkday, andyay isshapenmay igure,—“afay icknesssay, ayay oresay aceplay, ifyay eway aymay
osay allcay ityay, inyay youryay iritspay, athhay immediatelyyay itsyay appropriateyay
anifestationmay inyay youryay odilybay amefray. Ouldway youyay, ereforethay, atthay youryay
ysicianphay ealhay ethay odilybay evilyay? Owhay aymay isthay ebay, unlessyay youyay irstfay aylay
openyay otay imhay ethay oundway oryay oubletray inyay youryay oulsay?”

o!—not“nay otay ee!—notthay otay anyay earthlyyay ysicianphay!” iedcray Mray.
Immesdaleday, assionatelypay, andyay urningtay ishay eyesyay, ullfay andyay ightbray, andyay
ithway ayay indkay ofyay iercenessfay, onyay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay. ot“nay otay eethay!
Utbay ifyay ityay ebay ethay oul’ssay iseaseday, enthay oday Iyay ommitcay yselfmay otay ethay oneyay
Ysicianphay ofyay ethay oulsay! Ehay, ifyay ityay andstay ithway ishay oodgay easureplay, ancay
urecay; oryay ehay ancay illkay! Etlay imhay oday ithway emay asyay, inyay ishay usticejay andyay
isdomway, ehay allshay eesay oodgay. Utbay owhay artyay outhay, atthay eddlestmay inyay isthay
atter?—thatmay aresday ustthray imselfhay etweenbay ethay ufferersay andyay ishay Odgay?”

Ithway ayay anticfray esturegay ehay ushedray outyay ofyay ethay oomray.

it“ay isyay asyay ellway otay avehay ademay isthay epstay,” aidsay Ogerray Illingworthchay otay
imselfhay, ookinglay afteryay ethay inistermay ithway ayay avegray ilesmay. ere“thay isyay
othingnay ostlay. Eway allshay ebay iendsfray againyay anonyay. Utbay eesay, ownay, owhay
assionpay akestay oldhay uponyay isthay anmay, andyay urriethhay imhay outyay ofyay imselfhay! Asyay
ithway oneyay assionpay, osay ithway anotheryay! Ehay athhay oneday ayay ildway ingthay erenowyay,
isthay iouspay Astermay Immesdaleday, inyay ethay othay assionpay ofyay ishay earthay!”

illustration[ay: Ethay Eechlay andyay ishay Atientpay]

Ityay ovedpray otnay ifficultday otay e-establishray ethay intimacyyay ofyay ethay otway
ompanionscay, onyay ethay amesay ootingfay andyay inyay ethay amesay egreeday asyay eretoforehay.
Ethay youngyay ergymanclay, afteryay ayay ewfay ourshay ofyay ivacypray, asway ensiblesay atthay
ethay isorderday ofyay ishay ervesnay adhay urriedhay imhay intoyay anyay unseemlyyay outbreakyay
ofyay empertay, ichwhay erethay adhay eenbay othingnay inyay ethay ysician’sphay ordsway otay
excuseyay oryay alliatepay. Ehay arvelledmay, indeedyay, atyay ethay iolencevay ithway ichwhay
ehay adhay ustthray ackbay ethay indkay oldyay anmay, enwhay erelymay offeringpray ethay adviceyay
ichwhay ityay asway ishay utyday otay estowbay, andyay ichwhay ethay inistermay imselfhay adhay
expresslyyay oughtsay. Ithway esethay emorsefulray eelingsfay, ehay ostlay onay imetay inyay
akingmay ethay amplestyay apologiesyay, andyay esoughtbay ishay iendfray illstay otay
ontinuecay ethay arecay, ichwhay, ifyay otnay uccessfulsay inyay estoringray imhay otay
ealthhay, adhay, inyay allyay obabilitypray, eenbay ethay eansmay ofyay olongingpray ishay
eeblefay existenceyay otay atthay ourhay. Ogerray Illingworthchay eadilyray assentedyay,
andyay entway onyay ithway ishay edicalmay upervisionsay ofyay ethay inistermay; oingday ishay
estbay orfay imhay, inyay allyay oodgay aithfay, utbay alwaysyay uittingqay ethay atient’spay
apartmentyay, atyay ethay oseclay ofyay ayay ofessionalpray interviewyay, ithway ayay ysteriousmay
andyay uzzledpay ilesmay uponyay ishay ipslay. Isthay expressionyay asway invisibleyay inyay Mray.
Immesdale’sday esencepray, utbay ewgray onglystray evidentyay asyay ethay ysicianphay
ossedcray ethay esholdthray.

a“ay areray asecay!” ehay utteredmay. i“ay ustmay eedsnay ooklay eeperday intoyay ityay. Ayay
angestray ympathysay etwixtbay oulsay andyay odybay! Ereway ityay onlyyay orfay ethay art’syay
akesay, Iyay ustmay earchsay isthay attermay otay ethay ottombay!”

Ityay amecay otay asspay, otnay onglay afteryay ethay enescay aboveyay ecordedray, atthay ethay
Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, atyay oondaynay, andyay entirelyyay unawaresyay, ellfay intoyay
ayay eepday, eepday umberslay, ittingsay inyay ishay airchay, ithway ayay argelay ack-letterblay
olumevay openyay eforebay imhay onyay ethay abletay. Ityay ustmay avehay eenbay ayay orkway ofyay astvay
abilityyay inyay ethay omniferoussay oolschay ofyay iteraturelay. Ethay ofoundpray epthday ofyay
ethay inister’smay eposeray asway ethay oremay emarkableray, inasmuchyay asyay ehay asway oneyay
ofyay osethay ersonspay osewhay eepslay, ordinarilyyay, isyay asyay ightlay, asyay itfulfay, andyay
asyay easilyyay aredscay awayyay, asyay ayay allsmay irdbay oppinghay onyay ayay igtway. Otay uchsay anyay
unwontedyay emotenessray, oweverhay, adhay ishay iritspay ownay ithdrawnway intoyay
itselfyay, atthay ehay irredstay otnay inyay ishay airchay, enwhay oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, ithoutway anyyay extraordinaryyay ecautionpray, amecay intoyay ethay
oomray. Ethay ysicianphay advancedyay irectlyday inyay ontfray ofyay ishay atientpay, aidlay
ishay andhay uponyay ishay osombay, andyay ustthray asideyay ethay estmentvay, atthay,
ithertohay, adhay alwaysyay overedcay ityay evenyay omfray ethay ofessionalpray eyeyay.

Enthay, indeedyay, Mray. Immesdaleday udderedshay, andyay ightlyslay irredstay.

Afteryay ayay iefbray ausepay, ethay ysicianphay urnedtay awayyay.

Utbay, ithway atwhay ayay ildway ooklay ofyay onderway, oyjay, andyay orrorhay! Ithway atwhay ayay
astlyghay aptureray, asyay ityay ereway, ootay ightymay otay ebay expressedyay onlyyay ybay ethay
eyeyay andyay eaturesfay, andyay ereforethay urstingbay orthfay oughthray ethay olewhay
uglinessyay ofyay ishay igurefay, andyay akingmay itselfyay evenyay iotouslyray anifestmay ybay
ethay extravagantyay esturesgay ithway ichwhay ehay ewthray upyay ishay armsyay owardstay ethay
eilingcay, andyay ampedstay ishay ootfay uponyay ethay oorflay! Adhay ayay anmay eensay oldyay
Ogerray Illingworthchay, atyay atthay omentmay ofyay ishay ecstasyyay, ehay ouldway avehay adhay
onay eednay otay askyay owhay Atansay omportscay imselfhay, enwhay ayay eciouspray umanhay oulsay
isyay ostlay otay eavenhay, andyay onway intoyay ishay ingdomkay.

Utbay atwhay istinguishedday ethay ysician’sphay ecstasyyay omfray Atan’ssay asway ethay
aittray ofyay onderway inyay ityay!
