                            illustration[ay]

                                  Ixay.

                       Ethay Interioryay Ofyay Ayay Earthay.


Afteryay ethay incidentyay astlay escribedday, ethay intercourseyay etweenbay ethay
ergymanclay andyay ethay ysicianphay, oughthay externallyyay ethay amesay, asway eallyray ofyay
anotheryay aracterchay anthay ityay adhay eviouslypray eenbay. Ethay intellectyay ofyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay adhay ownay ayay ufficientlysay ainplay athpay eforebay ityay. Ityay asway otnay,
indeedyay, eciselypray atthay ichwhay ehay adhay aidlay outyay orfay imselfhay otay eadtray.
Almcay, entlegay, assionlesspay, asyay ehay appearedyay, erethay asway yetyay, eway earfay, ayay
uietqay epthday ofyay alicemay, ithertohay atentlay, utbay activeyay ownay, inyay isthay
unfortunateyay oldyay anmay, ichwhay edlay imhay otay imagineyay ayay oremay intimateyay evengeray
anthay anyyay ortalmay adhay everyay eakedwray uponyay anyay enemyyay. Otay akemay imselfhay ethay
oneyay ustedtray iendfray, otay omwhay ouldshay ebay onfidedcay allyay ethay earfay, ethay
emorseray, ethay agonyyay, ethay ineffectualyay epentanceray, ethay ackwardbay ushray ofyay
infulsay oughtsthay, expelledyay inyay ainvay! Allyay atthay uiltygay orrowsay, iddenhay omfray
ethay orldway, osewhay eatgray earthay ouldway avehay itiedpay andyay orgivenfay, otay ebay
evealedray otay imhay, ethay Itilesspay, otay imhay, ethay Unforgivingyay! Allyay atthay arkday
easuretray otay ebay avishedlay onyay ethay eryvay anmay, otay omwhay othingnay elseyay ouldcay osay
adequatelyyay aypay ethay ebtday ofyay engeancevay!

Ethay ergyman’sclay yshay andyay ensitivesay eserveray adhay alkedbay isthay emeschay.
Ogerray Illingworthchay, oweverhay, asway inclinedyay otay ebay ardlyhay, ifyay atyay allyay,
esslay atisfiedsay ithway ethay aspectyay ofyay affairsyay, ichwhay Ovidence—usingpray ethay
avengeryay andyay ishay ictimvay orfay itsyay ownyay urposespay, andyay, erchancepay, ardoningpay
erewhay ityay eemedsay ostmay otay unish—hadpay ubstitutedsay orfay ishay ackblay evicesday.
Ayay evelationray, ehay ouldcay almostyay aysay, adhay eenbay antedgray otay imhay. Ityay
atteredmay ittlelay, orfay ishay objectyay, etherwhay elestialcay, oryay omfray atwhay otheryay
egionray. Ybay itsyay aidyay, inyay allyay ethay ubsequentsay elationsray etwixtbay imhay andyay
Mray. Immesdaleday, otnay erelymay ethay externalyay esencepray, utbay ethay eryvay inmostyay
oulsay, ofyay ethay atterlay, eemedsay otay ebay oughtbray outyay eforebay ishay eyesyay, osay atthay
ehay ouldcay eesay andyay omprehendcay itsyay everyyay ovementmay. Ehay ecamebay,
enceforththay, otnay ayay ectatorspay onlyyay, utbay ayay iefchay actoryay, inyay ethay oorpay
inister’smay interioryay orldway. Ehay ouldcay ayplay uponyay imhay asyay ehay osechay. Ouldway
ehay arouseyay imhay ithway ayay obthray ofyay agonyyay? Ethay ictimvay asway oreverfay onyay ethay
ackray; ityay eedednay onlyyay otay owknay ethay ingspray atthay ontrolledcay ethay
engine;—andyay ethay ysicianphay ewknay ityay ellway! Ouldway ehay artlestay imhay ithway
uddensay earfay? Asyay atyay ethay avingway ofyay ayay agician’smay andway, uproseyay ayay islygray
antom,—uprosephay ayay ousandthay antoms,—inphay anymay apesshay, ofyay eathday, oryay
oremay awfulyay ameshay, allyay ockingflay oundray aboutyay ethay ergymanclay, andyay ointingpay
ithway eirthay ingersfay atyay ishay eastbray!

Allyay isthay asway accomplishedyay ithway ayay ubtletysay osay erfectpay, atthay ethay
inistermay, oughthay ehay adhay onstantlycay ayay imday erceptionpay ofyay omesay evilyay
influenceyay atchingway overyay imhay, ouldcay evernay aingay ayay owledgeknay ofyay itsyay
actualyay aturenay. Uetray, ehay ookedlay oubtfullyday, earfully,—evenfay, atyay imestay,
ithway orrorhay andyay ethay itternessbay ofyay atred,—athay ethay eformedday igurefay ofyay
ethay oldyay ysicianphay. Ishay esturesgay, ishay aitgay, ishay izzledgray eardbay, ishay
ightestslay andyay ostmay indifferentyay actsyay, ethay eryvay ashionfay ofyay ishay armentsgay,
ereway odiousyay inyay ethay ergyman’sclay ightsay; ayay okentay implicitlyyay otay ebay eliedray
onyay, ofyay ayay eeperday antipathyyay inyay ethay eastbray ofyay ethay atterlay anthay ehay asway
illingway otay acknowledgeyay otay imselfhay. Orfay, asyay ityay asway impossibleyay otay assignyay
ayay easonray orfay uchsay istrustday andyay abhorrenceyay, osay Mray. Immesdaleday,
onsciouscay atthay ethay oisonpay ofyay oneyay orbidmay otspay asway infectingyay ishay eart’shay
entireyay ubstancesay, attributedyay allyay ishay esentimentspray otay onay otheryay ausecay.
Ehay ooktay imselfhay otay asktay orfay ishay adbay ympathiessay inyay eferenceray otay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, isregardedday ethay essonlay atthay ehay ouldshay avehay awndray omfray
emthay, andyay idday ishay estbay otay ootray emthay outyay. Unableyay otay accomplishyay isthay, ehay
everthelessnay, asyay ayay attermay ofyay inciplepray, ontinuedcay ishay abitshay ofyay ocialsay
amiliarityfay ithway ethay oldyay anmay, andyay usthay avegay imhay onstantcay opportunitiesyay
orfay erfectingpay ethay urposepay otay ich—poorwhay, orlornfay eaturecray atthay ehay
asway, andyay oremay etchedwray anthay ishay ictim—thevay avengeryay adhay evotedday
imselfhay.

Ilewhay usthay ufferingsay underyay odilybay iseaseday, andyay awedgnay andyay orturedtay ybay
omesay ackblay oubletray ofyay ethay oulsay, andyay ivengay overyay otay ethay achinationsmay ofyay
ishay eadliestday enemyyay, ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday adhay achievedyay ayay
illiantbray opularitypay inyay ishay acredsay officeyay. Ehay onway ityay, indeedyay, inyay eatgray
artpay, ybay ishay orrowssay. Ishay intellectualyay iftsgay, ishay oralmay erceptionspay,
ishay owerpay ofyay experiencingyay andyay ommunicatingcay emotionyay, ereway eptkay inyay ayay
atestay ofyay eternaturalpray activityyay ybay ethay ickpray andyay anguishyay ofyay ishay ailyday
ifelay. Ishay amefay, oughthay illstay onyay itsyay upwardyay opeslay, alreadyyay overshadowedyay
ethay oberersay eputationsray ofyay ishay ellow-clergymenfay, eminentyay asyay everalsay ofyay
emthay ereway. Erethay ereway olarsschay amongyay emthay, owhay adhay entspay oremay yearsyay inyay
acquiringyay abstruseyay orelay, onnectedcay ithway ethay ivineday ofessionpray, anthay
Mray. Immesdaleday adhay ivedlay; andyay owhay ightmay ellway, ereforethay, ebay oremay
ofoundlypray ersedvay inyay uchsay olidsay andyay aluablevay attainmentsyay anthay eirthay
youthfulyay otherbray. Erethay ereway enmay, ootay, ofyay ayay urdierstay exturetay ofyay indmay
anthay ishay, andyay endowedyay ithway ayay arfay eatergray areshay ofyay ewdshray, ardhay, ironyay,
oryay anitegray understandingyay; ichwhay, ulyday ingledmay ithway ayay airfay oportionpray
ofyay octrinalday ingredientyay, onstitutescay ayay ighlyhay espectableray,
efficaciousyay, andyay unamiableyay arietyvay ofyay ethay ericalclay eciesspay. Erethay ereway
othersyay, againyay, uetray aintlysay athersfay, osewhay acultiesfay adhay eenbay
elaboratedyay ybay earyway oiltay amongyay eirthay ooksbay, andyay ybay atientpay oughtthay,
andyay etherealizedyay, oreovermay, ybay iritualspay ommunicationscay ithway ethay
etterbay orldway, intoyay ichwhay eirthay uritypay ofyay ifelay adhay almostyay introducedyay
esethay olyhay ersonagespay, ithway eirthay armentsgay ofyay ortalitymay illstay ingingclay
otay emthay. Allyay atthay eythay ackedlay asway ethay iftgay atthay escendedday uponyay ethay
osenchay isciplesday atyay Entecostpay, inyay onguestay ofyay ameflay; ymbolizingsay, ityay
ouldway eemsay, otnay ethay owerpay ofyay eechspay inyay oreignfay andyay unknownyay anguageslay,
utbay atthay ofyay addressingyay ethay olewhay umanhay otherhoodbray inyay ethay eart’shay
ativenay anguagelay. Esethay athersfay, otherwiseyay osay apostolicyay, ackedlay
Eaven’shay astlay andyay arestray attestationyay ofyay eirthay officeyay, ethay Onguetay ofyay
Ameflay. Eythay ouldway avehay ainlyvay ought—hadsay eythay everyay eameddray ofyay
eeking—tosay expressyay ethay ighesthay uthstray oughthray ethay umblesthay ediummay ofyay
amiliarfay ordsway andyay imagesyay. Eirthay oicesvay amecay ownday, afaryay andyay
indistinctlyyay, omfray ethay upperyay eightshay erewhay eythay abituallyhay eltdway.

illustration[ay: Ethay Irginsvay ofyay ethay Urchchay]

Otnay improbablyyay, ityay asway otay isthay atterlay assclay ofyay enmay atthay Mray.
Immesdaleday, ybay anymay ofyay ishay aitstray ofyay aracterchay, aturallynay elongedbay. Otay
ethay ighhay ountain-peaksmay ofyay aithfay andyay anctitysay ehay ouldway avehay imbedclay,
adhay otnay ethay endencytay eenbay artedthway ybay ethay urdenbay, ateverwhay ityay ightmay
ebay, ofyay imecray oryay anguishyay, eneathbay ichwhay ityay asway ishay oomday otay ottertay. Ityay
eptkay imhay ownday, onyay ayay evellay ithway ethay owestlay; imhay, ethay anmay ofyay etherealyay
attributesyay, osewhay oicevay ethay angelsyay ightmay elseyay avehay istenedlay otay andyay
answeredyay! Utbay isthay eryvay urdenbay ityay asway, atthay avegay imhay ympathiessay osay
intimateyay ithway ethay infulsay otherhoodbray ofyay ankindmay; osay atthay ishay earthay
ibratedvay inyay unisonyay ithway eirsthay, andyay eceivedray eirthay ainpay intoyay itselfyay,
andyay entsay itsyay ownyay obthray ofyay ainpay oughthray ayay ousandthay otheryay eartshay, inyay
ushesgay ofyay adsay, ersuasivepay eloquenceyay. Oftenestyay ersuasivepay, utbay
ometimessay erribletay! Ethay eoplepay ewknay otnay ethay owerpay atthay ovedmay emthay
usthay. Eythay eemedday ethay youngyay ergymanclay ayay iraclemay ofyay olinesshay. Eythay
anciedfay imhay ethay outhpiecemay ofyay Eaven’shay essagesmay ofyay isdomway, andyay ebukeray,
andyay ovelay. Inyay eirthay eyesyay, ethay eryvay oundgray onyay ichwhay ehay odtray asway
anctifiedsay. Ethay irginsvay ofyay ishay urchchay ewgray alepay aroundyay imhay, ictimsvay ofyay
ayay assionpay osay imbuedyay ithway eligiousray entimentsay atthay eythay imaginedyay ityay otay
ebay allyay eligionray, andyay oughtbray ityay openlyyay, inyay eirthay itewhay osomsbay, asyay
eirthay ostmay acceptableyay acrificesay eforebay ethay altaryay. Ethay agedyay embersmay ofyay
ishay ockflay, eholdingbay Mray. Immesdale’sday amefray osay eeblefay, ilewhay eythay ereway
emselvesthay osay uggedray inyay eirthay infirmityyay, elievedbay atthay ehay ouldway ogay
eavenwardhay eforebay emthay, andyay enjoinedyay ityay uponyay eirthay ildrenchay, atthay
eirthay oldyay onesbay ouldshay ebay uriedbay oseclay otay eirthay youngyay astor’spay olyhay
avegray. Andyay, allyay isthay imetay, erchancepay, enwhay oorpay Mray. Immesdaleday asway
inkingthay ofyay ishay avegray, ehay uestionedqay ithway imselfhay etherwhay ethay assgray
ouldway everyay owgray onyay ityay, ecausebay anyay accursedyay ingthay ustmay erethay ebay uriedbay!

Ityay isyay inconceivableyay, ethay agonyyay ithway ichwhay isthay ublicpay enerationvay
orturedtay imhay! Ityay asway ishay enuinegay impulseyay otay adoreyay ethay uthtray, andyay otay
eckonray allyay ingsthay adow-likeshay, andyay utterlyyay evoidday ofyay eightway oryay aluevay,
atthay adhay otnay itsyay ivineday essenceyay asyay ethay ifelay ithinway eirthay ifelay. Enthay,
atwhay asway e?—ahay ubstance?—orsay ethay immestday ofyay allyay adowsshay? Ehay ongedlay
otay eakspay outyay, omfray ishay ownyay ulpitpay, atyay ethay ullfay eighthay ofyay ishay oicevay,
andyay elltay ethay eoplepay atwhay ehay asway. i“ay, omwhay youyay eholdbay inyay esethay ackblay
armentsgay ofyay ethay iesthood,—ipray, owhay ascendyay ethay acredsay eskday, andyay urntay
ymay alepay acefay eavenwardhay, akingtay uponyay yselfmay otay oldhay ommunioncay, inyay youryay
ehalfbay, ithway ethay Ostmay Ighhay Omniscience,—iyay, inyay osewhay ailyday ifelay youyay
iscernday ethay anctitysay ofyay Enoch,—iyay, osewhay ootstepsfay, asyay youyay upposesay,
eavelay ayay eamglay alongyay ymay earthlyyay acktray, erebywhay ethay ilgrimspay atthay allshay
omecay afteryay emay aymay ebay uidedgay otay ethay egionsray ofyay ethay est,—iblay, owhay avehay
aidlay ethay andhay ofyay aptismbay uponyay youryay ildren,—ichay, owhay avehay eathedbray ethay
artingpay ayerpray overyay youryay yingday iendsfray, otay omwhay ethay Amenyay oundedsay
aintlyfay omfray ayay orldway ichwhay eythay adhay uitted,—iqay, youryay astorpay, omwhay youyay
osay everenceray andyay usttray, amyay utterlyyay ayay ollutionpay andyay ayay ielay!”

Oremay anthay onceyay, Mray. Immesdaleday adhay onegay intoyay ethay ulpitpay, ithway ayay
urposepay evernay otay omecay ownday itsyay epsstay, untilyay ehay ouldshay avehay okenspay
ordsway ikelay ethay aboveyay. Oremay anthay onceyay, ehay adhay earedclay ishay oatthray, andyay
awndray inyay ethay onglay, eepday, andyay emuloustray eathbray, ichwhay, enwhay entsay orthfay
againyay, ouldway omecay urdenedbay ithway ethay ackblay ecretsay ofyay ishay oulsay. Oremay
anthay once—nayyay, oremay anthay ayay undredhay imes—hetay adhay actuallyyay okenspay!
Okenspay! Utbay owhay? Ehay adhay oldtay ishay earershay atthay ehay asway altogetheryay ilevay,
ayay ilervay ompanioncay ofyay ethay ilestvay, ethay orstway ofyay innerssay, anyay abominationyay,
ayay ingthay ofyay unimaginableyay iniquityyay; andyay atthay ethay onlyyay onderway asway, atthay
eythay idday otnay eesay ishay etchedwray odybay ivelledshray upyay eforebay eirthay eyesyay, ybay
ethay urningbay athwray ofyay ethay Almightyyay! Ouldcay erethay ebay ainerplay eechspay anthay
isthay? Ouldway otnay ethay eoplepay artstay upyay inyay eirthay eatssay, ybay ayay imultaneoussay
impulseyay, andyay eartay imhay ownday outyay ofyay ethay ulpitpay ichwhay ehay efiledday? Otnay osay,
indeedyay! Eythay eardhay ityay allyay, andyay idday utbay everenceray imhay ethay oremay. Eythay
ittlelay uessedgay atwhay eadlyday urportpay urkedlay inyay osethay elf-condemningsay
ordsway. e“thay odlygay youthyay!” aidsay eythay amongyay emselvesthay. e“thay aintsay onyay
earthyay! Alasyay, ifyay ehay iscernday uchsay infulnesssay inyay ishay ownyay itewhay oulsay, atwhay
orridhay ectaclespay ouldway ehay eholdbay inyay inethay oryay inemay!” Ethay inistermay ellway
ew—subtleknay, utbay emorsefulray ypocritehay atthay ehay as!—theway ightlay inyay
ichwhay ishay aguevay onfessioncay ouldway ebay iewedvay. Ehay adhay ivenstray otay utpay ayay
eatchay uponyay imselfhay ybay akingmay ethay avowalyay ofyay ayay uiltygay onsciencecay, utbay
adhay ainedgay onlyyay oneyay otheryay insay, andyay ayay elf-acknowledgedsay ameshay, ithoutway
ethay omentarymay eliefray ofyay eingbay elf-deceivedsay. Ehay adhay okenspay ethay eryvay
uthtray, andyay ansformedtray ityay intoyay ethay eriestvay alsehoodfay. Andyay yetyay, ybay ethay
onstitutioncay ofyay ishay aturenay, ehay ovedlay ethay uthtray, andyay oathedlay ethay ielay,
asyay ewfay enmay everyay idday. Ereforethay, aboveyay allyay ingsthay elseyay, ehay oathedlay ishay
iserablemay elfsay!

Ishay inwardyay oubletray ovedray imhay otay acticespray oremay inyay accordanceyay ithway ethay
oldyay, orruptedcay aithfay ofyay Omeray, anthay ithway ethay etterbay ightlay ofyay ethay urchchay
inyay ichwhay ehay adhay eenbay ornbay andyay edbray. Inyay Mray. Immesdale’sday ecretsay osetclay,
underyay ocklay andyay eykay, erethay asway ayay oodyblay ourgescay. Oftentimesyay, isthay
Otestantpray andyay Uritanpay ivineday adhay iedplay ityay onyay ishay ownyay ouldersshay;
aughinglay itterlybay atyay imselfhay ethay ilewhay, andyay itingsmay osay uchmay ethay oremay
itilesslypay ecausebay ofyay atthay itterbay aughlay. Ityay asway ishay ustomcay, ootay, asyay ityay
ashay eenbay atthay ofyay anymay otheryay iouspay Uritanspay, otay ast,—notfay, oweverhay,
ikelay emthay, inyay orderyay otay urifypay ethay odybay andyay enderray ityay ethay itterfay ediummay
ofyay elestialcay illuminationyay, utbay igorouslyray, andyay untilyay ishay eesknay
embledtray eneathbay imhay, asyay anyay actyay ofyay enancepay. Ehay eptkay igilsvay, ikewiselay,
ightnay afteryay ightnay, ometimessay inyay utteryay arknessday; ometimessay ithway ayay
immeringglay amplay; andyay ometimessay, iewingvay ishay ownyay acefay inyay ayay
ooking-glasslay, ybay ethay ostmay owerfulpay ightlay ichwhay ehay ouldcay owthray uponyay
ityay. Ehay usthay ypifiedtay ethay onstantcay introspectionyay erewithwhay ehay orturedtay,
utbay ouldcay otnay urifypay, imselfhay. Inyay esethay engthenedlay igilsvay, ishay ainbray
oftenyay eeledray, andyay isionsvay eemedsay otay itflay eforebay imhay; erhapspay eensay
oubtfullyday, andyay ybay ayay aintfay ightlay ofyay eirthay ownyay, inyay ethay emoteray imnessday
ofyay ethay amberchay, oryay oremay ividlyvay, andyay oseclay esidebay imhay, ithinway ethay
ooking-glasslay. Ownay ityay asway ayay erdhay ofyay iabolicday apesshay, atthay innedgray andyay
ockedmay atyay ethay alepay inistermay, andyay eckonedbay imhay awayyay ithway emthay; ownay ayay
oupgray ofyay iningshay angelsyay, owhay ewflay upwardyay eavilyhay, asyay orrow-ladensay, utbay
ewgray oremay etherealyay asyay eythay oseray. Ownay amecay ethay eadday iendsfray ofyay ishay
youthyay, andyay ishay ite-beardedwhay atherfay, ithway ayay aint-likesay ownfray, andyay ishay
othermay, urningtay erhay acefay awayyay asyay eshay assedpay ybay. Ostghay ofyay ayay
other,—thinnestmay antasyfay ofyay ayay other,—methinksmay eshay ightmay yetyay avehay
ownthray ayay ityingpay anceglay owardstay erhay onsay! Andyay ownay, oughthray ethay amberchay
ichwhay esethay ectralspay oughtsthay adhay ademay osay astlyghay, idedglay Esterhay
Ynnepray, eadinglay alongyay ittlelay Earlpay, inyay erhay arletscay arbgay, andyay ointingpay
erhay orefingerfay, irstfay atyay ethay arletscay etterlay onyay erhay osombay, andyay enthay atyay
ethay ergyman’sclay ownyay eastbray.

Onenay ofyay esethay isionsvay everyay uiteqay eludedday imhay. Atyay anyyay omentmay, ybay anyay
effortyay ofyay ishay illway, ehay ouldcay iscernday ubstancessay oughthray eirthay istymay
acklay ofyay ubstancesay, andyay onvincecay imselfhay atthay eythay ereway otnay olidsay inyay
eirthay aturenay, ikelay yonderyay abletay ofyay arvedcay oakyay, oryay atthay igbay, uaresqay,
eathern-boundlay andyay azen-claspedbray olumevay ofyay ivinityday. Utbay, orfay allyay
atthay, eythay ereway, inyay oneyay ensesay, ethay uesttray andyay ostmay ubstantialsay ingsthay
ichwhay ethay oorpay inistermay ownay ealtday ithway. Ityay isyay ethay unspeakableyay iserymay
ofyay ayay ifelay osay alsefay asyay ishay, atthay ityay ealsstay ethay ithpay andyay ubstancesay outyay
ofyay ateverwhay ealitiesray erethay areyay aroundyay usyay, andyay ichwhay ereway eantmay ybay
Eavenhay otay ebay ethay irit’sspay oyjay andyay utrimentnay. Otay ethay untrueyay anmay, ethay
olewhay universeyay isyay alse,—itfay isyay impalpable,—ityay inksshray otay othingnay
ithinway ishay aspgray. Andyay ehay imselfhay, inyay osay arfay asyay ehay owsshay imselfhay inyay ayay
alsefay ightlay, ecomesbay ayay adowshay, oryay, indeedyay, easescay otay existyay. Ethay onlyyay
uthtray atthay ontinuedcay otay ivegay Mray. Immesdaleday ayay ealray existenceyay onyay isthay
earthyay, asway ethay anguishyay inyay ishay inmostyay oulsay, andyay ethay undissembledyay
expressionyay ofyay ityay inyay ishay aspectyay. Adhay ehay onceyay oundfay owerpay otay ilesmay, andyay
earway ayay acefay ofyay ayetygay, erethay ouldway avehay eenbay onay uchsay anmay!

Onyay oneyay ofyay osethay uglyyay ightsnay, ichwhay eway avehay aintlyfay intedhay atyay, utbay
orbornefay otay icturepay orthfay, ethay inistermay artedstay omfray ishay airchay. Ayay ewnay
oughtthay adhay uckstray imhay. Erethay ightmay ebay ayay oment’smay eacepay inyay ityay.
Attiringyay imselfhay ithway asyay uchmay arecay asyay ifyay ityay adhay eenbay orfay ublicpay
orshipway, andyay eciselypray inyay ethay amesay annermay, ehay olestay oftlysay ownday ethay
aircasestay, undidyay ethay oorday, andyay issuedyay orthfay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iixay.

                         Ethay Inister’smay Igilvay.


Alkingway inyay ethay adowshay ofyay ayay eamdray, asyay ityay ereway, andyay erhapspay actuallyyay
underyay ethay influenceyay ofyay ayay eciesspay ofyay omnambulismsay, Mray. Immesdaleday
eachedray ethay otspay erewhay, ownay osay onglay incesay, Esterhay Ynnepray adhay ivedlay
oughthray erhay irstfay ourshay ofyay ublicpay ignominyyay. Ethay amesay atformplay oryay
affoldscay, ackblay andyay eather-stainedway ithway ethay ormstay oryay unshinesay ofyay
evensay onglay yearsyay, andyay oot-wornfay, ootay, ithway ethay eadtray ofyay anymay ulpritscay
owhay adhay incesay ascendedyay ityay, emainedray andingstay eneathbay ethay alconybay ofyay
ethay eeting-housemay. Ethay inistermay entway upyay ethay epsstay.

Ityay asway anyay obscureyay ightnay ofyay earlyyay Aymay. Anyay unvariedyay allpay ofyay oudclay
uffledmay ethay olewhay expanseyay ofyay yskay omfray enithzay otay orizonhay. Ifyay ethay amesay
ultitudemay ichwhay adhay oodstay asyay eye-witnessesyay ilewhay Esterhay Ynnepray
ustainedsay erhay unishmentpay ouldcay ownay avehay eenbay ummonedsay orthfay, eythay
ouldway avehay iscernedday onay acefay aboveyay ethay atformplay, ornay ardlyhay ethay
outlineyay ofyay ayay umanhay apeshay, inyay ethay arkday aygray ofyay ethay idnightmay. Utbay ethay
owntay asway allyay asleepyay. Erethay asway onay erilpay ofyay iscoveryday. Ethay inistermay
ightmay andstay erethay, ifyay ityay osay easedplay imhay, untilyay orningmay ouldshay eddenray
inyay ethay eastyay, ithoutway otheryay iskray anthay atthay ethay ankday andyay illchay ight-airnay
ouldway eepcray intoyay ishay amefray, andyay iffenstay ishay ointsjay ithway eumatismrhay,
andyay ogclay ishay oatthray ithway atarrhcay andyay oughcay; erebythay efraudingday ethay
expectantyay audienceyay ofyay o-morrow’stay ayerpray andyay ermonsay. Onay eyeyay ouldcay eesay
imhay, avesay atthay ever-wakefulyay oneyay ichwhay adhay eensay imhay inyay ishay osetclay,
ieldingway ethay oodyblay ourgescay. Ywhay, enthay, adhay ehay omecay itherhay? Asway ityay utbay
ethay ockerymay ofyay enitencepay? Ayay ockerymay, indeedyay, utbay inyay ichwhay ishay oulsay
ifledtray ithway itselfyay! Ayay ockerymay atyay ichwhay angelsyay ushedblay andyay eptway, ilewhay
iendsfay ejoicedray, ithway eeringjay aughterlay! Ehay adhay eenbay ivendray itherhay ybay
ethay impulseyay ofyay atthay Emorseray ichwhay oggedday imhay everywhereyay, andyay osewhay ownyay
istersay andyay oselyclay inkedlay ompanioncay asway atthay Owardicecay ichwhay
invariablyyay ewdray imhay ackbay, ithway erhay emuloustray ipegray, ustjay enwhay ethay
otheryay impulseyay adhay urriedhay imhay otay ethay ergevay ofyay ayay isclosureday. Oorpay,
iserablemay anmay! atwhay ightray adhay infirmityyay ikelay ishay otay urdenbay itselfyay ithway
imecray? Imecray isyay orfay ethay iron-nervedyay, owhay avehay eirthay oicechay eitheryay otay
endureyay ityay, oryay, ifyay ityay esspray ootay ardhay, otay exertyay eirthay iercefay andyay avagesay
engthstray orfay ayay oodgay urposepay, andyay ingflay ityay offyay atyay onceyay! Isthay eeblefay andyay
ostmay ensitivesay ofyay iritsspay ouldcay oday eithernay, yetyay ontinuallycay idday oneyay
ingthay oryay anotheryay, ichwhay intertwinedyay, inyay ethay amesay inextricableyay otknay,
ethay agonyyay ofyay eaven-defyinghay uiltgay andyay ainvay epentanceray.

Andyay usthay, ilewhay andingstay onyay ethay affoldscay, inyay isthay ainvay owshay ofyay
expiationyay, Mray. Immesdaleday asway overcomeyay ithway ayay eatgray orrorhay ofyay indmay, asyay
ifyay ethay universeyay ereway azinggay atyay ayay arletscay okentay onyay ishay akednay eastbray,
ightray overyay ishay earthay. Onyay atthay otspay, inyay eryvay uthtray, erethay asway, andyay
erethay adhay onglay eenbay, ethay awinggnay andyay oisonouspay oothtay ofyay odilybay ainpay.
Ithoutway anyyay effortyay ofyay ishay illway, oryay owerpay otay estrainray imselfhay, ehay
iekedshray aloudyay; anyay outcryyay atthay entway ealingpay oughthray ethay ightnay, andyay
asway eatenbay ackbay omfray oneyay ousehay otay anotheryay, andyay everberatedray omfray ethay
illshay inyay ethay ackgroundbay; asyay ifyay ayay ompanycay ofyay evilsday, etectingday osay uchmay
iserymay andyay errortay inyay ityay, adhay ademay ayay aythingplay ofyay ethay oundsay, andyay ereway
andyingbay ityay otay andyay ofray.

it“ay isyay oneday!” utteredmay ethay inistermay, overingcay ishay acefay ithway ishay andshay.
e“thay olewhay owntay illway awakeyay, andyay urryhay orthfay, andyay indfay emay erehay!”

Utbay ityay asway otnay osay. Ethay iekshray adhay erhapspay oundedsay ithway ayay arfay eatergray
owerpay, otay ishay ownyay artledstay earsyay, anthay ityay actuallyyay ossessedpay. Ethay owntay
idday otnay awakeyay; oryay, ifyay ityay idday, ethay owsydray umberersslay istookmay ethay ycray
eitheryay orfay omethingsay ightfulfray inyay ayay eamdray, oryay orfay ethay oisenay ofyay
itchesway; osewhay oicesvay, atyay atthay eriodpay, ereway oftenyay eardhay otay asspay overyay
ethay ettlementssay oryay onelylay ottagescay, asyay eythay oderay ithway Atansay oughthray
ethay airyay. Ethay ergymanclay, ereforethay, earinghay onay ymptomssay ofyay isturbanceday,
uncoveredyay ishay eyesyay andyay ookedlay aboutyay imhay. Atyay oneyay ofyay ethay amber-windowschay
ofyay Overnorgay Ellingham’sbay ansionmay, ichwhay oodstay atyay omesay istanceday, onyay ethay
inelay ofyay anotheryay eetstray, ehay eheldbay ethay appearanceyay ofyay ethay oldyay agistratemay
imselfhay, ithway ayay amplay inyay ishay andhay, ayay itewhay ight-capnay onyay ishay eadhay, andyay ayay
onglay itewhay owngay envelopingyay ishay igurefay. Ehay ookedlay ikelay ayay ostghay, evokedyay
unseasonablyyay omfray ethay avegray. Ethay ycray adhay evidentlyyay artledstay imhay. Atyay
anotheryay indowway ofyay ethay amesay ousehay, oreovermay, appearedyay oldyay Istressmay
Ibbinshay, ethay Overnor’sgay istersay, alsoyay ithway ayay amplay, ichwhay, evenyay usthay arfay
offyay, evealedray ethay expressionyay ofyay erhay oursay andyay iscontentedday acefay. Eshay
ustthray orthfay erhay eadhay omfray ethay atticelay, andyay ookedlay anxiouslyyay upwardyay.
Eyondbay ethay adowshay ofyay ayay oubtday, isthay enerablevay itch-ladyway adhay eardhay Mray.
Immesdale’sday outcryyay, andyay interpretedyay ityay, ithway itsyay ultitudinousmay echoesyay
andyay everberationsray, asyay ethay amorclay ofyay ethay iendsfay andyay ight-hagsnay, ithway
omwhay eshay asway ellway ownknay otay akemay excursionsyay intoyay ethay orestfay.

Etectingday ethay eamglay ofyay Overnorgay Ellingham’sbay amplay, ethay oldyay adylay
uicklyqay extinguishedyay erhay ownyay, andyay anishedvay. Ossiblypay, eshay entway upyay
amongyay ethay oudsclay. Ethay inistermay awsay othingnay urtherfay ofyay erhay otionsmay. Ethay
agistratemay, afteryay ayay aryway observationyay ofyay ethay arkness,—intoday ichwhay,
everthelessnay, ehay ouldcay eesay utbay ittlelay urtherfay anthay ehay ightmay intoyay ayay
ill-stone,—retiredmay omfray ethay indowway.

Ethay inistermay ewgray omparativelycay almcay. Ishay eyesyay, oweverhay, ereway oonsay
eetedgray ybay ayay ittlelay, immeringglay ightlay, ichwhay, atyay irstfay ayay onglay ayway offyay,
asway approachingyay upyay ethay eetstray. Ityay ewthray ayay eamglay ofyay ecognitionray onyay erehay
ayay ostpay, andyay erethay ayay arden-fencegay, andyay erehay ayay atticedlay indow-paneway, andyay
erethay ayay umppay, ithway itsyay ullfay oughtray ofyay aterway, andyay erehay, againyay, anyay
archedyay oorday ofyay oakyay, ithway anyay ironyay ockerknay, andyay ayay oughray oglay orfay ethay
oorstepday. Ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday otednay allyay esethay inutemay
articularspay, evenyay ilewhay irmlyfay onvincedcay atthay ethay oomday ofyay ishay
existenceyay asway ealingstay onwardyay, inyay ethay ootstepsfay ichwhay ehay ownay eardhay;
andyay atthay ethay eamglay ofyay ethay anternlay ouldway allfay uponyay imhay, inyay ayay ewfay
omentsmay oremay, andyay evealray ishay ong-hiddenlay ecretsay. Asyay ethay ightlay ewdray
earernay, ehay eheldbay, ithinway itsyay illuminatedyay irclecay, ishay otherbray
ergyman,—orclay, otay eakspay oremay accuratelyyay, ishay ofessionalpray atherfay, asyay
ellway asyay ighlyhay aluedvay iend,—thefray Everendray Mray. Ilsonway; owhay, asyay Mray.
Immesdaleday ownay onjecturedcay, adhay eenbay ayingpray atyay ethay edsidebay ofyay omesay
yingday anmay. Andyay osay ehay adhay. Ethay oodgay oldyay inistermay amecay eshlyfray omfray ethay
eath-chamberday ofyay Overnorgay Inthropway, owhay adhay assedpay omfray earthyay otay
eavenhay ithinway atthay eryvay ourhay. Andyay ownay, urroundedsay, ikelay ethay aint-likesay
ersonagespay ofyay oldenyay imestay, ithway ayay adiantray alohay, atthay orifiedglay imhay
amidyay isthay oomyglay ightnay ofyay in,—assay ifyay ethay epartedday Overnorgay adhay eftlay
imhay anyay inheritanceyay ofyay ishay oryglay, oryay asyay ifyay ehay adhay aughtcay uponyay imselfhay
ethay istantday ineshay ofyay ethay elestialcay itycay, ilewhay ookinglay itherwardthay otay
eesay ethay iumphanttray ilgrimpay asspay ithinway itsyay ates,—nowgay, inyay ortshay, oodgay
Atherfay Ilsonway asway ovingmay omewardhay, aidingyay ishay ootstepsfay ithway ayay ightedlay
anternlay! Ethay immerglay ofyay isthay uminarylay uggestedsay ethay aboveyay onceitscay otay
Mray. Immesdaleday, owhay iled,—naysmay, almostyay aughedlay atyay em,—andthay enthay
onderedway ifyay ehay ereway oinggay admay.

Asyay ethay Everendray Mray. Ilsonway assedpay esidebay ethay affoldscay, oselyclay
ufflingmay ishay Enevagay oakclay aboutyay imhay ithway oneyay armyay, andyay oldinghay ethay
anternlay eforebay ishay eastbray ithway ethay otheryay, ethay inistermay ouldcay ardlyhay
estrainray imselfhay omfray eakingspay.

a“ay oodgay eveningyay otay youyay, enerablevay Atherfay Ilsonway! Omecay upyay itherhay, Iyay
aypray youyay, andyay asspay ayay easantplay ourhay ithway emay!”

Oodgay eavenshay! Adhay Mray. Immesdaleday actuallyyay okenspay? Orfay oneyay instantyay, ehay
elievedbay atthay esethay ordsway adhay assedpay ishay ipslay. Utbay eythay ereway utteredyay
onlyyay ithinway ishay imaginationyay. Ethay enerablevay Atherfay Ilsonway ontinuedcay otay
epstay owlyslay onwardyay, ookinglay arefullycay atyay ethay uddymay athwaypay eforebay ishay
eetfay, andyay evernay onceyay urningtay ishay eadhay owardstay ethay uiltygay atformplay.
Enwhay ethay ightlay ofyay ethay immeringglay anternlay adhay adedfay uiteqay awayyay, ethay
inistermay iscoveredday, ybay ethay aintnessfay ichwhay amecay overyay imhay, atthay ethay
astlay ewfay omentsmay adhay eenbay ayay isiscray ofyay erribletay anxietyyay; althoughyay ishay
indmay adhay ademay anyay involuntaryyay effortyay otay elieveray itselfyay ybay ayay indkay ofyay
uridlay ayfulnessplay.

Ortlyshay afterwardsyay, ethay ikelay islygray ensesay ofyay ethay umoroushay againyay olestay
inyay amongyay ethay olemnsay antomsphay ofyay ishay oughtthay. Ehay eltfay ishay imbslay owinggray
iffstay ithway ethay unaccustomedyay illinesschay ofyay ethay ightnay, andyay oubtedday
etherwhay ehay ouldshay ebay ableyay otay escendday ethay epsstay ofyay ethay affoldscay.
Orningmay ouldway eakbray, andyay indfay imhay erethay. Ethay eighborhoodnay ouldway eginbay
otay ouseray itselfyay. Ethay earliestyay iserray, omingcay orthfay inyay ethay imday
ilighttway, ouldway erceivepay ayay aguelyvay efinedday igurefay aloftyay onyay ethay aceplay
ofyay ameshay; andyay, alfhay azedcray etwixtbay alarmyay andyay uriositycay, ouldway ogay,
ockingknay omfray oorday otay oorday, ummoningsay allyay ethay eoplepay otay eholdbay ethay
ost—asghay ehay eedsnay ustmay inkthay it—ofyay omesay efunctday ansgressortray. Ayay
uskyday umulttay ouldway apflay itsyay ingsway omfray oneyay ousehay otay anotheryay. En—thethay
orningmay ightlay illstay axingway onger—oldstray atriarchspay ouldway iseray upyay inyay
eatgray astehay, eachyay inyay ishay annelflay owngay, andyay atronlymay amesday, ithoutway
ausingpay otay utpay offyay eirthay ight-gearnay. Ethay olewhay ibetray ofyay ecorousday
ersonagespay, owhay adhay evernay eretoforehay eenbay eensay ithway ayay inglesay airhay ofyay
eirthay eadshay awryyay, ouldway artstay intoyay ublicpay iewvay, ithway ethay isorderday ofyay ayay
ightmarenay inyay eirthay aspectsyay. Oldyay Overnorgay Ellinghambay ouldway omecay imlygray
orthfay, ithway ishay Ingkay Ames’sjay uffray astenedfay askewyay; andyay Istressmay
Ibbinshay, ithway omesay igstway ofyay ethay orestfay ingingclay otay erhay irtsskay, andyay
ookinglay ourersay anthay everyay, asyay avinghay ardlyhay otgay ayay inkway ofyay eepslay afteryay
erhay ightnay ideray; andyay oodgay Atherfay Ilsonway, ootay, afteryay endingspay alfhay ethay
ightnay atyay ayay eath-bedday, andyay ikinglay illyay otay ebay isturbedday, usthay earlyyay, outyay
ofyay ishay eamsdray aboutyay ethay orifiedglay aintssay. Itherhay, ikewiselay, ouldway omecay
ethay eldersyay andyay eaconsday ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday urchchay, andyay ethay youngyay
irginsvay owhay osay idolizedyay eirthay inistermay, andyay adhay ademay ayay ineshray orfay imhay
inyay eirthay itewhay osomsbay; ichwhay ownay, ybay ethay ybay, inyay eirthay urryhay andyay
onfusioncay, eythay ouldway antlyscay avehay ivengay emselvesthay imetay otay overcay ithway
eirthay erchiefskay. Allyay eoplepay, inyay ayay ordway, ouldway omecay umblingstay overyay
eirthay esholdsthray, andyay urningtay upyay eirthay amazedyay andyay orror-strickenhay
isagesvay aroundyay ethay affoldscay. Omwhay ouldway eythay iscernday erethay, ithway ethay
edray easternyay ightlay uponyay ishay owbray? Omwhay, utbay ethay Everendray Arthuryay
Immesdaleday, alfhay ozenfray otay eathday, overwhelmedyay ithway ameshay, andyay andingstay
erewhay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay oodstay!

Arriedcay awayyay ybay ethay otesquegray orrorhay ofyay isthay icturepay, ethay inistermay,
unawaresyay, andyay otay ishay ownyay infiniteyay alarmyay, urstbay intoyay ayay eatgray ealpay ofyay
aughterlay. Ityay asway immediatelyyay espondedray otay ybay ayay ightlay, airyyay, ildishchay
aughlay, inyay ichwhay, ithway ayay illthray ofyay ethay eart,—buthay ehay ewknay otnay etherwhay
ofyay exquisiteyay ainpay, oryay easureplay asyay acute,—heyay ecognizedray ethay onestay ofyay
ittlelay Earlpay.

earl“pay! Ittlelay Earlpay!” iedcray ehay afteryay ayay oment’smay ausepay; enthay,
uppressingsay ishay oice,—“hestervay! Esterhay Ynnepray! Areyay youyay erethay?”

yes“ay; ityay isyay Esterhay Ynnepray!” eshay epliedray, inyay ayay onetay ofyay urprisesay; andyay
ethay inistermay eardhay erhay ootstepsfay approachingyay omfray ethay idewalksay, alongyay
ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay assingpay. it“ay isyay Iyay, andyay ymay ittlelay Earlpay.”

ence“whay omecay youyay, Esterhay?” askedyay ethay inistermay. at“whay entsay youyay itherhay?”

i“ay avehay eenbay atchingway atyay ayay eath-bedday,” answeredyay Esterhay Ynne;—“atpray
Overnorgay Inthrop’sway eath-bedday, andyay avehay akentay ishay easuremay orfay ayay oberay,
andyay amyay ownay oinggay omewardhay otay ymay ellingdway.”

ome“cay upyay itherhay, Esterhay, outhay andyay ittlelay Earlpay,” aidsay ethay Everendray Mray.
Immesdaleday. ye“ay avehay othbay eenbay erehay eforebay, utbay Iyay asway otnay ithway youyay.
Omecay upyay itherhay onceyay againyay, andyay eway illway andstay allyay eethray ogethertay!”

Eshay ilentlysay ascendedyay ethay epsstay, andyay oodstay onyay ethay atformplay, oldinghay
ittlelay Earlpay ybay ethay andhay. Ethay inistermay eltfay orfay ethay ild’schay otheryay
andhay, andyay ooktay ityay. Ethay omentmay atthay ehay idday osay, erethay amecay atwhay eemedsay ayay
umultuoustay ushray ofyay ewnay ifelay, otheryay ifelay anthay ishay ownyay, ouringpay ikelay ayay
orrenttay intoyay ishay earthay, andyay urryinghay oughthray allyay ishay einsvay, asyay ifyay ethay
othermay andyay ethay ildchay ereway ommunicatingcay eirthay italvay armthway otay ishay
alf-torpidhay ystemsay. Ethay eethray ormedfay anyay electricyay ainchay.

inister“may!” isperedwhay ittlelay Earlpay.

at“whay ouldstway outhay aysay, ildchay?” askedyay Mray. Immesdaleday.

ilt“way outhay andstay erehay ithway othermay andyay emay, o-morrowtay oontidenay?”
inquiredyay Earlpay.

ay“nay; otnay osay, ymay ittlelay Earlpay,” answeredyay ethay inistermay; orfay, ithway ethay
ewnay energyyay ofyay ethay omentmay, allyay ethay eaddray ofyay ublicpay exposureyay, atthay adhay
osay onglay eenbay ethay anguishyay ofyay ishay ifelay, adhay eturnedray uponyay imhay; andyay ehay
asway alreadyyay emblingtray atyay ethay onjunctioncay inyay ich—withwhay ayay angestray oyjay,
evertheless—henay ownay oundfay imselfhay. ot“nay osay, ymay ildchay. Iyay allshay,
indeedyay, andstay ithway ythay othermay andyay eethay oneyay otheryay ayday, utbay otnay
o-morrowtay.”

Earlpay aughedlay, andyay attemptedyay otay ullpay awayyay erhay andhay. Utbay ethay inistermay
eldhay ityay astfay.

a“ay omentmay ongerlay, ymay ildchay!” aidsay ehay.

ut“bay iltway outhay omisepray,” askedyay Earlpay, o“tay aketay ymay andhay, andyay other’smay
andhay, o-morrowtay oontidenay?”

ot“nay enthay, Earlpay,” aidsay ethay inistermay, ut“bay anotheryay imetay.”

and“ay atwhay otheryay imetay?” ersistedpay ethay ildchay.

at“ay ethay eatgray udgmentjay ayday,” isperedwhay ethay inister,—andmay, angelystray
enoughyay, ethay ensesay atthay ehay asway ayay ofessionalpray eachertay ofyay ethay uthtray
impelledyay imhay otay answeryay ethay ildchay osay. en“thay, andyay erethay, eforebay ethay
udgment-seatjay, ythay othermay, andyay outhay, andyay Iyay ustmay andstay ogethertay. Utbay
ethay aylightday ofyay isthay orldway allshay otnay eesay ouryay eetingmay!”

Earlpay aughedlay againyay.

illustration[ay: ey“thay oodstay inyay ethay oonnay ofyay atthay angestray endorsplay”]

Utbay, eforebay Mray. Immesdaleday adhay oneday eakingspay, ayay ightlay eamedglay arfay andyay
ideway overyay allyay ethay uffledmay yskay. Ityay asway oubtlessday ausedcay ybay oneyay ofyay osethay
eteorsmay, ichwhay ethay ight-watchernay aymay osay oftenyay observeyay urningbay outyay otay
asteway, inyay ethay acantvay egionsray ofyay ethay atmosphereyay. Osay owerfulpay asway itsyay
adianceray, atthay ityay oroughlythay illuminatedyay ethay enseday ediummay ofyay oudclay
etwixtbay ethay yskay andyay earthyay. Ethay eatgray aultvay ightenedbray, ikelay ethay omeday
ofyay anyay immenseyay amplay. Ityay owedshay ethay amiliarfay enescay ofyay ethay eetstray, ithway
ethay istinctnessday ofyay id-daymay, utbay alsoyay ithway ethay awfulnessyay atthay isyay
alwaysyay impartedyay otay amiliarfay objectsyay ybay anyay unaccustomedyay ightlay. Ethay
oodenway ouseshay, ithway eirthay uttingjay oriesstay andyay uaintqay able-peaksgay; ethay
oorstepsday andyay esholdsthray, ithway ethay earlyyay assgray ingingspray upyay aboutyay
emthay; ethay arden-plotsgay, ackblay ithway eshlyfray urnedtay earthyay; ethay
eel-trackwhay, ittlelay ornway, andyay, evenyay inyay ethay arket-placemay, arginedmay ithway
eengray onyay eitheryay ide;—allsay ereway isiblevay, utbay ithway ayay ingularitysay ofyay
aspectyay atthay eemedsay otay ivegay anotheryay oralmay interpretationyay otay ethay ingsthay
ofyay isthay orldway anthay eythay adhay everyay ornebay eforebay. Andyay erethay oodstay ethay
inistermay, ithway ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay; andyay Esterhay Ynnepray, ithway ethay
embroideredyay etterlay immeringglay onyay erhay osombay; andyay ittlelay Earlpay, erselfhay
ayay ymbolsay, andyay ethay onnectingcay inklay etweenbay osethay otway. Eythay oodstay inyay ethay
oonnay ofyay atthay angestray andyay olemnsay endorsplay, asyay ifyay ityay ereway ethay ightlay atthay
isyay otay evealray allyay ecretssay, andyay ethay aybreakday atthay allshay uniteyay allyay owhay
elongbay otay oneyay anotheryay.

Erethay asway itchcraftway inyay ittlelay Earl’spay eyesyay, andyay erhay acefay, asyay eshay
ancedglay upwardyay atyay ethay inistermay, oreway atthay aughtynay ilesmay ichwhay ademay itsyay
expressionyay equentlyfray osay elvishyay. Eshay ithdrewway erhay andhay omfray Mray.
Immesdale’sday, andyay ointedpay acrossyay ethay eetstray. Utbay ehay aspedclay othbay ishay
andshay overyay ishay eastbray, andyay astcay ishay eyesyay owardstay ethay enithzay.

Othingnay asway oremay ommoncay, inyay osethay aysday, anthay otay interpretyay allyay eteoricmay
appearancesyay, andyay otheryay aturalnay enomenaphay, atthay occurredyay ithway esslay
egularityray anthay ethay iseray andyay etsay ofyay unsay andyay oonmay, asyay osay anymay
evelationsray omfray ayay upernaturalsay ourcesay. Usthay, ayay azingblay earspay, ayay ordsway
ofyay ameflay, ayay owbay, oryay ayay eafshay ofyay arrowsyay, eensay inyay ethay idnightmay yskay,
efiguredpray Indianyay arfareway. Estilencepay asway ownknay otay avehay eenbay orebodedfay
ybay ayay owershay ofyay imsoncray ightlay. Eway oubtday etherwhay anyyay arkedmay eventyay, orfay
oodgay oryay evilyay, everyay efellbay Ewnay Englandyay, omfray itsyay ettlementsay ownday otay
Evolutionaryray imestay, ofyay ichwhay ethay inhabitantsyay adhay otnay eenbay eviouslypray
arnedway ybay omesay ectaclespay ofyay isthay aturenay. Otnay eldomsay, ityay adhay eenbay eensay
ybay ultitudesmay. Ofteneryay, oweverhay, itsyay edibilitycray estedray onyay ethay aithfay
ofyay omesay onelylay eye-witnessyay, owhay eheldbay ethay onderway oughthray ethay oloredcay,
agnifyingmay, andyay istortingday ediummay ofyay ishay imaginationyay, andyay apedshay ityay
oremay istinctlyday inyay ishay after-thoughtyay. Ityay asway, indeedyay, ayay ajesticmay ideayay,
atthay ethay estinyday ofyay ationsnay ouldshay ebay evealedray, inyay esethay awfulyay
ieroglyphicshay, onyay ethay opecay ofyay eavenhay. Ayay ollscray osay ideway ightmay otnay ebay
eemedday ootay expansiveyay orfay Ovidencepray otay itewray ayay eople’spay oomday uponyay. Ethay
eliefbay asway ayay avoritefay oneyay ithway ouryay orefathersfay, asyay etokeningbay atthay
eirthay infantyay ommonwealthcay asway underyay ayay elestialcay uardianshipgay ofyay
eculiarpay intimacyyay andyay ictnessstray. Utbay atwhay allshay eway aysay, enwhay anyay
individualyay iscoversday ayay evelationray addressedyay otay imselfhay aloneyay, onyay ethay
amesay astvay eetshay ofyay ecordray! Inyay uchsay ayay asecay, ityay ouldcay onlyyay ebay ethay
ymptomsay ofyay ayay ighlyhay isorderedday entalmay atestay, enwhay ayay anmay, enderedray
orbidlymay elf-contemplativesay ybay onglay, intenseyay, andyay ecretsay ainpay, adhay
extendedyay ishay egotismyay overyay ethay olewhay expanseyay ofyay aturenay, untilyay ethay
irmamentfay itselfyay ouldshay appearyay onay oremay anthay ayay ittingfay agepay orfay ishay
oul’ssay istoryhay andyay atefay!

Eway imputeyay ityay, ereforethay, olelysay otay ethay iseaseday inyay ishay ownyay eyeyay andyay
earthay, atthay ethay inistermay, ookinglay upwardyay otay ethay enithzay, eheldbay erethay
ethay appearanceyay ofyay anyay immenseyay etter,—thelay etterlay A,—markedyay outyay inyay
ineslay ofyay ullday edray ightlay. Otnay utbay ethay eteormay aymay avehay ownshay itselfyay atyay
atthay ointpay, urningbay uskilyday oughthray ayay eilvay ofyay oudclay; utbay ithway onay uchsay
apeshay asyay ishay uiltygay imaginationyay avegay ityay; oryay, atyay eastlay, ithway osay ittlelay
efinitenessday, atthay another’syay uiltgay ightmay avehay eensay anotheryay ymbolsay inyay
ityay.

Erethay asway ayay ingularsay ircumstancecay atthay aracterizedchay Mray. Immesdale’sday
ychologicalpsay atestay, atyay isthay omentmay. Allyay ethay imetay atthay ehay azedgay upwardyay
otay ethay enithzay, ehay asway, everthelessnay, erfectlypay awareyay atthay ittlelay Earlpay
asway ointingpay erhay ingerfay owardstay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, owhay oodstay atyay
onay eatgray istanceday omfray ethay affoldscay. Ethay inistermay appearedyay otay eesay imhay,
ithway ethay amesay anceglay atthay iscernedday ethay iraculousmay etterlay. Otay ishay
eaturesfay, asyay otay allyay otheryay objectsyay, ethay eteoricmay ightlay impartedyay ayay ewnay
expressionyay; oryay ityay ightmay ellway ebay atthay ethay ysicianphay asway otnay arefulcay
enthay, asyay atyay allyay otheryay imestay, otay idehay ethay alevolencemay ithway ichwhay ehay
ookedlay uponyay ishay ictimvay. Ertainlycay, ifyay ethay eteormay indledkay upyay ethay yskay,
andyay isclosedday ethay earthyay, ithway anyay awfulnessyay atthay admonishedyay Esterhay
Ynnepray andyay ethay ergymanclay ofyay ethay ayday ofyay udgmentjay, enthay ightmay Ogerray
Illingworthchay avehay assedpay ithway emthay orfay ethay arch-fiendyay, andingstay erethay
ithway ayay ilesmay andyay owlscay, otay aimclay ishay ownyay. Osay ividvay asway ethay expressionyay,
oryay osay intenseyay ethay inister’smay erceptionpay ofyay ityay, atthay ityay eemedsay illstay otay
emainray aintedpay onyay ethay arknessday, afteryay ethay eteormay adhay anishedvay, ithway anyay
effectyay asyay ifyay ethay eetstray andyay allyay ingsthay elseyay ereway atyay onceyay annihilatedyay.

o“whay isyay atthay anmay, Esterhay?” aspedgay Mray. Immesdaleday, overcomeyay ithway
errortay. i“ay ivershay atyay imhay! Ostday outhay owknay ethay anmay? Iyay atehay imhay, Esterhay!”

Eshay ememberedray erhay oathyay, andyay asway ilentsay.

i“ay elltay eethay, ymay oulsay iversshay atyay imhay!” utteredmay ethay inistermay againyay.
o“whay isyay ehay? Owhay isyay ehay? Anstcay outhay oday othingnay orfay emay? Iyay avehay ayay amelessnay
orrorhay ofyay ethay anmay!”

inister“may,” aidsay ittlelay Earlpay, i“ay ancay elltay eethay owhay ehay isyay!”

uickly“qay, enthay, ildchay!” aidsay ethay inistermay, endingbay ishay earyay oseclay otay
erhay ipslay. uickly!—and“qay asyay owlay asyay outhay anstcay isperwhay.”

Earlpay umbledmay omethingsay intoyay ishay earyay, atthay oundedsay, indeedyay, ikelay umanhay
anguagelay, utbay asway onlyyay uchsay ibberishgay asyay ildrenchay aymay ebay eardhay amusingyay

ow“hay ewestknay outhay atthay Iyay asway erehay?” askedyay ethay inistermay, earfullyfay.

youyay.”

i“ay illway ogay omehay ithway youyay,” aidsay Mray. Immesdaleday.

Ithway ayay illchay espondencyday, ikelay oneyay awakingyay, allyay ervelessnay, omfray anyay
uglyyay eamdray, ehay yieldedyay imselfhay otay ethay ysicianphay, andyay asway edlay awayyay.

ichwhay asway eldhay otay ebay ethay ichestray andyay ostmay owerfulpay, andyay ethay ostmay

yes“ay, ityay eemssay otay ebay ymay oveglay, indeedyay!”

                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iiixay.

                        Anotheryay Iewvay Ofyay Esterhay.


Inyay erhay atelay ingularsay interviewyay ithway Mray. Immesdaleday, Esterhay Ynnepray asway
ockedshay atyay ethay onditioncay otay ichwhay eshay oundfay ethay ergymanclay educedray. Ishay
ervenay eemedsay absolutelyyay estroyedday. Ishay oralmay orcefay asway abasedyay intoyay
oremay anthay ildishchay eaknessway. Ityay ovelledgray elplesshay onyay ethay oundgray, evenyay
ilewhay ishay intellectualyay acultiesfay etainedray eirthay istinepray engthstray, oryay
adhay erhapspay acquiredyay ayay orbidmay energyyay, ichwhay iseaseday onlyyay ouldcay avehay
ivengay emthay. Ithway erhay owledgeknay ofyay ayay aintray ofyay ircumstancescay iddenhay omfray
allyay othersyay, eshay ouldcay eadilyray inferyay atthay, esidesbay ethay egitimatelay
actionyay ofyay ishay ownyay onsciencecay, ayay erribletay achinerymay adhay eenbay oughtbray otay
earbay, andyay asway illstay operatingyay, onyay Mray. Immesdale’sday ell-beingway andyay
eposeray. Owingknay atwhay isthay oorpay, allenfay anmay adhay onceyay eenbay, erhay olewhay
oulsay asway ovedmay ybay ethay udderingshay errortay ithway ichwhay ehay adhay appealedyay otay
er,—thehay outcastyay oman,—forway upportsay againstyay ishay instinctivelyyay
iscoveredday enemyyay. Eshay ecidedday, oreovermay, atthay ehay adhay ayay ightray otay erhay
utmostyay aidyay. Ittlelay accustomedyay, inyay erhay onglay eclusionsay omfray ocietysay, otay
easuremay erhay ideasyay ofyay ightray andyay ongwray ybay anyyay andardstay externalyay otay
erselfhay, Esterhay aw—orsay eemedsay otay ee—thatsay erethay aylay ayay esponsibilityray
uponyay erhay, inyay eferenceray otay ethay ergymanclay, ichwhay eshay owedyay otay onay otheryay,
ornay otay ethay olewhay orldway esidesbay. Ethay inkslay atthay unitedyay erhay otay ethay estray
ofyay umanhay ind—linkskay ofyay owersflay, oryay ilksay, oryay oldgay, oryay ateverwhay ethay
aterial—hadmay allyay eenbay okenbray. Erehay asway ethay ironyay inklay ofyay utualmay imecray,
ichwhay eithernay ehay ornay eshay ouldcay eakbray. Ikelay allyay otheryay iestay, ityay oughtbray
alongyay ithway ityay itsyay obligationsyay.

Esterhay Ynnepray idday otnay ownay occupyyay eciselypray ethay amesay ositionpay inyay ichwhay
eway eheldbay erhay uringday ethay earlieryay eriodspay ofyay erhay ignominyyay. Yearsyay adhay
omecay andyay onegay. Earlpay asway ownay evensay yearsyay oldyay. Erhay othermay, ithway ethay
arletscay etterlay onyay erhay eastbray, itteringglay inyay itsyay antasticfay embroideryyay,
adhay onglay eenbay ayay amiliarfay objectyay otay ethay owns-peopletay. Asyay isyay aptyay otay ebay
ethay asecay enwhay ayay ersonpay andsstay outyay inyay anyyay ominencepray eforebay ethay
ommunitycay, andyay, atyay ethay amesay imetay, interferesyay eithernay ithway ublicpay ornay
individualyay interestsyay andyay onveniencecay, ayay eciesspay ofyay eneralgay egardray adhay
ultimatelyyay owngray upyay inyay eferenceray otay Esterhay Ynnepray. Ityay isyay otay ethay editcray
ofyay umanhay aturenay, atthay, exceptyay erewhay itsyay elfishnesssay isyay oughtbray intoyay
ayplay, ityay oveslay oremay eadilyray anthay ityay ateshay. Atredhay, ybay ayay adualgray andyay
uietqay ocesspray, illway evenyay ebay ansformedtray otay ovelay, unlessyay ethay angechay ebay
impededyay ybay ayay ontinuallycay ewnay irritationyay ofyay ethay originalyay eelingfay ofyay
ostilityhay. Inyay isthay attermay ofyay Esterhay Ynnepray, erethay asway eithernay
irritationyay ornay irksomenessyay. Eshay evernay attledbay ithway ethay ublicpay, utbay
ubmittedsay, uncomplaininglyyay, otay itsyay orstway usageyay; eshay ademay onay aimclay uponyay
ityay, inyay equitalray orfay atwhay eshay ufferedsay; eshay idday otnay eighway uponyay itsyay
ympathiessay. Enthay, alsoyay, ethay amelessblay uritypay ofyay erhay ifelay uringday allyay
esethay yearsyay inyay ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay etsay apartyay otay infamyyay, asway eckonedray
argelylay inyay erhay avorfay. Ithway othingnay ownay otay oselay, inyay ethay ightsay ofyay
ankindmay, andyay ithway onay opehay, andyay eeminglysay onay ishway, ofyay aininggay anythingyay,
ityay ouldcay onlyyay ebay ayay enuinegay egardray orfay irtuevay atthay adhay oughtbray ackbay ethay
oorpay andererway otay itsyay athspay.

illustration[ay: Esterhay inyay ethay Ousehay ofyay Ourningmay]

Ityay asway erceivedpay, ootay, atthay ilewhay Esterhay evernay utpay orwardfay evenyay ethay
umblesthay itletay otay areshay inyay ethay orld’sway ivileges,—furtherpray anthay otay
eathebray ethay ommoncay airyay, andyay earnyay ailyday eadbray orfay ittlelay Earlpay andyay
erselfhay ybay ethay aithfulfay aborlay ofyay erhay ands,—shehay asway uickqay otay
acknowledgeyay erhay isterhoodsay ithway ethay aceray ofyay anmay, eneverwhay enefitsbay
ereway otay ebay onferredcay. Onenay osay eadyray asyay eshay otay ivegay ofyay erhay ittlelay
ubstancesay otay everyyay emandday ofyay overtypay; evenyay oughthay ethay itter-heartedbay
auperpay ewthray ackbay ayay ibegay inyay equitalray ofyay ethay oodfay oughtbray egularlyray otay
ishay oorday, oryay ethay armentsgay oughtwray orfay imhay ybay ethay ingersfay atthay ouldcay
avehay embroideredyay ayay onarch’smay oberay. Onenay osay elf-devotedsay asyay Esterhay,
enwhay estilencepay alkedstay oughthray ethay owntay. Inyay allyay easonssay ofyay alamitycay,
indeedyay, etherwhay eneralgay oryay ofyay individualsyay, ethay outcastyay ofyay ocietysay atyay
onceyay oundfay erhay aceplay. Eshay amecay, otnay asyay ayay uestgay, utbay asyay ayay ightfulray
inmateyay, intoyay ethay ouseholdhay atthay asway arkenedday ybay oubletray; asyay ifyay itsyay
oomyglay ilighttway ereway ayay ediummay inyay ichwhay eshay asway entitledyay otay oldhay
intercourseyay ithway erhay ellow-creaturesfay. Erethay immeredglay ethay embroideredyay
etterlay, ithway omfortcay inyay itsyay unearthlyyay ayray. Elsewhereyay ethay okentay ofyay insay,
ityay asway ethay apertay ofyay ethay ick-chambersay. Ityay adhay evenyay ownthray itsyay eamglay, inyay
ethay ufferer’ssay ardhay extremityyay, acrossyay ethay ergevay ofyay imetay. Ityay adhay ownshay
imhay erewhay otay etsay ishay ootfay, ilewhay ethay ightlay ofyay earthyay asway astfay ecomingbay
imday, andyay ereyay ethay ightlay ofyay uturityfay ouldcay eachray imhay. Inyay uchsay
emergenciesyay, Ester’shay aturenay owedshay itselfyay armway andyay ichray; ayay
ell-springway ofyay umanhay endernesstay, unfailingyay otay everyyay ealray emandday, andyay
inexhaustibleyay ybay ethay argestlay. Erhay eastbray, ithway itsyay adgebay ofyay ameshay, asway
utbay ethay oftersay illowpay orfay ethay eadhay atthay eedednay oneyay. Eshay asway
elf-ordainedsay ayay Istersay ofyay Ercymay; oryay, eway aymay atherray aysay, ethay orld’sway
eavyhay andhay adhay osay ordainedyay erhay, enwhay eithernay ethay orldway ornay eshay ookedlay
orwardfay otay isthay esultray. Ethay etterlay asway ethay ymbolsay ofyay erhay allingcay. Uchsay
elpfulnesshay asway oundfay inyay er,—sohay uchmay owerpay otay oday, andyay owerpay otay
ympathize,—thatsay anymay eoplepay efusedray otay interpretyay ethay arletscay Ayay ybay
itsyay originalyay ignificationsay. Eythay aidsay atthay ityay eantmay Ableyay; osay ongstray
asway Esterhay Ynnepray, ithway ayay oman’sway engthstray.

Ityay asway onlyyay ethay arkenedday ousehay atthay ouldcay ontaincay erhay. Enwhay unshinesay
amecay againyay, eshay asway otnay erethay. Erhay adowshay adhay adedfay acrossyay ethay
esholdthray. Ethay elpfulhay inmateyay adhay epartedday, ithoutway oneyay ackwardbay
anceglay otay athergay upyay ethay eedmay ofyay atitudegray, ifyay anyyay ereway inyay ethay eartshay
ofyay osethay omwhay eshay adhay ervedsay osay ealouslyzay. Eetingmay emthay inyay ethay
eetstray, eshay evernay aisedray erhay eadhay otay eceiveray eirthay eetinggray. Ifyay eythay
ereway esoluteray otay accostyay erhay, eshay aidlay erhay ingerfay onyay ethay arletscay
etterlay, andyay assedpay onyay. Isthay ightmay ebay idepray, utbay asway osay ikelay umilityhay,
atthay ityay oducedpray allyay ethay ofteningsay influenceyay ofyay ethay atterlay ualityqay onyay
ethay ublicpay indmay. Ethay ublicpay isyay espoticday inyay itsyay empertay; ityay isyay apablecay
ofyay enyingday ommoncay usticejay, enwhay ootay enuouslystray emandedday asyay ayay ightray;
utbay uiteqay asyay equentlyfray ityay awardsyay oremay anthay usticejay, enwhay ethay appealyay
isyay ademay, asyay espotsday ovelay otay avehay ityay ademay, entirelyyay otay itsyay enerositygay.
Interpretingyay Esterhay Ynne’spray eportmentday asyay anyay appealyay ofyay isthay aturenay,
ocietysay asway inclinedyay otay owshay itsyay ormerfay ictimvay ayay oremay enignbay
ountenancecay anthay eshay aredcay otay ebay avoredfay ithway, oryay, erchancepay, anthay eshay
eservedday.

Ethay ulersray, andyay ethay iseway andyay earnedlay enmay ofyay ethay ommunitycay, ereway ongerlay
inyay acknowledgingyay ethay influenceyay ofyay Ester’shay oodgay ualitiesqay anthay ethay
eoplepay. Ethay ejudicespray ichwhay eythay aredshay inyay ommoncay ithway ethay atterlay
ereway ortifiedfay inyay emselvesthay ybay anyay ironyay ameworkfray ofyay easoningray, atthay
ademay ityay ayay arfay oughertay aborlay otay expelyay emthay. Ayday ybay ayday, everthelessnay,
eirthay oursay andyay igidray inkleswray ereway elaxingray intoyay omethingsay ichwhay, inyay
ethay ueday oursecay ofyay yearsyay, ightmay owgray otay ebay anyay expressionyay ofyay almostyay
enevolencebay. Usthay ityay asway ithway ethay enmay ofyay ankray, onyay omwhay eirthay eminentyay
ositionpay imposedyay ethay uardianshipgay ofyay ethay ublicpay oralsmay. Individualsyay inyay
ivatepray ifelay, eanwhilemay, adhay uiteqay orgivenfay Esterhay Ynnepray orfay erhay
ailtyfray; aynay, oremay, eythay adhay egunbay otay ooklay uponyay ethay arletscay etterlay asyay
ethay okentay, otnay ofyay atthay oneyay insay, orfay ichwhay eshay adhay ornebay osay onglay andyay
earydray ayay enancepay, utbay ofyay erhay anymay oodgay eedsday incesay. o“day youyay eesay atthay
omanway ithway ethay embroideredyay adgebay?” eythay ouldway aysay otay angersstray. it“ay isyay
ouryay Ester,—thehay own’stay ownyay Esterhay, owhay isyay osay indkay otay ethay oorpay, osay
elpfulhay otay ethay icksay, osay omfortablecay otay ethay afflictedyay!” Enthay, ityay isyay
uetray, ethay opensitypray ofyay umanhay aturenay otay elltay ethay eryvay orstway ofyay itselfyay,
enwhay embodiedyay inyay ethay ersonpay ofyay anotheryay, ouldway onstraincay emthay otay
isperwhay ethay ackblay andalscay ofyay ygonebay yearsyay. Ityay asway onenay ethay esslay ayay
actfay, oweverhay, atthay, inyay ethay eyesyay ofyay ethay eryvay enmay owhay okespay usthay, ethay
arletscay etterlay adhay ethay effectyay ofyay ethay osscray onyay ayay un’snay osombay. Ityay
impartedyay otay ethay earerway ayay indkay ofyay acrednesssay, ichwhay enabledyay erhay otay alkway
ecurelysay amidyay allyay erilpay. Adhay eshay allenfay amongyay ievesthay, ityay ouldway avehay
eptkay erhay afesay. Ityay asway eportedray, andyay elievedbay ybay anymay, atthay anyay Indianyay
adhay awndray ishay arrowyay againstyay ethay adgebay, andyay atthay ethay issilemay uckstray ityay,
utbay ellfay armlesshay otay ethay oundgray.

Ethay effectyay ofyay ethay ymbol—orsay, atherray, ofyay ethay ositionpay inyay espectray otay
ocietysay atthay asway indicatedyay ybay it—onyay ethay indmay ofyay Esterhay Ynnepray
erselfhay, asway owerfulpay andyay eculiarpay. Allyay ethay ightlay andyay acefulgray oliagefay
ofyay erhay aracterchay adhay eenbay itheredway upyay ybay isthay ed-hotray andbray, andyay adhay
onglay agoyay allenfay awayyay, eavinglay ayay arebay andyay arshhay outlineyay, ichwhay ightmay
avehay eenbay epulsiveray, adhay eshay ossessedpay iendsfray oryay ompanionscay otay ebay
epelledray ybay ityay. Evenyay ethay attractivenessyay ofyay erhay ersonpay adhay undergoneyay ayay
imilarsay angechay. Ityay ightmay ebay artlypay owingyay otay ethay udiedstay austerityyay ofyay
erhay essdray, andyay artlypay otay ethay acklay ofyay emonstrationday inyay erhay annersmay. Ityay
asway ayay adsay ansformationtray, ootay, atthay erhay ichray andyay uxuriantlay airhay adhay
eitheryay eenbay utcay offyay, oryay asway osay ompletelycay iddenhay ybay ayay apcay, atthay otnay ayay
iningshay ocklay ofyay ityay everyay onceyay ushedgay intoyay ethay unshinesay. Ityay asway ueday inyay
artpay otay allyay esethay ausescay, utbay illstay oremay otay omethingsay elseyay, atthay erethay
eemedsay otay ebay onay ongerlay anythingyay inyay Ester’shay acefay orfay Ovelay otay elldway
uponyay; othingnay inyay Ester’shay ormfay, oughthay ajesticmay andyay atue-likestay, atthay
Assionpay ouldway everyay eamdray ofyay aspingclay inyay itsyay embraceyay; othingnay inyay
Ester’shay osombay, otay akemay ityay everyay againyay ethay illowpay ofyay Affectionyay. Omesay
attributeyay adhay epartedday omfray erhay, ethay ermanencepay ofyay ichwhay adhay eenbay
essentialyay otay eepkay erhay ayay omanway. Uchsay isyay equentlyfray ethay atefay, andyay uchsay
ethay ernstay evelopmentday, ofyay ethay emininefay aracterchay andyay ersonpay, enwhay ethay
omanway ashay encounteredyay, andyay ivedlay oughthray, anyay experienceyay ofyay eculiarpay
everitysay. Ifyay eshay ebay allyay endernesstay, eshay illway ieday. Ifyay eshay urvivesay, ethay
endernesstay illway eitheryay ebay ushedcray outyay ofyay erhay, or—andyay ethay outwardyay
emblancesay isyay ethay ame—crushedsay osay eeplyday intoyay erhay earthay atthay ityay ancay
evernay owshay itselfyay oremay. Ethay atterlay isyay erhapspay ethay uesttray eorythay. Eshay
owhay ashay onceyay eenbay omanway, andyay easedcay otay ebay osay, ightmay atyay anyyay omentmay
ecomebay ayay omanway againyay ifyay erethay ereway onlyyay ethay agicmay ouchtay otay effectyay ethay
ansfigurationtray. Eway allshay eesay etherwhay Esterhay Ynnepray ereway everyay
afterwardsyay osay ouchedtay, andyay osay ansfiguredtray.

Uchmay ofyay ethay arblemay oldnesscay ofyay Ester’shay impressionyay asway otay ebay
attributedyay otay ethay ircumstancecay, atthay erhay ifelay adhay urnedtay, inyay ayay eatgray
easuremay, omfray assionpay andyay eelingfay, otay oughtthay. Andingstay aloneyay inyay ethay
orld,—aloneway, asyay otay anyyay ependenceday onyay ocietysay, andyay ithway ittlelay Earlpay
otay ebay uidedgay andyay otected,—alonepray, andyay opelesshay ofyay etrievingray erhay
ositionpay, evenyay adhay eshay otnay ornedscay otay onsidercay ityay esirable,—sheday astcay
awayyay ethay agmentsfray ofyay ayay okenbray ainchay. Ethay orld’sway awlay asway onay awlay orfay
erhay indmay. Ityay asway anyay ageyay inyay ichwhay ethay umanhay intellectyay, ewlynay
emancipatedyay, adhay akentay ayay oremay activeyay andyay ayay iderway angeray anthay orfay anymay
enturiescay eforebay. Enmay ofyay ethay ordsway adhay overthrownyay oblesnay andyay ingskay.
Enmay olderbay anthay esethay adhay overthrownyay andyay earranged—notray actuallyyay, utbay
ithinway ethay eresphay ofyay eorythay, ichwhay asway eirthay ostmay ealray abode—theyay
olewhay ystemsay ofyay ancientyay ejudicepray, erewithwhay asway inkedlay uchmay ofyay
ancientyay inciplepray. Esterhay Ynnepray imbibedyay isthay iritspay. Eshay assumedyay ayay
eedomfray ofyay eculationspay, enthay ommoncay enoughyay onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay
Atlanticyay, utbay ichwhay ouryay orefathersfay, adhay eythay ownknay ityay, ouldway avehay
eldhay otay ebay ayay eadlierday imecray anthay atthay igmatizedstay ybay ethay arletscay
etterlay. Inyay erhay onesomelay ottagecay, ybay ethay ea-shoresay, oughtsthay isitedvay
erhay, uchsay asyay aredday otay enteryay onay otheryay ellingdway inyay Ewnay Englandyay; adowyshay
uestsgay, atthay ouldway avehay eenbay asyay erilouspay asyay emonsday otay eirthay
entertaineryay, ouldcay eythay avehay eenbay eensay osay uchmay asyay ockingknay atyay erhay
oorday.

Ityay isyay emarkableray, atthay ersonspay owhay eculatespay ethay ostmay oldlybay oftenyay
onformcay ithway ethay ostmay erfectpay uietudeqay otay ethay externalyay egulationsray ofyay
ocietysay. Ethay oughtthay ufficessay emthay, ithoutway investingyay itselfyay inyay ethay
eshflay andyay oodblay ofyay actionyay. Osay ityay eemedsay otay ebay ithway Esterhay. Yetyay, adhay
ittlelay Earlpay evernay omecay otay erhay omfray ethay iritualspay orldway, ityay ightmay avehay
eenbay arfay otherwiseyay. Enthay, eshay ightmay avehay omecay ownday otay usyay inyay istoryhay,
andhay inyay andhay ithway Annyay Utchinsonhay, asyay ethay oundressfay ofyay ayay eligiousray
ectsay. Eshay ightmay, inyay oneyay ofyay erhay asesphay, avehay eenbay ayay ophetesspray. Eshay
ightmay, andyay otnay improbablyyay ouldway, avehay ufferedsay eathday omfray ethay ernstay
ibunalstray ofyay ethay eriodpay, orfay attemptingyay otay undermineyay ethay oundationsfay
ofyay ethay Uritanpay establishmentyay. Utbay, inyay ethay educationyay ofyay erhay ildchay, ethay
other’smay enthusiasmyay ofyay oughtthay adhay omethingsay otay eakwray itselfyay uponyay.
Ovidencepray, inyay ethay ersonpay ofyay isthay ittlelay irlgay, adhay assignedyay otay
Ester’shay argechay ethay ermgay andyay ossomblay ofyay omanhoodway, otay ebay erishedchay andyay
evelopedday amidyay ayay osthay ofyay ifficultiesday. Everythingyay asway againstyay erhay. Ethay
orldway asway ostilehay. Ethay ild’schay ownyay aturenay adhay omethingsay ongwray inyay ityay,
ichwhay ontinuallycay etokenedbay atthay eshay adhay eenbay ornbay amiss,—theyay
effluenceyay ofyay erhay other’smay awlesslay assion,—andpay oftenyay impelledyay Esterhay
otay askyay, inyay itternessbay ofyay earthay, etherwhay ityay ereway orfay illyay oryay oodgay atthay
ethay oorpay ittlelay eaturecray adhay eenbay ornbay atyay allyay.

Indeedyay, ethay amesay arkday uestionqay oftenyay oseray intoyay erhay indmay, ithway
eferenceray otay ethay olewhay aceray ofyay omanhoodway. Asway existenceyay orthway
acceptingyay, evenyay otay ethay appiesthay amongyay emthay? Asyay oncernedcay erhay ownyay
individualyay existenceyay, eshay adhay onglay agoyay ecidedday inyay ethay egativenay, andyay
ismissedday ethay ointpay asyay ettledsay. Ayay endencytay otay eculationspay, oughthay ityay
aymay eepkay omanway uietqay, asyay ityay oesday anmay, yetyay akesmay erhay adsay. Eshay iscernsday,
ityay aymay ebay, uchsay ayay opelesshay asktay eforebay erhay. Asyay ayay irstfay epstay, ethay olewhay
ystemsay ofyay ocietysay isyay otay ebay orntay ownday, andyay uiltbay upyay anewyay. Enthay, ethay
eryvay aturenay ofyay ethay oppositeyay exsay, oryay itsyay onglay ereditaryhay abithay, ichwhay
ashay ecomebay ikelay aturenay, isyay otay ebay essentiallyyay odifiedmay, eforebay omanway
ancay ebay allowedyay otay assumeyay atwhay eemssay ayay airfay andyay uitablesay ositionpay.
Inallyfay, allyay otheryay ifficultiesday eingbay obviatedyay, omanway annotcay aketay
advantageyay ofyay esethay eliminarypray eformsray, untilyay eshay erselfhay allshay avehay
undergoneyay ayay illstay ightiermay angechay; inyay ichwhay, erhapspay, ethay etherealyay
essenceyay, ereinwhay eshay ashay erhay uesttray ifelay, illway ebay oundfay otay avehay
evaporatedyay. Ayay omanway evernay overcomesyay esethay oblemspray ybay anyyay exerciseyay ofyay
oughtthay. Eythay areyay otnay otay ebay olvedsay, oryay onlyyay inyay oneyay ayway. Ifyay erhay earthay
ancechay otay omecay uppermostyay, eythay anishvay. Usthay, Esterhay Ynnepray, osewhay
earthay adhay ostlay itsyay egularray andyay ealthyhay obthray, anderedway ithoutway ayay ewclay
inyay ethay arkday abyrinthlay ofyay indmay; ownay urnedtay asideyay ybay anyay insurmountableyay
ecipicepray; ownay artingstay ackbay omfray ayay eepday asmchay. Erethay asway ildway andyay
astlyghay eneryscay allyay aroundyay erhay, andyay ayay omehay andyay omfortcay owherenay. Atyay
imestay, ayay earfulfay oubtday ovestray otay ossesspay erhay oulsay, etherwhay ityay ereway otnay
etterbay otay endsay Earlpay atyay onceyay otay eavenhay, andyay ogay erselfhay otay uchsay
uturityfay asyay Eternalyay Usticejay ouldshay ovidepray.

Ethay arletscay etterlay adhay otnay oneday itsyay officeyay.

Ownay, oweverhay, erhay interviewyay ithway ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, onyay ethay
ightnay ofyay ishay igilvay, adhay ivengay erhay ayay ewnay emethay ofyay eflectionray, andyay eldhay
upyay otay erhay anyay objectyay atthay appearedyay orthyway ofyay anyyay exertionyay andyay acrificesay
orfay itsyay attainmentyay. Eshay adhay itnessedway ethay intenseyay iserymay eneathbay
ichwhay ethay inistermay uggledstray, oryay, otay eakspay oremay accuratelyyay, adhay easedcay
otay ugglestray. Eshay awsay atthay ehay oodstay onyay ethay ergevay ofyay unacylay, ifyay ehay adhay
otnay alreadyyay eppedstay acrossyay ityay. Ityay asway impossibleyay otay oubtday, atthay,
ateverwhay ainfulpay efficacyyay erethay ightmay ebay inyay ethay ecretsay ingstay ofyay
emorseray, ayay eadlierday enomvay adhay eenbay infusedyay intoyay ityay ybay ethay andhay atthay
offeredpray eliefray. Ayay ecretsay enemyyay adhay eenbay ontinuallycay ybay ishay idesay,
underyay ethay emblancesay ofyay ayay iendfray andyay elperhay, andyay adhay availedyay imselfhay ofyay
ethay opportunitiesyay usthay affordedyay orfay amperingtay ithway ethay elicateday
ingsspray ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday aturenay. Esterhay ouldcay otnay utbay askyay erselfhay,
etherwhay erethay adhay otnay originallyyay eenbay ayay efectday ofyay uthtray, ouragecay, andyay
oyaltylay, onyay erhay ownyay artpay, inyay allowingyay ethay inistermay otay ebay ownthray intoyay ayay
ositionpay erewhay osay uchmay evilyay asway otay ebay orebodedfay, andyay othingnay
auspiciousyay otay ebay opedhay. Erhay onlyyay ustificationjay aylay inyay ethay actfay, atthay
eshay adhay eenbay ableyay otay iscernday onay ethodmay ofyay escuingray imhay omfray ayay ackerblay
uinray anthay adhay overwhelmedyay erselfhay, exceptyay ybay acquiescingyay inyay Ogerray
Illingworth’schay emeschay ofyay isguiseday. Underyay atthay impulseyay, eshay adhay ademay
erhay oicechay, andyay adhay osenchay, asyay ityay ownay appearedyay, ethay oremay etchedwray
alternativeyay ofyay ethay otway. Eshay eterminedday otay edeemray erhay erroryay, osay arfay asyay
ityay ightmay yetyay ebay ossiblepay. Engthenedstray ybay yearsyay ofyay ardhay andyay olemnsay
ialtray, eshay eltfay erselfhay onay ongerlay osay inadequateyay otay opecay ithway Ogerray
Illingworthchay asyay onyay atthay ightnay, abasedyay ybay insay, andyay alfhay addenedmay ybay
ethay ignominyyay atthay asway illstay ewnay, enwhay eythay adhay alkedtay ogethertay inyay ethay
ison-chamberpray. Eshay adhay imbedclay erhay ayway, incesay enthay, otay ayay igherhay
ointpay. Ethay oldyay anmay, onyay ethay otheryay andhay, adhay oughtbray imselfhay earernay otay
erhay evellay, oryay erhapspay elowbay ityay, ybay ethay evengeray ichwhay ehay adhay oopedstay
orfay.

Inyay inefay, Esterhay Ynnepray esolvedray otay eetmay erhay ormerfay usbandhay, andyay oday
atwhay ightmay ebay inyay erhay owerpay orfay ethay escueray ofyay ethay ictimvay onyay omwhay ehay
adhay osay evidentlyyay etsay ishay ipegray. Ethay occasionyay asway otnay onglay otay eeksay. Oneyay
afternoonyay, alkingway ithway Earlpay inyay ayay etiredray artpay ofyay ethay eninsulapay, eshay
eheldbay ethay oldyay ysicianphay, ithway ayay asketbay onyay oneyay armyay, andyay ayay affstay inyay ethay
otheryay andhay, oopingstay alongyay ethay oundgray, inyay uestqay ofyay ootsray andyay erbshay otay
oncoctcay ishay edicinesmay ithalway.
