                            illustration[ay]

                                 Ivxay.

                       Esterhay Andyay Ethay Ysicianphay.


Esterhay adebay ittlelay Earlpay unray ownday otay ethay arginmay ofyay ethay aterway, andyay ayplay
ithway ethay ellsshay andyay angledtay ea-weedsay, untilyay eshay ouldshay avehay alkedtay
awhileyay ithway yonderyay atherergay ofyay erbshay. Osay ethay ildchay ewflay awayyay ikelay ayay
irdbay, andyay, akingmay arebay erhay allsmay itewhay eetfay, entway atteringpay alongyay ethay
oistmay arginmay ofyay ethay easay. Erehay andyay erethay eshay amecay otay ayay ullfay opstay, andyay
eepedpay uriouslycay intoyay ayay oolpay, eftlay ybay ethay etiringray idetay asyay ayay irrormay
orfay Earlpay otay eesay erhay acefay inyay. Orthfay eepedpay atyay erhay, outyay ofyay ethay oolpay,
ithway arkday, isteningglay urlscay aroundyay erhay eadhay, andyay anyay elf-smileyay inyay erhay
eyesyay, ethay imageyay ofyay ayay ittlelay aidmay, omwhay Earlpay, avinghay onay otheryay
aymateplay, invitedyay otay aketay erhay andhay, andyay unray ayay aceray ithway erhay. Utbay ethay
isionaryvay ittlelay aidmay, onyay erhay artpay, eckonedbay ikewiselay, asyay ifyay otay
ay,—“thissay isyay ayay etterbay aceplay! Omecay outhay intoyay ethay oolpay!” Andyay Earlpay,
eppingstay inyay, id-legmay eepday, eheldbay erhay ownyay itewhay eetfay atyay ethay ottombay;
ilewhay, outyay ofyay ayay illstay owerlay epthday, amecay ethay eamglay ofyay ayay indkay ofyay
agmentaryfray ilesmay, oatingflay otay andyay ofray inyay ethay agitatedyay aterway.

Eanwhilemay, erhay othermay adhay accostedyay ethay ysicianphay.

i“ay ouldway eakspay ayay ordway ithway youyay,” aidsay e,—“ashay ordway atthay oncernscay usyay
uchmay.”

aha“ay! andyay isyay ityay Istressmay Esterhay atthay ashay ayay ordway orfay oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay?” answeredyay ehay, aisingray imselfhay omfray ishay oopingstay
osturepay. ith“way allyay ymay earthay! Ywhay, Istressmay, Iyay earhay oodgay idingstay ofyay youyay
onyay allyay andshay! Onay ongerlay agoyay anthay yester-eveyay, ayay agistratemay, ayay iseway andyay
odlygay anmay, asway iscoursingday ofyay youryay affairsyay, Istressmay Esterhay, andyay
isperedwhay emay atthay erethay adhay eenbay uestionqay oncerningcay youyay inyay ethay
ouncilcay. Ityay asway ebatedday etherwhay oryay onay, ithway afetysay otay ethay ommoncay ealway,
yonderyay arletscay etterlay ightmay ebay akentay offyay youryay osombay. Onyay ymay ifelay,
Esterhay, Iyay ademay ymay entreatyyay otay ethay orshipfulway agistratemay atthay ityay ightmay
ebay oneday orthwithfay!”

it“ay ieslay otnay inyay ethay easureplay ofyay ethay agistratesmay otay aketay offyay isthay
adgebay,” almlycay epliedray Esterhay. ere“way Iyay orthyway otay ebay uitqay ofyay ityay, ityay
ouldway allfay awayyay ofyay itsyay ownyay aturenay, oryay ebay ansformedtray intoyay omethingsay
atthay ouldshay eakspay ayay ifferentday urportpay.”

ay“nay, enthay, earway ityay, ifyay ityay uitsay youyay etterbay,” ejoinedray ehay. a“ay omanway
ustmay eedsnay ollowfay erhay ownyay ancyfay, ouchingtay ethay adornmentyay ofyay erhay ersonpay.
Ethay etterlay isyay aylygay embroideredyay, andyay owsshay ightray avelybray onyay youryay
osombay!”

Allyay isthay ilewhay, Esterhay adhay eenbay ookinglay eadilystay atyay ethay oldyay anmay, andyay
asway ockedshay, asyay ellway asyay onder-smittenway, otay iscernday atwhay ayay angechay adhay
eenbay oughtwray uponyay imhay ithinway ethay astpay evensay yearsyay. Ityay asway otnay osay uchmay
atthay ehay adhay owngray olderyay; orfay oughthay ethay acestray ofyay advancingyay ifelay ereway
isiblevay, ehay orebay ishay ageyay ellway, andyay eemedsay otay etainray ayay iryway igorvay andyay
alertnessyay. Utbay ethay ormerfay aspectyay ofyay anyay intellectualyay andyay udiousstay anmay,
almcay andyay uietqay, ichwhay asway atwhay eshay estbay ememberedray inyay imhay, adhay
altogetheryay anishedvay, andyay eenbay ucceededsay ybay anyay eageryay, earchingsay,
almostyay iercefay, yetyay arefullycay uardedgay ooklay. Ityay eemedsay otay ebay ishay ishway
andyay urposepay otay askmay isthay expressionyay ithway ayay ilesmay; utbay ethay atterlay
ayedplay imhay alsefay, andyay ickeredflay overyay ishay isagevay osay erisivelyday, atthay
ethay ectatorspay ouldcay eesay ishay acknessblay allyay ethay etterbay orfay ityay. Everyay andyay
anonyay, ootay, erethay amecay ayay areglay ofyay edray ightlay outyay ofyay ishay eyesyay; asyay ifyay ethay
oldyay an’smay oulsay ereway onyay irefay, andyay eptkay onyay oulderingsmay uskilyday ithinway
ishay eastbray, untilyay, ybay omesay asualcay uffpay ofyay assionpay, ityay asway ownblay intoyay ayay
omentarymay ameflay. Isthay ehay epressedray, asyay eedilyspay asyay ossiblepay, andyay
ovestray otay ooklay asyay ifyay othingnay ofyay ethay indkay adhay appenedhay.

Inyay ayay ordway, oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay asway ayay ikingstray evidenceyay ofyay an’smay
acultyfay ofyay ansformingtray imselfhay intoyay ayay evilday, ifyay ehay illway onlyyay, orfay ayay
easonableray acespay ofyay imetay, undertakeyay ayay evil’sday officeyay. Isthay unhappyyay
ersonpay adhay effectedyay uchsay ayay ansformationtray, ybay evotingday imselfhay, orfay
evensay yearsyay, otay ethay onstantcay analysisyay ofyay ayay earthay ullfay ofyay orturetay, andyay
erivingday ishay enjoymentyay encethay, andyay addingyay uelfay otay osethay ieryfay orturestay
ichwhay ehay analyzedyay andyay oatedglay overyay.

Ethay arletscay etterlay urnedbay onyay Esterhay Ynne’spray osombay. Erehay asway anotheryay
uinray, ethay esponsibilityray ofyay ichwhay amecay artlypay omehay otay erhay.

at“whay eesay youyay inyay ymay acefay,” askedyay ethay ysicianphay, at“thay youyay ooklay atyay ityay
osay earnestlyyay?”

omething“say atthay ouldway akemay emay eepway, ifyay erethay ereway anyyay earstay itterbay
enoughyay orfay ityay,” answeredyay eshay. ut“bay etlay ityay asspay! Ityay isyay ofyay yonderyay
iserablemay anmay atthay Iyay ouldway eakspay.”

and“ay atwhay ofyay imhay?” iedcray Ogerray Illingworthchay, eagerlyyay, asyay ifyay ehay ovedlay
ethay opictay, andyay ereway adglay ofyay anyay opportunityyay otay iscussday ityay ithway ethay onlyyay
ersonpay ofyay omwhay ehay ouldcay akemay ayay onfidantcay. ot“nay otay idehay ethay uthtray,
Istressmay Esterhay, ymay oughtsthay appenhay ustjay ownay otay ebay usybay ithway ethay
entlemangay. Osay eakspay eelyfray; andyay Iyay illway akemay answeryay.”

en“whay eway astlay akespay ogethertay,” aidsay Esterhay, ow“nay evensay yearsyay agoyay, ityay
asway youryay easureplay otay extortyay ayay omisepray ofyay ecrecysay, asyay ouchingtay ethay
ormerfay elationray etwixtbay yourselfyay andyay emay. Asyay ethay ifelay andyay oodgay amefay ofyay
yonderyay anmay ereway inyay youryay andshay, erethay eemedsay onay oicechay otay emay, avesay otay
ebay ilentsay, inyay accordanceyay ithway youryay ehestbay. Yetyay ityay asway otnay ithoutway
eavyhay isgivingsmay atthay Iyay usthay oundbay yselfmay; orfay, avinghay astcay offyay allyay
utyday owardstay otheryay umanhay eingsbay, erethay emainedray ayay utyday owardstay imhay;
andyay omethingsay isperedwhay emay atthay Iyay asway etrayingbay ityay, inyay edgingplay yselfmay
otay eepkay youryay ounselcay. Incesay atthay ayday, onay anmay isyay osay earnay otay imhay asyay youyay.
Youyay eadtray ehindbay ishay everyyay ootstepfay. Youyay areyay esidebay imhay, eepingslay andyay
akingway. Youyay earchsay ishay oughtsthay. Youyay urrowbay andyay ankleray inyay ishay earthay!
Youryay utchclay isyay onyay ishay ifelay, andyay youyay ausecay imhay otay ieday ailyday ayay ivinglay
eathday; andyay illstay ehay owsknay youyay otnay. Inyay ermittingpay isthay, Iyay avehay urelysay
actedyay ayay alsefay artpay ybay ethay onlyyay anmay otay omwhay ethay owerpay asway eftlay emay otay ebay
uetray!”

at“whay oicechay adhay youyay?” askedyay Ogerray Illingworthchay. y“may ingerfay, ointedpay
atyay isthay anmay, ouldway avehay urledhay imhay omfray ishay ulpitpay intoyay ayay
ungeon,—thenceday, eradventurepay, otay ethay allowsgay!”

it“ay adhay eenbay etterbay osay!” aidsay Esterhay Ynnepray.

at“whay evilyay avehay Iyay oneday ethay anmay?” askedyay Ogerray Illingworthchay againyay. i“ay
elltay eethay, Esterhay Ynnepray, ethay ichestray eefay atthay everyay ysicianphay earnedyay
omfray onarchmay ouldcay otnay avehay oughtbay uchsay arecay asyay Iyay avehay astedway onyay isthay
iserablemay iestpray! Utbay orfay ymay aidyay, ishay ifelay ouldway avehay urnedbay awayyay inyay
ormentstay, ithinway ethay irstfay otway yearsyay afteryay ethay erpetrationpay ofyay ishay
imecray andyay inethay. Orfay, Esterhay, ishay iritspay ackedlay ethay engthstray atthay
ouldcay avehay ornebay upyay, asyay inethay ashay, eneathbay ayay urdenbay ikelay ythay arletscay
etterlay. Oyay, Iyay ouldcay evealray ayay oodlygay ecretsay! Utbay enoughyay! Atwhay artyay ancay
oday, Iyay avehay exhaustedyay onyay imhay. Atthay ehay ownay eathesbray, andyay eepscray aboutyay onyay
earthyay, isyay owingyay allyay otay emay!”

etter“bay ehay adhay iedday atyay onceyay!” aidsay Esterhay Ynnepray.

yea“ay, omanway, outhay ayestsay ulytray!” iedcray oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay,
ettinglay ethay uridlay irefay ofyay ishay earthay azeblay outyay eforebay erhay eyesyay. etter“bay
adhay ehay iedday atyay onceyay! Evernay idday ortalmay uffersay atwhay isthay anmay ashay
ufferedsay. Andyay allyay, allyay, inyay ethay ightsay ofyay ishay orstway enemyyay! Ehay ashay eenbay
onsciouscay ofyay emay. Ehay ashay eltfay anyay influenceyay ellingdway alwaysyay uponyay imhay
ikelay ayay ursecay. Ehay ewknay, ybay omesay iritualspay ense,—forsay ethay Eatorcray evernay
ademay anotheryay eingbay osay ensitivesay asyay is,—hethay ewknay atthay onay iendlyfray
andhay asway ullingpay atyay ishay eart-stringshay, andyay atthay anyay eyeyay asway ookinglay
uriouslycay intoyay imhay, ichwhay oughtsay onlyyay evilyay, andyay oundfay ityay. Utbay ehay ewknay
otnay atthay ethay eyeyay andyay andhay ereway inemay! Ithway ethay uperstitionsay ommoncay otay
ishay otherhoodbray, ehay anciedfay imselfhay ivengay overyay otay ayay iendfay, otay ebay
orturedtay ithway ightfulfray eamsdray, andyay esperateday oughtsthay, ethay ingstay ofyay
emorseray, andyay espairday ofyay ardonpay; asyay ayay oretastefay ofyay atwhay awaitsyay imhay
eyondbay ethay avegray. Utbay ityay asway ethay onstantcay adowshay ofyay ymay esence!—thepray
osestclay opinquitypray ofyay ethay anmay omwhay ehay adhay ostmay ilelyvay onged!—andwray
owhay adhay owngray otay existyay onlyyay ybay isthay erpetualpay oisonpay ofyay ethay irestday
evengeray! Yeayay, indeed!—heyay idday otnay err!—thereyay asway ayay iendfay atyay ishay
elbowyay! Ayay ortalmay anmay, ithway onceyay ayay umanhay earthay, ashay ecomebay ayay iendfay orfay
ishay especialyay ormenttay!”

Ethay unfortunateyay ysicianphay, ilewhay utteringyay esethay ordsway, iftedlay ishay
andshay ithway ayay ooklay ofyay orrorhay, asyay ifyay ehay adhay eheldbay omesay ightfulfray apeshay,
ichwhay ehay ouldcay otnay ecognizeray, usurpingyay ethay aceplay ofyay ishay ownyay imageyay inyay
ayay assglay. Ityay asway oneyay ofyay osethay oments—whichmay ometimessay occuryay onlyyay atyay
ethay intervalyay ofyay years—whenyay ayay an’smay oralmay aspectyay isyay aithfullyfay
evealedray otay ishay ind’smay eyeyay. Otnay improbablyyay, ehay adhay evernay eforebay iewedvay
imselfhay asyay ehay idday ownay.

ast“hay outhay otnay orturedtay imhay enoughyay?” aidsay Esterhay, oticingnay ethay oldyay
an’smay ooklay. as“hay ehay otnay aidpay eethay allyay?”

o!—no!—he“nay ashay utbay increasedyay ethay ebtday!” answeredyay ethay ysicianphay; andyay
asyay ehay oceededpray ishay annermay ostlay itsyay iercerfay aracteristicschay, andyay
ubsidedsay intoyay oomglay. ost“day outhay ememberray emay, Esterhay, asyay Iyay asway inenay
yearsyay agoneyay? Evenyay enthay, Iyay asway inyay ethay autumnyay ofyay ymay aysday, ornay asway ityay ethay
earlyyay autumnyay. Utbay allyay ymay ifelay adhay eenbay ademay upyay ofyay earnestyay, udiousstay,
oughtfulthay, uietqay yearsyay, estowedbay aithfullyfay orfay ethay increaseyay ofyay inemay
ownyay owledgeknay, andyay aithfullyfay, ootay, oughthay isthay atterlay objectyay asway utbay
asualcay otay ethay other,—faithfullyyay orfay ethay advancementyay ofyay umanhay elfareway.
Onay ifelay adhay eenbay oremay eacefulpay andyay innocentyay anthay inemay; ewfay iveslay osay
ichray ithway enefitsbay onferredcay. Ostday outhay ememberray emay? Asway Iyay otnay, oughthay
youyay ightmay eemday emay oldcay, everthelessnay ayay anmay oughtfulthay orfay othersyay,
avingcray ittlelay orfay imself,—kindhay, uetray, ustjay, andyay ofyay onstantcay, ifyay otnay
armway affectionsyay? Asway Iyay otnay allyay isthay?”

all“ay isthay, andyay oremay,” aidsay Esterhay.

and“ay atwhay amyay Iyay ownay?” emandedday ehay, ookinglay intoyay erhay acefay, andyay
ermittingpay ethay olewhay evilyay ithinway imhay otay ebay ittenwray onyay ishay eaturesfay. i“ay
avehay alreadyyay oldtay eethay atwhay Iyay amyay! Ayay iendfay! Owhay ademay emay osay?”

it“ay asway yselfmay!” iedcray Esterhay, udderingshay. it“ay asway Iyay, otnay esslay anthay
ehay. Ywhay asthay outhay otnay avengedyay yselfthay onyay emay?”

i“ay avehay eftlay eethay otay ethay arletscay etterlay,” epliedray Ogerray Illingworthchay.
if“ay atthay avehay otnay avengedyay emay, Iyay ancay oday onay oremay!”

Ehay aidlay ishay ingerfay onyay ityay, ithway ayay ilesmay.

it“ay ashay avengedyay eethay!” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray.

i“ay udgedjay onay esslay,” aidsay ethay ysicianphay. and“ay ownay, atwhay ouldstway outhay
ithway emay ouchingtay isthay anmay?”

i“ay ustmay evealray ethay ecretsay,” answeredyay Esterhay, irmlyfay. e“hay ustmay iscernday
eethay inyay ythay uetray aracterchay. Atwhay aymay ebay ethay esultray, Iyay owknay otnay. Utbay
isthay onglay ebtday ofyay onfidencecay, ueday omfray emay otay imhay, osewhay anebay andyay uinray
Iyay avehay eenbay, allshay atyay engthlay ebay aidpay. Osay arfay asyay oncernscay ethay overthrowyay
oryay eservationpray ofyay ishay airfay amefay andyay ishay earthlyyay atestay, andyay erchancepay
ishay ifelay, ehay isyay inyay ythay andshay. Ornay oday I,—whomyay ethay arletscay etterlay ashay
isciplinedday otay uthtray, oughthay ityay ebay ethay uthtray ofyay ed-hotray ironyay, enteringyay
intoyay ethay oul,—norsay oday Iyay erceivepay uchsay advantageyay inyay ishay ivinglay anyyay
ongerlay ayay ifelay ofyay astlyghay emptinessyay, atthay Iyay allshay oopstay otay imploreyay ythay
ercymay. Oday ithway imhay asyay outhay iltway! Erethay isyay onay oodgay orfay im,—nohay oodgay
orfay e,—nomay oodgay orfay eethay! Erethay isyay onay oodgay orfay ittlelay Earlpay! Erethay isyay
onay athpay otay uidegay usyay outyay ofyay isthay ismalday azemay!”

oman“way, Iyay ouldcay ellnighway itypay eethay!” aidsay Ogerray Illingworthchay, unableyay
otay estrainray ayay illthray ofyay admirationyay ootay; orfay erethay asway ayay ualityqay almostyay
ajesticmay inyay ethay espairday ichwhay eshay expressedyay. ou“thay adsthay eatgray
elementsyay. Eradventurepay, adsthay outhay etmay earlieryay ithway ayay etterbay ovelay anthay
inemay, isthay evilyay adhay otnay eenbay. Iyay itypay eethay, orfay ethay oodgay atthay ashay eenbay
astedway inyay ythay aturenay!”

and“ay Iyay eethay,” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray, or“fay ethay atredhay atthay ashay
ansformedtray ayay iseway andyay ustjay anmay otay ayay iendfay! Iltway outhay yetyay urgepay ityay outyay
ofyay eethay, andyay ebay onceyay oremay umanhay? Ifyay otnay orfay ishay akesay, enthay oublyday orfay
inethay ownyay! Orgivefay, andyay eavelay ishay urtherfay etributionray otay ethay Owerpay
atthay aimsclay ityay! Iyay aidsay, utbay ownay, atthay erethay ouldcay ebay onay oodgay eventyay orfay
imhay, oryay eethay, oryay emay, owhay areyay erehay anderingway ogethertay inyay isthay oomyglay
azemay ofyay evilyay, andyay umblingstay, atyay everyyay epstay, overyay ethay uiltgay erewithwhay
eway avehay ewnstray ouryay athpay. Ityay isyay otnay osay! Erethay ightmay ebay oodgay orfay eethay,
andyay eethay aloneyay, incesay outhay asthay eenbay eeplyday ongedwray, andyay asthay ityay atyay
ythay illway otay ardonpay. Iltway outhay ivegay upyay atthay onlyyay ivilegepray? Iltway outhay
ejectray atthay icelesspray enefitbay?”

eace“pay, Esterhay, eacepay!” epliedray ethay oldyay anmay, ithway oomyglay ernnessstay.
it“ay isyay otnay antedgray emay otay ardonpay. Iyay avehay onay uchsay owerpay asyay outhay ellesttay
emay ofyay. Ymay oldyay aithfay, onglay orgottenfay, omescay ackbay otay emay, andyay explainsyay
allyay atthay eway oday, andyay allyay eway uffersay. Ybay ythay irstfay epstay awryyay outhay idstday
antplay ethay ermgay ofyay evilyay; utbay incesay atthay omentmay, ityay ashay allyay eenbay ayay arkday
ecessitynay. Yeyay atthay avehay ongedwray emay areyay otnay infulsay, avesay inyay ayay indkay ofyay
ypicaltay illusionyay; eithernay amyay Iyay iend-likefay, owhay avehay atchedsnay ayay iend’sfay
officeyay omfray ishay andshay. Ityay isyay ouryay atefay. Etlay ethay ackblay owerflay ossomblay asyay
ityay aymay! Ownay ogay ythay aysway, andyay ealday asyay outhay iltway ithway yonderyay anmay.”

Ehay avedway ishay andhay, andyay etookbay imselfhay againyay otay ishay employmentyay ofyay
atheringgay erbshay.

illustration[ay: Andrakemay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Xvay.

                           Esterhay Andyay Earlpay.


Osay Ogerray Illingworth—achay eformedday oldyay igurefay, ithway ayay acefay atthay
auntedhay en’smay emoriesmay ongerlay anthay eythay iked—tooklay eavelay ofyay Esterhay
Ynnepray, andyay entway oopingstay awayyay alongyay ethay earthyay. Ehay atheredgay erehay andyay
erethay anyay erbhay, oryay ubbedgray upyay ayay ootray, andyay utpay ityay intoyay ethay asketbay onyay ishay
armyay. Ishay aygray eardbay almostyay ouchedtay ethay oundgray, asyay ehay eptcray onwardyay.
Esterhay azedgay afteryay imhay ayay ittlelay ilewhay, ookinglay ithway ayay alf-fantastichay
uriositycay otay eesay etherwhay ethay endertay assgray ofyay earlyyay ingspray ouldway otnay ebay
ightedblay eneathbay imhay, andyay owshay ethay averingway acktray ofyay ishay ootstepsfay,
eresay andyay ownbray, acrossyay itsyay eerfulchay erdurevay. Eshay onderedway atwhay ortsay ofyay
erbshay eythay ereway, ichwhay ethay oldyay anmay asway osay eduloussay otay athergay. Ouldway
otnay ethay earthyay, uickenedqay otay anyay evilyay urposepay ybay ethay ympathysay ofyay ishay
eyeyay, eetgray imhay ithway oisonouspay ubsshray, ofyay eciesspay ithertohay unknownyay,
atthay ouldway artstay upyay underyay ishay ingersfay? Oryay ightmay ityay ufficesay imhay, atthay
everyyay olesomewhay owthgray ouldshay ebay onvertedcay intoyay omethingsay eleteriousday
andyay alignantmay atyay ishay ouchtay? Idday ethay unsay, ichwhay oneshay osay ightlybray
everywhereyay elseyay, eallyray allfay uponyay imhay? Oryay asway erethay, asyay ityay atherray
eemedsay, ayay irclecay ofyay ominousyay adowshay ovingmay alongyay ithway ishay eformityday,
icheverwhay ayway ehay urnedtay imselfhay? Andyay itherwhay asway ehay ownay oinggay? Ouldway
ehay otnay uddenlysay inksay intoyay ethay earthyay, eavinglay ayay arrenbay andyay astedblay
otspay, erewhay, inyay ueday oursecay ofyay imetay, ouldway ebay eensay eadlyday ightshadenay,
ogwoodday, enbanehay, andyay ateverwhay elseyay ofyay egetablevay ickednessway ethay
imateclay ouldcay oducepray, allyay ourishingflay ithway ideoushay uxuriancelay? Oryay
ouldway ehay eadspray at’sbay ingsway andyay eeflay awayyay, ookinglay osay uchmay ethay uglieryay,
ethay igherhay ehay oseray owardstay eavenhay?

illustration[ay: e“hay atheredgay erbshay erehay andyay erethay”]

e“bay ityay insay oryay onay,” aidsay Esterhay Ynnepray, itterlybay, asyay eshay illstay azedgay
afteryay imhay, i“ay atehay ethay anmay!”

Eshay upbraidedyay erselfhay orfay ethay entimentsay, utbay ouldcay otnay overcomeyay oryay
essenlay ityay. Attemptingyay otay oday osay, eshay oughtthay ofyay osethay ong-pastlay aysday,
inyay ayay istantday andlay, enwhay ehay usedyay otay emergeyay atyay eventideyay omfray ethay
eclusionsay ofyay ishay udystay, andyay itsay ownday inyay ethay irelightfay ofyay eirthay omehay,
andyay inyay ethay ightlay ofyay erhay uptialnay ilesmay. Ehay eedednay otay askbay imselfhay inyay
atthay ilesmay, ehay aidsay, inyay orderyay atthay ethay illchay ofyay osay anymay onelylay ourshay
amongyay ishay ooksbay ightmay ebay akentay offyay ethay olar’sschay earthay. Uchsay enesscay
adhay onceyay appearedyay otnay otherwiseyay anthay appyhay, utbay ownay, asyay iewedvay oughthray
ethay ismalday ediummay ofyay erhay ubsequentsay ifelay, eythay assedclay emselvesthay
amongyay erhay ugliestyay emembrancesray. Eshay arvelledmay owhay uchsay enesscay ouldcay
avehay eenbay! Eshay arvelledmay owhay eshay ouldcay everyay avehay eenbay oughtwray uponyay otay
arrymay imhay! Eshay eemedday ityay erhay imecray ostmay otay ebay epentedray ofyay, atthay eshay
adhay everyay enduredyay, andyay eciprocatedray, ethay ukewarmlay aspgray ofyay ishay andhay,
andyay adhay ufferedsay ethay ilesmay ofyay erhay ipslay andyay eyesyay otay inglemay andyay eltmay
intoyay ishay ownyay. Andyay ityay eemedsay ayay oulerfay offenceyay ommittedcay ybay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, anthay anyyay ichwhay adhay incesay eenbay oneday imhay, atthay, inyay ethay
imetay enwhay erhay earthay ewknay onay etterbay, ehay adhay ersuadedpay erhay otay ancyfay
erselfhay appyhay ybay ishay idesay.

yes“ay, Iyay atehay imhay!” epeatedray Esterhay, oremay itterlybay anthay eforebay. e“hay
etrayedbay emay! Ehay ashay oneday emay orseway ongwray anthay Iyay idday imhay!”

Etlay enmay embletray otay inway ethay andhay ofyay omanway, unlessyay eythay inway alongyay ithway
ityay ethay utmostyay assionpay ofyay erhay earthay! Elseyay ityay aymay ebay eirthay iserablemay
ortunefay, asyay ityay asway Ogerray Illingworth’schay, enwhay omesay ightiermay ouchtay
anthay eirthay ownyay aymay avehay awakenedyay allyay erhay ensibilitiessay, otay ebay
eproachedray evenyay orfay ethay almcay ontentcay, ethay arblemay imageyay ofyay appinesshay,
ichwhay eythay illway avehay imposedyay uponyay erhay asyay ethay armway ealityray. Utbay Esterhay
oughtyay onglay agoyay otay avehay oneday ithway isthay injusticeyay. Atwhay idday ityay etokenbay?
Adhay evensay onglay yearsyay, underyay ethay orturetay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay,
inflictedyay osay uchmay ofyay iserymay, andyay oughtwray outyay onay epentanceray?

Ethay emotionsyay ofyay atthay iefbray acespay, ilewhay eshay oodstay azinggay afteryay ethay
ookedcray igurefay ofyay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ewthray ayay arkday ightlay onyay
Ester’shay atestay ofyay indmay, evealingray uchmay atthay eshay ightmay otnay otherwiseyay
avehay acknowledgedyay otay erselfhay.

Ehay eingbay onegay, eshay ummonedsay ackbay erhay ildchay.

earl“pay! Ittlelay Earlpay! Erewhay areyay youyay?”

illustration[ay: Earlpay onyay ethay Ea-shoresay]

Earlpay, osewhay activityyay ofyay iritspay evernay aggedflay, adhay eenbay atyay onay osslay orfay
amusementyay ilewhay erhay othermay alkedtay ithway ethay oldyay atherergay ofyay erbshay. Atyay
irstfay, asyay alreadyyay oldtay, eshay adhay irtedflay ancifullyfay ithway erhay ownyay imageyay
inyay ayay oolpay ofyay aterway, eckoningbay ethay antomphay orthfay, and—asyay ityay eclinedday
otay enture—seekingvay ayay assagepay orfay erselfhay intoyay itsyay eresphay ofyay
impalpableyay earthyay andyay unattainableyay yskay. Oonsay indingfay, oweverhay, atthay
eitheryay eshay oryay ethay imageyay asway unrealyay, eshay urnedtay elsewhereyay orfay etterbay
astimepay. Eshay ademay ittlelay oatsbay outyay ofyay irch-barkbay, andyay eightedfray emthay
ithway ail-shellssnay, andyay entsay outyay oremay enturesvay onyay ethay ightymay eepday anthay
anyyay erchantmay inyay Ewnay Englandyay; utbay ethay argerlay artpay ofyay emthay ounderedfay
earnay ethay oreshay. Eshay eizedsay ayay ivelay orseshoehay ybay ethay ailtay, andyay ademay
izepray ofyay everalsay ive-fingersfay, andyay aidlay outyay ayay elly-fishjay otay eltmay inyay
ethay armway unsay. Enthay eshay ooktay upyay ethay itewhay oamfay, atthay eakedstray ethay inelay
ofyay ethay advancingyay idetay, andyay ewthray ityay uponyay ethay eezebray, amperingscay afteryay
ityay, ithway ingedway ootstepsfay, otay atchcay ethay eatgray ow-flakessnay ereyay eythay
ellfay. Erceivingpay ayay ockflay ofyay each-birdsbay, atthay edfay andyay utteredflay alongyay
ethay oreshay, ethay aughtynay ildchay ickedpay upyay erhay apronyay ullfay ofyay ebblespay, andyay,
eepingcray omfray ockray otay ockray afteryay esethay allsmay ea-fowlsay, isplayedday
emarkableray exterityday inyay eltingpay emthay. Oneyay ittlelay aygray irdbay, ithway ayay
itewhay eastbray, Earlpay asway almostyay uresay, adhay eenbay ithay ybay ayay ebblepay, andyay
utteredflay awayyay ithway ayay okenbray ingway. Utbay enthay ethay elf-childyay ighedsay, andyay
avegay upyay erhay ortspay; ecausebay ityay ievedgray erhay otay avehay oneday armhay otay ayay
ittlelay eingbay atthay asway asyay ildway asyay ethay ea-breezesay, oryay asyay ildway asyay Earlpay
erselfhay.

Erhay inalfay employmentyay asway otay athergay ea-weedsay, ofyay ariousvay indskay, andyay
akemay erselfhay ayay arfscay, oryay antlemay, andyay ayay ead-dresshay, andyay usthay assumeyay ethay
aspectyay ofyay ayay ittlelay ermaidmay. Eshay inheritedyay erhay other’smay iftgay orfay
evisingday aperydray andyay ostumecay. Asyay ethay astlay ouchtay otay erhay ermaid’smay arbgay,
Earlpay ooktay omesay eel-grassyay, andyay imitatedyay, asyay estbay eshay ouldcay, onyay erhay ownyay
osombay, ethay ecorationday ithway ichwhay eshay asway osay amiliarfay onyay erhay other’smay.
Ayay etter,—thelay etterlay A,—butyay eshlyfray eengray, insteadyay ofyay arletscay! Ethay
ildchay entbay erhay inchay uponyay erhay eastbray, andyay ontemplatedcay isthay eviceday ithway
angestray interestyay; evenyay asyay ifyay ethay oneyay onlyyay ingthay orfay ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay
entsay intoyay ethay orldway asway otay akemay outyay itsyay iddenhay importyay.

i“ay onderway ifyay othermay illway askyay emay atwhay ityay eansmay?” oughtthay Earlpay.

Ustjay enthay, eshay eardhay erhay other’smay oicevay, andyay ittingflay alongyay asyay ightlylay
asyay oneyay ofyay ethay ittlelay ea-birdssay, appearedyay eforebay Esterhay Ynnepray,
ancingday, aughinglay, andyay ointingpay erhay ingerfay otay ethay ornamentyay uponyay erhay
osombay.

y“may ittlelay Earlpay,” aidsay Esterhay, afteryay ayay oment’smay ilencesay, e“thay eengray
etterlay, andyay onyay ythay ildishchay osombay, ashay onay urportpay. Utbay ostday outhay owknay,
ymay ildchay, atwhay isthay etterlay eansmay ichwhay ythay othermay isyay oomedday otay earway?”

yes“ay, othermay,” aidsay ethay ildchay. it“ay isyay ethay eatgray etterlay Ayay. Outhay asthay
aughttay emay inyay ethay orn-bookhay.”

Esterhay ookedlay eadilystay intoyay erhay ittlelay acefay; utbay, oughthay erethay asway
atthay ingularsay expressionyay ichwhay eshay adhay osay oftenyay emarkedray inyay erhay ackblay
eyesyay, eshay ouldcay otnay atisfysay erselfhay etherwhay Earlpay eallyray attachedyay anyyay
eaningmay otay ethay ymbolsay. Eshay eltfay ayay orbidmay esireday otay ascertainyay ethay
ointpay.

ost“day outhay owknay, ildchay, ereforewhay ythay othermay earsway isthay etterlay?”

uly“tray oday Iyay!” answeredyay Earlpay, ookinglay ightlybray intoyay erhay other’smay acefay.
it“ay isyay orfay ethay amesay easonray atthay ethay inistermay eepskay ishay andhay overyay ishay
earthay!”

and“ay atwhay easonray isyay atthay?” askedyay Esterhay, alfhay ilingsmay atyay ethay absurdyay
incongruityyay ofyay ethay ild’schay observationyay; utbay, onyay econdsay oughtsthay,
urningtay alepay. at“whay ashay ethay etterlay otay oday ithway anyyay earthay, avesay inemay?”

ay“nay, othermay, Iyay avehay oldtay allyay Iyay owknay,” aidsay Earlpay, oremay eriouslysay anthay
eshay asway ontway otay eakspay. ask“ay yonderyay oldyay anmay omwhay outhay asthay eenbay alkingtay
ithway! Ityay aymay ebay ehay ancay elltay. Utbay inyay oodgay earnestyay ownay, othermay earday,
atwhay oesday isthay arletscay etterlay ean?—andmay ywhay ostday outhay earway ityay onyay ythay
osom?—andbay ywhay oesday ethay inistermay eepkay ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay?”

Eshay ooktay erhay other’smay andhay inyay othbay erhay ownyay, andyay azedgay intoyay erhay eyesyay
ithway anyay earnestnessyay atthay asway eldomsay eensay inyay erhay ildway andyay apriciouscay
aracterchay. Ethay oughtthay occurredyay otay Esterhay, atthay ethay ildchay ightmay eallyray
ebay eekingsay otay approachyay erhay ithway ildlikechay onfidencecay, andyay oingday atwhay
eshay ouldcay, andyay asyay intelligentlyyay asyay eshay ewknay owhay, otay establishyay ayay
eeting-pointmay ofyay ympathysay. Ityay owedshay Earlpay inyay anyay unwontedyay aspectyay.
Eretoforehay, ethay othermay, ilewhay ovinglay erhay ildchay ithway ethay intensityyay ofyay ayay
olesay affectionyay, adhay ooledschay erselfhay otay opehay orfay ittlelay otheryay eturnray
anthay ethay aywardnessway ofyay anyay Aprilyay eezebray; ichwhay endsspay itsyay imetay inyay airyyay
ortspay, andyay ashay itsyay ustsgay ofyay inexplicableyay assionpay, andyay isyay etulantpay inyay
itsyay estbay ofyay oodsmay, andyay illschay ofteneryay anthay aressescay youyay, enwhay youyay aketay
ityay otay youryay osombay; inyay equitalray ofyay ichwhay isdemeanorsmay, ityay illway
ometimessay, ofyay itsyay ownyay aguevay urposepay, isskay youryay eekchay ithway ayay indkay ofyay
oubtfulday endernesstay, andyay ayplay entlygay ithway youryay airhay, andyay enthay ebay onegay
aboutyay itsyay otheryay idleyay usinessbay, eavinglay ayay eamydray easureplay atyay youryay
earthay. Andyay isthay, oreovermay, asway ayay other’smay estimateyay ofyay ethay ild’schay
ispositionday. Anyyay otheryay observeryay ightmay avehay eensay ewfay utbay unamiableyay
aitstray, andyay avehay ivengay emthay ayay arfay arkerday oloringcay. Utbay ownay ethay ideayay
amecay onglystray intoyay Ester’shay indmay, atthay Earlpay, ithway erhay emarkableray
ecocitypray andyay acutenessyay, ightmay alreadyyay avehay approachedyay ethay ageyay enwhay
eshay ouldcay ebay ademay ayay iendfray, andyay intrustedyay ithway asyay uchmay ofyay erhay other’smay
orrowssay asyay ouldcay ebay impartedyay, ithoutway irreverenceyay eitheryay otay ethay arentpay
oryay ethay ildchay. Inyay ethay ittlelay aoschay ofyay Earl’spay aracterchay erethay ightmay ebay
eensay emerging—andyay ouldcay avehay eenbay, omfray ethay eryvay irst—thefay eadfaststay
inciplespray ofyay anyay unflinchingyay ourage,—ancay uncontrollableyay ill,—away
urdystay idepray, ichwhay ightmay ebay isciplinedday intoyay elf-respect,—andsay ayay
itterbay ornscay ofyay anymay ingsthay, ichwhay, enwhay examinedyay, ightmay ebay oundfay otay
avehay ethay ainttay ofyay alsehoodfay inyay emthay. Eshay ossessedpay affectionsyay, ootay,
oughthay ithertohay acridyay andyay isagreeableday, asyay areyay ethay ichestray avorsflay ofyay
unripeyay uitfray. Ithway allyay esethay erlingstay attributesyay, oughtthay Esterhay, ethay
evilyay ichwhay eshay inheritedyay omfray erhay othermay ustmay ebay eatgray indeedyay, ifyay ayay
oblenay omanway oday otnay owgray outyay ofyay isthay elfishyay ildchay.

Earl’spay inevitableyay endencytay otay overhay aboutyay ethay enigmayay ofyay ethay arletscay
etterlay eemedsay anyay innateyay ualityqay ofyay erhay eingbay. Omfray ethay earliestyay epochyay
ofyay erhay onsciouscay ifelay, eshay adhay enteredyay uponyay isthay asyay erhay appointedyay
issionmay. Esterhay adhay oftenyay anciedfay atthay Ovidencepray adhay ayay esignday ofyay
usticejay andyay etributionray, inyay endowingyay ethay ildchay ithway isthay arkedmay
opensitypray; utbay evernay, untilyay ownay, adhay eshay ethoughtbay erselfhay otay askyay,
etherwhay, inkedlay ithway atthay esignday, erethay ightmay otnay ikewiselay ebay ayay
urposepay ofyay ercymay andyay eneficencebay. Ifyay ittlelay Earlpay ereway entertainedyay
ithway aithfay andyay usttray, asyay ayay iritspay essengermay onay esslay anthay anyay earthlyyay
ildchay, ightmay ityay otnay ebay erhay errandyay otay oothesay awayyay ethay orrowsay atthay aylay
oldcay inyay erhay other’smay earthay, andyay onvertedcay ityay intoyay ayay omb?—andtay otay elphay
erhay otay overcomeyay ethay assionpay, onceyay osay ildway, andyay evenyay yetyay eithernay eadday
ornay asleepyay, utbay onlyyay imprisonedyay ithinway ethay amesay omb-liketay earthay?

Uchsay ereway omesay ofyay ethay oughtsthay atthay ownay irredstay inyay Ester’shay indmay, ithway
asyay uchmay ivacityvay ofyay impressionyay asyay ifyay eythay adhay actuallyyay eenbay isperedwhay
intoyay erhay earyay. Andyay erethay asway ittlelay Earlpay, allyay isthay ilewhay, oldinghay erhay
other’smay andhay inyay othbay erhay ownyay, andyay urningtay erhay acefay upwardyay, ilewhay eshay
utpay esethay earchingsay uestionsqay, onceyay, andyay againyay, andyay illstay ayay irdthay
imetay.

at“whay oesday ethay etterlay eanmay, other?—andmay ywhay ostday outhay earway it?—andyay
ywhay oesday ethay inistermay eepkay ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay?”

at“whay allshay Iyay aysay?” oughtthay Esterhay otay erselfhay. o“nay! Ifyay isthay ebay ethay
icepray ofyay ethay ild’schay ympathysay, Iyay annotcay aypay ityay.”

Enthay eshay okespay aloudyay.

illy“say Earlpay,” aidsay eshay, at“whay uestionsqay areyay esethay? Erethay areyay anymay
ingsthay inyay isthay orldway atthay ayay ildchay ustmay otnay askyay aboutyay. Atwhay owknay Iyay ofyay
ethay inister’smay earthay? Andyay asyay orfay ethay arletscay etterlay, Iyay earway ityay orfay ethay
akesay ofyay itsyay old-threadgay.”

Inyay allyay ethay evensay ygonebay yearsyay, Esterhay Ynnepray adhay evernay eforebay eenbay
alsefay otay ethay ymbolsay onyay erhay osombay. Ityay aymay ebay atthay ityay asway ethay alismantay
ofyay ayay ernstay andyay everesay, utbay yetyay ayay uardiangay iritspay, owhay ownay orsookfay erhay;
asyay ecognizingray atthay, inyay itespay ofyay ishay ictstray atchway overyay erhay earthay, omesay
ewnay evilyay adhay eptcray intoyay ityay, oryay omesay oldyay oneyay adhay evernay eenbay expelledyay.
Asyay orfay ittlelay Earlpay, ethay earnestnessyay oonsay assedpay outyay ofyay erhay acefay.

Utbay ethay ildchay idday otnay eesay itfay otay etlay ethay attermay opdray. Otway oryay eethray
imestay, asyay erhay othermay andyay eshay entway omewardhay, andyay asyay oftenyay atyay
upper-timesay, andyay ilewhay Esterhay asway uttingpay erhay otay edbay, andyay onceyay afteryay
eshay eemedsay otay ebay airlyfay asleepyay, Earlpay ookedlay upyay, ithway ischiefmay
eamingglay inyay erhay ackblay eyesyay.

other“may,” aidsay eshay, at“whay oesday ethay arletscay etterlay eanmay?”

Andyay ethay extnay orningmay, ethay irstfay indicationyay ethay ildchay avegay ofyay eingbay
awakeyay asway ybay oppingpay upyay erhay eadhay omfray ethay illowpay, andyay akingmay atthay
otheryay inquiryyay, ichwhay eshay adhay osay unaccountablyyay onnectedcay ithway erhay
investigationsyay aboutyay ethay arletscay etterlay:—

other!—mother!—why“may oesday ethay inistermay eepkay ishay andhay overyay ishay
earthay?”

old“hay ythay onguetay, aughtynay ildchay!” answeredyay erhay othermay, ithway anyay
asperityyay atthay eshay adhay evernay ermittedpay otay erselfhay eforebay. o“day otnay easetay
emay; elseyay Iyay allshay utshay eethay intoyay ethay arkday osetclay!”

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Ixvay.

                            Ayay Orestfay Alkway.


Esterhay Ynnepray emainedray onstantcay inyay erhay esolveray otay akemay ownknay otay Mray.
Immesdaleday, atyay ateverwhay iskray ofyay esentpray ainpay oryay ulterioryay onsequencescay,
ethay uetray aracterchay ofyay ethay anmay owhay adhay eptcray intoyay ishay intimacyyay. Orfay
everalsay aysday, oweverhay, eshay ainlyvay oughtsay anyay opportunityyay ofyay addressingyay
imhay inyay omesay ofyay ethay editativemay alksway ichwhay eshay ewknay imhay otay ebay inyay ethay
abithay ofyay akingtay, alongyay ethay oresshay ofyay ethay eninsulapay, oryay onyay ethay oodedway
illshay ofyay ethay eighboringnay ountrycay. Erethay ouldway avehay eenbay onay andalscay,
indeedyay, ornay erilpay otay ethay olyhay itenesswhay ofyay ethay ergyman’sclay oodgay amefay,
adhay eshay isitedvay imhay inyay ishay ownyay udystay; erewhay anymay ayay enitentpay, ereyay ownay,
adhay onfessedcay inssay ofyay erhapspay asyay eepday ayay yeday asyay ethay oneyay etokenedbay ybay
ethay arletscay etterlay. Utbay, artlypay atthay eshay eadeddray ethay ecretsay oryay
undisguisedyay interferenceyay ofyay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, andyay artlypay atthay
erhay onsciouscay earthay imputedyay uspicionsay erewhay onenay ouldcay avehay eenbay eltfay,
andyay artlypay atthay othbay ethay inistermay andyay eshay ouldway eednay ethay olewhay ideway
orldway otay eathebray inyay, ilewhay eythay alkedtay ogether,—fortay allyay esethay
easonsray, Esterhay evernay oughtthay ofyay eetingmay imhay inyay anyyay arrowernay ivacypray
anthay eneathbay ethay openyay yskay.

Atyay astlay, ilewhay attendingyay inyay ayay ick-chambersay, itherwhay ethay Everendray Mray.
Immesdaleday adhay eenbay ummonedsay otay akemay ayay ayerpray, eshay earntlay atthay ehay adhay
onegay, ethay ayday eforebay, otay isitvay ethay Apostleyay Eliotyay, amongyay ishay Indianyay
onvertscay. Ehay ouldway obablypray eturnray, ybay ayay ertaincay ourhay, inyay ethay
afternoonyay ofyay ethay orrowmay. Etimesbay, ereforethay, ethay extnay ayday, Esterhay ooktay
ittlelay Earl,—whopay asway ecessarilynay ethay ompanioncay ofyay allyay erhay other’smay
expeditionsyay, oweverhay inconvenientyay erhay esence,—andpray etsay orthfay.

Ethay oadray, afteryay ethay otway ayfarersway adhay ossedcray omfray ethay eninsulapay otay
ethay ainlandmay, asway onay otheryay anthay ayay ootpathfay. Ityay aggledstray onwardyay intoyay
ethay ysterymay ofyay ethay imevalpray orestfay. Isthay emmedhay ityay inyay osay arrowlynay, andyay
oodstay osay ackblay andyay enseday onyay eitheryay idesay, andyay isclosedday uchsay imperfectyay
impsesglay ofyay ethay yskay aboveyay, atthay, otay Ester’shay indmay, ityay imagedyay otnay amissyay
ethay oralmay ildernessway inyay ichwhay eshay adhay osay onglay eenbay anderingway. Ethay ayday
asway illchay andyay ombresay. Overheadyay asway ayay aygray expanseyay ofyay oudclay, ightlyslay
irredstay, oweverhay, ybay ayay eezebray; osay atthay ayay eamglay ofyay ickeringflay unshinesay
ightmay ownay andyay enthay ebay eensay atyay itsyay olitarysay ayplay alongyay ethay athpay. Isthay
ittingflay eerfulnesschay asway alwaysyay atyay ethay artherfay extremityyay ofyay omesay onglay
istavay oughthray ethay orestfay. Ethay ortivespay unlight—feeblysay ortivespay, atyay
estbay, inyay ethay edominantpray ensivenesspay ofyay ethay ayday andyay ene—withdrewscay
itselfyay asyay eythay amecay ighnay, andyay eftlay ethay otsspay erewhay ityay adhay ancedday ethay
earierdray, ecausebay eythay adhay opedhay otay indfay emthay ightbray.

other“may,” aidsay ittlelay Earlpay, e“thay unshinesay oesday otnay ovelay youyay. Ityay unsray
awayyay andyay ideshay itselfyay, ecausebay ityay isyay afraidyay ofyay omethingsay onyay youryay
osombay. Ownay, eesay! Erethay ityay isyay, ayingplay, ayay oodgay ayway offyay. Andstay youyay
erehay, andyay etlay emay unray andyay atchcay ityay. Iyay amyay utbay ayay ildchay. Ityay illway otnay eeflay
omfray emay; orfay Iyay earway othingnay onyay ymay osombay yetyay!”

or“nay everyay illway, ymay ildchay, Iyay opehay,” aidsay Esterhay.

and“ay ywhay otnay, othermay?” askedyay Earlpay, oppingstay ortshay, ustjay atyay ethay
eginningbay ofyay erhay aceray. ill“way otnay ityay omecay ofyay itsyay ownyay accordyay, enwhay Iyay amyay
ayay omanway owngray?”

un“ray awayyay, ildchay,” answeredyay erhay othermay, and“ay atchcay ethay unshinesay! Ityay
illway oonsay ebay onegay.”

Earlpay etsay orthfay, atyay ayay eatgray acepay, andyay, asyay Esterhay iledsmay otay erceivepay,
idday actuallyyay atchcay ethay unshinesay, andyay oodstay aughinglay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay
ityay, allyay ightenedbray ybay itsyay endorsplay, andyay intillatingscay ithway ethay
ivacityvay excitedyay ybay apidray otionmay. Ethay ightlay ingeredlay aboutyay ethay onelylay
ildchay, asyay ifyay adglay ofyay uchsay ayay aymateplay, untilyay erhay othermay adhay awndray
almostyay ighnay enoughyay otay epstay intoyay ethay agicmay irclecay ootay.

it“ay illway ogay ownay,” aidsay Earlpay, akingshay erhay eadhay.

ee“say!” answeredyay Esterhay, ilingsmay. ow“nay Iyay ancay etchstray outyay ymay andhay, andyay
aspgray omesay ofyay ityay.”

Asyay eshay attemptedyay otay oday osay, ethay unshinesay anishedvay; oryay, otay udgejay omfray
ethay ightbray expressionyay atthay asway ancingday onyay Earl’spay eaturesfay, erhay othermay
ouldcay avehay anciedfay atthay ethay ildchay adhay absorbedyay ityay intoyay erselfhay, andyay
ouldway ivegay ityay orthfay againyay, ithway ayay eamglay aboutyay erhay athpay, asyay eythay ouldshay
ungeplay intoyay omesay oomierglay adeshay. Erethay asway onay otheryay attributeyay atthay osay
uchmay impressedyay erhay ithway ayay ensesay ofyay ewnay andyay untransmittedyay igorvay inyay
Earl’spay aturenay, asyay isthay ever-failingnay ivacityvay ofyay iritsspay; eshay adhay otnay
ethay iseaseday ofyay adnesssay, ichwhay almostyay allyay ildrenchay, inyay esethay atterlay
aysday, inherityay, ithway ethay ofulascray, omfray ethay oublestray ofyay eirthay
ancestorsyay. Erhapspay isthay ootay asway ayay iseaseday, andyay utbay ethay eflexray ofyay ethay
ildway energyyay ithway ichwhay Esterhay adhay oughtfay againstyay erhay orrowssay, eforebay
Earl’spay irthbay. Ityay asway ertainlycay ayay oubtfulday armchay, impartingyay ayay ardhay,
etallicmay ustrelay otay ethay ild’schay aracterchay. Eshay anted—whatway omesay eoplepay
antway oughoutthray ife—alay iefgray atthay ouldshay eeplyday ouchtay erhay, andyay usthay
umanizehay andyay akemay erhay apablecay ofyay ympathysay. Utbay erethay asway imetay enoughyay
yetyay orfay ittlelay Earlpay.

ome“cay, ymay ildchay!” aidsay Esterhay, ookinglay aboutyay erhay omfray ethay otspay erewhay
Earlpay adhay oodstay illstay inyay ethay unshinesay. e“way illway itsay ownday ayay ittlelay ayway
ithinway ethay oodway, andyay estray ourselvesyay.”

i“ay amyay otnay awearyyay, othermay,” epliedray ethay ittlelay irlgay. ut“bay youyay aymay itsay
ownday, ifyay youyay illway elltay emay ayay orystay eanwhilemay.”

a“ay orystay, ildchay!” aidsay Esterhay. and“ay aboutyay atwhay?”

o“ay, ayay orystay aboutyay ethay Ackblay Anmay,” answeredyay Earlpay, akingtay oldhay ofyay erhay
other’smay owngay, andyay ookinglay upyay, alfhay earnestlyyay, alfhay ischievouslymay,
intoyay erhay acefay. ow“hay ehay auntshay isthay orestfay, andyay arriescay ayay ookbay ithway
im,—ahay igbay, eavyhay ookbay, ithway ironyay aspsclay; andyay owhay isthay uglyyay Ackblay Anmay
offersyay ishay ookbay andyay anyay ironyay enpay otay everybodyyay atthay eetsmay imhay erehay amongyay
ethay eestray; andyay eythay areyay otay itewray eirthay amesnay ithway eirthay ownyay oodblay. Andyay
enthay ehay etssay ishay arkmay onyay eirthay osomsbay! Idstday outhay everyay eetmay ethay Ackblay
Anmay, othermay?”

and“ay owhay oldtay youyay isthay orystay, Earlpay?” askedyay erhay othermay, ecognizingray ayay
ommoncay uperstitionsay ofyay ethay eriodpay.

it“ay asway ethay oldyay ameday inyay ethay imney-cornerchay, atyay ethay ousehay erewhay youyay
atchedway astlay ightnay,” aidsay ethay ildchay. ut“bay eshay anciedfay emay asleepyay ilewhay
eshay asway alkingtay ofyay ityay. Eshay aidsay atthay ayay ousandthay andyay ayay ousandthay eoplepay
adhay etmay imhay erehay, andyay adhay ittenwray inyay ishay ookbay, andyay avehay ishay arkmay onyay
emthay. Andyay atthay ugly-temperedyay adylay, oldyay Istressmay Ibbinshay, asway oneyay. Andyay,
othermay, ethay oldyay ameday aidsay atthay isthay arletscay etterlay asway ethay Ackblay An’smay
arkmay onyay eethay, andyay atthay ityay owsglay ikelay ayay edray ameflay enwhay outhay eetestmay
imhay atyay idnightmay, erehay inyay ethay arkday oodway. Isyay ityay uetray, othermay? Andyay ostday
outhay ogay otay eetmay imhay inyay ethay ight-timenay?”

idst“day outhay everyay awakeyay, andyay indfay ythay othermay onegay?” askedyay Esterhay.

ot“nay atthay Iyay ememberray,” aidsay ethay ildchay. if“ay outhay earestfay otay eavelay emay inyay
ouryay ottagecay, outhay ightestmay aketay emay alongyay ithway eethay. Iyay ouldway eryvay
adlyglay ogay! Utbay, othermay, elltay emay ownay! Isyay erethay uchsay ayay Ackblay Anmay? Andyay
idstday outhay everyay eetmay imhay? Andyay isyay isthay ishay arkmay?”

ilt“way outhay etlay emay ebay atyay eacepay, ifyay Iyay onceyay elltay eethay?” askedyay erhay othermay.

yes“ay, ifyay outhay ellesttay emay allyay,” answeredyay Earlpay.

once“ay inyay ymay ifelay Iyay etmay ethay Ackblay Anmay!” aidsay erhay othermay. is“thay arletscay
etterlay isyay ishay arkmay!”

Usthay onversingcay, eythay enteredyay ufficientlysay eepday intoyay ethay oodway otay
ecuresay emselvesthay omfray ethay observationyay ofyay anyyay asualcay assengerpay alongyay
ethay orestfay acktray. Erehay eythay atsay ownday onyay ayay uxuriantlay eaphay ofyay ossmay;
ichwhay, atyay omesay epochyay ofyay ethay ecedingpray enturycay, adhay eenbay ayay iganticgay
inepay, ithway itsyay ootsray andyay unktray inyay ethay arksomeday adeshay, andyay itsyay eadhay
aloftyay inyay ethay upperyay atmosphereyay. Ityay asway ayay ittlelay ellday erewhay eythay adhay
eatedsay emselvesthay, ithway ayay eaf-strewnlay ankbay isingray entlygay onyay eitheryay
idesay, andyay ayay ookbray owingflay oughthray ethay idstmay, overyay ayay edbay ofyay allenfay andyay
owneddray eaveslay. Ethay eestray impendingyay overyay ityay adhay ungflay ownday eatgray
anchesbray, omfray imetay otay imetay, ichwhay okedchay upyay ethay urrentcay andyay ompelledcay
ityay otay ormfay eddiesyay andyay ackblay epthsday atyay omesay ointspay; ilewhay, inyay itsyay
iftersway andyay ivelierlay assagespay, erethay appearedyay ayay annel-waychay ofyay
ebblespay, andyay ownbray, arklingspay andsay. Ettinglay ethay eyesyay ollowfay alongyay ethay
oursecay ofyay ethay eamstray, eythay ouldcay atchcay ethay eflectedray ightlay omfray itsyay
aterway, atyay omesay ortshay istanceday ithinway ethay orestfay, utbay oonsay ostlay allyay
acestray ofyay ityay amidyay ethay ewildermentbay ofyay ee-trunkstray andyay underbrushyay, andyay
erehay andyay erethay ayay ugehay ockray overedcay overyay ithway aygray ichenslay. Allyay esethay
iantgay eestray andyay owldersbay ofyay anitegray eemedsay intentyay onyay akingmay ayay ysterymay
ofyay ethay oursecay ofyay isthay allsmay ookbray; earingfay, erhapspay, atthay, ithway itsyay
ever-ceasingnay oquacitylay, ityay ouldshay isperwhay alestay outyay ofyay ethay earthay ofyay
ethay oldyay orestfay encewhay ityay owedflay, oryay irrormay itsyay evelationsray onyay ethay
oothsmay urfacesay ofyay ayay oolpay. Ontinuallycay, indeedyay, asyay ityay olestay onwardyay, ethay
eamletstray eptkay upyay ayay abblebay, indkay, uietqay, oothingsay, utbay elancholymay,
ikelay ethay oicevay ofyay ayay youngyay ildchay atthay asway endingspay itsyay infancyyay ithoutway
ayfulnessplay, andyay ewknay otnay owhay otay ebay errymay amongyay adsay acquaintanceyay andyay
eventsyay ofyay ombresay uehay.

o“ay ookbray! Oyay oolishfay andyay iresometay ittlelay ookbray!” iedcray Earlpay, afteryay
isteninglay awhileyay otay itsyay alktay. y“whay artyay outhay osay adsay? Uckplay upyay ayay iritspay,
andyay oday otnay ebay allyay ethay imetay ighingsay andyay urmuringmay!”

Utbay ethay ookbray, inyay ethay oursecay ofyay itsyay ittlelay ifetimelay amongyay ethay
orest-treesfay, adhay onegay oughthray osay olemnsay anyay experienceyay atthay ityay ouldcay
otnay elphay alkingtay aboutyay ityay, andyay eemedsay otay avehay othingnay elseyay otay aysay.
Earlpay esembledray ethay ookbray, inasmuchyay asyay ethay urrentcay ofyay erhay ifelay ushedgay
omfray ayay ell-springway asyay ysteriousmay, andyay adhay owedflay oughthray enesscay
adowedshay asyay eavilyhay ithway oomglay. Utbay, unlikeyay ethay ittlelay eamstray, eshay
ancedday andyay arkledspay, andyay attledpray airilyyay alongyay erhay oursecay.

at“whay oesday isthay adsay ittlelay ookbray aysay, othermay?” inquiredyay eshay.

if“ay outhay adsthay ayay orrowsay ofyay inethay ownyay, ethay ookbray ightmay elltay eethay ofyay
ityay,” answeredyay erhay othermay, even“ay asyay ityay isyay ellingtay emay ofyay inemay! Utbay ownay,
Earlpay, Iyay earhay ayay ootstepfay alongyay ethay athpay, andyay ethay oisenay ofyay oneyay uttingpay
asideyay ethay anchesbray. Iyay ouldway avehay eethay etakebay yselfthay otay ayplay, andyay
eavelay emay otay eakspay ithway imhay atthay omescay yonderyay.”

is“ay ityay ethay Ackblay Anmay?” askedyay Earlpay.

ilt“way outhay ogay andyay ayplay, ildchay?” epeatedray erhay othermay. ut“bay oday otnay aystray
arfay intoyay ethay oodway. Andyay aketay eedhay atthay outhay omecay atyay ymay irstfay allcay.”

yes“ay, othermay,” answeredyay Earlpay. ut“bay ifyay ityay ebay ethay Ackblay Anmay, iltway outhay
otnay etlay emay aystay ayay omentmay, andyay ooklay atyay imhay, ithway ishay igbay ookbay underyay ishay
armyay?”

o“gay, illysay ildchay!” aidsay erhay othermay, impatientlyyay. it“ay isyay onay Ackblay Anmay!
Outhay anstcay eesay imhay ownay, oughthray ethay eestray. Ityay isyay ethay inistermay!”

and“ay osay ityay isyay!” aidsay ethay ildchay. and“ay, othermay, ehay ashay ishay andhay overyay ishay
earthay! Isyay ityay ecausebay, enwhay ethay inistermay otewray ishay amenay inyay ethay ookbay,
ethay Ackblay Anmay etsay ishay arkmay inyay atthay aceplay? Utbay ywhay oesday ehay otnay earway ityay
outsideyay ishay osombay, asyay outhay ostday, othermay?”

o“gay ownay, ildchay, andyay outhay altshay easetay emay asyay outhay iltway anotheryay imetay,”
iedcray Esterhay Ynnepray. ut“bay oday otnay aystray arfay. Eepkay erewhay outhay anstcay earhay
ethay abblebay ofyay ethay ookbray.”

Ethay ildchay entway ingingsay awayyay, ollowingfay upyay ethay urrentcay ofyay ethay ookbray,
andyay ivingstray otay inglemay ayay oremay ightsomelay adencecay ithway itsyay elancholymay
oicevay. Utbay ethay ittlelay eamstray ouldway otnay ebay omfortedcay, andyay illstay eptkay
ellingtay itsyay unintelligibleyay ecretsay ofyay omesay eryvay ournfulmay ysterymay atthay
adhay appened—orhay akingmay ayay opheticpray amentationlay aboutyay omethingsay atthay
asway yetyay otay appen—withinhay ethay ergevay ofyay ethay ismalday orestfay. Osay Earlpay,
owhay adhay enoughyay ofyay adowshay inyay erhay ownyay ittlelay ifelay, osechay otay eakbray offyay
allyay acquaintanceyay ithway isthay epiningray ookbray. Eshay etsay erselfhay, ereforethay,
otay atheringgay ioletsvay andyay ood-anemonesway, andyay omesay arletscay olumbinescay
atthay eshay oundfay owinggray inyay ethay evicescray ofyay ayay ighhay ockray.

Enwhay erhay elf-childyay adhay epartedday, Esterhay Ynnepray ademay ayay epstay oryay otway
owardstay ethay acktray atthay edlay oughthray ethay orestfay, utbay illstay emainedray
underyay ethay eepday adowshay ofyay ethay eestray. Eshay eheldbay ethay inistermay advancingyay
alongyay ethay athpay, entirelyyay aloneyay, andyay eaninglay onyay ayay affstay ichwhay ehay adhay
utcay ybay ethay aysideway. Ehay ookedlay aggardhay andyay eeblefay, andyay etrayedbay ayay
ervelessnay espondencyday inyay ishay airyay, ichwhay adhay evernay osay emarkablyray
aracterizedchay imhay inyay ishay alksway aboutyay ethay ettlementsay, ornay inyay anyyay otheryay
ituationsay erewhay ehay eemedday imselfhay iablelay otay oticenay. Erehay ityay asway
ofullyway isiblevay, inyay isthay intenseyay eclusionsay ofyay ethay orestfay, ichwhay ofyay
itselfyay ouldway avehay eenbay ayay eavyhay ialtray otay ethay iritsspay. Erethay asway ayay
istlessnesslay inyay ishay aitgay; asyay ifyay ehay awsay onay easonray orfay akingtay oneyay epstay
artherfay, ornay eltfay anyyay esireday otay oday osay, utbay ouldway avehay eenbay adglay, ouldcay
ehay ebay adglay ofyay anythingyay, otay ingflay imselfhay ownday atyay ethay ootray ofyay ethay
earestnay eetray, andyay ielay erethay assivepay, orevermorefay. Ethay eaveslay ightmay
estrewbay imhay, andyay ethay oilsay aduallygray accumulateyay andyay ormfay ayay ittlelay
illockhay overyay ishay amefray, onay attermay etherwhay erethay ereway ifelay inyay ityay oryay onay.
Eathday asway ootay efiniteday anyay objectyay otay ebay ishedway orfay, oryay avoidedyay.

Otay Ester’shay eyeyay, ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday exhibitedyay onay ymptomsay ofyay
ositivepay andyay ivaciousvay ufferingsay, exceptyay atthay, asyay ittlelay Earlpay adhay
emarkedray, ehay eptkay ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iixvay.

                    Ethay Astorpay Andyay Ishay Arishionerpay.


Owlyslay asyay ethay inistermay alkedway, ehay adhay almostyay onegay ybay, eforebay Esterhay
Ynnepray ouldcay athergay oicevay enoughyay otay attractyay ishay observationyay. Atyay
engthlay, eshay ucceededsay.

arthur“ay Immesdaleday!” eshay aidsay, aintlyfay atyay irstfay; enthay ouderlay, utbay
oarselyhay. arthur“ay Immesdaleday!”

o“whay eaksspay?” answeredyay ethay inistermay.

Atheringgay imselfhay uicklyqay upyay, ehay oodstay oremay erectyay, ikelay ayay anmay akentay ybay
urprisesay inyay ayay oodmay otay ichwhay ehay asway eluctantray otay avehay itnessesway.
Owingthray ishay eyesyay anxiouslyyay inyay ethay irectionday ofyay ethay oicevay, ehay
indistinctlyyay eheldbay ayay ormfay underyay ethay eestray, adclay inyay armentsgay osay
ombresay, andyay osay ittlelay elievedray omfray ethay aygray ilighttway intoyay ichwhay ethay
oudedclay yskay andyay ethay eavyhay oliagefay adhay arkenedday ethay oontidenay, atthay ehay
ewknay otnay etherwhay ityay ereway ayay omanway oryay ayay adowshay. Ityay aymay ebay, atthay ishay
athwaypay oughthray ifelay asway auntedhay usthay, ybay ayay ectrespay atthay adhay olenstay
outyay omfray amongyay ishay oughtsthay.

Ehay ademay ayay epstay ighernay, andyay iscoveredday ethay arletscay etterlay.

ester“hay! Esterhay Ynnepray!” aidsay ehay. is“ay ityay outhay? Artyay outhay inyay ifelay?”

even“ay osay!” eshay answeredyay. in“ay uchsay ifelay asyay ashay eenbay inemay esethay evensay
yearsyay astpay! Andyay outhay, Arthuryay Immesdaleday, ostday outhay yetyay ivelay?”

Ityay asway onay onderway atthay eythay usthay uestionedqay oneyay another’syay actualyay andyay
odilybay existenceyay, andyay evenyay oubtedday ofyay eirthay ownyay. Osay angelystray idday eythay
eetmay, inyay ethay imday oodway, atthay ityay asway ikelay ethay irstfay encounteryay, inyay ethay
orldway eyondbay ethay avegray, ofyay otway iritsspay owhay adhay eenbay intimatelyyay
onnectedcay inyay eirthay ormerfay ifelay, utbay ownay oodstay oldlycay udderingshay, inyay
utualmay eaddray; asyay otnay yetyay amiliarfay ithway eirthay atestay, ornay ontedway otay ethay
ompanionshipcay ofyay isembodiedday eingsbay. Eachyay ayay ostghay, andyay awe-strickenyay atyay
ethay otheryay ostghay! Eythay ereway awe-strickenyay ikewiselay atyay emselvesthay;
ecausebay ethay isiscray ungflay ackbay otay emthay eirthay onsciousnesscay, andyay
evealedray otay eachyay earthay itsyay istoryhay andyay experienceyay, asyay ifelay evernay oesday,
exceptyay atyay uchsay eathlessbray epochsyay. Ethay oulsay eheldbay itsyay eaturesfay inyay ethay
irrormay ofyay ethay assingpay omentmay. Ityay asway ithway earfay, andyay emulouslytray, andyay,
asyay ityay ereway, ybay ayay owslay, eluctantray ecessitynay, atthay Arthuryay Immesdaleday utpay
orthfay ishay andhay, illchay asyay eathday, andyay ouchedtay ethay illchay andhay ofyay Esterhay
Ynnepray. Ethay aspgray, oldcay asyay ityay asway, ooktay awayyay atwhay asway eariestdray inyay ethay
interviewyay. Eythay ownay eltfay emselvesthay, atyay eastlay, inhabitantsyay ofyay ethay amesay
eresphay.

Ithoutway ayay ordway oremay oken,—neitherspay ehay ornay eshay assumingyay ethay uidancegay,
utbay ithway anyay unexpressedyay onsent,—theycay idedglay ackbay intoyay ethay adowshay ofyay
ethay oodsway, encewhay Esterhay adhay emergedyay, andyay atsay ownday onyay ethay eaphay ofyay ossmay
erewhay eshay andyay Earlpay adhay eforebay eenbay ittingsay. Enwhay eythay oundfay oicevay otay
eakspay, ityay asway, atyay irstfay, onlyyay otay utteryay emarksray andyay inquiriesyay uchsay asyay
anyyay otway acquaintanceyay ightmay avehay ademay, aboutyay ethay oomyglay yskay, ethay
eateningthray ormstay, andyay, extnay, ethay ealthhay ofyay eachyay. Usthay eythay entway
onwardyay, otnay oldlybay, utbay epstay ybay epstay, intoyay ethay emesthay atthay ereway
oodingbray eepestday inyay eirthay eartshay. Osay onglay estrangedyay ybay atefay andyay
ircumstancescay, eythay eedednay omethingsay ightslay andyay asualcay otay unray eforebay,
andyay owthray openyay ethay oorsday ofyay intercourseyay, osay atthay eirthay ealray oughtsthay
ightmay ebay edlay acrossyay ethay esholdthray.

Afteryay ayay ilewhay, ethay inistermay ixedfay ishay eyesyay onyay Esterhay Ynne’spray.

ester“hay,” aidsay ehay, ast“hay outhay oundfay eacepay?”

Eshay iledsmay earilydray, ookinglay ownday uponyay erhay osombay.

ast“hay outhay?” eshay askedyay.

one!—nothing“nay utbay espairday!” ehay answeredyay. at“whay elseyay ouldcay Iyay ooklay
orfay, eingbay atwhay Iyay amyay, andyay eadinglay uchsay ayay ifelay asyay inemay? Ereway Iyay anyay
atheist,—ayay anmay evoidday ofyay onscience,—acay etchwray ithway oarsecay andyay utalbray
instincts,—iyay ightmay avehay oundfay eacepay, onglay ereyay ownay. Aynay, Iyay evernay
ouldshay avehay ostlay ityay! Utbay, asyay attersmay andstay ithway ymay oulsay, ateverwhay ofyay
oodgay apacitycay erethay originallyyay asway inyay emay, allyay ofyay Od’sgay iftsgay atthay ereway
ethay oicestchay avehay ecomebay ethay inistersmay ofyay iritualspay ormenttay. Esterhay, Iyay
amyay ostmay iserablemay!”

e“thay eoplepay everenceray eethay,” aidsay Esterhay. and“ay urelysay outhay orkestway
oodgay amongyay emthay! Othday isthay ingbray eethay onay omfortcay?”

ore“may iserymay, Ester!—onlyhay ethay oremay iserymay!” answeredyay ethay ergymanclay,
ithway ayay itterbay ilesmay. as“ay oncernscay ethay oodgay ichwhay Iyay aymay appearyay otay oday, Iyay
avehay onay aithfay inyay ityay. Ityay ustmay eedsnay ebay ayay elusionday. Atwhay ancay ayay uinedray
oulsay, ikelay inemay, effectyay owardstay ethay edemptionray ofyay otheryay ouls?—orsay ayay
ollutedpay oulsay owardstay eirthay urificationpay? Andyay asyay orfay ethay eople’spay
everenceray, ouldway atthay ityay ereway urnedtay otay ornscay andyay atredhay! Anstcay outhay
eemday ityay, Esterhay, ayay onsolationcay, atthay Iyay ustmay andstay upyay inyay ymay ulpitpay, andyay
eetmay osay anymay eyesyay urnedtay upwardyay otay ymay acefay, asyay ifyay ethay ightlay ofyay eavenhay
ereway eamingbay omfray it!—mustyay eesay ymay ockflay ungryhay orfay ethay uthtray, andyay
isteninglay otay ymay ordsway asyay ifyay ayay onguetay ofyay Entecostpay ereway eaking!—andspay
enthay ooklay inwardyay, andyay iscernday ethay ackblay ealityray ofyay atwhay eythay idolizeyay?
Iyay avehay aughedlay, inyay itternessbay andyay agonyyay ofyay earthay, atyay ethay ontrastcay
etweenbay atwhay Iyay eemsay andyay atwhay Iyay amyay! Andyay Atansay aughslay atyay ityay!”

you“ay ongwray yourselfyay inyay isthay,” aidsay Esterhay, entlygay. you“ay avehay eeplyday
andyay orelysay epentedray. Youryay insay isyay eftlay ehindbay youyay, inyay ethay aysday onglay
astpay. Youryay esentpray ifelay isyay otnay esslay olyhay, inyay eryvay uthtray, anthay ityay eemssay
inyay eople’spay eyesyay. Isyay erethay onay ealityray inyay ethay enitencepay usthay ealedsay andyay
itnessedway ybay oodgay orksway? Andyay ereforewhay ouldshay ityay otnay ingbray youyay eacepay?”

o“nay, Esterhay, onay!” epliedray ethay ergymanclay. ere“thay isyay onay ubstancesay inyay ityay!
Ityay isyay oldcay andyay eadday, andyay ancay oday othingnay orfay emay! Ofyay enancepay, Iyay avehay adhay
enoughyay! Ofyay enitencepay, erethay ashay eenbay onenay! Elseyay, Iyay ouldshay onglay agoyay
avehay ownthray offyay esethay armentsgay ofyay ockmay olinesshay, andyay avehay ownshay yselfmay
otay ankindmay asyay eythay illway eesay emay atyay ethay udgment-seatjay. Appyhay areyay youyay,
Esterhay, atthay earway ethay arletscay etterlay openlyyay uponyay youryay osombay! Inemay
urnsbay inyay ecretsay! Outhay ittlelay owestknay atwhay ayay eliefray ityay isyay, afteryay ethay
ormenttay ofyay ayay evensay yearsyay’ eatchay, otay ooklay intoyay anyay eyeyay atthay ecognizesray
emay orfay atwhay Iyay amyay! Adhay Iyay oneyay iend,—orfray ereway ityay ymay orstway enemy!—toyay
omwhay, enwhay ickenedsay ithway ethay aisespray ofyay allyay otheryay enmay, Iyay ouldcay ailyday
etakebay yselfmay, andyay ebay ownknay asyay ethay ilestvay ofyay allyay innerssay, ethinksmay ymay
oulsay ightmay eepkay itselfyay aliveyay erebythay. Evenyay usthay uchmay ofyay uthtray ouldway
avesay emay! Utbay, ownay, ityay isyay allyay alsehood!—allfay emptiness!—allyay eathday!”

Esterhay Ynnepray ookedlay intoyay ishay acefay, utbay esitatedhay otay eakspay. Yetyay,
utteringyay ishay ong-restrainedlay emotionsyay osay ehementlyvay asyay ehay idday, ishay
ordsway erehay offeredyay erhay ethay eryvay ointpay ofyay ircumstancescay inyay ichwhay otay
interposeyay atwhay eshay amecay otay aysay. Eshay onqueredcay erhay earsfay, andyay okespay.

uch“say ayay iendfray asyay outhay asthay evenyay ownay ishedway orfay,” aidsay eshay, ith“way omwhay
otay eepway overyay ythay insay, outhay asthay inyay emay, ethay artnerpay ofyay it!”—againyay eshay
esitatedhay, utbay oughtbray outyay ethay ordsway ithway anyay effort.—“thouyay asthay onglay
adhay uchsay anyay enemyyay, andyay ellestdway ithway imhay, underyay ethay amesay oofray!”

Ethay inistermay artedstay otay ishay eetfay, aspinggay orfay eathbray, andyay utchingclay atyay
ishay earthay, asyay ifyay ehay ouldway avehay orntay ityay outyay ofyay ishay osombay.

a“hay! Atwhay ayestsay outhay!” iedcray ehay. an“ay enemyyay! Andyay underyay inemay ownyay oofray!
Atwhay eanmay youyay?”

Esterhay Ynnepray asway ownay ullyfay ensiblesay ofyay ethay eepday injuryyay orfay ichwhay eshay
asway esponsibleray otay isthay unhappyyay anmay, inyay ermittingpay imhay otay ielay orfay osay
anymay yearsyay, oryay, indeedyay, orfay ayay inglesay omentmay, atyay ethay ercymay ofyay oneyay osewhay
urposespay ouldcay otnay ebay otheryay anthay alevolentmay. Ethay eryvay ontiguitycay ofyay
ishay enemyyay, eneathbay ateverwhay askmay ethay atterlay ightmay oncealcay imselfhay, asway
enoughyay otay isturbday ethay agneticmay eresphay ofyay ayay eingbay osay ensitivesay asyay
Arthuryay Immesdaleday. Erethay adhay eenbay ayay eriodpay enwhay Esterhay asway esslay aliveyay
otay isthay onsiderationcay; oryay, erhapspay, inyay ethay isanthropymay ofyay erhay ownyay
oubletray, eshay eftlay ethay inistermay otay earbay atwhay eshay ightmay icturepay otay
erselfhay asyay ayay oremay olerabletay oomday. Utbay ofyay atelay, incesay ethay ightnay ofyay ishay
igilvay, allyay erhay ympathiessay owardstay imhay adhay eenbay othbay oftenedsay andyay
invigoratedyay. Eshay ownay eadray ishay earthay oremay accuratelyyay. Eshay oubtedday otnay,
atthay ethay ontinualcay esencepray ofyay Ogerray Illingworth,—thechay ecretsay oisonpay
ofyay ishay alignitymay, infectingyay allyay ethay airyay aboutyay im,—andhay ishay authorizedyay
interferenceyay, asyay ayay ysicianphay, ithway ethay inister’smay ysicalphay andyay
iritualspay infirmities,—thatyay esethay adbay opportunitiesyay adhay eenbay urnedtay
otay ayay uelcray urposepay. Ybay eansmay ofyay emthay, ethay ufferer’ssay onsciencecay adhay
eenbay eptkay inyay anyay irritatedyay atestay, ethay endencytay ofyay ichwhay asway, otnay otay
urecay ybay olesomewhay ainpay, utbay otay isorganizeday andyay orruptcay ishay iritualspay
eingbay. Itsyay esultray, onyay earthyay, ouldcay ardlyhay ailfay otay ebay insanityyay, andyay
ereafterhay, atthay eternalyay alienationyay omfray ethay Oodgay andyay Uetray, ofyay ichwhay
adnessmay isyay erhapspay ethay earthlyyay ypetay.

Uchsay asway ethay uinray otay ichwhay eshay adhay oughtbray ethay anmay, once,—nayyay, ywhay
ouldshay eway otnay eakspay it?—stillyay osay assionatelypay ovedlay! Esterhay eltfay atthay
ethay acrificesay ofyay ethay ergyman’sclay oodgay amenay, andyay eathday itselfyay, asyay eshay
adhay alreadyyay oldtay Ogerray Illingworthchay, ouldway avehay eenbay infinitelyyay
eferablepray otay ethay alternativeyay ichwhay eshay adhay akentay uponyay erselfhay otay
oosechay. Andyay ownay, atherray anthay avehay adhay isthay ievousgray ongwray otay onfesscay,
eshay ouldway adlyglay avehay ainlay ownday onyay ethay orest-leavesfay, andyay iedday erethay,
atyay Arthuryay Immesdale’sday eetfay.

o“ay Arthuryay,” iedcray eshay, orgive“fay emay! Inyay allyay ingsthay elseyay, Iyay avehay ivenstray
otay ebay uetray! Uthtray asway ethay oneyay irtuevay ichwhay Iyay ightmay avehay eldhay astfay, andyay
idday oldhay astfay, oughthray allyay extremityyay; avesay enwhay ythay ood,—thygay
ife,—thylay ame,—werefay utpay inyay uestionqay! Enthay Iyay onsentedcay otay ayay
eceptionday. Utbay ayay ielay isyay evernay oodgay, evenyay oughthay eathday eatenthray onyay ethay
otheryay idesay! Ostday outhay otnay eesay atwhay Iyay ouldway aysay? Atthay oldyay an!—themay
ysician!—hephay omwhay eythay allcay Ogerray Illingworth!—hechay asway ymay
usbandhay!”

illustration[ay: ilt“way outhay yetyay orgivefay emay?”]

Ethay inistermay ookedlay atyay erhay, orfay anyay instantyay, ithway allyay atthay iolencevay ofyay
assionpay, ich—intermixedwhay, inyay oremay apesshay anthay oneyay, ithway ishay igherhay,
urerpay, oftersay ualities—wasqay, inyay actfay, ethay ortionpay ofyay imhay ichwhay ethay
Evilday aimedclay, andyay oughthray ichwhay ehay oughtsay otay inway ethay estray. Evernay asway
erethay ayay ackerblay oryay ayay iercerfay ownfray anthay Esterhay ownay encounteredyay. Orfay
ethay iefbray acespay atthay ityay astedlay, ityay asway ayay arkday ansfigurationtray. Utbay ishay
aracterchay adhay eenbay osay uchmay enfeebledyay ybay ufferingsay, atthay evenyay itsyay
owerlay energiesyay ereway incapableyay ofyay oremay anthay ayay emporarytay ugglestray. Ehay
anksay ownday onyay ethay oundgray, andyay uriedbay ishay acefay inyay ishay andshay.

i“ay ightmay avehay ownknay ityay,” urmuredmay ehay. i“ay idday owknay ityay! Asway otnay ethay
ecretsay oldtay emay, inyay ethay aturalnay ecoilray ofyay ymay earthay, atyay ethay irstfay ightsay
ofyay imhay, andyay asyay oftenyay asyay Iyay avehay eensay imhay incesay? Ywhay idday Iyay otnay
understandyay? Oyay Esterhay Ynnepray, outhay ittlelay, ittlelay owestknay allyay ethay
orrorhay ofyay isthay ingthay! Andyay ethay ame!—theshay indelicacy!—theyay orriblehay
uglinessyay ofyay isthay exposureyay ofyay ayay icksay andyay uiltygay earthay otay ethay eryvay eyeyay
atthay ouldway oatglay overyay ityay! Omanway, omanway, outhay artyay accountableyay orfay isthay!
Iyay annotcay orgivefay eethay!”

ou“thay altshay orgivefay emay!” iedcray Esterhay, ingingflay erselfhay onyay ethay allenfay
eaveslay esidebay imhay. et“lay Odgay unishpay! Outhay altshay orgivefay!”

Ithway uddensay andyay esperateday endernesstay, eshay ewthray erhay armsyay aroundyay imhay,
andyay essedpray ishay eadhay againstyay erhay osombay; ittlelay aringcay oughthay ishay eekchay
estedray onyay ethay arletscay etterlay. Ehay ouldway avehay eleasedray imselfhay, utbay
ovestray inyay ainvay otay oday osay. Esterhay ouldway otnay etsay imhay eefray, estlay ehay ouldshay
ooklay erhay ernlystay inyay ethay acefay. Allyay ethay orldway adhay ownedfray onyay er,—forhay
evensay onglay yearsyay adhay ityay ownedfray uponyay isthay onelylay oman,—andway illstay eshay
orebay ityay allyay, ornay everyay onceyay urnedtay awayyay erhay irmfay, adsay eyesyay. Eavenhay,
ikewiselay, adhay ownedfray uponyay erhay, andyay eshay adhay otnay iedday. Utbay ethay ownfray ofyay
isthay alepay, eakway, infulsay, andyay orrow-strickensay anmay asway atwhay Esterhay ouldcay
otnay earbay andyay ivelay!

ilt“way outhay yetyay orgivefay emay?” eshay epeatedray, overyay andyay overyay againyay. ilt“way
outhay otnay ownfray? Iltway outhay orgivefay?”

i“ay oday orgivefay youyay, Esterhay,” epliedray ethay inistermay, atyay engthlay, ithway ayay
eepday utteranceyay, outyay ofyay anyay abyssyay ofyay adnesssay, utbay onay angeryay. i“ay eelyfray

orstway innerssay inyay ethay orldway. Erethay isyay oneyay orseway anthay evenyay ethay ollutedpay
iestpray! Atthay oldyay an’smay evengeray ashay eenbay ackerblay anthay ymay insay. Ehay ashay
iolatedvay, inyay oldcay oodblay, ethay anctitysay ofyay ayay umanhay earthay. Outhay andyay Iyay,
Esterhay, evernay idday osay!”

ever“nay, evernay!” isperedwhay eshay. at“whay eway idday adhay ayay onsecrationcay ofyay itsyay

ush“hay, Esterhay!” aidsay Arthuryay Immesdaleday, isingray omfray ethay oundgray. o“nay; Iyay
avehay otnay orgottenfay!”

Eythay atsay ownday againyay, idesay ybay idesay, andyay andhay aspedclay inyay andhay, onyay ethay
ossymay unktray ofyay ethay allenfay eetray. Ifelay adhay evernay oughtbray emthay ayay oomierglay
ourhay; ityay asway ethay ointpay itherwhay eirthay athwaypay adhay osay onglay eenbay endingtay,
andyay arkeningday everyay, asyay ityay olestay along;—andyay yetyay ityay enclosedyay ayay armchay
atthay ademay emthay ingerlay uponyay ityay, andyay aimclay anotheryay, andyay anotheryay, andyay,
afteryay allyay, anotheryay omentmay. Ethay orestfay asway obscureyay aroundyay emthay, andyay
eakedcray ithway ayay astblay atthay asway assingpay oughthray ityay. Ethay oughsbay ereway
ossingtay eavilyhay aboveyay eirthay eadshay; ilewhay oneyay olemnsay oldyay eetray oanedgray
olefullyday otay anotheryay, asyay ifyay ellingtay ethay adsay orystay ofyay ethay airpay atthay atsay
eneathbay, oryay onstrainedcay otay orebodefay evilyay otay omecay.

Andyay yetyay eythay ingeredlay. Owhay earydray ookedlay ethay orest-trackfay atthay edlay
ackwardbay otay ethay ettlementsay, erewhay Esterhay Ynnepray ustmay aketay upyay againyay ethay
urdenbay ofyay erhay ignominyyay, andyay ethay inistermay ethay ollowhay ockerymay ofyay ishay
oodgay amenay! Osay eythay ingeredlay anyay instantyay ongerlay. Onay oldengay ightlay adhay
everyay eenbay osay eciouspray asyay ethay oomglay ofyay isthay arkday orestfay. Erehay, eensay
onlyyay ybay ishay eyesyay, ethay arletscay etterlay eednay otnay urnbay intoyay ethay osombay ofyay
ethay allenfay omanway! Erehay, eensay onlyyay ybay erhay eyesyay, Arthuryay Immesdaleday,
alsefay otay Odgay andyay anmay, ightmay ebay, orfay oneyay omentmay, uetray!

Ehay artedstay atyay ayay oughtthay atthay uddenlysay occurredyay otay imhay.

ester“hay,” iedcray ehay, ere“hay isyay ayay ewnay orrorhay! Ogerray Illingworthchay owsknay
youryay urposepay otay evealray ishay uetray aracterchay. Illway ehay ontinuecay, enthay, otay
eepkay ouryay ecretsay? Atwhay illway ownay ebay ethay oursecay ofyay ishay evengeray?”

ere“thay isyay ayay angestray ecrecysay inyay ishay aturenay,” epliedray Esterhay,
oughtfullythay; and“ay ityay ashay owngray uponyay imhay ybay ethay iddenhay acticespray ofyay
ishay evengeray. Iyay eemday ityay otnay ikelylay atthay ehay illway etraybay ethay ecretsay. Ehay
illway oubtlessday eeksay otheryay eansmay ofyay atiatingsay ishay arkday assionpay.”

and“ay I!—howyay amyay Iyay otay ivelay ongerlay, eathingbray ethay amesay airyay ithway isthay

engthstray otay aketay advantageyay ofyay ityay.”

itselfyay erectyay. oth“day ethay universeyay ielay ithinway ethay ompasscay ofyay yonderyay

avesay otay ielay ownday andyay ieday! Ivegay upyay isthay amenay ofyay Arthuryay Immesdaleday, andyay
akemay yselfthay anotheryay, andyay ayay ighhay oneyay, uchsay asyay outhay anstcay earway ithoutway
earfay oryay ameshay. Ywhay ouldstshay outhay arrytay osay uchmay asyay oneyay otheryay ayday inyay ethay
ormentstay atthay avehay osay awedgnay intoyay ythay ife!—thatlay avehay ademay eethay
eeblefay otay illway andyay otay o!—thatday illway eavelay eethay owerlesspay evenyay otay

o“ay Esterhay!” iedcray Arthuryay Immesdaleday, inyay osewhay eyesyay ayay itfulfay ightlay,

alone“ay, Esterhay!”

ou“thay altshay otnay ogay aloneyay!” answeredyay eshay, inyay ayay eepday isperwhay.

Enthay, allyay asway okenspay!

                            illustration[ay]

                                Iiixvay.

                         Ayay Oodflay Ofyay Unshinesay.


Arthuryay Immesdaleday azedgay intoyay Ester’shay acefay ithway ayay ooklay inyay ichwhay opehay
andyay oyjay oneshay outyay, indeedyay, utbay ithway earfay etwixtbay emthay, andyay ayay indkay ofyay
orrorhay atyay erhay oldnessbay, owhay adhay okenspay atwhay ehay aguelyvay intedhay atyay, utbay
aredday otnay eakspay.

Utbay Esterhay Ynnepray, ithway ayay indmay ofyay ativenay ouragecay andyay activityyay, andyay orfay
osay onglay ayay eriodpay otnay erelymay estrangedyay, utbay outlawedyay, omfray ocietysay, adhay
abituatedhay erselfhay otay uchsay atitudelay ofyay eculationspay asyay asway altogetheryay
oreignfay otay ethay ergymanclay. Eshay adhay anderedway, ithoutway uleray oryay uidancegay,
inyay ayay oralmay ildernessway; asyay astvay, asyay intricateyay andyay adowyshay, asyay ethay
untamedyay orestfay, amidyay ethay oomglay ofyay ichwhay eythay ereway ownay oldinghay ayay
olloquycay atthay asway otay ecideday eirthay atefay. Erhay intellectyay andyay earthay adhay
eirthay omehay, asyay ityay ereway, inyay esertday acesplay, erewhay eshay oamedray asyay eelyfray
asyay ethay ildway Indianyay inyay ishay oodsway. Orfay yearsyay astpay eshay adhay ookedlay omfray
isthay estrangedyay ointpay ofyay iewvay atyay umanhay institutionsyay, andyay ateverwhay
iestspray oryay egislatorslay adhay establishedyay; iticisingcray allyay ithway ardlyhay
oremay everenceray anthay ethay Indianyay ouldway eelfay orfay ethay ericalclay andbay, ethay
udicialjay oberay, ethay illorypay, ethay allowsgay, ethay iresidefay, oryay ethay urchchay.
Ethay endencytay ofyay erhay atefay andyay ortunesfay adhay eenbay otay etsay erhay eefray. Ethay
arletscay etterlay asway erhay assportpay intoyay egionsray erewhay otheryay omenway aredday
otnay eadtray. Ameshay, Espairday, Olitudesay! Esethay adhay eenbay erhay
eachers,—sterntay andyay ildway ones,—andyay eythay adhay ademay erhay ongstray, utbay
aughttay erhay uchmay amissyay.

Ethay inistermay, onyay ethay otheryay andhay, adhay evernay onegay oughthray anyay experienceyay
alculatedcay otay eadlay imhay eyondbay ethay opescay ofyay enerallygay eceivedray awslay;
althoughyay, inyay ayay inglesay instanceyay, ehay adhay osay earfullyfay ansgressedtray oneyay
ofyay ethay ostmay acredsay ofyay emthay. Utbay isthay adhay eenbay ayay insay ofyay assionpay, otnay ofyay
inciplepray, ornay evenyay urposepay. Incesay atthay etchedwray epochyay, ehay adhay
atchedway, ithway orbidmay ealzay andyay inutenessmay, otnay ishay acts,—foryay osethay ityay
asway easyyay otay arrange,—butyay eachyay eathbray ofyay emotionyay, andyay ishay everyyay
oughtthay. Atyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay ocialsay ystemsay, asyay ethay ergymenclay ofyay atthay
ayday oodstay, ehay asway onlyyay ethay oremay ammelledtray ybay itsyay egulationsray, itsyay
inciplespray, andyay evenyay itsyay ejudicespray. Asyay ayay iestpray, ethay ameworkfray ofyay ishay
orderyay inevitablyyay emmedhay imhay inyay. Asyay ayay anmay owhay adhay onceyay innedsay, utbay owhay
eptkay ishay onsciencecay allyay aliveyay andyay ainfullypay ensitivesay ybay ethay ettingfray
ofyay anyay unhealedyay oundway, ehay ightmay avehay eenbay upposedsay afersay ithinway ethay
inelay ofyay irtuevay anthay ifyay ehay adhay evernay innedsay atyay allyay.

Usthay, eway eemsay otay eesay atthay, asyay egardedray Esterhay Ynnepray, ethay olewhay evensay
yearsyay ofyay outlawyay andyay ignominyyay adhay eenbay ittlelay otheryay anthay ayay eparationpray
orfay isthay eryvay ourhay. Utbay Arthuryay Immesdaleday! Ereway uchsay ayay anmay onceyay oremay
otay allfay, atwhay eaplay ouldcay ebay urgedyay inyay extenuationyay ofyay ishay imecray? Onenay;
unlessyay ityay availyay imhay omewhatsay, atthay ehay asway okenbray ownday ybay onglay andyay
exquisiteyay ufferingsay; atthay ishay indmay asway arkenedday andyay onfusedcay ybay ethay
eryvay emorseray ichwhay arrowedhay ityay; atthay, etweenbay eeingflay asyay anyay avowedyay
iminalcray, andyay emainingray asyay ayay ypocritehay, onsciencecay ightmay indfay ityay ardhay
otay ikestray ethay alancebay; atthay ityay asway umanhay otay avoidyay ethay erilpay ofyay eathday
andyay infamyyay, andyay ethay inscrutableyay achinationsmay ofyay anyay enemyyay; atthay,
inallyfay, otay isthay oorpay ilgrimpay, onyay ishay earydray andyay esertday athpay, aintfay,
icksay, iserablemay, erethay appearedyay ayay impseglay ofyay umanhay affectionyay andyay
ympathysay, ayay ewnay ifelay, andyay ayay uetray oneyay, inyay exchangeyay orfay ethay eavyhay oomday
ichwhay ehay asway ownay expiatingyay. Andyay ebay ethay ernstay andyay adsay uthtray okenspay,
atthay ethay eachbray ichwhay uiltgay ashay onceyay ademay intoyay ethay umanhay oulsay isyay
evernay, inyay isthay ortalmay atestay, epairedray. Ityay aymay ebay atchedway andyay uardedgay;
osay atthay ethay enemyyay allshay otnay orcefay ishay ayway againyay intoyay ethay itadelcay, andyay
ightmay evenyay, inyay ishay ubsequentsay assaultsyay, electsay omesay otheryay avenueyay, inyay
eferencepray otay atthay erewhay ehay adhay ormerlyfay ucceededsay. Utbay erethay isyay illstay
ethay uinedray allway, andyay, earnay ityay, ethay ealthystay eadtray ofyay ethay oefay atthay
ouldway inway overyay againyay ishay unforgottenyay iumphtray.

Ethay ugglestray, ifyay erethay ereway oneyay, eednay otnay ebay escribedday. Etlay ityay
ufficesay, atthay ethay ergymanclay esolvedray otay eeflay, andyay otnay aloneyay.

if“ay, inyay allyay esethay astpay evensay yearsyay,” oughtthay ehay, i“ay ouldcay ecallray oneyay
instantyay ofyay eacepay oryay opehay, Iyay ouldway yetyay endureyay, orfay ethay akesay ofyay atthay
earnestyay ofyay Eaven’shay ercymay. Utbay ow,—sincenay Iyay amyay irrevocablyyay
oomed,—whereforeday ouldshay Iyay otnay atchsnay ethay olacesay allowedyay otay ethay
ondemnedcay ulpritcay eforebay ishay executionyay? Oryay, ifyay isthay ebay ethay athpay otay ayay
etterbay ifelay, asyay Esterhay ouldway ersuadepay emay, Iyay urelysay ivegay upyay onay airerfay
ospectpray ybay ursuingpay ityay! Eithernay ancay Iyay anyyay ongerlay ivelay ithoutway erhay
ompanionshipcay; osay owerfulpay isyay eshay otay ustain,—sosay endertay otay oothesay! Oyay
Outhay otay omwhay Iyay areday otnay iftlay inemay eyesyay, iltway Outhay yetyay ardonpay emay!”

ou“thay iltway ogay!” aidsay Esterhay, almlycay, asyay ehay etmay erhay anceglay.

Ethay ecisionday onceyay ademay, ayay owglay ofyay angestray enjoymentyay ewthray itsyay
