ickeringflay ightnessbray overyay ethay oubletray ofyay ishay eastbray. Ityay asway ethay
exhilaratingyay effect—uponyay ayay isonerpray ustjay escapedyay omfray ethay ungeonday ofyay
ishay ownyay eart—ofhay eathingbray ethay ildway, eefray atmosphereyay ofyay anyay
unredeemedyay, unchristianizedyay, awlesslay egionray. Ishay iritspay oseray, asyay ityay
ereway, ithway ayay oundbay, andyay attainedyay ayay earernay ospectpray ofyay ethay yskay, anthay
oughoutthray allyay ethay iserymay ichwhay adhay eptkay imhay ovellinggray onyay ethay earthyay.
Ofyay ayay eeplyday eligiousray emperamenttay, erethay asway inevitablyyay ayay ingetay ofyay ethay
evotionalday inyay ishay oodmay.

o“day Iyay eelfay oyjay againyay?” iedcray ehay, onderingway atyay imselfhay. ethought“may ethay
ermgay ofyay ityay asway eadday inyay emay! Oyay Esterhay, outhay artyay ymay etterbay angelyay! Iyay eemsay
otay avehay ungflay yself—sickmay, in-stainedsay, andyay orrow-blackened—downsay
uponyay esethay orest-leavesfay, andyay otay avehay isenray upyay allyay ademay anewyay, andyay ithway
ewnay owerspay otay orifyglay Imhay atthay athhay eenbay ercifulmay! Isthay isyay alreadyyay ethay
etterbay ifelay! Ywhay idday eway otnay indfay ityay oonersay?”

et“lay usyay otnay ooklay ackbay,” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray. e“thay astpay isyay onegay!
Ereforewhay ouldshay eway ingerlay uponyay ityay ownay? Eesay! Ithway isthay ymbolsay, Iyay undoyay
ityay allyay, andyay akemay ityay asyay ityay adhay evernay eenbay!”

Osay eakingspay, eshay undidyay ethay aspclay atthay astenedfay ethay arletscay etterlay,
andyay, akingtay ityay omfray erhay osombay, ewthray ityay otay ayay istanceday amongyay ethay
itheredway eaveslay. Ethay ysticmay okentay alightedyay onyay ethay itherhay ergevay ofyay ethay
eamstray. Ithway ayay and’shay eadthbray artherfay ightflay ityay ouldway avehay allenfay intoyay
ethay aterway, andyay avehay ivengay ethay ittlelay ookbray anotheryay oeway otay arrycay
onwardyay, esidesbay ethay unintelligibleyay aletay ichwhay ityay illstay eptkay urmuringmay
aboutyay. Utbay erethay aylay ethay embroideredyay etterlay, itteringglay ikelay ayay ostlay
eweljay, ichwhay omesay ill-fatedyay andererway ightmay ickpay upyay, andyay enceforththay ebay
auntedhay ybay angestray antomsphay ofyay uiltgay, inkingssay ofyay ethay earthay, andyay
unaccountableyay isfortunemay.

illustration[ay: Ayay Eamglay ofyay Unshinesay]

Ethay igmastay onegay, Esterhay eavedhay ayay onglay, eepday ighsay, inyay ichwhay ethay urdenbay
ofyay ameshay andyay anguishyay epartedday omfray erhay iritspay. Oyay exquisiteyay eliefray! Eshay
adhay otnay ownknay ethay eightway, untilyay eshay eltfay ethay eedomfray! Ybay anotheryay
impulseyay, eshay ooktay offyay ethay ormalfay apcay atthay onfinedcay erhay airhay; andyay ownday
ityay ellfay uponyay erhay ouldersshay, arkday andyay ichray, ithway atyay onceyay ayay adowshay andyay ayay
ightlay inyay itsyay abundanceyay, andyay impartingyay ethay armchay ofyay oftnesssay otay erhay
eaturesfay. Erethay ayedplay aroundyay erhay outhmay, andyay eamedbay outyay ofyay erhay eyesyay, ayay
adiantray andyay endertay ilesmay, atthay eemedsay ushinggay omfray ethay eryvay earthay ofyay
omanhoodway. Ayay imsoncray ushflay asway owingglay onyay erhay eekchay, atthay adhay eenbay
onglay osay alepay. Erhay exsay, erhay youthyay, andyay ethay olewhay ichnessray ofyay erhay
eautybay, amecay ackbay omfray atwhay enmay allcay ethay irrevocableyay astpay, andyay
usteredclay emselvesthay, ithway erhay aidenmay opehay, andyay ayay appinesshay eforebay
unknownyay, ithinway ethay agicmay irclecay ofyay isthay ourhay. Andyay, asyay ifyay ethay oomglay ofyay
ethay earthyay andyay yskay adhay eenbay utbay ethay effluenceyay ofyay esethay otway ortalmay
eartshay, ityay anishedvay ithway eirthay orrowsay. Allyay atyay onceyay, asyay ithway ayay uddensay
ilesmay ofyay eavenhay, orthfay urstbay ethay unshinesay, ouringpay ayay eryvay oodflay intoyay
ethay obscureyay orestfay, addeningglay eachyay eengray eaflay, ansmutingtray ethay yellowyay
allenfay onesyay otay oldgay, andyay eamingglay adownyay ethay aygray unkstray ofyay ethay olemnsay
eestray. Ethay objectsyay atthay adhay ademay ayay adowshay ithertohay, embodiedyay ethay
ightnessbray ownay. Ethay oursecay ofyay ethay ittlelay ookbray ightmay ebay acedtray ybay itsyay
errymay eamglay afaryay intoyay ethay ood’sway earthay ofyay ysterymay, ichwhay adhay ecomebay ayay
ysterymay ofyay oyjay.

Uchsay asway ethay ympathysay ofyay Ature—thatnay ildway, eathenhay Aturenay ofyay ethay
orestfay, evernay ubjugatedsay ybay umanhay awlay, ornay illuminedyay ybay igherhay
uth—withtray ethay issblay ofyay esethay otway iritsspay! Ovelay, etherwhay ewlynay ornbay,
oryay arousedyay omfray ayay eath-likeday umberslay, ustmay alwaysyay eatecray ayay unshinesay,
illingfay ethay earthay osay ullfay ofyay adianceray, atthay ityay overflowsyay uponyay ethay
outwardyay orldway. Adhay ethay orestfay illstay eptkay itsyay oomglay, ityay ouldway avehay eenbay
ightbray inyay Ester’shay eyesyay, andyay ightbray inyay Arthuryay Immesdale’sday!

Esterhay ookedlay atyay imhay ithway ethay illthray ofyay anotheryay oyjay.

ou“thay ustmay owknay Earlpay!” aidsay eshay. our“ay ittlelay Earlpay! Outhay asthay eensay
er,—yeshay, Iyay owknay it!—butyay outhay iltway eesay erhay ownay ithway otheryay eyesyay. Eshay
isyay ayay angestray ildchay! Iyay ardlyhay omprehendcay erhay! Utbay outhay iltway ovelay erhay
earlyday, asyay Iyay oday, andyay iltway adviseyay emay owhay otay ealday ithway erhay.”

ost“day outhay inkthay ethay ildchay illway ebay adglay otay owknay emay?” askedyay ethay
inistermay, omewhatsay uneasilyyay. i“ay avehay onglay unkshray omfray ildrenchay,
ecausebay eythay oftenyay owshay ayay istrust,—aday ackwardnessbay otay ebay amiliarfay
ithway emay. Iyay avehay evenyay eenbay afraidyay ofyay ittlelay Earlpay!”

ah“ay, atthay asway adsay!” answeredyay ethay othermay. ut“bay eshay illway ovelay eethay
earlyday, andyay outhay erhay. Eshay isyay otnay arfay offyay. Iyay illway allcay erhay! Earlpay!
Earlpay!”

i“ay eesay ethay ildchay,” observedyay ethay inistermay. yonder“ay eshay isyay, andingstay inyay
ayay eakstray ofyay unshinesay, ayay oodgay ayway offyay, onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay ookbray.
Osay outhay inkestthay ethay ildchay illway ovelay emay?”

Esterhay iledsmay, andyay againyay alledcay otay Earlpay, owhay asway isiblevay, atyay omesay
istanceday, asyay ethay inistermay adhay escribedday erhay, ikelay ayay ight-apparelledbray
isionvay, inyay ayay unbeamsay, ichwhay ellfay ownday uponyay erhay oughthray anyay archyay ofyay
oughsbay. Ethay ayray uiveredqay otay andyay ofray, akingmay erhay igurefay imday oryay
istinct,—nowday ikelay ayay ealray ildchay, ownay ikelay ayay ild’schay irit,—asspay ethay
endorsplay entway andyay amecay againyay. Eshay eardhay erhay other’smay oicevay, andyay
approachedyay owlyslay oughthray ethay orestfay.

Earlpay adhay otnay oundfay ethay ourhay asspay earisomelyway, ilewhay erhay othermay atsay
alkingtay ithway ethay ergymanclay. Ethay eatgray ackblay orest—sternfay asyay ityay owedshay
itselfyay otay osethay owhay oughtbray ethay uiltgay andyay oublestray ofyay ethay orldway intoyay
itsyay osom—becamebay ethay aymateplay ofyay ethay onelylay infantyay, asyay ellway asyay ityay
ewknay owhay. Ombresay asyay ityay asway, ityay utpay onyay ethay indestkay ofyay itsyay oodsmay otay
elcomeway erhay. Ityay offeredyay erhay ethay artridge-berriespay, ethay owthgray ofyay ethay
ecedingpray autumnyay, utbay ipeningray onlyyay inyay ethay ingspray, andyay ownay edray asyay
opsdray ofyay oodblay uponyay ethay itheredway eaveslay. Esethay Earlpay atheredgay, andyay asway
easedplay ithway eirthay ildway avorflay. Ethay allsmay enizensday ofyay ethay ildernessway
ardlyhay ooktay ainspay otay ovemay outyay ofyay erhay athpay. Ayay artridgepay, indeedyay, ithway ayay
oodbray ofyay entay ehindbay erhay, anray orwardfay eateninglythray, utbay oonsay epentedray
ofyay erhay iercenessfay, andyay uckedclay otay erhay youngyay onesyay otnay otay ebay afraidyay. Ayay
igeonpay, aloneyay onyay ayay owlay anchbray, allowedyay Earlpay otay omecay eneathbay, andyay
utteredyay ayay oundsay asyay uchmay ofyay eetinggray asyay alarmyay. Ayay uirrelsqay, omfray ethay
oftylay epthsday ofyay ishay omesticday eetray, atteredchay eitheryay inyay angeryay oryay
erriment,—formay ayay uirrelsqay isyay uchsay ayay olericchay andyay umoroushay ittlelay
ersonagepay, atthay ityay isyay ardhay otay istinguishday etweenbay ishay oods,—somay ehay
atteredchay atyay ethay ildchay, andyay ungflay ownday ayay utnay uponyay erhay eadhay. Ityay asway ayay
astlay year’syay utnay, andyay alreadyyay awedgnay ybay ishay arpshay oothtay. Ayay oxfay,
artledstay omfray ishay eepslay ybay erhay ightlay ootstepfay onyay ethay eaveslay, ookedlay
inquisitivelyyay atyay Earlpay, asyay oubtingday etherwhay ityay ereway etterbay otay ealstay
offyay, oryay enewray ishay apnay onyay ethay amesay otspay. Ayay olfway, ityay isyay aid,—butsay erehay
ethay aletay ashay urelysay apsedlay intoyay ethay improbable,—cameyay upyay, andyay eltsmay ofyay
Earl’spay oberay, andyay offeredyay ishay avagesay eadhay otay ebay attedpay ybay erhay andhay.
Ethay uthtray eemssay otay ebay, oweverhay, atthay ethay other-forestmay, andyay esethay ildway
ingsthay ichwhay ityay ourishednay, allyay ecognizedray ayay indredkay ildnessway inyay ethay
umanhay ildchay.

Andyay eshay asway entlergay erehay anthay inyay ethay assy-marginedgray eetsstray ofyay ethay
ettlementsay, oryay inyay erhay other’smay ottagecay. Ethay owersflay appearedyay otay owknay
ityay; andyay oneyay andyay anotheryay isperedwhay asyay eshay assedpay, adorn“ay yselfthay ithway
emay, outhay eautifulbay ildchay, adornyay yselfthay ithway e!”—andmay, otay easeplay
emthay, Earlpay atheredgay ethay ioletsvay, andyay anemonesyay, andyay olumbinescay, andyay
omesay igstway ofyay ethay eshestfray eengray, ichwhay ethay oldyay eestray eldhay ownday eforebay
erhay eyesyay. Ithway esethay eshay ecoratedday erhay airhay, andyay erhay youngyay aistway, andyay
ecamebay ayay ymph-childnay, oryay anyay infantyay yaddray, oryay ateverwhay elseyay asway inyay
osestclay ympathysay ithway ethay antiqueyay oodway. Inyay uchsay uisegay adhay Earlpay
adornedyay erselfhay, enwhay eshay eardhay erhay other’smay oicevay, andyay amecay owlyslay
ackbay.

Owlyslay; orfay eshay awsay ethay ergymanclay.




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Ixxay.

                     Ethay Ildchay Atyay Ethay Ook-sidebray.


ou“thay iltway ovelay erhay earlyday,” epeatedray Esterhay Ynnepray, asyay eshay andyay ethay
inistermay atsay atchingway ittlelay Earlpay. ost“day outhay otnay inkthay erhay
eautifulbay? Andyay eesay ithway atwhay aturalnay illskay eshay ashay ademay osethay implesay
owersflay adornyay erhay! Adhay eshay atheredgay earlspay, andyay iamondsday, andyay ubiesray,
inyay ethay oodway, eythay ouldcay otnay avehay ecomebay erhay etterbay. Eshay isyay ayay endidsplay
ildchay! Utbay Iyay owknay osewhay owbray eshay ashay!”

ost“day outhay owknay, Esterhay,” aidsay Arthuryay Immesdaleday, ithway anyay unquietyay
ilesmay, at“thay isthay earday ildchay, ippingtray aboutyay alwaysyay atyay ythay idesay, athhay
ausedcay emay anymay anyay alarmyay? Ethought—omay Esterhay, atwhay ayay oughtthay isyay atthay,
andyay owhay erribletay otay eaddray it!—thatyay ymay ownyay eaturesfay ereway artlypay
epeatedray inyay erhay acefay, andyay osay ikinglystray atthay ethay orldway ightmay eesay emthay!
Utbay eshay isyay ostlymay inethay!”

o“nay, onay! Otnay ostlymay!” answeredyay ethay othermay, ithway ayay endertay ilesmay. a“ay
ittlelay ongerlay, andyay outhay eedestnay otnay otay ebay afraidyay otay acetray osewhay ildchay
eshay isyay. Utbay owhay angelystray eautifulbay eshay ookslay, ithway osethay
ild-flowersway inyay erhay airhay! Ityay isyay asyay ifyay oneyay ofyay ethay airiesfay, omwhay eway eftlay
inyay ouryay earday oldyay Englandyay, adhay eckedday erhay outyay otay eetmay usyay.”

Ityay asway ithway ayay eelingfay ichwhay eithernay ofyay emthay adhay everyay eforebay
experiencedyay, atthay eythay atsay andyay atchedway Earl’spay owslay advanceyay. Inyay erhay
asway isiblevay ethay ietay atthay unitedyay emthay. Eshay adhay eenbay offeredyay otay ethay
orldway, esethay evensay yearsyay astpay, asyay ethay ivinglay ieroglyphichay, inyay ichwhay
asway evealedray ethay ecretsay eythay osay arklyday oughtsay otay ide,—allhay ittenwray inyay
isthay ymbol,—allsay ainlyplay anifest,—hadmay erethay eenbay ayay ophetpray oryay
agicianmay illedskay otay eadray ethay aracterchay ofyay ameflay! Andyay Earlpay asway ethay
onenessyay ofyay eirthay eingbay. Ebay ethay oregonefay evilyay atwhay ityay ightmay, owhay ouldcay
eythay oubtday atthay eirthay earthlyyay iveslay andyay uturefay estiniesday ereway
onjoinedcay, enwhay eythay eheldbay atyay onceyay ethay aterialmay unionyay, andyay ethay
iritualspay ideayay, inyay omwhay eythay etmay, andyay ereway otay elldway immortallyyay
ogethertay? Oughtsthay ikelay ese—andthay erhapspay otheryay oughtsthay, ichwhay eythay
idday otnay acknowledgeyay oryay efine—threwday anyay aweyay aboutyay ethay ildchay, asyay eshay
amecay onwardyay.

et“lay erhay eesay othingnay ange—nostray assionpay ornay eagerness—inyay ythay ayway ofyay
accostingyay erhay,” isperedwhay Esterhay. our“ay Earlpay isyay ayay itfulfay andyay antasticfay
ittlelay elfyay, ometimessay. Especiallyyay, eshay isyay eldomsay oleranttay ofyay emotionyay,
enwhay eshay oesday otnay ullyfay omprehendcay ethay ywhay andyay ereforewhay. Utbay ethay
ildchay athhay ongstray affectionsyay! Eshay oveslay emay, andyay illway ovelay eethay!”

ou“thay anstcay otnay inkthay,” aidsay ethay inistermay, ancingglay asideyay atyay Esterhay
Ynnepray, ow“hay ymay earthay eadsdray isthay interviewyay, andyay yearnsyay orfay ityay! Utbay,
inyay uthtray, asyay Iyay alreadyyay oldtay eethay, ildrenchay areyay otnay eadilyray onway otay ebay
amiliarfay ithway emay. Eythay illway otnay imbclay ymay eeknay, ornay attlepray inyay ymay earyay,
ornay answeryay otay ymay ilesmay; utbay andstay apartyay, andyay eyeyay emay angelystray. Evenyay
ittlelay abesbay, enwhay Iyay aketay emthay inyay ymay armsyay, eepway itterlybay. Yetyay Earlpay,
icetway inyay erhay ittlelay ifetimelay, athhay eenbay indkay otay emay! Ethay irstfay
ime,—thoutay owestknay ityay ellway! Ethay astlay asway enwhay outhay edstlay erhay ithway
eethay otay ethay ousehay ofyay yonderyay ernstay oldyay Overnorgay.”

and“ay outhay idstday eadplay osay avelybray inyay erhay ehalfbay andyay inemay!” answeredyay ethay
othermay. i“ay ememberray ityay; andyay osay allshay ittlelay Earlpay. Earfay othingnay! Eshay
aymay ebay angestray andyay yshay atyay irstfay, utbay illway oonsay earnlay otay ovelay eethay!”

Ybay isthay imetay Earlpay adhay eachedray ethay arginmay ofyay ethay ookbray, andyay oodstay onyay
ethay artherfay idesay, azinggay ilentlysay atyay Esterhay andyay ethay ergymanclay, owhay
illstay atsay ogethertay onyay ethay ossymay ee-trunktray, aitingway otay eceiveray erhay.
Ustjay erewhay eshay adhay ausedpay, ethay ookbray ancedchay otay ormfay ayay oolpay, osay oothsmay
andyay uietqay atthay ityay eflectedray ayay erfectpay imageyay ofyay erhay ittlelay igurefay, ithway
allyay ethay illiantbray icturesquenesspay ofyay erhay eautybay, inyay itsyay adornmentyay ofyay
owersflay andyay eathedwray oliagefay, utbay oremay efinedray andyay iritualizedspay anthay
ethay ealityray. Isthay imageyay, osay earlynay identicalyay ithway ethay ivinglay Earlpay,
eemedsay otay ommunicatecay omewhatsay ofyay itsyay ownyay adowyshay andyay intangibleyay
ualityqay otay ethay ildchay erselfhay. Ityay asway angestray, ethay ayway inyay ichwhay Earlpay
oodstay, ookinglay osay eadfastlystay atyay emthay oughthray ethay imday ediummay ofyay ethay
orest-gloomfay; erselfhay, eanwhilemay, allyay orifiedglay ithway ayay ayray ofyay
unshinesay, atthay asway attractedyay itherwardthay asyay ybay ayay ertaincay ympathysay. Inyay
ethay ookbray eneathbay oodstay anotheryay ild,—anotherchay andyay ethay ame,—withsay
ikewiselay itsyay ayray ofyay oldengay ightlay. Esterhay eltfay erselfhay, inyay omesay
indistinctyay andyay antalizingtay annermay, estrangedyay omfray Earlpay; asyay ifyay ethay
ildchay, inyay erhay onelylay ambleray oughthray ethay orestfay, adhay ayedstray outyay ofyay ethay
eresphay inyay ichwhay eshay andyay erhay othermay eltdway ogethertay, andyay asway ownay ainlyvay
eekingsay otay eturnray otay ityay.

Erethay asway othbay uthtray andyay erroryay inyay ethay impressionyay; ethay ildchay andyay
othermay ereway estrangedyay, utbay oughthray Ester’shay aultfay, otnay Earl’spay. Incesay
ethay atterlay ambledray omfray erhay idesay, anotheryay inmateyay adhay eenbay admittedyay
ithinway ethay irclecay ofyay ethay other’smay eelingsfay, andyay osay odifiedmay ethay aspectyay
ofyay emthay allyay, atthay Earlpay, ethay eturningray andererway, ouldcay otnay indfay erhay
ontedway aceplay, andyay ardlyhay ewknay erewhay eshay asway.

i“ay avehay ayay angestray ancyfay,” observedyay ethay ensitivesay inistermay, at“thay isthay
ookbray isyay ethay oundarybay etweenbay otway orldsway, andyay atthay outhay anstcay evernay
eetmay ythay Earlpay againyay. Oryay isyay eshay anyay elfishyay iritspay, owhay, asyay ethay egendslay
ofyay ouryay ildhoodchay aughttay usyay, isyay orbiddenfay otay osscray ayay unningray eamstray?
Aypray astenhay erhay; orfay isthay elayday ashay alreadyyay impartedyay ayay emortray otay ymay
ervesnay.”

ome“cay, earestday ildchay!” aidsay Esterhay, encouraginglyyay, andyay etchingstray outyay
othbay erhay armsyay. ow“hay owslay outhay artyay! Enwhay asthay outhay eenbay osay uggishslay
eforebay ownay? Erehay isyay ayay iendfray ofyay inemay, owhay ustmay ebay ythay iendfray alsoyay.
Outhay iltway avehay icetway asyay uchmay ovelay, enceforwardhay, asyay ythay othermay aloneyay
ouldcay ivegay eethay! Eaplay acrossyay ethay ookbray, andyay omecay otay usyay. Outhay anstcay
eaplay ikelay ayay youngyay eerday!”

illustration[ay: Ethay Ildchay atyay ethay Ook-sidebray]

Earlpay, ithoutway espondingray inyay anyyay annermay otay esethay oney-sweethay
expressionsyay, emainedray onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay ookbray. Ownay eshay ixedfay
erhay ightbray, ildway eyesyay onyay erhay othermay, ownay onyay ethay inistermay, andyay ownay
includedyay emthay othbay inyay ethay amesay anceglay; asyay ifyay otay etectday andyay explainyay otay
erselfhay ethay elationray ichwhay eythay orebay otay oneyay anotheryay. Orfay omesay
unaccountableyay easonray, asyay Arthuryay Immesdaleday eltfay ethay ild’schay eyesyay uponyay
imselfhay, ishay and—withhay atthay esturegay osay abitualhay asyay otay avehay ecomebay
involuntary—stoleyay overyay ishay earthay. Atyay engthlay, assumingyay ayay ingularsay airyay
ofyay authorityyay, Earlpay etchedstray outyay erhay andhay, ithway ethay allsmay orefingerfay
extendedyay, andyay ointingpay evidentlyyay owardstay erhay other’smay eastbray. Andyay
eneathbay, inyay ethay irrormay ofyay ethay ookbray, erethay asway ethay ower-girdledflay andyay
unnysay imageyay ofyay ittlelay Earlpay, ointingpay erhay allsmay orefingerfay ootay.

ou“thay angestray ildchay, ywhay ostday outhay otnay omecay otay emay?” exclaimedyay Esterhay.

Earlpay illstay ointedpay ithway erhay orefingerfay; andyay ayay ownfray atheredgay onyay erhay
owbray; ethay oremay impressiveyay omfray ethay ildishchay, ethay almostyay aby-likebay
aspectyay ofyay ethay eaturesfay atthay onveyedcay ityay. Asyay erhay othermay illstay eptkay
eckoningbay otay erhay, andyay arrayingyay erhay acefay inyay ayay olidayhay uitsay ofyay
unaccustomedyay ilessmay, ethay ildchay ampedstay erhay ootfay ithway ayay yetyay oremay
imperiousyay ooklay andyay esturegay. Inyay ethay ookbray, againyay, asway ethay antasticfay
eautybay ofyay ethay imageyay, ithway itsyay eflectedray ownfray, itsyay ointedpay ingerfay, andyay
imperiousyay esturegay, ivinggay emphasisyay otay ethay aspectyay ofyay ittlelay Earlpay.

asten“hay, Earlpay; oryay Iyay allshay ebay angryyay ithway eethay!” iedcray Esterhay Ynnepray,
owhay, oweverhay inuredyay otay uchsay ehaviorbay onyay ethay elf-child’syay artpay atyay otheryay
easonssay, asway aturallynay anxiousyay orfay ayay oremay eemlysay eportmentday ownay. eap“lay
acrossyay ethay ookbray, aughtynay ildchay, andyay unray itherhay! Elseyay Iyay ustmay omecay otay
eethay!”

Utbay Earlpay, otnay ayay itwhay artledstay atyay erhay other’smay eatsthray, anyyay oremay anthay
ollifiedmay ybay erhay entreatiesyay, ownay uddenlysay urstbay intoyay ayay itfay ofyay assionpay,
esticulatinggay iolentlyvay, andyay owingthray erhay allsmay igurefay intoyay ethay ostmay
extravagantyay ontortionscay. Eshay accompaniedyay isthay ildway outbreakyay ithway
iercingpay ieksshray, ichwhay ethay oodsway everberatedray onyay allyay idessay; osay atthay,
aloneyay asyay eshay asway inyay erhay ildishchay andyay unreasonableyay athwray, ityay eemedsay asyay
ifyay ayay iddenhay ultitudemay ereway endinglay erhay eirthay ympathysay andyay
encouragementyay. Eensay inyay ethay ookbray, onceyay oremay, asway ethay adowyshay athwray ofyay
Earl’spay imageyay, ownedcray andyay irdledgay ithway owersflay, utbay ampingstay itsyay
ootfay, ildlyway esticulatinggay, andyay, inyay ethay idstmay ofyay allyay, illstay ointingpay
itsyay allsmay orefingerfay atyay Ester’shay osombay!

i“ay eesay atwhay ailsyay ethay ildchay,” isperedwhay Esterhay otay ethay ergymanclay, andyay
urningtay alepay inyay itespay ofyay ayay ongstray effortyay otay oncealcay erhay oubletray andyay
annoyanceyay. ildren“chay illway otnay abideyay anyyay, ethay ightestslay, angechay inyay ethay
accustomedyay aspectyay ofyay ingsthay atthay areyay ailyday eforebay eirthay eyesyay. Earlpay
issesmay omethingsay ichwhay eshay ashay alwaysyay eensay emay earway!”

i“ay aypray youyay,” answeredyay ethay inistermay, if“ay outhay asthay anyyay eansmay ofyay
acifyingpay ethay ildchay, oday ityay orthwithfay! Avesay ityay ereway ethay ankeredcay athwray
ofyay anyay oldyay itchway, ikelay Istressmay Ibbinshay,” addedyay ehay, attemptingyay otay
ilesmay, i“ay owknay othingnay atthay Iyay ouldway otnay oonersay encounteryay anthay isthay
assionpay inyay ayay ildchay. Inyay Earl’spay youngyay eautybay, asyay inyay ethay inkledwray itchway,
ityay ashay ayay eternaturalpray effectyay. Acifypay erhay, ifyay outhay ovestlay emay!”

Esterhay urnedtay againyay owardstay Earlpay, ithway ayay imsoncray ushblay uponyay erhay
eekchay, ayay onsciouscay anceglay asideyay atyay ethay ergymanclay, andyay enthay ayay eavyhay
ighsay; ilewhay, evenyay eforebay eshay adhay imetay otay eakspay, ethay ushblay yieldedyay otay ayay
eadlyday allorpay.

earl“pay,” aidsay eshay, adlysay, ook“lay ownday atyay ythay eetfay! Ere!—beforethay
ee!—onthay ethay itherhay idesay ofyay ethay ookbray!”

Ethay ildchay urnedtay erhay eyesyay otay ethay ointpay indicatedyay; andyay erethay aylay ethay
arletscay etterlay, osay oseclay uponyay ethay arginmay ofyay ethay eamstray, atthay ethay oldgay
embroideryyay asway eflectedray inyay ityay.

ing“bray ityay itherhay!” aidsay Esterhay.

ome“cay outhay andyay aketay ityay upyay!” answeredyay Earlpay.

as“way everyay uchsay ayay ildchay!” observedyay Esterhay, asideyay otay ethay inistermay. o“ay, Iyay
avehay uchmay otay elltay eethay aboutyay erhay! Utbay, inyay eryvay uthtray, eshay isyay ightray asyay
egardsray isthay atefulhay okentay. Iyay ustmay earbay itsyay orturetay yetyay ayay ittlelay
onger,—onlylay ayay ewfay aysday onger,—untillay eway allshay avehay eftlay isthay
egionray, andyay ooklay ackbay itherhay asyay otay ayay andlay ichwhay eway avehay eameddray ofyay.
Ethay orestfay annotcay idehay ityay! Ethay id-oceanmay allshay aketay ityay omfray ymay andhay,
andyay allowsway ityay upyay oreverfay!”

Ithway esethay ordsway, eshay advancedyay otay ethay arginmay ofyay ethay ookbray, ooktay upyay ethay
arletscay etterlay, andyay astenedfay ityay againyay intoyay erhay osombay. Opefullyhay, utbay ayay
omentmay agoyay, asyay Esterhay adhay okenspay ofyay owningdray ityay inyay ethay eepday easay, erethay
asway ayay ensesay ofyay inevitableyay oomday uponyay erhay, asyay eshay usthay eceivedray ackbay
isthay eadlyday ymbolsay omfray ethay andhay ofyay atefay. Eshay adhay ungflay ityay intoyay
infiniteyay ace!—shespay adhay awndray anyay our’shay eefray eath!—andbray erehay againyay
asway ethay arletscay iserymay, itteringglay onyay ethay oldyay otspay! Osay ityay everyay isyay,
etherwhay usthay ypifiedtay oryay onay, atthay anyay evilyay eedday investsyay itselfyay ithway ethay
aracterchay ofyay oomday. Esterhay extnay atheredgay upyay ethay eavyhay essestray ofyay erhay
airhay, andyay onfinedcay emthay eneathbay erhay apcay. Asyay ifyay erethay ereway ayay itheringway
ellspay inyay ethay adsay etterlay, erhay eautybay, ethay armthway andyay ichnessray ofyay erhay
omanhoodway, epartedday, ikelay adingfay unshinesay; andyay ayay aygray adowshay eemedsay otay
allfay acrossyay erhay.

Enwhay ethay earydray angechay asway oughtwray, eshay extendedyay erhay andhay otay Earlpay.

ost“day outhay owknay ythay othermay ownay, ildchay?” askedyay eshay, eproachfullyray, utbay
ithway ayay ubduedsay onetay. ilt“way outhay omecay acrossyay ethay ookbray, andyay ownyay ythay
othermay, ownay atthay eshay ashay erhay ameshay uponyay er,—nowhay atthay eshay isyay adsay?”

yes“ay; ownay Iyay illway!” answeredyay ethay ildchay, oundingbay acrossyay ethay ookbray, andyay
aspingclay Esterhay inyay erhay armsyay. ow“nay outhay artyay ymay othermay indeedyay! Andyay Iyay amyay
ythay ittlelay Earlpay!”

Inyay ayay oodmay ofyay endernesstay atthay asway otnay usualyay ithway erhay, eshay ewdray ownday erhay
other’smay eadhay, andyay issedkay erhay owbray andyay othbay erhay eekschay. Utbay en—bythay ayay
indkay ofyay ecessitynay atthay alwaysyay impelledyay isthay ildchay otay alloyyay ateverwhay
omfortcay eshay ightmay ancechay otay ivegay ithway ayay obthray ofyay anguish—pearlyay utpay upyay
erhay outhmay, andyay issedkay ethay arletscay etterlay ootay!

at“thay asway otnay indkay!” aidsay Esterhay. en“whay outhay asthay ownshay emay ayay ittlelay
ovelay, outhay ockestmay emay!”

y“whay othday ethay inistermay itsay yonderyay?” askedyay Earlpay.

e“hay aitsway otay elcomeway eethay,” epliedray erhay othermay. ome“cay outhay, andyay
entreatyay ishay essingblay! Ehay oveslay eethay, ymay ittlelay Earlpay, andyay oveslay ythay
othermay ootay. Iltway outhay otnay ovelay imhay? Omecay! ehay ongslay otay eetgray eethay!”

oth“day ehay ovelay usyay?” aidsay Earlpay, ookinglay upyay, ithway acuteyay intelligenceyay,
intoyay erhay other’smay acefay. ill“way ehay ogay ackbay ithway usyay, andhay inyay andhay, eway
eethray ogethertay, intoyay ethay owntay?”

ot“nay ownay, earday ildchay,” answeredyay Esterhay. ut“bay inyay aysday otay omecay ehay illway
alkway andhay inyay andhay ithway usyay. Eway illway avehay ayay omehay andyay iresidefay ofyay ouryay
ownyay; andyay outhay altshay itsay uponyay ishay eeknay; andyay ehay illway eachtay eethay anymay
ingsthay, andyay ovelay eethay earlyday. Outhay iltway ovelay imhay; iltway outhay otnay?”

and“ay illway ehay alwaysyay eepkay ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay?” inquiredyay Earlpay.

oolish“fay ildchay, atwhay ayay uestionqay isyay atthay!” exclaimedyay erhay othermay. ome“cay
andyay askyay ishay essingblay!”

Utbay, etherwhay influencedyay ybay ethay ealousyjay atthay eemssay instinctiveyay ithway
everyyay ettedpay ildchay owardstay ayay angerousday ivalray, oryay omfray ateverwhay apricecay
ofyay erhay eakishfray aturenay, Earlpay ouldway owshay onay avorfay otay ethay ergymanclay. Ityay
asway onlyyay ybay anyay exertionyay ofyay orcefay atthay erhay othermay oughtbray erhay upyay otay
imhay, anginghay ackbay, andyay anifestingmay erhay eluctanceray ybay oddyay imacesgray; ofyay
ichwhay, everyay incesay erhay abyhoodbay, eshay adhay ossessedpay ayay ingularsay arietyvay,
andyay ouldcay ansformtray erhay obilemay ysiognomyphay intoyay ayay eriessay ofyay ifferentday
aspectsyay, ithway ayay ewnay ischiefmay inyay emthay, eachyay andyay allyay. Ethay
inister—painfullymay embarrassedyay, utbay opinghay atthay ayay isskay ightmay ovepray ayay
alismantay otay admityay imhay intoyay ethay ild’schay indlierkay egards—bentray orwardfay,
andyay impressedyay oneyay onyay erhay owbray. Ereuponhay, Earlpay okebray awayyay omfray erhay
othermay, andyay, unningray otay ethay ookbray, oopedstay overyay ityay, andyay athedbay erhay
oreheadfay, untilyay ethay unwelcomeyay isskay asway uiteqay ashedway offyay, andyay iffusedday
oughthray ayay onglay apselay ofyay ethay idingglay aterway. Eshay enthay emainedray apartyay,
ilentlysay atchingway Esterhay andyay ethay ergymanclay; ilewhay eythay alkedtay
ogethertay, andyay ademay uchsay arrangementsyay asyay ereway uggestedsay ybay eirthay ewnay
ositionpay, andyay ethay urposespay oonsay otay ebay ulfilledfay.

Andyay ownay isthay atefulfay interviewyay adhay omecay otay ayay oseclay. Ethay ellday asway otay ebay
eftlay ayay olitudesay amongyay itsyay arkday, oldyay eestray, ichwhay, ithway eirthay
ultitudinousmay onguestay, ouldway isperwhay onglay ofyay atwhay adhay assedpay erethay,
andyay onay ortalmay ebay ethay iserway. Andyay ethay elancholymay ookbray ouldway addyay isthay
otheryay aletay otay ethay ysterymay ithway ichwhay itsyay ittlelay earthay asway alreadyyay
overburdenedyay, andyay ereofwhay ityay illstay eptkay upyay ayay urmuringmay abblebay, ithway
otnay ayay itwhay oremay eerfulnesschay ofyay onetay anthay orfay agesyay eretoforehay.

illustration[ay]




                            illustration[ay]

                                  Xxay.

                        Ethay Inistermay Inyay Ayay Azemay.


Asyay ethay inistermay epartedday, inyay advanceyay ofyay Esterhay Ynnepray andyay ittlelay
Earlpay, ehay ewthray ayay ackwardbay anceglay; alfhay expectingyay atthay ehay ouldshay
iscoverday onlyyay omesay aintlyfay acedtray eaturesfay oryay outlineyay ofyay ethay othermay
andyay ethay ildchay, owlyslay adingfay intoyay ethay ilighttway ofyay ethay oodsway. Osay eatgray
ayay icissitudevay inyay ishay ifelay ouldcay otnay atyay onceyay ebay eceivedray asyay ealray. Utbay
erethay asway Esterhay, adclay inyay erhay aygray oberay, illstay andingstay esidebay ethay
ee-trunktray, ichwhay omesay astblay adhay overthrownyay ayay onglay antiquityyay agoyay, andyay
ichwhay imetay adhay everyay incesay eenbay overingcay ithway ossmay, osay atthay esethay otway
atedfay onesyay, ithway earth’syay eaviesthay urdenbay onyay emthay, ightmay erethay itsay ownday
ogethertay, andyay indfay ayay inglesay our’shay estray andyay olacesay. Andyay erethay asway
Earlpay, ootay, ightlylay ancingday omfray ethay arginmay ofyay ethay ook,—nowbray atthay
ethay intrusiveyay irdthay ersonpay asway one,—andgay akingtay erhay oldyay aceplay ybay erhay
other’smay idesay. Osay ethay inistermay adhay otnay allenfay asleepyay andyay eameddray!

Inyay orderyay otay eefray ishay indmay omfray isthay indistinctnessyay andyay uplicityday ofyay
impressionyay, ichwhay exedvay ityay ithway ayay angestray isquietudeday, ehay ecalledray andyay
oremay oroughlythay efinedday ethay ansplay ichwhay Esterhay andyay imselfhay adhay
etchedskay orfay eirthay epartureday. Ityay adhay eenbay eterminedday etweenbay emthay,
atthay ethay Oldyay Orldway, ithway itsyay owdscray andyay itiescay, offeredyay emthay ayay oremay
eligibleyay eltershay andyay oncealmentcay anthay ethay ildsway ofyay Ewnay Englandyay, oryay allyay
Americayay, ithway itsyay alternativesyay ofyay anyay Indianyay igwamway, oryay ethay ewfay
ettlementssay ofyay Europeansyay, atteredscay inlythay alongyay ethay eaboardsay. Otnay otay
eakspay ofyay ethay ergyman’sclay ealthhay, osay inadequateyay otay ustainsay ethay
ardshipshay ofyay ayay orestfay ifelay, ishay ativenay iftsgay, ishay ulturecay, andyay ishay
entireyay evelopmentday, ouldway ecuresay imhay ayay omehay onlyyay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay
ivilizationcay andyay efinementray; ethay igherhay ethay atestay, ethay oremay elicatelyday
adaptedyay otay ityay ethay anmay. Inyay urtherancefay ofyay isthay oicechay, ityay osay appenedhay
atthay ayay ipshay aylay inyay ethay arborhay; oneyay ofyay osethay uestionableqay uiserscray,
equentfray atyay atthay ayday, ichwhay, ithoutway eingbay absolutelyyay outlawsyay ofyay ethay
eepday, yetyay oamedray overyay itsyay urfacesay ithway ayay emarkableray irresponsibilityyay
ofyay aracterchay. Isthay esselvay adhay ecentlyray arrivedyay omfray ethay Anishspay Ainmay,
andyay, ithinway eethray aysday’ imetay, ouldway ailsay orfay Istolbray. Esterhay
Ynne—whosepray ocationvay, asyay ayay elf-enlistedsay Istersay ofyay Aritychay, adhay
oughtbray erhay acquaintedyay ithway ethay aptaincay andyay ew—couldcray aketay uponyay
erselfhay otay ecuresay ethay assagepay ofyay otway individualsyay andyay ayay ildchay, ithway allyay
ethay ecrecysay ichwhay ircumstancescay enderedray oremay anthay esirableday.

Ethay inistermay adhay inquiredyay ofyay Esterhay, ithway onay ittlelay interestyay, ethay
ecisepray imetay atyay ichwhay ethay esselvay ightmay ebay expectedyay otay epartday. Ityay ouldway
obablypray ebay onyay ethay ourthfay ayday omfray ethay esentpray. at“thay isyay ostmay
ortunatefay!” ehay adhay enthay aidsay otay imselfhay. Ownay, ywhay ethay Everendray Mray.
Immesdaleday onsideredcay ityay osay eryvay ortunatefay, eway esitatehay otay evealray.
Evertheless,—tonay oldhay othingnay ackbay omfray ethay eader,—itray asway ecausebay,
onyay ethay irdthay ayday omfray ethay esentpray, ehay asway otay eachpray ethay Electionyay
Ermonsay; andyay, asyay uchsay anyay occasionyay ormedfay anyay onorablehay epochyay inyay ethay ifelay
ofyay ayay Ewnay Englandyay ergymanclay, ehay ouldcay otnay avehay ancedchay uponyay ayay oremay
uitablesay odemay andyay imetay ofyay erminatingtay ishay ofessionalpray areercay. at“ay
eastlay, eythay allshay aysay ofyay emay,” oughtthay isthay exemplaryyay anmay, at“thay Iyay
eavelay onay ublicpay utyday unperformedyay, ornay illyay erformedpay!” Adsay, indeedyay,
atthay anyay introspectionyay osay ofoundpray andyay acuteyay asyay isthay oorpay inister’smay
ouldshay ebay osay iserablymay eceivedday! Eway avehay adhay, andyay aymay illstay avehay,
orseway ingsthay otay elltay ofyay imhay; utbay onenay, eway apprehendyay, osay itiablypay eakway;
onay evidenceyay, atyay onceyay osay ightslay andyay irrefragableyay, ofyay ayay ubtlesay iseaseday,
atthay adhay onglay incesay egunbay otay eatyay intoyay ethay ealray ubstancesay ofyay ishay
aracterchay. Onay anmay, orfay anyyay onsiderablecay eriodpay, ancay earway oneyay acefay otay
imselfhay, andyay anotheryay otay ethay ultitudemay, ithoutway inallyfay ettinggay
ewilderedbay asyay otay ichwhay aymay ebay ethay uetray.

Ethay excitementyay ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday eelingsfay, asyay ehay eturnedray omfray ishay
interviewyay ithway Esterhay, entlay imhay unaccustomedyay ysicalphay energyyay, andyay
urriedhay imhay ownwardtay atyay ayay apidray acepay. Ethay athwaypay amongyay ethay oodsway
eemedsay ilderway, oremay uncouthyay ithway itsyay uderay aturalnay obstaclesyay, andyay esslay
oddentray ybay ethay ootfay ofyay anmay, anthay ehay ememberedray ityay onyay ishay outwardyay
ourneyjay. Utbay ehay eapedlay acrossyay ethay ashyplay acesplay, ustthray imselfhay
oughthray ethay ingingclay underbrushyay, imbedclay ethay ascentyay, ungedplay intoyay ethay
ollowhay, andyay overcameyay, inyay ortshay, allyay ethay ifficultiesday ofyay ethay acktray,
ithway anyay unweariableyay activityyay atthay astonishedyay imhay. Ehay ouldcay otnay utbay
ecallray owhay eeblyfay, andyay ithway atwhay equentfray ausespay orfay eathbray, ehay adhay
oiledtay overyay ethay amesay oundgray, onlyyay otway aysday eforebay. Asyay ehay ewdray earnay ethay
owntay, ehay ooktay anyay impressionyay ofyay angechay omfray ethay eriessay ofyay amiliarfay
objectsyay atthay esentedpray emselvesthay. Ityay eemedsay otnay yesterdayyay, otnay oneyay,
ornay otway, utbay anymay aysday, oryay evenyay yearsyay agoyay, incesay ehay adhay uittedqay emthay.
Erethay, indeedyay, asway eachyay ormerfay acetray ofyay ethay eetstray, asyay ehay ememberedray
ityay, andyay allyay ethay eculiaritiespay ofyay ethay ouseshay, ithway ethay ueday ultitudemay
ofyay able-peaksgay, andyay ayay eathercockway atyay everyyay ointpay erewhay ishay emorymay
uggestedsay oneyay. Otnay ethay esslay, oweverhay, amecay isthay importunatelyyay
obtrusiveyay ensesay ofyay angechay. Ethay amesay asway uetray asyay egardedray ethay
acquaintancesyay omwhay ehay etmay, andyay allyay ethay ell-knownway apesshay ofyay umanhay
ifelay, aboutyay ethay ittlelay owntay. Eythay ookedlay eithernay olderyay ornay youngeryay
ownay; ethay eardsbay ofyay ethay agedyay ereway onay iterwhay, ornay ouldcay ethay eepingcray
abebay ofyay yesterdayyay alkway onyay ishay eetfay o-daytay; ityay asway impossibleyay otay
escribeday inyay atwhay espectray eythay ifferedday omfray ethay individualsyay onyay omwhay ehay
adhay osay ecentlyray estowedbay ayay artingpay anceglay; andyay yetyay ethay inister’smay
eepestday ensesay eemedsay otay informyay imhay ofyay eirthay utabilitymay. Ayay imilarsay
impressionyay uckstray imhay ostmay emarkablyray, asyay ehay assedpay underyay ethay allsway ofyay
ishay ownyay urchchay. Ethay edificeyay adhay osay eryvay angestray, andyay yetyay osay amiliarfay,
anyay aspectyay, atthay Mray. Immesdale’sday indmay ibratedvay etweenbay otway ideasyay;
eitheryay atthay ehay adhay eensay ityay onlyyay inyay ayay eamdray ithertohay, oryay atthay ehay asway
erelymay eamingdray aboutyay ityay ownay.

Isthay enomenonphay, inyay ethay ariousvay apesshay ichwhay ityay assumedyay, indicatedyay onay
externalyay angechay, utbay osay uddensay andyay importantyay ayay angechay inyay ethay ectatorspay
ofyay ethay amiliarfay enescay, atthay ethay interveningyay acespay ofyay ayay inglesay ayday adhay
operatedyay onyay ishay onsciousnesscay ikelay ethay apselay ofyay yearsyay. Ethay inister’smay
ownyay illway, andyay Ester’shay illway, andyay ethay atefay atthay ewgray etweenbay emthay, adhay
oughtwray isthay ansformationtray. Ityay asway ethay amesay owntay asyay eretoforehay; utbay
ethay amesay inistermay eturnedray otnay omfray ethay orestfay. Ehay ightmay avehay aidsay otay
ethay iendsfray owhay eetedgray im,—“ihay amyay otnay ethay anmay orfay omwhay youyay aketay emay!
Iyay eftlay imhay yonderyay inyay ethay orestfay, ithdrawnway intoyay ayay ecretsay ellday, ybay ayay
ossymay ee-trunktray, andyay earnay ayay elancholymay ookbray! Ogay, eeksay youryay inistermay,
andyay eesay ifyay ishay emaciatedyay igurefay, ishay inthay eekchay, ishay itewhay, eavyhay,
ain-wrinkledpay owbray, ebay otnay ungflay ownday erethay, ikelay ayay ast-offcay
armentgay!” Ishay iendsfray, onay oubtday, ouldway illstay avehay insistedyay ithway
im,—“thouhay artyay yselfthay ethay an!”—butmay ethay erroryay ouldway avehay eenbay eirthay
ownyay, otnay ishay.

Eforebay Mray. Immesdaleday eachedray omehay, ishay inneryay anmay avegay imhay otheryay
evidencesyay ofyay ayay evolutionray inyay ethay eresphay ofyay oughtthay andyay eelingfay. Inyay
uthtray, othingnay ortshay ofyay ayay otaltay angechay ofyay ynastyday andyay oralmay odecay, inyay
atthay interioryay ingdomkay, asway adequateyay otay accountyay orfay ethay impulsesyay ownay
ommunicatedcay otay ethay unfortunateyay andyay artledstay inistermay. Atyay everyyay epstay
ehay asway incitedyay otay oday omesay angestray, ildway, ickedway ingthay oryay otheryay, ithway ayay
ensesay atthay ityay ouldway ebay atyay onceyay involuntaryyay andyay intentionalyay; inyay itespay
ofyay imselfhay, yetyay owinggray outyay ofyay ayay ofounderpray elfsay anthay atthay ichwhay
opposedyay ethay impulseyay. Orfay instanceyay, ehay etmay oneyay ofyay ishay ownyay eaconsday. Ethay
oodgay oldyay anmay addressedyay imhay ithway ethay aternalpay affectionyay andyay atriarchalpay
ivilegepray, ichwhay ishay enerablevay ageyay, ishay uprightyay andyay olyhay aracterchay,
andyay ishay ationstay inyay ethay Urchchay, entitledyay imhay otay useyay; andyay, onjoinedcay
ithway isthay, ethay eepday, almostyay orshippingway espectray, ichwhay ethay inister’smay
ofessionalpray andyay ivatepray aimsclay alikeyay emandedday. Evernay asway erethay ayay oremay
eautifulbay exampleyay ofyay owhay ethay ajestymay ofyay ageyay andyay isdomway aymay omportcay
ithway ethay obeisanceyay andyay espectray enjoinedyay uponyay ityay, asyay omfray ayay owerlay
ocialsay ankray, andyay inferioryay orderyay ofyay endowmentyay, owardstay ayay igherhay. Ownay,
uringday ayay onversationcay ofyay omesay otway oryay eethray omentsmay etweenbay ethay
Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday andyay isthay excellentyay andyay oary-beardedhay eaconday,
ityay asway onlyyay ybay ethay ostmay arefulcay elf-controlsay atthay ethay ormerfay ouldcay
efrainray omfray utteringyay ertaincay asphemousblay uggestionssay atthay oseray intoyay
ishay indmay, espectingray ethay ommunioncay uppersay. Ehay absolutelyyay embledtray andyay
urnedtay alepay asyay ashesyay, estlay ishay onguetay ouldshay agway itselfyay, inyay utteranceyay
ofyay esethay orriblehay attersmay, andyay eadplay ishay ownyay onsentcay orfay osay oingday,
ithoutway ishay avinghay airlyfay ivengay ityay. Andyay, evenyay ithway isthay errortay inyay ishay
earthay, ehay ouldcay ardlyhay avoidyay aughinglay, otay imagineyay owhay ethay anctifiedsay
oldyay atriarchalpay eaconday ouldway avehay eenbay etrifiedpay ybay ishay inister’smay
impietyyay!

Againyay, anotheryay incidentyay ofyay ethay amesay aturenay. Urryinghay alongyay ethay eetstray,
ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday encounteredyay ethay eldestyay emalefay embermay ofyay
ishay urchchay; ayay ostmay iouspay andyay exemplaryyay oldyay ameday; oorpay, idowedway,
onelylay, andyay ithway ayay earthay asyay ullfay ofyay eminiscencesray aboutyay erhay eadday
usbandhay andyay ildrenchay, andyay erhay eadday iendsfray ofyay onglay agoyay, asyay ayay
urial-groundbay isyay ullfay ofyay oriedstay avestonesgray. Yetyay allyay isthay, ichwhay
ouldway elseyay avehay eenbay uchsay eavyhay orrowsay, asway ademay almostyay ayay olemnsay oyjay
otay erhay evoutday oldyay oulsay, ybay eligiousray onsolationscay andyay ethay uthstray ofyay
Ipturescray, erewithwhay eshay adhay edfay erselfhay ontinuallycay orfay oremay anthay
irtythay yearsyay. Andyay, incesay Mray. Immesdaleday adhay akentay erhay inyay argechay, ethay
oodgay andam’sgray iefchay earthlyyay omfort—whichcay, unlessyay ityay adhay eenbay
ikewiselay ayay eavenlyhay omfortcay, ouldcay avehay eenbay onenay atyay all—wasyay otay eetmay
erhay astorpay, etherwhay asuallycay, oryay ofyay etsay urposepay, andyay ebay efreshedray ithway
ayay ordway ofyay armway, agrantfray, eaven-breathinghay Ospelgay uthtray, omfray ishay
elovedbay ipslay, intoyay erhay ulledday, utbay apturouslyray attentiveyay earyay. Utbay, onyay
isthay occasionyay, upyay otay ethay omentmay ofyay uttingpay ishay ipslay otay ethay oldyay oman’sway
earyay, Mray. Immesdaleday, asyay ethay eatgray enemyyay ofyay oulssay ouldway avehay ityay, ouldcay
ecallray onay exttay ofyay Ipturescray, ornay aughtyay elseyay, exceptyay ayay iefbray, ithypay,
andyay, asyay ityay enthay appearedyay otay imhay, unanswerableyay argumentyay againstyay ethay
immortalityyay ofyay ethay umanhay oulsay. Ethay instilmentyay ereofthay intoyay erhay indmay
ouldway obablypray avehay ausedcay isthay agedyay istersay otay opdray ownday eadday, atyay
onceyay, asyay ybay ethay effectyay ofyay anyay intenselyyay oisonouspay infusionyay. Atwhay ehay
eallyray idday isperwhay, ethay inistermay ouldcay evernay afterwardsyay ecollectray.
Erethay asway, erhapspay, ayay ortunatefay isorderday inyay ishay utteranceyay, ichwhay
ailedfay otay impartyay anyyay istinctday ideayay otay ethay oodgay idow’sway omprehensioncay,
oryay ichwhay Ovidencepray interpretedyay afteryay ayay ethodmay ofyay itsyay ownyay. Assuredlyyay,
asyay ethay inistermay ookedlay ackbay, ehay eheldbay anyay expressionyay ofyay ivineday
atitudegray andyay ecstasyyay atthay eemedsay ikelay ethay ineshay ofyay ethay elestialcay itycay
onyay erhay acefay, osay inkledwray andyay ashyyay alepay.

Againyay, ayay irdthay instanceyay. Afteryay artingpay omfray ethay oldyay urch-memberchay, ehay
etmay ethay youngestyay istersay ofyay emthay allyay. Ityay asway ayay aidenmay ewlynay on—andway
onway ybay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdale’sday ownyay ermonsay, onyay ethay Abbathsay afteryay
ishay igil—tovay arterbay ethay ansitorytray easuresplay ofyay ethay orldway orfay ethay
eavenlyhay opehay, atthay asway otay assumeyay ighterbray ubstancesay asyay ifelay ewgray arkday
aroundyay erhay, andyay ichwhay ouldway ildgay ethay utteryay oomglay ithway inalfay oryglay. Eshay
asway airfay andyay urepay asyay ayay ilylay atthay adhay oomedblay inyay Aradisepay. Ethay inistermay
ewknay ellway atthay ehay asway imselfhay enshrinedyay ithinway ethay ainlessstay anctitysay
ofyay erhay earthay, ichwhay unghay itsyay owysnay urtainscay aboutyay ishay imageyay, impartingyay
otay eligionray ethay armthway ofyay ovelay, andyay otay ovelay ayay eligiousray uritypay. Atansay,
atthay afternoonyay, adhay urelysay edlay ethay oorpay youngyay irlgay awayyay omfray erhay
other’smay idesay, andyay ownthray erhay intoyay ethay athwaypay ofyay isthay orelysay emptedtay,
or—shallyay eway otnay atherray ay?—thissay ostlay andyay esperateday anmay. Asyay eshay ewdray
ighnay, ethay arch-fiendyay isperedwhay imhay otay ondensecay intoyay allsmay ompasscay andyay
opdray intoyay erhay endertay osombay ayay ermgay ofyay evilyay atthay ouldway ebay uresay otay
ossomblay arklyday oonsay, andyay earbay ackblay uitfray etimesbay. Uchsay asway ishay ensesay
ofyay owerpay overyay isthay irginvay oulsay, ustingtray imhay asyay eshay idday, atthay ethay
inistermay eltfay otentpay otay ightblay allyay ethay ieldfay ofyay innocenceyay ithway utbay oneyay
ickedway ooklay, andyay evelopday allyay itsyay oppositeyay ithway utbay ayay ordway. O—withsay ayay
ightiermay ugglestray anthay ehay adhay yetyay ustained—hesay eldhay ishay Enevagay oakclay
eforebay ishay acefay, andyay urriedhay onwardyay, akingmay onay ignsay ofyay ecognitionray,
andyay eavinglay ethay youngyay istersay otay igestday ishay udenessray asyay eshay ightmay. Eshay
ansackedray erhay onscience,—whichcay asway ullfay ofyay armlesshay ittlelay attersmay,
ikelay erhay ocketpay oryay erhay ork-bag,—andway ooktay erselfhay otay asktay, oorpay
ingthay! orfay ayay ousandthay imaginaryyay aultsfay; andyay entway aboutyay erhay ouseholdhay
utiesday ithway ollensway eyelidsyay ethay extnay orningmay.

Eforebay ethay inistermay adhay imetay otay elebratecay ishay ictoryvay overyay isthay astlay
emptationtay, ehay asway onsciouscay ofyay anotheryay impulseyay, oremay udicrouslay, andyay
almostyay asyay orriblehay. Ityay as,—weway ushblay otay elltay it,—ityay asway otay opstay
ortshay inyay ethay oadray, andyay eachtay omesay eryvay ickedway ordsway otay ayay otknay ofyay
ittlelay Uritanpay ildrenchay owhay ereway ayingplay erethay, andyay adhay utbay ustjay egunbay
otay alktay. Enyingday imselfhay isthay eakfray, asyay unworthyyay ofyay ishay othclay, ehay etmay
ayay unkendray eamansay, oneyay ofyay ethay ip’sshay ewcray omfray ethay Anishspay Ainmay. Andyay,
erehay, incesay ehay adhay osay aliantlyvay orbornefay allyay otheryay ickednessway, oorpay
Mray. Immesdaleday ongedlay, atyay eastlay, otay akeshay andshay ithway ethay arrytay
ackguardblay, andyay ecreateray imselfhay ithway ayay ewfay improperyay estsjay, uchsay asyay
issoluteday ailorssay osay aboundyay ithway, andyay ayay olleyvay ofyay oodgay, oundray, olidsay,
atisfactorysay, andyay eaven-defyinghay oathsyay! Ityay asway otnay osay uchmay ayay etterbay
inciplepray asyay artlypay ishay aturalnay oodgay astetay, andyay illstay oremay ishay
uckramedbay abithay ofyay ericalclay ecorumday, atthay arriedcay imhay afelysay oughthray
ethay atterlay isiscray.

at“whay isyay ityay atthay auntshay andyay emptstay emay usthay?” iedcray ethay inistermay otay
imselfhay, atyay engthlay, ausingpay inyay ethay eetstray, andyay ikingstray ishay andhay
againstyay ishay oreheadfay. am“ay Iyay admay? oryay amyay Iyay ivengay overyay utterlyyay otay ethay
iendfay? Idday Iyay akemay ayay ontractcay ithway imhay inyay ethay orestfay, andyay ignsay ityay ithway
ymay oodblay? Andyay oesday ehay ownay ummonsay emay otay itsyay ulfilmentfay, ybay uggestingsay
ethay erformancepay ofyay everyyay ickednessway ichwhay ishay ostmay oulfay imaginationyay
ancay onceivecay?”

Atyay ethay omentmay enwhay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday usthay ommunedcay ithway
imselfhay, andyay uckstray ishay oreheadfay ithway ishay andhay, oldyay Istressmay Ibbinshay,
ethay eputedray itch-ladyway, isyay aidsay otay avehay eenbay assingpay ybay. Eshay ademay ayay
eryvay andgray appearanceyay; avinghay onyay ayay ighhay ead-dresshay, ayay ichray owngay ofyay
elvetvay, andyay ayay uffray oneday upyay ithway ethay amousfay yellowyay archstay, ofyay ichwhay Annyay
Urnertay, erhay especialyay iendfray, adhay aughttay erhay ethay ecretsay, eforebay isthay
astlay oodgay adylay adhay eenbay angedhay orfay Irsay Omasthay Overbury’syay urdermay.
Etherwhay ethay itchway adhay eadray ethay inister’smay oughtsthay, oryay onay, eshay amecay otay
ayay ullfay opstay, ookedlay ewdlyshray intoyay ishay acefay, iledsmay aftilycray,
and—thoughyay ittlelay ivengay otay onversecay ithway ergymen—beganclay ayay
onversationcay.

o“say, everendray Irsay, youyay avehay ademay ayay isitvay intoyay ethay orestfay,” observedyay
ethay itch-ladyway, oddingnay erhay ighhay ead-dresshay atyay imhay. e“thay extnay imetay, Iyay
aypray youyay otay allowyay emay onlyyay ayay airfay arningway, andyay Iyay allshay ebay oudpray otay earbay
youyay ompanycay. Ithoutway akingtay overmuchyay uponyay yselfmay, ymay oodgay ordway illway ogay
arfay owardstay aininggay anyyay angestray entlemangay ayay airfay eceptionray omfray yonderyay
otentatepay youyay otway ofyay!”

i“ay ofesspray, adammay,” answeredyay ethay ergymanclay, ithway ayay avegray obeisanceyay,
uchsay asyay ethay ady’slay ankray emandedday, andyay ishay ownyay ood-breedinggay ademay
imperative,—“iyay ofesspray, onyay ymay onsciencecay andyay aracterchay, atthay Iyay amyay
utterlyyay ewilderedbay asyay ouchingtay ethay urportpay ofyay youryay ordsway! Iyay entway otnay
intoyay ethay orestfay otay eeksay ayay otentatepay; eithernay oday Iyay, atyay anyyay uturefay imetay,
esignday ayay isitvay itherthay, ithway ayay iewvay otay aininggay ethay avorfay ofyay uchsay ayay
ersonagepay. Ymay oneyay ufficientsay objectyay asway otay eetgray atthay iouspay iendfray ofyay
inemay, ethay Apostleyay Eliotyay, andyay ejoiceray ithway imhay overyay ethay anymay eciouspray
oulssay ehay athhay onway omfray eathendomhay!”

a“hay, ahay, ahay!” ackledcay ethay oldyay itch-ladyway, illstay oddingnay erhay ighhay
ead-dresshay atyay ethay inistermay. ell“way, ellway, eway ustmay eedsnay alktay usthay inyay
ethay aytimeday! Youyay arrycay ityay offyay ikelay anyay oldyay andhay! Utbay atyay idnightmay, andyay
inyay ethay orestfay, eway allshay avehay otheryay alktay ogethertay!”

Eshay assedpay onyay ithway erhay agedyay atelinessstay, utbay oftenyay urningtay ackbay erhay
eadhay andyay ilingsmay atyay imhay, ikelay oneyay illingway otay ecognizeray ayay ecretsay
intimacyyay ofyay onnectioncay.

ave“hay Iyay enthay oldsay yselfmay,” oughtthay ethay inistermay, o“tay ethay iendfay omwhay,
ifyay enmay aysay uetray, isthay yellow-starchedyay andyay elvetedvay oldyay aghay ashay osenchay
orfay erhay incepray andyay astermay!”

Ethay etchedwray inistermay! Ehay adhay ademay ayay argainbay eryvay ikelay ityay! Emptedtay ybay
ayay eamdray ofyay appinesshay, ehay adhay yieldedyay imselfhay, ithway eliberateday oicechay,
asyay ehay adhay evernay oneday eforebay, otay atwhay ehay ewknay asway eadlyday insay. Andyay ethay
infectiousyay oisonpay ofyay atthay insay adhay eenbay usthay apidlyray iffusedday
oughoutthray ishay oralmay ystemsay. Ityay adhay upefiedstay allyay essedblay impulsesyay,
andyay awakenedyay intoyay ividvay ifelay ethay olewhay otherhoodbray ofyay adbay onesyay. Ornscay,
itternessbay, unprovokedyay alignitymay, atuitousgray esireday ofyay illyay, idiculeray
ofyay ateverwhay asway oodgay andyay olyhay, allyay awokeyay, otay empttay, evenyay ilewhay eythay
ightenedfray imhay. Andyay ishay encounteryay ithway oldyay Istressmay Ibbinshay, ifyay ityay
ereway ayay ealray incidentyay, idday utbay owshay ishay ympathysay andyay ellowshipfay ithway
ickedway ortalsmay, andyay ethay orldway ofyay ervertedpay iritsspay.

Ehay adhay, ybay isthay imetay, eachedray ishay ellingdway, onyay ethay edgeyay ofyay ethay
urial-groundbay, andyay, asteninghay upyay ethay airsstay, ooktay efugeray inyay ishay udystay.
Ethay inistermay asway adglay otay avehay eachedray isthay eltershay, ithoutway irstfay
etrayingbay imselfhay otay ethay orldway ybay anyyay ofyay osethay angestray andyay ickedway
eccentricitiesyay otay ichwhay ehay adhay eenbay ontinuallycay impelledyay ilewhay assingpay
oughthray ethay eetsstray. Ehay enteredyay ethay accustomedyay oomray, andyay ookedlay aroundyay
imhay onyay itsyay ooksbay, itsyay indowsway, itsyay ireplacefay, andyay ethay apestriedtay
omfortcay ofyay ethay allsway, ithway ethay amesay erceptionpay ofyay angenessstray atthay adhay
auntedhay imhay oughoutthray ishay alkway omfray ethay orest-dellfay intoyay ethay owntay,
andyay itherwardthay. Erehay ehay adhay udiedstay andyay ittenwray; erehay, onegay oughthray
astfay andyay igilvay, andyay omecay orthfay alfhay aliveyay; erehay, ivenstray otay aypray;
erehay, ornebay ayay undredhay ousandthay agoniesyay! Erethay asway ethay Iblebay, inyay itsyay
ichray oldyay Ebrewhay, ithway Osesmay andyay ethay Ophetspray eakingspay otay imhay, andyay
Od’sgay oicevay oughthray allyay! Erethay, onyay ethay abletay, ithway ethay inkyyay enpay esidebay
ityay, asway anyay unfinishedyay ermonsay, ithway ayay entencesay okenbray inyay ethay idstmay,
erewhay ishay oughtsthay adhay easedcay otay ushgay outyay uponyay ethay agepay, otway aysday
eforebay. Ehay ewknay atthay ityay asway imselfhay, ethay inthay andyay ite-cheekedwhay
inistermay, owhay adhay oneday andyay ufferedsay esethay ingsthay, andyay ittenwray usthay arfay
intoyay ethay Electionyay Ermonsay! Utbay ehay eemedsay otay andstay apartyay, andyay eyeyay isthay
ormerfay elfsay ithway ornfulscay, ityingpay, utbay alf-envioushay uriositycay. Atthay
elfsay asway onegay. Anotheryay anmay adhay eturnedray outyay ofyay ethay orestfay; ayay iserway
oneyay; ithway ayay owledgeknay ofyay iddenhay ysteriesmay ichwhay ethay implicitysay ofyay ethay
ormerfay evernay ouldcay avehay eachedray. Ayay itterbay indkay ofyay owledgeknay atthay!

Ilewhay occupiedyay ithway esethay eflectionsray, ayay ockknay amecay atyay ethay oorday ofyay ethay
udystay, andyay ethay inistermay aidsay, ome“cay in!”—notyay ollywhay evoidday ofyay anyay ideayay
atthay ehay ightmay eholdbay anyay evilyay iritspay. Andyay osay ehay idday! Ityay asway oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay atthay enteredyay. Ethay inistermay oodstay, itewhay andyay eechlessspay,
ithway oneyay andhay onyay ethay Ebrewhay Ipturesscray, andyay ethay otheryay eadspray uponyay ishay
eastbray.

elcome“way omehay, everendray Irsay,” aidsay ethay ysicianphay. and“ay owhay oundfay youyay
atthay odlygay anmay, ethay Apostleyay Eliotyay? Utbay ethinksmay, earday Irsay, youyay ooklay
alepay; asyay ifyay ethay aveltray oughthray ethay ildernessway adhay eenbay ootay oresay orfay
youyay. Illway otnay ymay aidyay ebay equisiteray otay utpay youyay inyay earthay andyay engthstray otay
eachpray youryay Electionyay Ermonsay?”

ay“nay, Iyay inkthay otnay osay,” ejoinedray ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday. y“may
ourneyjay, andyay ethay ightsay ofyay ethay olyhay Apostleyay yonderyay, andyay ethay eefray airyay
ichwhay Iyay avehay eathedbray, avehay oneday emay oodgay, afteryay osay onglay onfinementcay inyay
ymay udystay. Iyay inkthay otay eednay onay oremay ofyay youryay ugsdray, ymay indkay ysicianphay,
oodgay oughthay eythay ebay, andyay administeredyay ybay ayay iendlyfray andhay.”

Allyay isthay imetay, Ogerray Illingworthchay asway ookinglay atyay ethay inistermay ithway
ethay avegray andyay intentyay egardray ofyay ayay ysicianphay owardstay ishay atientpay. Utbay,
inyay itespay ofyay isthay outwardyay owshay, ethay atterlay asway almostyay onvincedcay ofyay ethay
oldyay an’smay owledgeknay, oryay, atyay eastlay, ishay onfidentcay uspicionsay, ithway
espectray otay ishay ownyay interviewyay ithway Esterhay Ynnepray. Ethay ysicianphay ewknay
enthay, atthay, inyay ethay inister’smay egardray, ehay asway onay ongerlay ayay ustedtray
iendfray, utbay ishay itterestbay enemyyay. Osay uchmay eingbay ownknay, ityay ouldway appearyay
aturalnay atthay ayay artpay ofyay ityay ouldshay ebay expressedyay. Ityay isyay ingularsay,
oweverhay, owhay onglay ayay imetay oftenyay assespay eforebay ordsway embodyyay ingsthay; andyay
ithway atwhay ecuritysay otway ersonspay, owhay oosechay otay avoidyay ayay ertaincay ubjectsay,
aymay approachyay itsyay eryvay ergevay, andyay etireray ithoutway isturbingday ityay. Usthay,
ethay inistermay eltfay onay apprehensionyay atthay Ogerray Illingworthchay ouldway
ouchtay, inyay expressyay ordsway, uponyay ethay ealray ositionpay ichwhay eythay ustainedsay
owardstay oneyay anotheryay. Yetyay idday ethay ysicianphay, inyay ishay arkday ayway, eepcray
ightfullyfray earnay ethay ecretsay.

ere“way ityay otnay etterbay,” aidsay ehay, at“thay youyay useyay ymay oorpay illskay o-nighttay?
Erilyvay, earday Irsay, eway ustmay aketay ainspay otay akemay youyay ongstray andyay igorousvay
orfay isthay occasionyay ofyay ethay Electionyay iscourseday. Ethay eoplepay ooklay orfay eatgray
ingsthay omfray youyay; apprehendingyay atthay anotheryay yearyay aymay omecay aboutyay, andyay
indfay eirthay astorpay onegay.”

yea“ay, otay anotheryay orldway,” epliedray ethay inistermay, ithway iouspay esignationray.
eaven“hay antgray ityay ebay ayay etterbay oneyay; orfay, inyay oodgay oothsay, Iyay ardlyhay inkthay
otay arrytay ithway ymay ockflay oughthray ethay ittingflay easonssay ofyay anotheryay yearyay!
Utbay, ouchingtay youryay edicinemay, indkay Irsay, inyay ymay esentpray amefray ofyay odybay, Iyay
eednay ityay otnay.”

i“ay oyjay otay earhay ityay,” answeredyay ethay ysicianphay. it“ay aymay ebay atthay ymay
emediesray, osay onglay administeredyay inyay ainvay, eginbay ownay otay aketay ueday effectyay.
Appyhay anmay ereway Iyay, andyay ellway eservingday ofyay Ewnay England’syay atitudegray, ouldcay
Iyay achieveyay isthay urecay!”

i“ay ankthay youyay omfray ymay earthay, ostmay atchfulway iendfray,” aidsay ethay Everendray
Mray. Immesdaleday, ithway ayay olemnsay ilesmay. i“ay ankthay youyay, andyay ancay utbay equiteray
youryay oodgay eedsday ithway ymay ayerspray.”

a“ay oodgay an’smay ayerspray areyay oldengay ecompenseray!” ejoinedray oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay, asyay ehay ooktay ishay eavelay. yea“ay, eythay areyay ethay urrentcay oldgay
oincay ofyay ethay Ewnay Erusalemjay, ithway ethay Ing’skay ownyay int-markmay onyay emthay!”

Eftlay aloneyay, ethay inistermay ummonedsay ayay ervantsay ofyay ethay ousehay, andyay
equestedray oodfay, ichwhay, eingbay etsay eforebay imhay, ehay ateyay ithway avenousray
appetiteyay. Enthay, ingingflay ethay alreadyyay ittenwray agespay ofyay ethay Electionyay
Ermonsay intoyay ethay irefay, ehay orthwithfay eganbay anotheryay, ichwhay ehay otewray ithway
uchsay anyay impulsiveyay owflay ofyay oughtthay andyay emotionyay, atthay ehay anciedfay imselfhay
inspiredyay; andyay onlyyay onderedway atthay Eavenhay ouldshay eesay itfay otay ansmittray ethay
andgray andyay olemnsay usicmay ofyay itsyay oraclesyay oughthray osay oulfay anyay organ-pipeyay asyay
ehay. Oweverhay, eavinglay atthay ysterymay otay olvesay itselfyay, oryay ogay unsolvedyay
oreverfay, ehay ovedray ishay asktay onwardyay, ithway earnestyay astehay andyay ecstasyyay.
Usthay ethay ightnay edflay awayyay, asyay ifyay ityay ereway ayay ingedway eedstay, andyay ehay
areeringcay onyay ityay; orningmay amecay, andyay eepedpay, ushingblay, oughthray ethay
urtainscay; andyay atyay astlay unrisesay ewthray ayay oldengay eambay intoyay ethay udystay andyay
aidlay ityay ightray acrossyay ethay inister’smay edazzledbay eyesyay. Erethay ehay asway, ithway
ethay enpay illstay etweenbay ishay ingersfay, andyay ayay astvay, immeasurableyay acttray ofyay
ittenwray acespay ehindbay imhay!




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Ixxay.

                       Ethay Ewnay Englandyay Olidayhay.


Etimesbay inyay ethay orningmay ofyay ethay ayday onyay ichwhay ethay ewnay Overnorgay asway otay
eceiveray ishay officeyay atyay ethay andshay ofyay ethay eoplepay, Esterhay Ynnepray andyay
ittlelay Earlpay amecay intoyay ethay arket-placemay. Ityay asway alreadyyay ongedthray ithway
ethay aftsmencray andyay otheryay ebeianplay inhabitantsyay ofyay ethay owntay, inyay
onsiderablecay umbersnay; amongyay omwhay, ikewiselay, ereway anymay oughray iguresfay,
osewhay attireyay ofyay eer-skinsday arkedmay emthay asyay elongingbay otay omesay ofyay ethay
orestfay ettlementssay, ichwhay urroundedsay ethay ittlelay etropolismay ofyay ethay
olonycay.

Onyay isthay ublicpay olidayhay, asyay onyay allyay otheryay occasionsyay, orfay evensay yearsyay
astpay, Esterhay asway adclay inyay ayay armentgay ofyay oarsecay aygray othclay. Otnay oremay ybay
itsyay uehay anthay ybay omesay indescribableyay eculiaritypay inyay itsyay ashionfay, ityay adhay
ethay effectyay ofyay akingmay erhay adefay ersonallypay outyay ofyay ightsay andyay outlineyay;
ilewhay, againyay, ethay arletscay etterlay oughtbray erhay ackbay omfray isthay ilighttway
indistinctnessyay, andyay evealedray erhay underyay ethay oralmay aspectyay ofyay itsyay ownyay
illuminationyay. Erhay acefay, osay onglay amiliarfay otay ethay owns-peopletay, owedshay
ethay arblemay uietudeqay ichwhay eythay ereway accustomedyay otay eholdbay erethay. Ityay asway
ikelay ayay askmay; oryay, atherray, ikelay ethay ozenfray almnesscay ofyay ayay eadday oman’sway
eaturesfay; owingyay isthay earydray esemblanceray otay ethay actfay atthay Esterhay asway
actuallyyay eadday, inyay espectray otay anyyay aimclay ofyay ympathysay, andyay adhay epartedday
outyay ofyay ethay orldway ithway ichwhay eshay illstay eemedsay otay inglemay.

Ityay ightmay ebay, onyay isthay oneyay ayday, atthay erethay asway anyay expressionyay unseenyay
eforebay, ornay, indeedyay, ividvay enoughyay otay ebay etectedday ownay; unlessyay omesay
eternaturallypray iftedgay observeryay ouldshay avehay irstfay eadray ethay earthay, andyay
avehay afterwardsyay oughtsay ayay orrespondingcay evelopmentday inyay ethay ountenancecay
andyay ienmay. Uchsay ayay iritualspay eersay ightmay avehay onceivedcay, atthay, afteryay
ustainingsay ethay azegay ofyay ethay ultitudemay oughthray evensay iserablemay yearsyay asyay
ayay ecessitynay, ayay enancepay, andyay omethingsay ichwhay ityay asway ayay ernstay eligionray otay
endureyay, eshay ownay, orfay oneyay astlay imetay oremay, encounteredyay ityay eelyfray andyay
oluntarilyvay, inyay orderyay otay onvertcay atwhay adhay osay onglay eenbay agonyyay intoyay ayay
indkay ofyay iumphtray. ook“lay youryay astlay onyay ethay arletscay etterlay andyay itsyay
earer!”—theway eople’spay ictimvay andyay ife-longlay ond-slavebay, asyay eythay
anciedfay erhay, ightmay aysay otay emthay. yet“ay ayay ittlelay ilewhay, andyay eshay illway ebay
eyondbay youryay eachray! Ayay ewfay ourshay ongerlay, andyay ethay eepday, ysteriousmay oceanyay
illway uenchqay andyay idehay oreverfay ethay ymbolsay ichwhay yeyay avehay ausedcay otay urnbay
uponyay erhay osombay!” Ornay ereway ityay anyay inconsistencyyay ootay improbableyay otay ebay
assignedyay otay umanhay aturenay, ouldshay eway upposesay ayay eelingfay ofyay egretray inyay
Ester’shay indmay, atyay ethay omentmay enwhay eshay asway aboutyay otay inway erhay eedomfray
omfray ethay ainpay ichwhay adhay eenbay usthay eeplyday incorporatedyay ithway erhay eingbay.
Ightmay erethay otnay ebay anyay irresistibleyay esireday otay uaffqay ayay astlay, onglay,
eathlessbray aughtdray ofyay ethay upcay ofyay ormwoodway andyay aloesyay, ithway ichwhay earlynay
allyay erhay yearsyay ofyay omanhoodway adhay eenbay erpetuallypay avoredflay? Ethay ineway ofyay
ifelay, enceforthhay otay ebay esentedpray otay erhay ipslay, ustmay ebay indeedyay ichray,
eliciousday, andyay exhilaratingyay, inyay itsyay asedchay andyay oldengay eakerbay; oryay elseyay
eavelay anyay inevitableyay andyay earyway anguorlay, afteryay ethay eeslay ofyay itternessbay
erewithwhay eshay adhay eenbay uggeddray, asyay ithway ayay ordialcay ofyay intensestyay
otencypay.

Earlpay asway eckedday outyay ithway airyyay ayetygay. Ityay ouldway avehay eenbay impossibleyay
otay uessgay atthay isthay ightbray andyay unnysay apparitionyay owedyay itsyay existenceyay otay
ethay apeshay ofyay oomyglay aygray; oryay atthay ayay ancyfay, atyay onceyay osay orgeousgay andyay osay
elicateday asyay ustmay avehay eenbay equisiteray otay ontrivecay ethay ild’schay apparelyay,
asway ethay amesay atthay adhay achievedyay ayay asktay erhapspay oremay ifficultday, inyay
impartingyay osay istinctday ayay eculiaritypay otay Ester’shay implesay oberay. Ethay
essdray, osay operpray asway ityay otay ittlelay Earlpay, eemedsay anyay effluenceyay, oryay
inevitableyay evelopmentday andyay outwardyay anifestationmay ofyay erhay aracterchay, onay
oremay otay ebay eparatedsay omfray erhay anthay ethay any-huedmay illiancybray omfray ayay
utterfly’sbay ingway, oryay ethay aintedpay oryglay omfray ethay eaflay ofyay ayay ightbray
owerflay. Asyay ithway esethay, osay ithway ethay ildchay; erhay arbgay asway allyay ofyay oneyay ideayay
ithway erhay aturenay. Onyay isthay eventfulyay ayday, oreovermay, erethay asway ayay ertaincay
ingularsay inquietudeyay andyay excitementyay inyay erhay oodmay, esemblingray othingnay osay
uchmay asyay ethay immershay ofyay ayay iamondday, atthay arklesspay andyay ashesflay ithway ethay
ariedvay obbingsthray ofyay ethay eastbray onyay ichwhay ityay isyay isplayedday. Ildrenchay
avehay alwaysyay ayay ympathysay inyay ethay agitationsyay ofyay osethay onnectedcay ithway emthay;
alwaysyay, especiallyyay, ayay ensesay ofyay anyyay oubletray oryay impendingyay evolutionray, ofyay
ateverwhay indkay, inyay omesticday ircumstancescay; andyay ereforethay Earlpay, owhay asway
ethay emgay onyay erhay other’smay unquietyay osombay, etrayedbay, ybay ethay eryvay anceday ofyay
erhay iritsspay, ethay emotionsyay ichwhay onenay ouldcay etectday inyay ethay arblemay
assivenesspay ofyay Ester’shay owbray.

Isthay effervescenceyay ademay erhay itflay ithway ayay ird-likebay ovementmay, atherray
anthay alkway ybay erhay other’smay idesay. Eshay okebray ontinuallycay intoyay outsshay ofyay ayay
ildway, inarticulateyay, andyay ometimessay iercingpay usicmay. Enwhay eythay eachedray
ethay arket-placemay, eshay ecamebay illstay oremay estlessray, onyay erceivingpay ethay
irstay andyay ustlebay atthay enlivenedyay ethay otspay; orfay ityay asway usuallyyay oremay ikelay
ethay oadbray andyay onesomelay eengray eforebay ayay illagevay eeting-housemay, anthay ethay
entrecay ofyay ayay own’stay usinessbay.

y“whay, atwhay isyay isthay, othermay?” iedcray eshay. erefore“whay avehay allyay ethay eoplepay
eftlay eirthay orkway o-daytay? Isyay ityay ayay ay-dayplay orfay ethay olewhay orldway? Eesay,
erethay isyay ethay acksmithblay! Ehay ashay ashedway ishay ootysay acefay, andyay utpay onyay ishay
Abbath-daysay othesclay, andyay ookslay asyay ifyay ehay ouldway adlyglay ebay errymay, ifyay anyyay
indkay odybay ouldway onlyyay eachtay imhay owhay! Andyay erethay isyay Astermay Ackettbray, ethay
oldyay ailerjay, oddingnay andyay ilingsmay atyay emay. Ywhay oesday ehay oday osay, othermay?”

e“hay emembersray eethay ayay ittlelay abebay, ymay ildchay,” answeredyay Esterhay.

e“hay ouldshay otnay odnay andyay ilesmay atyay emay, orfay allyay at,—thethay ackblay, imgray,
ugly-eyedyay oldyay anmay!” aidsay Earlpay. e“hay aymay odnay atyay eethay, ifyay ehay illway; orfay
outhay artyay adclay inyay aygray, andyay earestway ethay arletscay etterlay. Utbay eesay,
othermay, owhay anymay acesfay ofyay angestray eoplepay, andyay Indiansyay amongyay emthay, andyay
ailorssay! Atwhay avehay eythay allyay omecay otay oday, erehay inyay ethay arket-placemay?”

ey“thay aitway otay eesay ethay ocessionpray asspay,” aidsay Esterhay. or“fay ethay Overnorgay
andyay ethay agistratesmay areyay otay ogay ybay, andyay ethay inistersmay, andyay allyay ethay eatgray
eoplepay andyay oodgay eoplepay, ithway ethay usicmay andyay ethay oldierssay archingmay
eforebay emthay.”

and“ay illway ethay inistermay ebay erethay?” askedyay Earlpay. and“ay illway ehay oldhay outyay
othbay ishay andshay otay emay, asyay enwhay outhay edstlay emay otay imhay omfray ethay
ook-sidebray?”

e“hay illway ebay erethay, ildchay,” answeredyay erhay othermay. ut“bay ehay illway otnay eetgray
eethay o-daytay; ornay ustmay outhay eetgray imhay.”

at“whay ayay angestray, adsay anmay isyay ehay!” aidsay ethay ildchay, asyay ifyay eakingspay artlypay
otay erselfhay. in“ay ethay arkday ight-timenay ehay allscay usyay otay imhay, andyay oldshay ythay
andhay andyay inemay, asyay enwhay eway oodstay ithway imhay onyay ethay affoldscay yonderyay. Andyay
inyay ethay eepday orestfay, erewhay onlyyay ethay oldyay eestray ancay earhay, andyay ethay ipstray
ofyay yskay eesay ityay, ehay alkstay ithway eethay, ittingsay onyay ayay eaphay ofyay ossmay! Andyay ehay
isseskay ymay oreheadfay, ootay, osay atthay ethay ittlelay ookbray ouldway ardlyhay ashway ityay
offyay! Utbay erehay, inyay ethay unnysay ayday, andyay amongyay allyay ethay eoplepay, ehay owsknay usyay
otnay; ornay ustmay eway owknay imhay! Ayay angestray, adsay anmay isyay ehay, ithway ishay andhay
alwaysyay overyay ishay earthay!”

e“bay uietqay, Earlpay! Outhay understandestyay otnay esethay ingsthay,” aidsay erhay
othermay. ink“thay otnay ownay ofyay ethay inistermay, utbay ooklay aboutyay eethay, andyay eesay
owhay eerychay isyay everybody’syay acefay o-daytay. Ethay ildrenchay avehay omecay omfray
eirthay oolsschay, andyay ethay owngray eoplepay omfray eirthay orkshopsway andyay eirthay
ieldsfay, onyay urposepay otay ebay appyhay. Orfay, o-daytay, ayay ewnay anmay isyay eginningbay otay
uleray overyay emthay; andyay o—assay ashay eenbay ethay ustomcay ofyay ankindmay everyay incesay ayay
ationnay asway irstfay athered—theygay akemay errymay andyay ejoiceray; asyay ifyay ayay oodgay
andyay oldengay yearyay ereway atyay engthlay otay asspay overyay ethay oorpay oldyay orldway!”

Ityay asway asyay Esterhay aidsay, inyay egardray otay ethay unwontedyay ollityjay atthay
ightenedbray ethay acesfay ofyay ethay eoplepay. Intoyay isthay estalfay easonsay ofyay ethay
year—asyay ityay alreadyyay asway, andyay ontinuedcay otay ebay uringday ethay eatergray artpay
ofyay otway enturies—thecay Uritanspay ompressedcay ateverwhay irthmay andyay ublicpay
oyjay eythay eemedday allowableyay otay umanhay infirmityyay; erebythay osay arfay
ispellingday ethay ustomarycay oudclay, atthay, orfay ethay acespay ofyay ayay inglesay
olidayhay, eythay appearedyay arcelyscay oremay avegray anthay ostmay otheryay ommunitiescay
atyay ayay eriodpay ofyay eneralgay afflictionyay.

Utbay eway erhapspay exaggerateyay ethay aygray oryay ablesay ingetay, ichwhay undoubtedlyyay
aracterizedchay ethay oodmay andyay annersmay ofyay ethay ageyay. Ethay ersonspay ownay inyay ethay
arket-placemay ofyay Ostonbay adhay otnay eenbay ornbay otay anyay inheritanceyay ofyay
Uritanicpay oomglay. Eythay ereway ativenay Englishmenyay, osewhay athersfay adhay ivedlay
inyay ethay unnysay ichnessray ofyay ethay Elizabethanyay epochyay; ayay imetay enwhay ethay ifelay
ofyay Englandyay, iewedvay asyay oneyay eatgray assmay, ouldway appearyay otay avehay eenbay asyay
atelystay, agnificentmay, andyay oyousjay, asyay ethay orldway ashay everyay itnessedway. Adhay
eythay ollowedfay eirthay ereditaryhay astetay, ethay Ewnay Englandyay ettlerssay ouldway
avehay illustratedyay allyay eventsyay ofyay ublicpay importanceyay ybay onfiresbay,
anquetsbay, ageantriespay, andyay ocessionspray. Ornay ouldway ityay avehay eenbay
impracticableyay, inyay ethay observanceyay ofyay ajesticmay eremoniescay, otay ombinecay
irthfulmay ecreationray ithway olemnitysay, andyay ivegay, asyay ityay ereway, ayay otesquegray
andyay illiantbray embroideryyay otay ethay eatgray oberay ofyay atestay, ichwhay ayay ationnay,
atyay uchsay estivalsfay, utspay onyay. Erethay asway omesay adowshay ofyay anyay attemptyay ofyay
isthay indkay inyay ethay odemay ofyay elebratingcay ethay ayday onyay ichwhay ethay oliticalpay
yearyay ofyay ethay olonycay ommencedcay. Ethay imday eflectionray ofyay ayay ememberedray
endorsplay, ayay olorlesscay andyay anifoldmay ilutedday epetitionray ofyay atwhay eythay adhay
eheldbay inyay oudpray oldyay Ondon,—welay illway otnay aysay atyay ayay oyalray oronationcay,
utbay atyay ayay Ordlay Ayor’smay ow,—mightshay ebay acedtray inyay ethay ustomscay ichwhay ouryay
orefathersfay institutedyay, ithway eferenceray otay ethay annualyay installationyay ofyay
agistratesmay. Ethay athersfay andyay oundersfay ofyay ethay ommonwealth—thecay
atesmanstay, ethay iestpray, andyay ethay oldier—deemedsay ityay ayay utyday enthay otay
assumeyay ethay outwardyay atestay andyay ajestymay, ichwhay, inyay accordanceyay ithway
antiqueyay ylestay, asway ookedlay uponyay asyay ethay operpray arbgay ofyay ublicpay oryay ocialsay
eminenceyay. Allyay amecay orthfay, otay ovemay inyay ocessionpray eforebay ethay eople’spay
eyeyay, andyay usthay impartyay ayay eedednay ignityday otay ethay implesay ameworkfray ofyay ayay
overnmentgay osay ewlynay onstructedcay.

Enthay, ootay, ethay eoplepay ereway ountenancedcay, ifyay otnay encouragedyay, inyay
elaxingray ethay everesay andyay oseclay applicationyay otay eirthay ariousvay odesmay ofyay
uggedray industryyay, ichwhay, atyay allyay otheryay imestay, eemedsay ofyay ethay amesay iecepay
andyay aterialmay ithway eirthay eligionray. Erehay, ityay isyay uetray, ereway onenay ofyay ethay
applicancesyay ichwhay opularpay errimentmay ouldway osay eadilyray avehay oundfay inyay ethay
Englandyay ofyay Elizabeth’syay imetay, oryay atthay ofyay Ames;—nojay uderay owsshay ofyay ayay
eatricalthay indkay; onay instrelmay, ithway ishay arphay andyay egendarylay alladbay, ornay
eemanglay, ithway anyay apeyay ancingday otay ishay usicmay; onay ugglerjay, ithway ishay ickstray
ofyay imicmay itchcraftway; onay Errymay Andrewyay, otay irstay upyay ethay ultitudemay ithway
estsjay, erhapspay undredshay ofyay yearsyay oldyay, utbay illstay effectiveyay, ybay eirthay
appealsyay otay ethay eryvay oadestbray ourcessay ofyay irthfulmay ympathysay. Allyay uchsay
ofessorspray ofyay ethay everalsay anchesbray ofyay ocularityjay ouldway avehay eenbay
ernlystay epressedray, otnay onlyyay ybay ethay igidray isciplineday ofyay awlay, utbay ybay ethay
eneralgay entimentsay ichwhay ivesgay awlay itsyay italityvay. Otnay ethay esslay, oweverhay,
ethay eatgray, onesthay acefay ofyay ethay eoplepay iledsmay, imlygray, erhapspay, utbay
idelyway ootay. Ornay ereway ortsspay antingway, uchsay asyay ethay olonistscay adhay
itnessedway, andyay aredshay inyay, onglay agoyay, atyay ethay ountrycay airsfay andyay onyay ethay
illage-greensvay ofyay Englandyay; andyay ichwhay ityay asway oughtthay ellway otay eepkay aliveyay
onyay isthay ewnay oilsay, orfay ethay akesay ofyay ethay ouragecay andyay anlinessmay atthay ereway
essentialyay inyay emthay. Estling-matcheswray, inyay ethay ifferentday ashionsfay ofyay
Ornwallcay andyay Evonshireday, ereway eensay erehay andyay erethay aboutyay ethay
arket-placemay; inyay oneyay ornercay, erethay asway ayay iendlyfray outbay atyay
uarterstaffqay; and—whatyay attractedyay ostmay interestyay ofyay all—onyay ethay
atformplay ofyay ethay illorypay, alreadyyay osay otednay inyay ouryay agespay, otway astersmay ofyay
efenceday ereway ommencingcay anyay exhibitionyay ithway ethay ucklerbay andyay oadswordbray.
Utbay, uchmay otay ethay isappointmentday ofyay ethay owdcray, isthay atterlay usinessbay asway
okenbray offyay ybay ethay interpositionyay ofyay ethay owntay eadlebay, owhay adhay onay ideayay ofyay
ermittingpay ethay ajestymay ofyay ethay awlay otay ebay iolatedvay ybay uchsay anyay abuseyay ofyay
oneyay ofyay itsyay onsecratedcay acesplay.

Ityay aymay otnay ebay ootay uchmay otay affirmyay, onyay ethay olewhay, e(thay eoplepay eingbay enthay
inyay ethay irstfay agesstay ofyay oylessjay eportmentday, andyay ethay offspringyay ofyay iressay
owhay adhay ownknay owhay otay ebay errymay, inyay eirthay ayday,) atthay eythay ouldway omparecay
avorablyfay, inyay ointpay ofyay olidayhay eepingkay, ithway eirthay escendantsday, evenyay
atyay osay onglay anyay intervalyay asyay ourselvesyay. Eirthay immediateyay osteritypay, ethay
enerationgay extnay otay ethay earlyyay emigrantsyay, oreway ethay ackestblay adeshay ofyay
Uritanismpay, andyay osay arkenedday ethay ationalnay isagevay ithway ityay, atthay allyay ethay
ubsequentsay yearsyay avehay otnay ufficedsay otay earclay ityay upyay. Eway avehay yetyay otay
earnlay againyay ethay orgottenfay artyay ofyay ayetygay.

Ethay icturepay ofyay umanhay ifelay inyay ethay arket-placemay, oughthay itsyay eneralgay inttay
asway ethay adsay aygray, ownbray, oryay ackblay ofyay ethay Englishyay emigrantsyay, asway yetyay
enlivenedyay ybay omesay iversityday ofyay uehay. Ayay artypay ofyay Indians—inyay eirthay
avagesay ineryfay ofyay uriouslycay embroideredyay eer-skinday obesray, ampum-beltsway,
edray andyay yellowyay ochreyay, andyay eathersfay, andyay armedyay ithway ethay owbay andyay arrowyay
andyay one-headedstay ear—stoodspay apartyay, ithway ountenancescay ofyay inflexibleyay
avitygray, eyondbay atwhay evenyay ethay Uritanpay aspectyay ouldcay attainyay. Ornay, ildway
asyay ereway esethay aintedpay arbariansbay, ereway eythay ethay ildestway eaturefay ofyay ethay
enescay. Isthay istinctionday ouldcay oremay ustlyjay ebay aimedclay ybay omesay
ariners,—amay artpay ofyay ethay ewcray ofyay ethay esselvay omfray ethay Anishspay
Ain,—whomay adhay omecay ashoreyay otay eesay ethay umorshay ofyay Electionyay Ayday. Eythay
ereway ough-lookingray esperadoesday, ithway un-blackenedsay acesfay, andyay anyay
immensityyay ofyay eardbay; eirthay ideway, ortshay ouserstray ereway onfinedcay aboutyay ethay
aistway ybay eltsbay, oftenyay aspedclay ithway ayay oughray ateplay ofyay oldgay, andyay
ustainingsay alwaysyay ayay onglay ifeknay, andyay, inyay omesay instancesyay, ayay ordsway. Omfray
eneathbay eirthay oad-brimmedbray atshay ofyay alm-leafpay eamedglay eyesyay ichwhay, evenyay
inyay ood-naturegay andyay errimentmay, adhay ayay indkay ofyay animalyay erocityfay. Eythay
ansgressedtray, ithoutway earfay oryay uplescray, ethay ulesray ofyay ehaviorbay atthay ereway
indingbay onyay allyay othersyay; okingsmay obaccotay underyay ethay eadle’sbay eryvay osenay,
althoughyay eachyay iffwhay ouldway avehay ostcay ayay ownsmantay ayay illingshay; andyay
uaffingqay, atyay eirthay easureplay, aughtsdray ofyay ineway oryay aqua-vitæyay omfray
