ocket-flaskspay, ichwhay eythay eelyfray enderedtay otay ethay apinggay owdcray aroundyay
emthay. Ityay emarkablyray aracterizedchay ethay incompleteyay oralitymay ofyay ethay ageyay,
igidray asyay eway allcay ityay, atthay ayay icenselay asway allowedyay ethay eafaringsay assclay,
otnay erelymay orfay eirthay eaksfray onyay oreshay, utbay orfay arfay oremay esperateday eedsday
onyay eirthay operpray elementyay. Ethay ailorsay ofyay atthay ayday ouldway ogay earnay otay ebay
arraignedyay asyay ayay iratepay inyay ouryay ownyay. Erethay ouldcay ebay ittlelay oubtday, orfay
instanceyay, atthay isthay eryvay ip’sshay ewcray, oughthay onay unfavorableyay ecimensspay
ofyay ethay auticalnay otherhoodbray, adhay eenbay uiltygay, asyay eway ouldshay asephray ityay,
ofyay epredationsday onyay ethay Anishspay ommercecay, uchsay asyay ouldway avehay erilledpay
allyay eirthay ecksnay inyay ayay odernmay ourtcay ofyay usticejay.

Utbay ethay easay, inyay osethay oldyay imestay, eavedhay, elledsway, andyay oamedfay, eryvay
uchmay atyay itsyay ownyay illway, oryay ubjectsay onlyyay otay ethay empestuoustay indway, ithway
ardlyhay anyyay attemptsyay atyay egulationray ybay umanhay awlay. Ethay uccaneerbay onyay ethay
aveway ightmay elinquishray ishay allingcay, andyay ecomebay atyay onceyay, ifyay ehay osechay, ayay
anmay ofyay obitypray andyay ietypay onyay andlay; ornay, evenyay inyay ethay ullfay areercay ofyay ishay
ecklessray ifelay, asway ehay egardedray asyay ayay ersonagepay ithway omwhay ityay asway
isreputableday otay affictray, oryay asuallycay associateyay. Usthay, ethay Uritanpay
eldersyay, inyay eirthay ackblay oaksclay, archedstay andsbay, andyay eeple-crownedstay
atshay, iledsmay otnay unbenignantlyyay atyay ethay amorclay andyay uderay eportmentday ofyay
esethay ollyjay eafaringsay enmay; andyay ityay excitedyay eithernay urprisesay ornay
animadversionyay, enwhay osay eputableray ayay itizencay asyay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay,
ethay ysicianphay, asway eensay otay enteryay ethay arket-placemay, inyay oseclay andyay
amiliarfay alktay ithway ethay ommandercay ofyay ethay uestionableqay esselvay.

Ethay atterlay asway ybay arfay ethay ostmay owyshay andyay allantgay igurefay, osay arfay asyay
apparelyay entway, anywhereyay otay ebay eensay amongyay ethay ultitudemay. Ehay oreway ayay
ofusionpray ofyay ibbonsray onyay ishay armentgay, andyay old-lacegay onyay ishay athay, ichwhay
asway alsoyay encircledyay ybay ayay oldgay ainchay, andyay urmountedsay ithway ayay eatherfay.
Erethay asway ayay ordsway atyay ishay idesay, andyay ayay ord-cutsway onyay ishay oreheadfay, ichwhay,
ybay ethay arrangementyay ofyay ishay airhay, ehay eemedsay anxiousyay atherray otay isplayday
anthay idehay. Ayay andsmanlay ouldcay ardlyhay avehay ornway isthay arbgay andyay ownshay isthay
acefay, andyay ornway andyay ownshay emthay othbay ithway uchsay ayay alliardgay airyay, ithoutway
undergoingyay ernstay uestionqay eforebay ayay agistratemay, andyay obablypray incurringyay
inefay oryay imprisonmentyay, oryay erhapspay anyay exhibitionyay inyay ethay ocksstay. Asyay
egardedray ethay ipmastershay, oweverhay, allyay asway ookedlay uponyay asyay ertainingpay otay
ethay aracterchay, asyay otay ayay ishfay ishay isteningglay alesscay.

Afteryay artingpay omfray ethay ysicianphay, ethay ommandercay ofyay ethay Istolbray ipshay
olledstray idlyyay oughthray ethay arket-placemay; untilyay, appeninghay otay approachyay
ethay otspay erewhay Esterhay Ynnepray asway andingstay, ehay appearedyay otay ecognizeray,
andyay idday otnay esitatehay otay addressyay erhay. Asyay asway usuallyyay ethay asecay ereverwhay
Esterhay oodstay, ayay allsmay acantvay area—ayay ortsay ofyay agicmay ircle—hadcay ormedfay
itselfyay aboutyay erhay, intoyay ichwhay, oughthay ethay eoplepay ereway elbowingyay oneyay
anotheryay atyay ayay ittlelay istanceday, onenay enturedvay, oryay eltfay isposedday otay
intrudeyay. Ityay asway ayay orciblefay ypetay ofyay ethay oralmay olitudesay inyay ichwhay ethay
arletscay etterlay envelopedyay itsyay atedfay earerway; artlypay ybay erhay ownyay eserveray,
andyay artlypay ybay ethay instinctiveyay, oughthay onay ongerlay osay unkindlyyay,
ithdrawalway ofyay erhay ellow-creaturesfay. Ownay, ifyay evernay eforebay, ityay answeredyay
ayay oodgay urposepay, ybay enablingyay Esterhay andyay ethay eamansay otay eakspay ogethertay
ithoutway iskray ofyay eingbay overheardyay; andyay osay angedchay asway Esterhay Ynne’spray
eputeray eforebay ethay ublicpay, atthay ethay atronmay inyay owntay ostmay eminentyay orfay
igidray oralitymay ouldcay otnay avehay eldhay uchsay intercourseyay ithway esslay esultray
ofyay andalscay anthay erselfhay.

o“say, istressmay,” aidsay ethay arinermay, i“ay ustmay idbay ethay ewardstay akemay eadyray
oneyay oremay erthbay anthay youyay argainedbay orfay! Onay earfay ofyay urvyscay oryay
ip-fevershay, isthay oyagevay! Atwhay ithway ethay ip’sshay urgeonsay andyay isthay otheryay
octorday, ouryay onlyyay angerday illway ebay omfray ugdray oryay illpay; oremay ybay okentay, asyay
erethay isyay ayay otlay ofyay apothecary’syay uffstay aboardyay, ichwhay Iyay adedtray orfay ithway ayay
Anishspay esselvay.”

at“whay eanmay youyay?” inquiredyay Esterhay, artledstay oremay anthay eshay ermittedpay otay
appearyay. ave“hay youyay anotheryay assengerpay?”

y“whay, owknay youyay otnay,” iedcray ethay ipmastershay, at“thay isthay ysicianphay
ere—chillingworthhay, ehay allscay imself—ishay indedmay otay ytray ymay abin-farecay
ithway youyay? Ayyay, ayyay, youyay ustmay avehay ownknay ityay; orfay ehay ellstay emay ehay isyay ofyay
youryay artypay, andyay ayay oseclay iendfray otay ethay entlemangay youyay okespay of,—heyay atthay
isyay inyay erilpay omfray esethay oursay oldyay Uritanpay ulersray!”

illustration[ay: Illingworth,—“smilechay ithway ayay inistersay eaningmay”]

ey“thay owknay eachyay otheryay ellway, indeedyay,” epliedray Esterhay, ithway ayay ienmay ofyay
almnesscay, oughthay inyay ethay utmostyay onsternationcay. ey“thay avehay onglay eltdway
ogethertay.”

Othingnay urtherfay assedpay etweenbay ethay arinermay andyay Esterhay Ynnepray. Utbay, atyay
atthay instantyay, eshay eheldbay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay imselfhay, andingstay inyay
ethay emotestray ornercay ofyay ethay arket-placemay, andyay ilingsmay onyay erhay; ayay ilesmay
ich—acrosswhay ethay ideway andyay ustlingbay uaresqay, andyay oughthray allyay ethay alktay
andyay aughterlay, andyay ariousvay oughtsthay, oodsmay, andyay interestsyay ofyay ethay
owd—conveyedcray ecretsay andyay earfulfay eaningmay.




                            illustration[ay]

                                 Iixxay.

                            Ethay Ocessionpray.


Eforebay Esterhay Ynnepray ouldcay allcay ogethertay erhay oughtsthay, andyay onsidercay
atwhay asway acticablepray otay ebay oneday inyay isthay ewnay andyay artlingstay aspectyay ofyay
affairsyay, ethay oundsay ofyay ilitarymay usicmay asway eardhay approachingyay alongyay ayay
ontiguouscay eetstray. Ityay enotedday ethay advanceyay ofyay ethay ocessionpray ofyay
agistratesmay andyay itizenscay, onyay itsyay ayway owardstay ethay eeting-housemay; erewhay,
inyay ompliancecay ithway ayay ustomcay usthay earlyyay establishedyay, andyay everyay incesay
observedyay, ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday asway otay eliverday anyay Electionyay
Ermonsay.

illustration[ay: Ewnay Englandyay Orthiesway]

Oonsay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay ocessionpray owedshay itselfyay, ithway ayay owslay andyay atelystay
archmay, urningtay ayay ornercay, andyay akingmay itsyay ayway acrossyay ethay arket-placemay.
Irstfay amecay ethay usicmay. Ityay omprisedcay ayay arietyvay ofyay instrumentsyay, erhapspay
imperfectlyyay adaptedyay otay oneyay anotheryay, andyay ayedplay ithway onay eatgray illskay;
utbay yetyay attainingyay ethay eatgray objectyay orfay ichwhay ethay armonyhay ofyay umdray andyay
arionclay addressesyay itselfyay otay ethay ultitude,—thatmay ofyay impartingyay ayay igherhay
andyay oremay eroichay airyay otay ethay enescay ofyay ifelay atthay assespay eforebay ethay eyeyay.
Ittlelay Earlpay atyay irstfay appedclay erhay andshay, utbay enthay ostlay, orfay anyay
instantyay, ethay estlessray agitationyay atthay adhay eptkay erhay inyay ayay ontinualcay
effervescenceyay oughoutthray ethay orningmay; eshay azedgay ilentlysay, andyay eemedsay
otay ebay ornebay upwardyay, ikelay ayay oatingflay ea-birdsay, onyay ethay onglay eaveshay andyay
ellssway ofyay oundsay. Utbay eshay asway oughtbray ackbay otay erhay ormerfay oodmay ybay ethay
immershay ofyay ethay unshinesay onyay ethay eaponsway andyay ightbray armoryay ofyay ethay
ilitarymay ompanycay, ichwhay ollowedfay afteryay ethay usicmay, andyay ormedfay ethay
onoraryhay escortyay ofyay ethay ocessionpray. Isthay odybay ofyay oldiery—whichsay illstay
ustainssay ayay orporatecay existenceyay, andyay archesmay ownday omfray astpay agesyay ithway
anyay ancientyay andyay onorablehay ame—wasfay omposedcay ofyay onay ercenarymay aterialsmay.
Itsyay anksray ereway illedfay ithway entlemengay, owhay eltfay ethay irringsstay ofyay
artialmay impulseyay, andyay oughtsay otay establishyay ayay indkay ofyay Ollegecay ofyay Armsyay,
erewhay, asyay inyay anyay associationyay ofyay Ightsknay Emplarstay, eythay ightmay earnlay ethay
iencescay, andyay, osay arfay asyay eacefulpay exerciseyay ouldway eachtay emthay, ethay
acticespray ofyay arway. Ethay ighhay estimationyay enthay acedplay uponyay ethay ilitarymay
aracterchay ightmay ebay eensay inyay ethay oftylay ortpay ofyay eachyay individualyay embermay
ofyay ethay ompanycay. Omesay ofyay emthay, indeedyay, ybay eirthay ervicessay inyay ethay Owlay
Ountriescay andyay onyay otheryay ieldsfay ofyay Europeanyay arfareway, adhay airlyfay onway
eirthay itletay otay assumeyay ethay amenay andyay omppay ofyay oldiershipsay. Ethay entireyay
arrayyay, oreovermay, adclay inyay urnishedbay eelstay, andyay ithway umageplay oddingnay
overyay eirthay ightbray orionsmay, adhay ayay illiancybray ofyay effectyay ichwhay onay odernmay
isplayday ancay aspireyay otay equalyay.

Andyay yetyay ethay enmay ofyay ivilcay eminenceyay, owhay amecay immediatelyyay ehindbay ethay
ilitarymay escortyay, ereway etterbay orthway ayay oughtfulthay observer’syay eyeyay. Evenyay
inyay outwardyay emeanorday, eythay owedshay ayay ampstay ofyay ajestymay atthay ademay ethay
arrior’sway aughtyhay idestray ooklay ulgarvay, ifyay otnay absurdyay. Ityay asway anyay ageyay
enwhay atwhay eway allcay alenttay adhay arfay esslay onsiderationcay anthay ownay, utbay ethay
assivemay aterialsmay ichwhay oducepray abilitystay andyay ignityday ofyay aracterchay ayay
eatgray ealday oremay. Ethay eoplepay ossessedpay, ybay ereditaryhay ightray, ethay
ualityqay ofyay everenceray; ichwhay, inyay eirthay escendantsday, ifyay ityay urvivesay atyay
allyay, existsyay inyay allersmay oportionpray, andyay ithway ayay astlyvay iminishedday orcefay,
inyay ethay electionsay andyay estimateyay ofyay ublicpay enmay. Ethay angechay aymay ebay orfay
oodgay oryay illyay, andyay isyay artlypay, erhapspay, orfay othbay. Inyay atthay oldyay ayday, ethay
Englishyay ettlersay onyay esethay uderay ores—havingshay eftlay ingkay, oblesnay, andyay
allyay egreesday ofyay awfulyay ankray ehindbay, ilewhay illstay ethay acultyfay andyay
ecessitynay ofyay everenceray ereway ongstray inyay im—bestowedhay ityay onyay ethay itewhay
airhay andyay enerablevay owbray ofyay ageyay; onyay ong-triedlay integrityyay; onyay olidsay
isdomway andyay ad-coloredsay experienceyay; onyay endowmentsyay ofyay atthay avegray andyay
eightyway orderyay ichwhay ivesgay ethay ideayay ofyay ermanencepay, andyay omescay underyay ethay
eneralgay efinitionday ofyay espectabilityray. Esethay imitivepray atesmenstay,
erefore,—bradstreetthay, Endicottyay, Udleyday, Ellinghambay, andyay eirthay
ompeers,—whocay ereway elevatedyay otay owerpay ybay ethay earlyyay oicechay ofyay ethay
eoplepay, eemsay otay avehay eenbay otnay oftenyay illiantbray, utbay istinguishedday ybay ayay
onderouspay obrietysay, atherray anthay activityyay ofyay intellectyay. Eythay adhay
ortitudefay andyay elf-reliancesay, andyay, inyay imetay ofyay ifficultyday oryay erilpay,
oodstay upyay orfay ethay elfareway ofyay ethay atestay ikelay ayay inelay ofyay iffsclay againstyay ayay
empestuoustay idetay. Ethay aitstray ofyay aracterchay erehay indicatedyay ereway ellway
epresentedray inyay ethay uaresqay astcay ofyay ountenancecay andyay argelay ysicalphay
evelopmentday ofyay ethay ewnay olonialcay agistratesmay. Osay arfay asyay ayay emeanorday ofyay
aturalnay authorityyay asway oncernedcay, ethay othermay ountrycay eednay otnay avehay eenbay
ashamedyay otay eesay esethay oremostfay enmay ofyay anyay actualyay emocracyday adoptedyay intoyay
ethay Ousehay ofyay Eerspay, oryay ademay ethay Ivypray Ouncilcay ofyay ethay overeignsay.

Extnay inyay orderyay otay ethay agistratesmay amecay ethay youngyay andyay eminentlyyay
istinguishedday ivineday, omfray osewhay ipslay ethay eligiousray iscourseday ofyay ethay
anniversaryyay asway expectedyay. Ishay asway ethay ofessionpray, atyay atthay erayay, inyay
ichwhay intellectualyay abilityyay isplayedday itselfyay arfay oremay anthay inyay oliticalpay
ifelay; or—leavingfay ayay igherhay otivemay outyay ofyay ethay uestion—itqay offeredyay
inducementsyay owerfulpay enoughyay, inyay ethay almostyay orshippingway espectray ofyay ethay
ommunitycay, otay inway ethay ostmay aspiringyay ambitionyay intoyay itsyay ervicesay. Evenyay
oliticalpay ower—aspay inyay ethay asecay ofyay Increaseyay Ather—wasmay ithinway ethay
aspgray ofyay ayay uccessfulsay iestpray.

Ityay asway ethay observationyay ofyay osethay owhay eheldbay imhay ownay, atthay evernay, incesay
Mray. Immesdaleday irstfay etsay ishay ootfay onyay ethay Ewnay Englandyay oreshay, adhay ehay
exhibitedyay uchsay energyyay asyay asway eensay inyay ethay aitgay andyay airyay ithway ichwhay ehay
eptkay ishay acepay inyay ethay ocessionpray. Erethay asway onay eeblenessfay ofyay epstay, asyay
atyay otheryay imestay; ishay amefray asway otnay entbay; ornay idday ishay andhay estray
ominouslyyay uponyay ishay earthay. Yetyay, ifyay ethay ergymanclay ereway ightlyray iewedvay,
ishay engthstray eemedsay otnay ofyay ethay odybay. Ityay ightmay ebay iritualspay, andyay
impartedyay otay imhay ybay angelicyay inistrationsmay. Ityay ightmay ebay ethay exhilarationyay
ofyay atthay otentpay ordialcay, ichwhay isyay istilledday onlyyay inyay ethay urnace-glowfay ofyay
earnestyay andyay ong-continuedlay oughtthay. Oryay, erchancepay, ishay ensitivesay
emperamenttay asway invigoratedyay ybay ethay oudlay andyay iercingpay usicmay, atthay
elledsway eavenwardhay, andyay upliftedyay imhay onyay itsyay ascendingyay aveway.
Everthelessnay, osay abstractedyay asway ishay ooklay, ityay ightmay ebay uestionedqay
etherwhay Mray. Immesdaleday evenyay eardhay ethay usicmay. Erethay asway ishay odybay,
ovingmay onwardyay, andyay ithway anyay unaccustomedyay orcefay. Utbay erewhay asway ishay indmay?
Arfay andyay eepday inyay itsyay ownyay egionray, usyingbay itselfyay, ithway eternaturalpray
activityyay, otay arshalmay ayay ocessionpray ofyay atelystay oughtsthay atthay ereway oonsay
otay issueyay encethay; andyay osay ehay awsay othingnay, eardhay othingnay, ewknay othingnay,
ofyay atwhay asway aroundyay imhay; utbay ethay iritualspay elementyay ooktay upyay ethay eeblefay
amefray, andyay arriedcay ityay alongyay, unconsciousyay ofyay ethay urdenbay, andyay onvertingcay
ityay otay iritspay ikelay itselfyay. Enmay ofyay uncommonyay intellectyay, owhay avehay owngray
orbidmay, ossesspay isthay occasionalyay owerpay ofyay ightymay effortyay, intoyay ichwhay
eythay owthray ethay ifelay ofyay anymay aysday, andyay enthay areyay ifelesslay orfay asyay anymay
oremay.

Esterhay Ynnepray, azinggay eadfastlystay atyay ethay ergymanclay, eltfay ayay earydray
influenceyay omecay overyay erhay, utbay ereforewhay oryay encewhay eshay ewknay otnay; unlessyay
atthay ehay eemedsay osay emoteray omfray erhay ownyay eresphay, andyay utterlyyay eyondbay erhay
eachray. Oneyay anceglay ofyay ecognitionray, eshay adhay imaginedyay, ustmay eedsnay asspay
etweenbay emthay. Eshay oughtthay ofyay ethay imday orestfay, ithway itsyay ittlelay ellday ofyay
olitudesay, andyay ovelay, andyay anguishyay, andyay ethay ossymay ee-trunktray, erewhay,
ittingsay andhay inyay andhay, eythay adhay ingledmay eirthay adsay andyay assionatepay alktay
ithway ethay elancholymay urmurmay ofyay ethay ookbray. Owhay eeplyday adhay eythay ownknay
eachyay otheryay enthay! Andyay asway isthay ethay anmay? Eshay ardlyhay ewknay imhay ownay! Ehay,
ovingmay oudlypray astpay, envelopedyay, asyay ityay ereway, inyay ethay ichray usicmay, ithway
ethay ocessionpray ofyay ajesticmay andyay enerablevay athersfay; ehay, osay unattainableyay
inyay ishay orldlyway ositionpay, andyay illstay oremay osay inyay atthay arfay istavay ofyay ishay
unsympathizingyay oughtsthay, oughthray ichwhay eshay ownay eheldbay imhay! Erhay iritspay
anksay ithway ethay ideayay atthay allyay ustmay avehay eenbay ayay elusionday, andyay atthay,
ividlyvay asyay eshay adhay eameddray ityay, erethay ouldcay ebay onay ealray ondbay etwixtbay ethay
ergymanclay andyay erselfhay. Andyay usthay uchmay ofyay omanway asway erethay inyay Esterhay,
atthay eshay ouldcay arcelyscay orgivefay im,—leasthay ofyay allyay ownay, enwhay ethay eavyhay
ootstepfay ofyay eirthay approachingyay Atefay ightmay ebay eardhay, earernay, earernay,
earer!—fornay eingbay ableyay osay ompletelycay otay ithdrawway imselfhay omfray eirthay
utualmay orldway; ilewhay eshay opedgray arklyday, andyay etchedstray orthfay erhay oldcay
andshay, andyay oundfay imhay otnay.

Earlpay eitheryay awsay andyay espondedray otay erhay other’smay eelingsfay, oryay erselfhay
eltfay ethay emotenessray andyay intangibilityyay atthay adhay allenfay aroundyay ethay
inistermay. Ilewhay ethay ocessionpray assedpay, ethay ildchay asway uneasyyay,
utteringflay upyay andyay ownday, ikelay ayay irdbay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay akingtay ightflay.
Enwhay ethay olewhay adhay onegay ybay, eshay ookedlay upyay intoyay Ester’shay acefay.

other“may,” aidsay eshay, as“way atthay ethay amesay inistermay atthay issedkay emay ybay ethay
ookbray?”

old“hay ythay eacepay, earday ittlelay Earlpay!” isperedwhay erhay othermay. e“way ustmay
otnay alwaysyay alktay inyay ethay arket-placemay ofyay atwhay appenshay otay usyay inyay ethay
orestfay.”

i“ay ouldcay otnay ebay uresay atthay ityay asway ehay; osay angestray ehay ookedlay,” ontinuedcay
ethay ildchay. else“ay Iyay ouldway avehay unray otay imhay, andyay idbay imhay isskay emay ownay,
eforebay allyay ethay eoplepay; evenyay asyay ehay idday yonderyay amongyay ethay arkday oldyay eestray.
Atwhay ouldway ethay inistermay avehay aidsay, othermay? Ouldway ehay avehay appedclay ishay
andhay overyay ishay earthay, andyay owledscay onyay emay, andyay idbay emay ebay onegay?”

at“whay ouldshay ehay aysay, Earlpay,” answeredyay Esterhay, ave“say atthay ityay asway onay
imetay otay isskay, andyay atthay isseskay areyay otnay otay ebay ivengay inyay ethay arket-placemay?
Ellway orfay eethay, oolishfay ildchay, atthay outhay idstday otnay eakspay otay imhay!”

Anotheryay adeshay ofyay ethay amesay entimentsay, inyay eferenceray otay Mray. Immesdaleday,
asway expressedyay ybay ayay ersonpay osewhay eccentricities—oryay insanityyay, asyay eway
ouldshay ermtay it—ledyay erhay otay oday atwhay ewfay ofyay ethay owns-peopletay ouldway avehay
enturedvay onyay; otay eginbay ayay onversationcay ithway ethay earerway ofyay ethay arletscay
etterlay, inyay ublicpay. Ityay asway Istressmay Ibbinshay, owhay, arrayedyay inyay eatgray
agnificencemay, ithway ayay ipletray uffray, ayay oideredbray omacherstay, ayay owngay ofyay
ichray elvetvay, andyay ayay old-headedgay anecay, adhay omecay orthfay otay eesay ethay
ocessionpray. Asyay isthay ancientyay adylay adhay ethay enownray ich(whay ubsequentlysay
ostcay erhay onay esslay ayay icepray anthay erhay ifelay) ofyay eingbay ayay incipalpray actoryay inyay
allyay ethay orksway ofyay ecromancynay atthay ereway ontinuallycay oinggay orwardfay, ethay
owdcray avegay ayway eforebay erhay, andyay eemedsay otay earfay ethay ouchtay ofyay erhay
armentgay, asyay ifyay ityay arriedcay ethay agueplay amongyay itsyay orgeousgay oldsfay. Eensay inyay
onjunctioncay ithway Esterhay Ynne,—kindlypray asyay osay anymay ownay eltfay owardstay
ethay atter,—thelay eaddray inspiredyay ybay Istressmay Ibbinshay asway oubledday, andyay
ausedcay ayay eneralgay ovementmay omfray atthay artpay ofyay ethay arket-placemay inyay ichwhay
ethay otway omenway oodstay.

ow“nay, atwhay ortalmay imaginationyay ouldcay onceivecay ityay!” isperedwhay ethay oldyay
adylay, onfidentiallycay, otay Esterhay. yonder“ay ivineday anmay! Atthay aintsay onyay
earthyay, asyay ethay eoplepay upholdyay imhay otay ebay, andyay as—iyay ustmay eedsnay ay—hesay
eallyray ookslay! Owhay, ownay, atthay awsay imhay asspay inyay ethay ocessionpray, ouldway
inkthay owhay ittlelay ilewhay ityay isyay incesay ehay entway orthfay outyay ofyay ishay
udy,—chewingstay ayay Ebrewhay exttay ofyay Ipturescray inyay ishay outhmay, Iyay
arrant,—toway aketay anyay airingyay inyay ethay orestfay! Ahayay! eway owknay atwhay atthay
eansmay, Esterhay Ynnepray! Utbay, ulytray, orsoothfay, Iyay indfay ityay ardhay otay elievebay
imhay ethay amesay anmay. Anymay ayay urch-memberchay awsay Iyay, alkingway ehindbay ethay
usicmay, atthay ashay ancedday inyay ethay amesay easuremay ithway emay, enwhay Omebodysay asway
iddlerfay, andyay, ityay ightmay ebay, anyay Indianyay owwowpay oryay ayay Aplandlay izardway
angingchay andshay ithway usyay! Atthay isyay utbay ayay ifletray, enwhay ayay omanway owsknay ethay
orldway. Utbay isthay inistermay! Ouldstcay outhay urelysay elltay, Esterhay, etherwhay ehay
asway ethay amesay anmay atthay encounteredyay eethay onyay ethay orest-pathfay?”

adam“may, Iyay owknay otnay ofyay atwhay youyay eakspay,” answeredyay Esterhay Ynnepray, eelingfay
Istressmay Ibbinshay otay ebay ofyay infirmyay indmay; yetyay angelystray artledstay andyay
awe-strickenyay ybay ethay onfidencecay ithway ichwhay eshay affirmedyay ayay ersonalpay
onnectioncay etweenbay osay anymay ersonspay erself(hay amongyay emthay) andyay ethay Evilyay
Oneyay. it“ay isyay otnay orfay emay otay alktay ightlylay ofyay ayay earnedlay andyay iouspay inistermay
ofyay ethay Ordway, ikelay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday!”

ie“fay, omanway, iefay!” iedcray ethay oldyay adylay, akingshay erhay ingerfay atyay Esterhay.
ost“day outhay inkthay Iyay avehay eenbay otay ethay orestfay osay anymay imestay, andyay avehay yetyay
onay illskay otay udgejay owhay elseyay ashay eenbay erethay? Yeayay; oughthay onay eaflay ofyay ethay
ildway arlandsgay, ichwhay eythay oreway ilewhay eythay ancedday, ebay eftlay inyay eirthay
airhay! Iyay owknay eethay, Esterhay; orfay Iyay eholdbay ethay okentay. Eway aymay allyay eesay ityay
inyay ethay unshinesay; andyay ityay owsglay ikelay ayay edray ameflay inyay ethay arkday. Outhay
earestway ityay openlyyay; osay erethay eednay ebay onay uestionqay aboutyay atthay. Utbay isthay
inistermay! Etlay emay elltay eethay, inyay inethay earyay! Enwhay ethay Ackblay Anmay eessay oneyay
ofyay ishay ownyay ervantssay, ignedsay andyay ealedsay, osay yshay ofyay owningyay otay ethay ondbay
asyay isyay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, ehay athhay ayay ayway ofyay orderingyay attersmay
osay atthay ethay arkmay allshay ebay isclosedday inyay openyay aylightday otay ethay eyesyay ofyay
allyay ethay orldway! Atwhay isyay ityay atthay ethay inistermay eekssay otay idehay, ithway ishay
andhay alwaysyay overyay ishay earthay? Ahay, Esterhay Ynnepray!”

at“whay isyay ityay, oodgay Istressmay Ibbinshay?” eagerlyyay askedyay ittlelay Earlpay. ast“hay
outhay eensay ityay?”

o“nay attermay, arlingday!” espondedray Istressmay Ibbinshay, akingmay Earlpay ayay
ofoundpray everenceray. ou“thay yselfthay iltway eesay ityay, oneyay imetay oryay anotheryay.
Eythay aysay, ildchay, outhay artyay ofyay ethay ineagelay ofyay ethay Incepray ofyay ethay Airyay!
Iltway outhay ideray ithway emay, omesay inefay ightnay, otay eesay ythay atherfay? Enthay outhay
altshay owknay ereforewhay ethay inistermay eepskay ishay andhay overyay ishay earthay!”

Aughinglay osay illyshray atthay allyay ethay arket-placemay ouldcay earhay erhay, ethay
eirdway oldyay entlewomangay ooktay erhay epartureday.

Ybay isthay imetay ethay eliminarypray ayerpray adhay eenbay offeredyay inyay ethay
eeting-housemay, andyay ethay accentsyay ofyay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday ereway
eardhay ommencingcay ishay iscourseday. Anyay irresistibleyay eelingfay eptkay Esterhay
earnay ethay otspay. Asyay ethay acredsay edificeyay asway ootay uchmay ongedthray otay admityay
anotheryay auditoryay, eshay ooktay upyay erhay ositionpay oseclay esidebay ethay affoldscay ofyay
ethay illorypay. Ityay asway inyay ufficientsay oximitypray otay ingbray ethay olewhay ermonsay
otay erhay earsyay, inyay ethay apeshay ofyay anyay indistinctyay, utbay ariedvay, urmurmay andyay
owflay ofyay ethay inister’smay eryvay eculiarpay oicevay.

Isthay ocalvay organyay asway inyay itselfyay ayay ichray endowmentyay; insomuchyay atthay ayay
istenerlay, omprehendingcay othingnay ofyay ethay anguagelay inyay ichwhay ethay eacherpray
okespay, ightmay illstay avehay eenbay ayedsway otay andyay ofray ybay ethay eremay onetay andyay
adencecay. Ikelay allyay otheryay usicmay, ityay eathedbray assionpay andyay athospay, andyay
emotionsyay ighhay oryay endertay, inyay ayay onguetay ativenay otay ethay umanhay earthay,
ereverwhay educatedyay. Uffledmay asyay ethay oundsay asway ybay itsyay assagepay oughthray ethay
urch-wallschay, Esterhay Ynnepray istenedlay ithway uchsay intentnessyay, andyay
ympathizedsay osay intimatelyyay, atthay ethay ermonsay adhay oughoutthray ayay eaningmay
orfay erhay, entirelyyay apartyay omfray itsyay indistinguishableyay ordsway. Esethay,
erhapspay, ifyay oremay istinctlyday eardhay, ightmay avehay eenbay onlyyay ayay ossergray
ediummay, andyay avehay oggedclay ethay iritualspay ensesay. Ownay eshay aughtcay ethay owlay
undertoneyay, asyay ofyay ethay indway inkingsay ownday otay eposeray itselfyay; enthay ascendedyay
ithway ityay, asyay ityay oseray oughthray ogressivepray adationsgray ofyay eetnesssway andyay
owerpay, untilyay itsyay olumevay eemedsay otay envelopyay erhay ithway anyay atmosphereyay ofyay
aweyay andyay olemnsay andeurgray. Andyay yetyay, ajesticmay asyay ethay oicevay ometimessay
ecamebay, erethay asway oreverfay inyay ityay anyay essentialyay aracterchay ofyay
aintivenessplay. Ayay oudlay oryay owlay expressionyay ofyay anguish,—theyay isperwhay, oryay
ethay iekshray, asyay ityay ightmay ebay onceivedcay, ofyay ufferingsay umanityhay, atthay
ouchedtay ayay ensibilitysay inyay everyyay osombay! Atyay imestay isthay eepday ainstray ofyay
athospay asway allyay atthay ouldcay ebay eardhay, andyay arcelyscay eardhay, ighingsay amidyay ayay
esolateday ilencesay. Utbay evenyay enwhay ethay inister’smay oicevay ewgray ighhay andyay
ommanding,—whencay ityay ushedgay irrepressiblyyay upward,—whenyay ityay assumedyay itsyay
utmostyay eadthbray andyay owerpay, osay overfillingyay ethay urchchay asyay otay urstbay itsyay
ayway oughthray ethay olidsay allsway, andyay iffuseday itselfyay inyay ethay openyay
air,—stillyay, ifyay ethay auditoryay istenedlay intentlyyay, andyay orfay ethay urposepay, ehay
ouldcay etectday ethay amesay ycray ofyay ainpay. Atwhay asway ityay? Ethay omplaintcay ofyay ayay
umanhay earthay, orrow-ladensay, erchancepay uiltygay, ellingtay itsyay ecretsay,
etherwhay ofyay uiltgay oryay orrowsay, otay ethay eatgray earthay ofyay ankindmay; eseechingbay
itsyay ympathysay oryay orgiveness,—atfay everyyay oment,—inmay eachyay accent,—andyay
evernay inyay ainvay! Ityay asway isthay ofoundpray andyay ontinualcay undertoneyay atthay avegay
ethay ergymanclay ishay ostmay appropriateyay owerpay.

Uringday allyay isthay imetay, Esterhay oodstay, atue-likestay, atyay ethay ootfay ofyay ethay
affoldscay. Ifyay ethay inister’smay oicevay adhay otnay eptkay erhay erethay, erethay ouldway
everthelessnay avehay eenbay anyay inevitableyay agnetismmay inyay atthay otspay, encewhay
eshay atedday ethay irstfay ourhay ofyay erhay ifelay ofyay ignominyyay. Erethay asway ayay ensesay
ithinway er,—toohay ill-definedyay otay ebay ademay ayay oughtthay, utbay eighingway
eavilyhay onyay erhay ind,—thatmay erhay olewhay orbyay ofyay ifelay, othbay eforebay andyay
afteryay, asway onnectedcay ithway isthay otspay, asyay ithway ethay oneyay ointpay atthay avegay
ityay unityyay.

Ittlelay Earlpay, eanwhilemay, adhay uittedqay erhay other’smay idesay, andyay asway
ayingplay atyay erhay ownyay illway aboutyay ethay arket-placemay. Eshay ademay ethay ombresay
owdcray eerfulchay ybay erhay erraticyay andyay isteningglay ayray; evenyay asyay ayay irdbay ofyay
ightbray umageplay illuminatesyay ayay olewhay eetray ofyay uskyday oliagefay, ybay artingday
otay andyay ofray, alfhay eensay andyay alfhay oncealedcay amidyay ethay ilighttway ofyay ethay
usteringclay eaveslay. Eshay adhay anyay undulatingyay, utbay, oftentimesyay, ayay arpshay andyay
irregularyay ovementmay. Ityay indicatedyay ethay estlessray ivacityvay ofyay erhay iritspay,
ichwhay o-daytay asway oublyday indefatigableyay inyay itsyay iptoetay anceday, ecausebay ityay
asway ayedplay uponyay andyay ibratedvay ithway erhay other’smay isquietudeday. Eneverwhay
Earlpay awsay anythingyay otay exciteyay erhay ever-activeyay andyay anderingway uriositycay,
eshay ewflay itherwardthay andyay, asyay eway ightmay aysay, eizedsay uponyay atthay anmay oryay
ingthay asyay erhay ownyay opertypray, osay arfay asyay eshay esiredday ityay; utbay ithoutway
yieldingyay ethay inutestmay egreeday ofyay ontrolcay overyay erhay otionsmay inyay equitalray.
Ethay Uritanspay ookedlay onyay, andyay, ifyay eythay iledsmay, ereway onenay ethay esslay
inclinedyay otay onouncepray ethay ildchay ayay emonday offspringyay, omfray ethay
indescribableyay armchay ofyay eautybay andyay eccentricityyay atthay oneshay oughthray erhay
ittlelay igurefay, andyay arkledspay ithway itsyay activityyay. Eshay anray andyay ookedlay ethay
ildway Indianyay inyay ethay acefay; andyay ehay ewgray onsciouscay ofyay ayay aturenay ilderway anthay
ishay ownyay. Encethay, ithway ativenay audacityyay, utbay illstay ithway ayay eserveray asyay
aracteristicchay, eshay ewflay intoyay ethay idstmay ofyay ayay oupgray ofyay arinersmay, ethay
arthy-cheekedsway ildway enmay ofyay ethay oceanyay, asyay ethay Indiansyay ereway ofyay ethay
andlay; andyay eythay azedgay onderinglyway andyay admiringlyyay atyay Earlpay, asyay ifyay ayay
akeflay ofyay ethay ea-foamsay adhay akentay ethay apeshay ofyay ayay ittlelay aidmay, andyay ereway
iftedgay ithway ayay oulsay ofyay ethay ea-firesay, atthay ashesflay eneathbay ethay owpray inyay
ethay ight-timenay.

Oneyay ofyay esethay eafaringsay en—themay ipmastershay, indeedyay, owhay adhay okenspay otay
Esterhay Ynne—waspray osay ittensmay ithway Earl’spay aspectyay, atthay ehay attemptedyay
otay aylay andshay uponyay erhay, ithway urposepay otay atchsnay ayay isskay. Indingfay ityay asyay
impossibleyay otay ouchtay erhay asyay otay atchcay ayay umming-birdhay inyay ethay airyay, ehay ooktay
omfray ishay athay ethay oldgay ainchay atthay asway istedtway aboutyay ityay, andyay ewthray ityay otay
ethay ildchay. Earlpay immediatelyyay inedtway ityay aroundyay erhay ecknay andyay aistway,
ithway uchsay appyhay illskay, atthay, onceyay eensay erethay, ityay ecamebay ayay artpay ofyay erhay,
andyay ityay asway ifficultday otay imagineyay erhay ithoutway ityay.

y“thay othermay isyay yonderyay omanway ithway ethay arletscay etterlay,” aidsay ethay eamansay.
ilt“way outhay arrycay erhay ayay essagemay omfray emay?”

if“ay ethay essagemay easesplay emay, Iyay illway,” answeredyay Earlpay.

en“thay elltay erhay,” ejoinedray ehay, at“thay Iyay akespay againyay ithway ethay
ack-a-visagedblay, ump-shoulderedhay oldyay octorday, andyay ehay engagesyay otay ingbray
ishay iendfray, ethay entlemangay eshay otsway ofyay, aboardyay ithway imhay. Osay etlay ythay
othermay aketay onay oughtthay, avesay orfay erselfhay andyay eethay. Iltway outhay elltay erhay
isthay, outhay itch-babyway?”

istress“may Ibbinshay ayssay ymay atherfay isyay ethay Incepray ofyay ethay Airyay!” iedcray
Earlpay, ithway ayay aughtynay ilesmay. if“ay outhay allestcay emay atthay illyay amenay, Iyay
allshay elltay imhay ofyay eethay; andyay ehay illway asechay ythay ipshay ithway ayay empesttay!”

Ursuingpay ayay igzagzay oursecay acrossyay ethay arket-placemay, ethay ildchay eturnedray
otay erhay othermay, andyay ommunicatedcay atwhay ethay arinermay adhay aidsay. Ester’shay
ongstray, almcay, eadfastlystay enduringyay iritspay almostyay anksay, atyay astlay, onyay
eholdingbay isthay arkday andyay imgray ountenancecay ofyay anyay inevitableyay oomday,
ich—atwhay ethay omentmay enwhay ayay assagepay eemedsay otay openyay orfay ethay inistermay
andyay erselfhay outyay ofyay eirthay abyrinthlay ofyay isery—showedmay itselfyay, ithway anyay
unrelentingyay ilesmay, ightray inyay ethay idstmay ofyay eirthay athpay.

Ithway erhay indmay arassedhay ybay ethay erribletay erplexitypay inyay ichwhay ethay
ipmaster’sshay intelligenceyay involvedyay erhay, eshay asway alsoyay ubjectedsay otay
anotheryay ialtray. Erethay ereway anymay eoplepay esentpray, omfray ethay ountrycay oundray
aboutyay, owhay adhay oftenyay eardhay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay, andyay otay omwhay ityay adhay
eenbay ademay errifictay ybay ayay undredhay alsefay oryay exaggeratedyay umorsray, utbay owhay
adhay evernay eheldbay ityay ithway eirthay ownyay odilybay eyesyay. Esethay, afteryay
exhaustingyay otheryay odesmay ofyay amusementyay, ownay ongedthray aboutyay Esterhay Ynnepray
ithway uderay andyay oorishbay intrusivenessyay. Unscrupulousyay asyay ityay asway, oweverhay,
ityay ouldcay otnay ingbray emthay earernay anthay ayay ircuitcay ofyay everalsay yardsyay. Atyay
atthay istanceday eythay accordinglyyay oodstay, ixedfay erethay ybay ethay entrifugalcay
orcefay ofyay ethay epugnanceray ichwhay ethay ysticmay ymbolsay inspiredyay. Ethay olewhay
anggay ofyay ailorssay, ikewiselay, observingyay ethay esspray ofyay ectatorsspay, andyay
earninglay ethay urportpay ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay, amecay andyay ustthray eirthay
unburntsay andyay esperado-lookingday acesfay intoyay ethay ingray. Evenyay ethay Indiansyay
ereway affectedyay ybay ayay ortsay ofyay oldcay adowshay ofyay ethay itewhay an’smay uriositycay,
andyay, idingglay oughthray ethay owdcray, astenedfay eirthay ake-likesnay ackblay eyesyay
onyay Ester’shay osombay; onceivingcay, erhapspay, atthay ethay earerway ofyay isthay
illiantlybray embroideredyay adgebay ustmay eedsnay ebay ayay ersonagepay ofyay ighhay
ignityday amongyay erhay eoplepay. Astlylay ethay inhabitantsyay ofyay ethay owntay eir(thay
ownyay interestyay inyay isthay orn-outway ubjectsay anguidlylay evivingray itselfyay, ybay
ympathysay ithway atwhay eythay awsay othersyay eelfay) oungedlay idlyyay otay ethay amesay
uarterqay, andyay ormentedtay Esterhay Ynnepray, erhapspay oremay anthay allyay ethay estray,
ithway eirthay oolcay, ell-acquaintedway azegay atyay erhay amiliarfay ameshay. Esterhay
awsay andyay ecognizedray ethay elfsamesay acesfay ofyay atthay oupgray ofyay atronsmay, owhay
adhay awaitedyay erhay orthcomingfay omfray ethay ison-doorpray, evensay yearsyay agoyay; allyay
avesay oneyay, ethay youngestyay andyay onlyyay ompassionatecay amongyay emthay, osewhay
urial-robebay eshay adhay incesay ademay. Atyay ethay inalfay ourhay, enwhay eshay asway osay
oonsay otay ingflay asideyay ethay urningbay etterlay, ityay adhay angelystray ecomebay ethay
entrecay ofyay oremay emarkray andyay excitementyay, andyay asway usthay ademay otay earsay erhay
eastbray oremay ainfullypay, anthay atyay anyyay imetay incesay ethay irstfay ayday eshay utpay ityay
onyay.

Ilewhay Esterhay oodstay inyay atthay agicmay irclecay ofyay ignominyyay, erewhay ethay unningcay
ueltycray ofyay erhay entencesay eemedsay otay avehay ixedfay erhay oreverfay, ethay
admirableyay eacherpray asway ookinglay ownday omfray ethay acredsay ulpitpay uponyay anyay
audienceyay osewhay eryvay inmostyay iritsspay adhay yieldedyay otay ishay ontrolcay. Ethay
aintedsay inistermay inyay ethay urchchay! Ethay omanway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay inyay ethay
arket-placemay! Atwhay imaginationyay ouldway avehay eenbay irreverentyay enoughyay otay
urmisesay atthay ethay amesay orchingscay igmastay asway onyay emthay othbay!

                            illustration[ay]

                                Iiixxay.

                 Ethay Evelationray Ofyay Ethay Arletscay Etterlay.


Ethay eloquentyay oicevay, onyay ichwhay ethay oulssay ofyay ethay isteninglay audienceyay adhay
eenbay ornebay aloftyay asyay onyay ethay ellingsway avesway ofyay ethay easay, atyay engthlay amecay
otay ayay ausepay. Erethay asway ayay omentarymay ilencesay, ofoundpray asyay atwhay ouldshay
ollowfay ethay utteranceyay ofyay oraclesyay. Enthay ensuedyay ayay urmurmay andyay alf-hushedhay
umulttay; asyay ifyay ethay auditorsyay, eleasedray omfray ethay ighhay ellspay atthay adhay
ansportedtray emthay intoyay ethay egionray ofyay another’syay indmay, ereway eturningray
intoyay emselvesthay, ithway allyay eirthay aweyay andyay onderway illstay eavyhay onyay emthay. Inyay
ayay omentmay oremay, ethay owdcray eganbay otay ushgay orthfay omfray ethay oorsday ofyay ethay
urchchay. Ownay atthay erethay asway anyay endyay, eythay eedednay otheryay eathbray, oremay itfay
otay upportsay ethay ossgray andyay earthlyyay ifelay intoyay ichwhay eythay elapsedray, anthay
atthay atmosphereyay ichwhay ethay eacherpray adhay onvertedcay intoyay ordsway ofyay ameflay,
andyay adhay urdenedbay ithway ethay ichray agrancefray ofyay ishay oughtthay.

Inyay ethay openyay airyay eirthay aptureray okebray intoyay eechspay. Ethay eetstray andyay ethay
arket-placemay absolutelyyay abbledbay, omfray idesay otay idesay, ithway applausesyay ofyay
ethay inistermay. Ishay earershay ouldcay otnay estray untilyay eythay adhay oldtay oneyay
anotheryay ofyay atwhay eachyay ewknay etterbay anthay ehay ouldcay elltay oryay earhay. Accordingyay
otay eirthay unitedyay estimonytay, evernay adhay anmay okenspay inyay osay iseway, osay ighhay,
andyay osay olyhay ayay iritspay, asyay ehay atthay akespay isthay ayday; ornay adhay inspirationyay
everyay eathedbray oughthray ortalmay ipslay oremay evidentlyyay anthay ityay idday oughthray
ishay. Itsyay influenceyay ouldcay ebay eensay, asyay ityay ereway, escendingday uponyay imhay, andyay
ossessingpay imhay, andyay ontinuallycay iftinglay imhay outyay ofyay ethay ittenwray
iscourseday atthay aylay eforebay imhay, andyay illingfay imhay ithway ideasyay atthay ustmay
avehay eenbay asyay arvellousmay otay imselfhay asyay otay ishay audienceyay. Ishay ubjectsay, ityay
appearedyay, adhay eenbay ethay elationray etweenbay ethay Eityday andyay ethay ommunitiescay
ofyay ankindmay, ithway ayay ecialspay eferenceray otay ethay Ewnay Englandyay ichwhay eythay
ereway erehay antingplay inyay ethay ildernessway. Andyay, asyay ehay ewdray owardstay ethay
oseclay, ayay iritspay asyay ofyay ophecypray adhay omecay uponyay imhay, onstrainingcay imhay otay
itsyay urposepay asyay ightilymay asyay ethay oldyay ophetspray ofyay Israelyay ereway
onstrainedcay; onlyyay ithway isthay ifferenceday, atthay, ereaswhay ethay Ewishjay eerssay
adhay enouncedday udgmentsjay andyay uinray onyay eirthay ountrycay, ityay asway ishay issionmay
otay oretellfay ayay ighhay andyay oriousglay estinyday orfay ethay ewlynay atheredgay eoplepay
ofyay ethay Ordlay. Utbay, oughoutthray ityay allyay, andyay oughthray ethay olewhay iscourseday,
erethay adhay eenbay ayay ertaincay eepday, adsay undertoneyay ofyay athospay, ichwhay ouldcay
otnay ebay interpretedyay otherwiseyay anthay asyay ethay aturalnay egretray ofyay oneyay oonsay otay
asspay awayyay. Yesyay; eirthay inistermay omwhay eythay osay oved—andlay owhay osay ovedlay
emthay allyay, atthay ehay ouldcay otnay epartday eavenwardhay ithoutway ayay igh—hadsay ethay
orebodingfay ofyay untimelyyay eathday uponyay imhay, andyay ouldway oonsay eavelay emthay inyay
eirthay earstay! Isthay ideayay ofyay ishay ansitorytray aystay onyay earthyay avegay ethay astlay
emphasisyay otay ethay effectyay ichwhay ethay eacherpray adhay oducedpray; ityay asway asyay ifyay
anyay angelyay, inyay ishay assagepay otay ethay iesskay, adhay akenshay ishay ightbray ingsway
overyay ethay eoplepay orfay anyay instant,—atyay onceyay ayay adowshay andyay ayay
endor,—andsplay adhay edshay ownday ayay owershay ofyay oldengay uthstray uponyay emthay.

Usthay, erethay adhay omecay otay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdale—asday otay ostmay enmay,
inyay eirthay ariousvay eressphay, oughthay eldomsay ecognizedray untilyay eythay eesay ityay
arfay ehindbay em—anthay epochyay ofyay ifelay oremay illiantbray andyay ullfay ofyay iumphtray
anthay anyyay eviouspray oneyay, oryay anthay anyyay ichwhay ouldcay ereafterhay ebay. Ehay oodstay,
atyay isthay omentmay, onyay ethay eryvay oudestpray eminenceyay ofyay uperioritysay, otay ichwhay
ethay iftsgay ofyay intellectyay, ichray orelay, evailingpray eloquenceyay, andyay ayay
eputationray ofyay itestwhay anctitysay, ouldcay exaltyay ayay ergymanclay inyay Ewnay
England’syay earliestyay aysday, enwhay ethay ofessionalpray aracterchay asway ofyay itselfyay
ayay oftylay edestalpay. Uchsay asway ethay ositionpay ichwhay ethay inistermay occupiedyay,
asyay ehay owedbay ishay eadhay orwardfay onyay ethay ushionscay ofyay ethay ulpitpay, atyay ethay
oseclay ofyay ishay Electionyay Ermonsay. Eanwhilemay Esterhay Ynnepray asway andingstay
esidebay ethay affoldscay ofyay ethay illorypay, ithway ethay arletscay etterlay illstay
urningbay onyay erhay eastbray!

Ownay asway eardhay againyay ethay angorclay ofyay ethay usicmay, andyay ethay easuredmay amptray
ofyay ethay ilitarymay escortyay, issuingyay omfray ethay urch-doorchay. Ethay ocessionpray
asway otay ebay arshalledmay encethay otay ethay own-halltay, erewhay ayay olemnsay anquetbay
ouldway ompletecay ethay eremoniescay ofyay ethay ayday.

Onceyay oremay, ereforethay, ethay aintray ofyay enerablevay andyay ajesticmay athersfay asway
eensay ovingmay oughthray ayay oadbray athwaypay ofyay ethay eoplepay, owhay ewdray ackbay
everentlyray, onyay eitheryay idesay, asyay ethay Overnorgay andyay agistratesmay, ethay oldyay
andyay iseway enmay, ethay olyhay inistersmay, andyay allyay atthay ereway eminentyay andyay
enownedray, advancedyay intoyay ethay idstmay ofyay emthay. Enwhay eythay ereway airlyfay inyay
ethay arket-placemay, eirthay esencepray asway eetedgray ybay ayay outshay. Is—thoughthay
oubtlessday ityay ightmay acquireyay additionalyay orcefay andyay olumevay omfray ethay
ildlikechay oyaltylay ichwhay ethay ageyay awardedyay otay itsyay ulers—wasray eltfay otay ebay
anyay irrepressibleyay outburstyay ofyay enthusiasmyay indledkay inyay ethay auditorsyay ybay
atthay ighhay ainstray ofyay eloquenceyay ichwhay asway yetyay everberatingray inyay eirthay
earsyay. Eachyay eltfay ethay impulseyay inyay imselfhay, andyay, inyay ethay amesay eathbray,
aughtcay ityay omfray ishay eighbornay. Ithinway ethay urchchay, ityay adhay ardlyhay eenbay
eptkay ownday; eneathbay ethay yskay, ityay ealedpay upwardyay otay ethay enithzay. Erethay ereway
umanhay eingsbay enoughyay, andyay enoughyay ofyay ighlyhay oughtwray andyay ymphonioussay
eelingfay, otay oducepray atthay oremay impressiveyay oundsay anthay ethay organyay onestay ofyay
ethay astblay, oryay ethay underthay, oryay ethay oarray ofyay ethay easay; evenyay atthay ightymay
ellsway ofyay anymay oicesvay, endedblay intoyay oneyay eatgray oicevay ybay ethay universalyay
impulseyay ichwhay akesmay ikewiselay oneyay astvay earthay outyay ofyay ethay anymay. Evernay,
omfray ethay oilsay ofyay Ewnay Englandyay, adhay onegay upyay uchsay ayay outshay! Evernay, onyay Ewnay
Englandyay oilsay, adhay oodstay ethay anmay osay onoredhay ybay ishay ortalmay ethrenbray asyay
ethay eacherpray!

Owhay aredfay ityay ithway imhay enthay? Ereway erethay otnay ethay illiantbray articlespay ofyay
ayay alohay inyay ethay airyay aboutyay ishay eadhay? Osay etherealizedyay ybay iritspay asyay ehay asway,
andyay osay apotheosizedyay ybay orshippingway admirersyay, idday ishay ootstepsfay, inyay ethay
ocessionpray, eallyray eadtray uponyay ethay ustday ofyay earthyay?

Asyay ethay anksray ofyay ilitarymay enmay andyay ivilcay athersfay ovedmay onwardyay, allyay eyesyay
ereway urnedtay owardstay ethay ointpay erewhay ethay inistermay asway eensay otay approachyay
amongyay emthay. Ethay outshay iedday intoyay ayay urmurmay, asyay oneyay ortionpay ofyay ethay owdcray
afteryay anotheryay obtainedyay ayay impseglay ofyay imhay. Owhay eeblefay andyay alepay ehay
ookedlay, amidyay allyay ishay iumphtray! Ethay energy—oryay aysay, atherray, ethay
inspirationyay ichwhay adhay eldhay imhay upyay, untilyay ehay ouldshay avehay eliveredday ethay
acredsay essagemay atthay oughtbray itsyay ownyay engthstray alongyay ithway ityay omfray
eaven—washay ithdrawnway, ownay atthay ityay adhay osay aithfullyfay erformedpay itsyay
officeyay. Ethay owglay, ichwhay eythay adhay ustjay eforebay eheldbay urningbay onyay ishay
eekchay, asway extinguishedyay, ikelay ayay ameflay atthay inkssay ownday opelesslyhay
amongyay ethay ate-decayinglay embersyay. Ityay eemedsay ardlyhay ethay acefay ofyay ayay anmay
aliveyay, ithway uchsay ayay eath-likeday uehay; ityay asway ardlyhay ayay anmay ithway ifelay inyay
imhay, atthay otteredtay onyay ishay athpay osay ervelesslynay, yetyay otteredtay, andyay idday
otnay allfay!

Oneyay ofyay ishay ericalclay ethren,—itbray asway ethay enerablevay Ohnjay
Ilson,—observingway ethay atestay inyay ichwhay Mray. Immesdaleday asway eftlay ybay ethay
etiringray aveway ofyay intellectyay andyay ensibilitysay, eppedstay orwardfay astilyhay otay
offeryay ishay upportsay. Ethay inistermay emulouslytray, utbay ecidedlyday, epelledray
ethay oldyay an’smay armyay. Ehay illstay alkedway onwardyay, ifyay atthay ovementmay ouldcay ebay
osay escribedday, ichwhay atherray esembledray ethay averingway effortyay ofyay anyay infantyay,
ithway itsyay other’smay armsyay inyay iewvay, outstretchedyay otay empttay imhay orwardfay. Andyay
ownay, almostyay imperceptibleyay asyay ereway ethay atterlay epsstay ofyay ishay ogresspray, ehay
adhay omecay oppositeyay ethay ell-rememberedway andyay eather-darkenedway affoldscay,
erewhay, onglay incesay, ithway allyay atthay earydray apselay ofyay imetay etweenbay, Esterhay
Ynnepray adhay encounteredyay ethay orld’sway ignominiousyay arestay. Erethay oodstay
Esterhay, oldinghay ittlelay Earlpay ybay ethay andhay! Andyay erethay asway ethay arletscay
etterlay onyay erhay eastbray! Ethay inistermay erehay ademay ayay ausepay; althoughyay ethay
usicmay illstay ayedplay ethay atelystay andyay ejoicingray archmay otay ichwhay ethay
ocessionpray ovedmay. Ityay ummonedsay imhay onward,—onwardyay otay ethay
estival!—butfay erehay ehay ademay ayay ausepay.

Ellinghambay, orfay ethay astlay ewfay omentsmay, adhay eptkay anyay anxiousyay eyeyay uponyay
imhay. Ehay ownay eftlay ishay ownyay aceplay inyay ethay ocessionpray, andyay advancedyay otay ivegay
assistanceyay; udgingjay, omfray Mray. Immesdale’sday aspectyay, atthay ehay ustmay
otherwiseyay inevitablyyay allfay. Utbay erethay asway omethingsay inyay ethay atter’slay
expressionyay atthay arnedway ackbay ethay agistratemay, althoughyay ayay anmay otnay eadilyray
obeyingyay ethay aguevay intimationsyay atthay asspay omfray oneyay iritspay otay anotheryay.
Ethay owdcray, eanwhilemay, ookedlay onyay ithway aweyay andyay onderway. Isthay earthlyyay
aintnessfay asway, inyay eirthay iewvay, onlyyay anotheryay asephay ofyay ethay inister’smay
elestialcay engthstray; ornay ouldway ityay avehay eemedsay ayay iraclemay ootay ighhay otay ebay
oughtwray orfay oneyay osay olyhay, adhay ehay ascendedyay eforebay eirthay eyesyay, axingway
immerday andyay ighterbray, andyay adingfay atyay astlay intoyay ethay ightlay ofyay eavenhay.

Ehay urnedtay owardstay ethay affoldscay, andyay etchedstray orthfay ishay armsyay.

ester“hay,” aidsay ehay, ome“cay itherhay! Omecay, ymay ittlelay Earlpay!”

Ityay asway ayay astlyghay ooklay ithway ichwhay ehay egardedray emthay; utbay erethay asway
omethingsay atyay onceyay endertay andyay angelystray iumphanttray inyay ityay. Ethay ildchay,
ithway ethay ird-likebay otionmay ichwhay asway oneyay ofyay erhay aracteristicschay, ewflay
otay imhay, andyay aspedclay erhay armsyay aboutyay ishay eesknay. Esterhay Ynne—slowlypray,
asyay ifyay impelledyay ybay inevitableyay atefay, andyay againstyay erhay ongeststray
ill—likewiseway ewdray earnay, utbay ausedpay eforebay eshay eachedray imhay. Atyay isthay
instantyay, oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay ustthray imselfhay oughthray ethay
owd,—orcray, erhapspay, osay arkday, isturbedday, andyay evilyay, asway ishay ooklay, ehay
oseray upyay outyay ofyay omesay ethernay egion,—toray atchsnay ackbay ishay ictimvay omfray
atwhay ehay oughtsay otay oday! Ebay atthay asyay ityay ightmay, ethay oldyay anmay ushedray orwardfay,
andyay aughtcay ethay inistermay ybay ethay armyay.

adman“may, oldhay! atwhay isyay youryay urposepay?” isperedwhay ehay. ave“way ackbay atthay
omanway! Astcay offyay isthay ildchay! Allyay allshay ebay ellway! Oday otnay ackenblay youryay
amefay, andyay erishpay inyay ishonorday! Iyay ancay yetyay avesay youyay! Ouldway youyay ingbray
infamyyay onyay youryay acredsay ofessionpray?”

a“hay, emptertay! Ethinksmay outhay artyay ootay atelay!” answeredyay ethay inistermay,
encounteringyay ishay eyeyay, earfullyfay, utbay irmlyfay. y“thay owerpay isyay otnay atwhay ityay
asway! Ithway Od’sgay elphay, Iyay allshay escapeyay eethay ownay!”

Ehay againyay extendedyay ishay andhay otay ethay omanway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay.

ester“hay Ynnepray,” iedcray ehay, ithway ayay iercingpay earnestnessyay, in“ay ethay amenay
ofyay Imhay, osay erribletay andyay osay ercifulmay, owhay ivesgay emay acegray, atyay isthay astlay
omentmay, otay oday at—forwhay ymay ownyay eavyhay insay andyay iserablemay agony—iyay
ithheldway yselfmay omfray oingday evensay yearsyay agoyay, omecay itherhay ownay, andyay inetway
ythay engthstray aboutyay emay! Ythay engthstray, Esterhay; utbay etlay ityay ebay uidedgay ybay
ethay illway ichwhay Odgay athhay antedgray emay! Isthay etchedwray andyay ongedwray oldyay anmay
isyay opposingyay ityay ithway allyay ishay ight!—withmay allyay ishay ownyay ightmay, andyay ethay
iend’sfay! Omecay, Esterhay, omecay! Upportsay emay upyay yonderyay affoldscay!”

Ethay owdcray asway inyay ayay umulttay. Ethay enmay ofyay ankray andyay ignityday, owhay oodstay oremay
immediatelyyay aroundyay ethay ergymanclay, ereway osay akentay ybay urprisesay, andyay osay
erplexedpay asyay otay ethay urportpay ofyay atwhay eythay aw,—unablesay otay eceiveray ethay
explanationyay ichwhay ostmay eadilyray esentedpray itselfyay, oryay otay imagineyay anyyay
other,—thatyay eythay emainedray ilentsay andyay inactiveyay ectatorsspay ofyay ethay
udgmentjay ichwhay Ovidencepray eemedsay aboutyay otay orkway. Eythay eheldbay ethay
inistermay, eaninglay onyay Ester’shay ouldershay, andyay upportedsay ybay erhay armyay
aroundyay imhay, approachyay ethay affoldscay, andyay ascendyay itsyay epsstay; ilewhay illstay
ethay ittlelay andhay ofyay ethay in-bornsay ildchay asway aspedclay inyay ishay. Oldyay Ogerray
Illingworthchay ollowedfay, asyay oneyay intimatelyyay onnectedcay ithway ethay amadray ofyay
uiltgay andyay orrowsay inyay ichwhay eythay adhay allyay eenbay actorsyay, andyay ellway entitledyay,
ereforethay, otay ebay esentpray atyay itsyay osingclay enescay.

adst“hay outhay oughtsay ethay olewhay earthyay overyay,” aidsay ehay, ookinglay arklyday atyay
ethay ergymanclay, ere“thay asway onay oneyay aceplay osay ecret,—nosay ighhay aceplay ornay
owlylay aceplay, erewhay outhay ouldstcay avehay escapedyay e,—savemay onyay isthay eryvay
affoldscay!”

anks“thay ebay otay Imhay owhay athhay edlay emay itherhay!” answeredyay ethay inistermay.

Yetyay ehay embledtray, andyay urnedtay otay Esterhay ithway anyay expressionyay ofyay oubtday andyay
anxietyyay inyay ishay eyesyay, otnay ethay esslay evidentlyyay etrayedbay, atthay erethay asway ayay
eeblefay ilesmay uponyay ishay ipslay.

is“ay otnay isthay etterbay,” urmuredmay ehay, an“thay atwhay eway eameddray ofyay inyay ethay
orestfay?”

i“ay owknay otnay! Iyay owknay otnay!” eshay urriedlyhay epliedray. etter“bay? Yeayay; osay eway
aymay othbay ieday, andyay ittlelay Earlpay ieday ithway usyay!”

or“fay eethay andyay Earlpay, ebay ityay asyay Odgay allshay orderyay,” aidsay ethay inistermay;
and“ay Odgay isyay ercifulmay! Etlay emay ownay oday ethay illway ichwhay ehay athhay ademay ainplay
eforebay ymay ightsay. Orfay, Esterhay, Iyay amyay ayay yingday anmay. Osay etlay emay akemay astehay
otay aketay ymay ameshay uponyay emay!”

Artlypay upportedsay ybay Esterhay Ynnepray, andyay oldinghay oneyay andhay ofyay ittlelay
Earl’spay, ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday urnedtay otay ethay ignifiedday andyay
enerablevay ulersray; otay ethay olyhay inistersmay, owhay ereway ishay ethrenbray; otay ethay
eoplepay, osewhay eatgray earthay asway oroughlythay appalledyay, yetyay overflowingyay
ithway earfultay ympathysay, asyay owingknay atthay omesay eepday ife-matter—whichlay,
ifyay ullfay ofyay insay, asway ullfay ofyay anguishyay andyay epentanceray ikewise—waslay ownay
otay ebay aidlay openyay otay emthay. Ethay unsay, utbay ittlelay astpay itsyay eridianmay, oneshay
ownday uponyay ethay ergymanclay, andyay avegay ayay istinctnessday otay ishay igurefay, asyay ehay
oodstay outyay omfray allyay ethay earthyay, otay utpay inyay ishay eaplay ofyay uiltygay atyay ethay arbay
ofyay Eternalyay Usticejay.

eople“pay ofyay Ewnay Englandyay!” iedcray ehay, ithway ayay oicevay atthay oseray overyay emthay,
ighhay, olemnsay, andyay ajestic,—yetmay adhay alwaysyay ayay emortray oughthray ityay, andyay
ometimessay ayay iekshray, ugglingstray upyay outyay ofyay ayay athomlessfay epthday ofyay emorseray
andyay oe,—“yeway, atthay avehay ovedlay e!—yemay, atthay avehay eemedday emay
oly!—beholdhay emay erehay, ethay oneyay innersay ofyay ethay orldway! Atyay ast!—atlay
ast!—ilay andstay uponyay ethay otspay erewhay, evensay yearsyay incesay, Iyay ouldshay avehay
oodstay; erehay, ithway isthay omanway, osewhay armyay, oremay anthay ethay ittlelay engthstray
erewithwhay Iyay avehay eptcray itherwardhay, ustainssay emay, atyay isthay eadfuldray
omentmay, omfray ovellinggray ownday uponyay ymay acefay! Olay, ethay arletscay etterlay
ichwhay Esterhay earsway! Yeyay avehay allyay udderedshay atyay ityay! Ereverwhay erhay alkway
athhay een,—whereverbay, osay iserablymay urdenedbay, eshay aymay avehay opedhay otay
indfay epose,—itray athhay astcay ayay uridlay eamglay ofyay aweyay andyay orriblehay
epugnanceray oundray aboutyay erhay. Utbay erethay oodstay oneyay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay youyay,
atyay osewhay andbray ofyay insay andyay infamyyay yeyay avehay otnay udderedshay!”

Ityay eemedsay, atyay isthay ointpay, asyay ifyay ethay inistermay ustmay eavelay ethay emainderray
ofyay ishay ecretsay undisclosedyay. Utbay ehay oughtfay ackbay ethay odilybay
eakness,—andway, illstay oremay, ethay aintnessfay ofyay eart,—thathay asway ivingstray
orfay ethay asterymay ithway imhay. Ehay ewthray offyay allyay assistanceyay, andyay eppedstay
assionatelypay orwardfay ayay acepay eforebay ethay omanway andyay ethay ildchay.

it“ay asway onyay imhay!” ehay ontinuedcay, ithway ayay indkay ofyay iercenessfay; osay
eterminedday asway ehay otay eakspay outyay ethay olewhay. od’s“gay eyeyay eheldbay ityay! Ethay
angelsyay ereway oreverfay ointingpay atyay ityay! Ethay Evilday ewknay ityay ellway, andyay
ettedfray ityay ontinuallycay ithway ethay ouchtay ofyay ishay urningbay ingerfay! Utbay ehay
idhay ityay unninglycay omfray enmay, andyay alkedway amongyay youyay ithway ethay ienmay ofyay ayay
iritspay, ournfulmay, ecausebay osay urepay inyay ayay infulsay orld!—andway adsay, ecausebay
ehay issedmay ishay eavenlyhay indredkay! Ownay, atyay ethay eath-hourday, ehay andsstay upyay
eforebay youyay! Ehay idsbay youyay ooklay againyay atyay Ester’shay arletscay etterlay! Ehay
ellstay youyay, atthay, ithway allyay itsyay ysteriousmay orrorhay, ityay isyay utbay ethay adowshay
ofyay atwhay ehay earsbay onyay ishay ownyay eastbray, andyay atthay evenyay isthay, ishay ownyay edray
igmastay, isyay onay oremay anthay ethay ypetay ofyay atwhay ashay earedsay ishay inmostyay earthay!
Andstay anyyay erehay atthay uestionqay Od’sgay udgmentjay onyay ayay innersay? Eholdbay!
Eholdbay ayay eadfuldray itnessway ofyay ityay!”

illustration[ay: all“shay eway otnay eetmay againyay?”]

Ithway ayay onvulsivecay otionmay, ehay oretay awayyay ethay inisterialmay andbay omfray
eforebay ishay eastbray. Ityay asway evealedray! Utbay ityay ereway irreverentyay otay escribeday
atthay evelationray. Orfay anyay instantyay, ethay azegay ofyay ethay orror-strickenhay
ultitudemay asway oncentredcay onyay ethay astlyghay iraclemay; ilewhay ethay inistermay
oodstay, ithway ayay ushflay ofyay iumphtray inyay ishay acefay, asyay oneyay owhay, inyay ethay
isiscray ofyay acutestyay ainpay, adhay onway ayay ictoryvay. Enthay, ownday ehay anksay uponyay ethay
affoldscay! Esterhay artlypay aisedray imhay, andyay upportedsay ishay eadhay againstyay erhay
osombay. Oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay eltknay ownday esidebay imhay, ithway ayay ankblay,
ullday ountenancecay, outyay ofyay ichwhay ethay ifelay eemedsay otay avehay epartedday.

ou“thay asthay escapedyay emay!” ehay epeatedray oremay anthay onceyay. ou“thay asthay escapedyay
emay!”

ay“may Odgay orgivefay eethay!” aidsay ethay inistermay. ou“thay, ootay, asthay eeplyday
innedsay!”

Ehay ithdrewway ishay yingday eyesyay omfray ethay oldyay anmay, andyay ixedfay emthay onyay ethay
omanway andyay ethay ildchay.

y“may ittlelay Earlpay,” aidsay ehay, eebly,—andfay erethay asway ayay eetsway andyay entlegay
ilesmay overyay ishay acefay, asyay ofyay ayay iritspay inkingsay intoyay eepday eposeray; aynay, ownay
atthay ethay urdenbay asway emovedray, ityay eemedsay almostyay asyay ifyay ehay ouldway ebay
ortivespay ithway ethay ild,—“dearchay ittlelay Earlpay, iltway outhay isskay emay ownay?
Outhay ouldstway otnay, yonderyay, inyay ethay orestfay! Utbay ownay outhay iltway?”

Earlpay issedkay ishay ipslay. Ayay ellspay asway okenbray. Ethay eatgray enescay ofyay iefgray,
inyay ichwhay ethay ildway infantyay orebay ayay artpay, adhay evelopedday allyay erhay
ympathiessay; andyay asyay erhay earstay ellfay uponyay erhay ather’sfay eekchay, eythay ereway
ethay edgeplay atthay eshay ouldway owgray upyay amidyay umanhay oyjay andyay orrowsay, ornay
oreverfay oday attlebay ithway ethay orldway, utbay ebay ayay omanway inyay ityay. Owardstay erhay
othermay, ootay, Earl’spay errandyay asyay ayay essengermay ofyay anguishyay asway allyay
ulfilledfay.

ester“hay,” aidsay ethay ergymanclay, arewell“fay!”

all“shay eway otnay eetmay againyay?” isperedwhay eshay, endingbay erhay acefay ownday oseclay
otay ishay. all“shay eway otnay endspay ouryay immortalyay ifelay ogethertay? Urelysay,
urelysay, eway avehay ansomedray oneyay anotheryay, ithway allyay isthay oeway! Outhay ookestlay
arfay intoyay eternityyay, ithway osethay ightbray yingday eyesyay! Enthay elltay emay atwhay
outhay eestsay?”

ush“hay, Esterhay, ushhay!” aidsay ehay, ithway emuloustray olemnitysay. e“thay awlay eway
oke!—thebray insay erehay osay awfullyyay evealed!—letray esethay aloneyay ebay inyay ythay
oughtsthay! Iyay earfay! Iyay earfay! Ityay aymay ebay, atthay, enwhay eway orgotfay ouryay
Od,—whengay eway iolatedvay ouryay everenceray eachyay orfay ethay other’syay oul,—itsay
asway enceforththay ainvay otay opehay atthay eway ouldcay eetmay ereafterhay, inyay anyay
everlastingyay andyay urepay eunionray. Odgay owsknay; andyay Ehay isyay ercifulmay! Ehay athhay
ovedpray ishay ercymay, ostmay ofyay allyay, inyay ymay afflictionsyay. Ybay ivinggay emay isthay
urningbay orturetay otay earbay uponyay ymay eastbray! Ybay endingsay yonderyay arkday andyay
erribletay oldyay anmay, otay eepkay ethay orturetay alwaysyay atyay ed-heatray! Ybay ingingbray
emay itherhay, otay ieday isthay eathday ofyay iumphanttray ignominyyay eforebay ethay eoplepay!
Adhay eitheryay ofyay esethay agoniesyay eenbay antingway, Iyay adhay eenbay ostlay oreverfay!
Aisedpray ebay ishay amenay! Ishay illway ebay oneday! Arewellfay!”

Atthay inalfay ordway amecay orthfay ithway ethay inister’smay expiringyay eathbray. Ethay
ultitudemay, ilentsay illtay enthay, okebray outyay inyay ayay angestray, eepday oicevay ofyay aweyay
andyay onderway, ichwhay ouldcay otnay asyay yetyay indfay utteranceyay, avesay inyay isthay urmurmay
atthay olledray osay eavilyhay afteryay ethay epartedday iritspay.

                            illustration[ay]

                                 Ivxxay.

                              Onclusioncay.


Afteryay anymay aysday, enwhay imetay ufficedsay orfay ethay eoplepay otay arrangeyay eirthay
oughtsthay inyay eferenceray otay ethay oregoingfay enescay, erethay asway oremay anthay oneyay
accountyay ofyay atwhay adhay eenbay itnessedway onyay ethay affoldscay.

Ostmay ofyay ethay ectatorsspay estifiedtay otay avinghay eensay, onyay ethay eastbray ofyay ethay
unhappyyay inistermay, ayay Arletscay Etter—thelay eryvay emblancesay ofyay atthay ornway ybay
Esterhay Ynne—imprintedpray inyay ethay eshflay. Asyay egardedray itsyay originyay, erethay
ereway ariousvay explanationsyay, allyay ofyay ichwhay ustmay ecessarilynay avehay eenbay
onjecturalcay. Omesay affirmedyay atthay ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, onyay ethay
eryvay ayday enwhay Esterhay Ynnepray irstfay oreway erhay ignominiousyay adgebay, adhay
egunbay ayay oursecay ofyay enance,—whichpay ehay afterwardsyay, inyay osay anymay utilefay
ethodsmay, ollowedfay out,—byyay inflictingyay ayay ideoushay orturetay onyay imselfhay.
Othersyay ontendedcay atthay ethay igmastay adhay otnay eenbay oducedpray untilyay ayay onglay
imetay ubsequentsay, enwhay oldyay Ogerray Illingworthchay, eingbay ayay otentpay
ecromancernay, adhay ausedcay ityay otay appearyay, oughthray ethay agencyyay ofyay agicmay andyay
oisonouspay ugsdray. Othersyay, again,—andyay osethay estbay ableyay otay appreciateyay
ethay inister’smay eculiarpay ensibilitysay, andyay ethay onderfulway operationyay ofyay
ishay iritspay uponyay ethay ody,—whisperedbay eirthay eliefbay, atthay ethay awfulyay
ymbolsay asway ethay effectyay ofyay ethay ever-activeyay oothtay ofyay emorseray, awinggnay
omfray ethay inmostyay earthay outwardlyyay, andyay atyay astlay anifestingmay Eaven’shay
eadfuldray udgmentjay ybay ethay isiblevay esencepray ofyay ethay etterlay. Ethay eaderray
aymay oosechay amongyay esethay eoriesthay. Eway avehay ownthray allyay ethay ightlay eway ouldcay
acquireyay uponyay ethay ortentpay, andyay ouldway adlyglay, ownay atthay ityay ashay oneday itsyay
officeyay, eraseyay itsyay eepday intpray outyay ofyay ouryay ownyay ainbray; erewhay onglay
editationmay ashay ixedfay ityay inyay eryvay undesirableyay istinctnessday.

Ityay isyay ingularsay, everthelessnay, atthay ertaincay ersonspay, owhay ereway
ectatorsspay ofyay ethay olewhay enescay, andyay ofessedpray evernay onceyay otay avehay
emovedray eirthay eyesyay omfray ethay Everendray Mray. Immesdaleday, eniedday atthay erethay
asway anyyay arkmay ateverwhay onyay ishay eastbray, oremay anthay onyay ayay ew-bornnay infant’syay.
Eithernay, ybay eirthay eportray, adhay ishay yingday ordsway acknowledgedyay, ornay evenyay
emotelyray impliedyay, anyyay, ethay ightestslay onnectioncay, onyay ishay artpay, ithway ethay
uiltgay orfay ichwhay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay osay onglay ornway ethay arletscay etterlay.
Accordingyay otay esethay ighlyhay espectableray itnessesway, ethay inistermay,
onsciouscay atthay ehay asway ying,—consciousday, alsoyay, atthay ethay everenceray ofyay
ethay ultitudemay acedplay imhay alreadyyay amongyay aintssay andyay angels,—hadyay
esiredday, ybay yieldingyay upyay ishay eathbray inyay ethay armsyay ofyay atthay allenfay omanway,
otay expressyay otay ethay orldway owhay utterlyyay ugatorynay isyay ethay oicestchay ofyay an’smay
ownyay ighteousnessray. Afteryay exhaustingyay ifelay inyay ishay effortsyay orfay ankind’smay
iritualspay oodgay, ehay adhay ademay ethay annermay ofyay ishay eathday ayay arablepay, inyay
orderyay otay impressyay onyay ishay admirersyay ethay ightymay andyay ournfulmay essonlay, atthay,
inyay ethay iewvay ofyay Infiniteyay Uritypay, eway areyay innerssay allyay alikeyay. Ityay asway otay
eachtay emthay, atthay ethay oliesthay amongyay usyay ashay utbay attainedyay osay arfay aboveyay
ishay ellowsfay asyay otay iscernday oremay earlyclay ethay Ercymay ichwhay ookslay ownday,
andyay epudiateray oremay utterlyyay ethay antomphay ofyay umanhay eritmay, ichwhay ouldway
ooklay aspiringlyyay upwardyay. Ithoutway isputingday ayay uthtray osay omentousmay, eway
ustmay ebay allowedyay otay onsidercay isthay ersionvay ofyay Mray. Immesdale’sday orystay asyay
onlyyay anyay instanceyay ofyay atthay ubbornstay idelityfay ithway ichwhay ayay an’smay
iends—andfray especiallyyay ayay ergyman’s—willclay ometimessay upholdyay ishay
aracterchay, enwhay oofspray, earclay asyay ethay id-daymay unshinesay onyay ethay arletscay
etterlay, establishyay imhay ayay alsefay andyay in-stainedsay eaturecray ofyay ethay ustday.

Ethay authorityyay ichwhay eway avehay ieflychay ollowed,—afay anuscriptmay ofyay oldyay
ateday, awndray upyay omfray ethay erbalvay estimonytay ofyay individualsyay, omesay ofyay omwhay
adhay ownknay Esterhay Ynnepray, ilewhay othersyay adhay eardhay ethay aletay omfray
ontemporarycay itnesses,—fullyway onfirmscay ethay iewvay akentay inyay ethay
oregoingfay agespay. Amongyay anymay oralsmay ichwhay esspray uponyay usyay omfray ethay oorpay
inister’smay iserablemay experienceyay, eway utpay onlyyay isthay intoyay ayay
entence:—“besay uetray! Ebay uetray! Ebay uetray! Owshay eelyfray otay ethay orldway, ifyay
otnay youryay orstway, yetyay omesay aittray erebywhay ethay orstway aymay ebay inferredyay!”

Othingnay asway oremay emarkableray anthay ethay angechay ichwhay ooktay aceplay, almostyay
immediatelyyay afteryay Mray. Immesdale’sday eathday, inyay ethay appearanceyay andyay
emeanorday ofyay ethay oldyay anmay ownknay asyay Ogerray Illingworthchay. Allyay ishay engthstray
andyay energy—allyay ishay italvay andyay intellectualyay orce—seemedfay atyay onceyay otay
esertday imhay; insomuchyay atthay ehay ositivelypay itheredway upyay, ivelledshray awayyay,
andyay almostyay anishedvay omfray ortalmay ightsay, ikelay anyay uprootedyay eedway atthay ieslay
iltingway inyay ethay unsay. Isthay unhappyyay anmay adhay ademay ethay eryvay inciplepray ofyay
ishay ifelay otay onsistcay inyay ethay ursuitpay andyay ystematicsay exerciseyay ofyay evengeray;
andyay enwhay, ybay itsyay ompletestcay iumphtray andyay onsummationcay, atthay evilyay
inciplepray asway eftlay ithway onay urtherfay aterialmay otay upportsay ityay, enwhay, inyay
ortshay, erethay asway onay oremay Evil’sday orkway onyay earthyay orfay imhay otay oday, ityay onlyyay
emainedray orfay ethay unhumanizedyay ortalmay otay etakebay imselfhay itherwhay ishay
Astermay ouldway indfay imhay askstay enoughyay, andyay aypay imhay ishay agesway ulyday. Utbay,
otay allyay esethay adowyshay eingsbay, osay onglay ouryay earnay acquaintances,—asyay ellway
Ogerray Illingworthchay asyay ishay ompanions,—wecay ouldway ainfay ebay ercifulmay. Ityay
isyay ayay uriouscay ubjectsay ofyay observationyay andyay inquiryyay, etherwhay atredhay andyay
ovelay ebay otnay ethay amesay ingthay atyay ottombay. Eachyay, inyay itsyay utmostyay evelopmentday,
upposessay ayay ighhay egreeday ofyay intimacyyay andyay eart-knowledgehay; eachyay endersray
oneyay individualyay ependentday orfay ethay oodfay ofyay ishay affectionsyay andyay iritualspay
ifelay uponyay anotheryay; eachyay eaveslay ethay assionatepay overlay, oryay ethay onay esslay
assionatepay aterhay, orlornfay andyay esolateday ybay ethay ithdrawalway ofyay ishay
ubjectsay. Ilosophicallyphay onsideredcay, ereforethay, ethay otway assionspay eemsay
essentiallyyay ethay amesay, exceptyay atthay oneyay appenshay otay ebay eensay inyay ayay
elestialcay adianceray, andyay ethay otheryay inyay ayay uskyday andyay uridlay owglay. Inyay ethay
iritualspay orldway, ethay oldyay ysicianphay andyay ethay inister—mutualmay ictimsvay asyay
eythay avehay een—maybay, unawaresyay, avehay oundfay eirthay earthlyyay ockstay ofyay
atredhay andyay antipathyyay ansmutedtray intoyay oldengay ovelay.

Eavinglay isthay iscussionday apartyay, eway avehay ayay attermay ofyay usinessbay otay
ommunicatecay otay ethay eaderray. Atyay oldyay Ogerray Illingworth’schay eceaseday,
ich(whay ooktay aceplay ithinway ethay yearyay,) andyay ybay ishay astlay illway andyay
estamenttay, ofyay ichwhay Overnorgay Ellinghambay andyay ethay Everendray Mray. Ilsonway
ereway executorsyay, ehay equeathedbay ayay eryvay onsiderablecay amountyay ofyay opertypray,
othbay erehay andyay inyay Englandyay, otay ittlelay Earlpay, ethay aughterday ofyay Esterhay
Ynnepray.

Osay Earl—thepay elf-child,—theyay emonday offspringyay, asyay omesay eoplepay, upyay otay
atthay epochyay, ersistedpay inyay onsideringcay er,—becamehay ethay ichestray eiresshay
ofyay erhay ayday, inyay ethay Ewnay Orldway. Otnay improbablyyay, isthay ircumstancecay
oughtwray ayay eryvay aterialmay angechay inyay ethay ublicpay estimationyay; andyay, adhay ethay
othermay andyay ildchay emainedray erehay, ittlelay Earlpay, atyay ayay arriageablemay eriodpay
ofyay ifelay, ightmay avehay ingledmay erhay ildway oodblay ithway ethay ineagelay ofyay ethay
evoutestday Uritanpay amongyay emthay allyay. Utbay, inyay onay onglay imetay afteryay ethay
ysician’sphay eathday, ethay earerway ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay isappearedday, andyay
Earlpay alongyay ithway erhay. Orfay anymay yearsyay, oughthay ayay aguevay eportray ouldway ownay
andyay enthay indfay itsyay ayway acrossyay ethay ea,—likesay ayay apelessshay iecepay ofyay
ift-wooddray osttay ashoreyay, ithway ethay initialsyay ofyay ayay amenay uponyay it,—yetyay onay
idingstay ofyay emthay unquestionablyyay authenticyay ereway eceivedray. Ethay orystay ofyay
ethay arletscay etterlay ewgray intoyay ayay egendlay. Itsyay ellspay, oweverhay, asway illstay
otentpay, andyay eptkay ethay affoldscay awfulyay erewhay ethay oorpay inistermay adhay iedday,
andyay ikewiselay ethay ottagecay ybay ethay ea-shoresay, erewhay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay
eltdway. Earnay isthay atterlay otspay, oneyay afternoonyay, omesay ildrenchay ereway atyay
ayplay, enwhay eythay eheldbay ayay alltay omanway, inyay ayay aygray oberay, approachyay ethay
ottage-doorcay. Inyay allyay osethay yearsyay ityay adhay evernay onceyay eenbay openedyay; utbay
eitheryay eshay unlockedyay ityay, oryay ethay ecayingday oodway andyay ironyay yieldedyay otay erhay
andhay, oryay eshay idedglay adow-likeshay oughthray esethay impediments,—andyay, atyay
allyay eventsyay, entway inyay.

Onyay ethay esholdthray eshay aused,—turnedpay artlypay ound,—forray, erchancepay,
ethay ideayay ofyay enteringyay allyay aloneyay, andyay allyay osay angedchay, ethay omehay ofyay osay
intenseyay ayay ormerfay ifelay, asway oremay earydray andyay esolateday anthay evenyay eshay
ouldcay earbay. Utbay erhay esitationhay asway onlyyay orfay anyay instantyay, oughthay onglay
enoughyay otay isplayday ayay arletscay etterlay onyay erhay eastbray.

illustration[ay: Ester’shay Eturnray]

Andyay Esterhay Ynnepray adhay eturnedray, andyay akentay upyay erhay ong-forsakenlay ameshay!
Utbay erewhay asway ittlelay Earlpay? Ifyay illstay aliveyay, eshay ustmay ownay avehay eenbay inyay
ethay ushflay andyay oomblay ofyay earlyyay omanhoodway. Onenay ew—norknay everyay earnedlay,
ithway ethay ulnessfay ofyay erfectpay ertainty—whethercay ethay elf-childyay adhay onegay
usthay untimelyyay otay ayay aidenmay avegray; oryay etherwhay erhay ildway, ichray aturenay adhay
eenbay oftenedsay andyay ubduedsay, andyay ademay apablecay ofyay ayay oman’sway entlegay
appinesshay. Utbay, oughthray ethay emainderray ofyay Ester’shay ifelay, erethay ereway
indicationsyay atthay ethay ecluseray ofyay ethay arletscay etterlay asway ethay objectyay ofyay
ovelay andyay interestyay ithway omesay inhabitantyay ofyay anotheryay andlay. Etterslay amecay,
ithway armorialyay ealssay uponyay emthay, oughthay ofyay earingsbay unknownyay otay Englishyay
eraldryhay. Inyay ethay ottagecay erethay ereway articlesyay ofyay omfortcay andyay uxurylay
uchsay asyay Esterhay evernay aredcay otay useyay, utbay ichwhay onlyyay ealthway ouldcay avehay
urchasedpay, andyay affectionyay avehay imaginedyay orfay erhay. Erethay ereway iflestray,
ootay, ittlelay ornamentsyay, eautifulbay okenstay ofyay ayay ontinualcay emembranceray,
atthay ustmay avehay eenbay oughtwray ybay elicateday ingersfay, atyay ethay impulseyay ofyay ayay
ondfay earthay. Andyay, onceyay, Esterhay asway eensay embroideringyay ayay aby-garmentbay,
ithway uchsay ayay avishlay ichnessray ofyay oldengay ancyfay asyay ouldway avehay aisedray ayay
ublicpay umulttay, adhay anyyay infantyay, usthay apparelledyay, eenbay ownshay otay ouryay
ober-huedsay ommunitycay.

Inyay inefay, ethay ossipsgay ofyay atthay ayday elieved,—andbay Mray. Urveyorsay Uepay, owhay
ademay investigationsyay ayay enturycay aterlay, elieved,—andbay oneyay ofyay ishay ecentray
uccessorssay inyay officeyay, oreovermay, aithfullyfay elieves,—thatbay Earlpay asway
otnay onlyyay aliveyay, utbay arriedmay, andyay appyhay, andyay indfulmay ofyay erhay othermay, andyay
atthay eshay ouldway ostmay oyfullyjay avehay entertainedyay atthay adsay andyay onelylay
othermay atyay erhay iresidefay.

Utbay erethay asway ayay oremay ealray ifelay orfay Esterhay Ynnepray erehay, inyay Ewnay Englandyay,
anthay inyay atthay unknownyay egionray erewhay Earlpay adhay oundfay ayay omehay. Erehay adhay
eenbay erhay insay; erehay, erhay orrowsay; andyay erehay asway yetyay otay ebay erhay enitencepay.
Eshay adhay eturnedray, ereforethay, andyay esumed,—ofray erhay ownyay eefray illway, orfay
otnay ethay erneststay agistratemay ofyay atthay ironyay eriodpay ouldway avehay imposedyay
it,—resumedyay ethay ymbolsay ofyay ichwhay eway avehay elatedray osay arkday ayay aletay. Evernay
afterwardsyay idday ityay uitqay erhay osombay. Utbay, inyay ethay apselay ofyay ethay oilsometay,
oughtfulthay, andyay elf-devotedsay yearsyay atthay ademay upyay Ester’shay ifelay, ethay
arletscay etterlay easedcay otay ebay ayay igmastay ichwhay attractedyay ethay orld’sway ornscay
andyay itternessbay, andyay ecamebay ayay ypetay ofyay omethingsay otay ebay orrowedsay overyay,
andyay ookedlay uponyay ithway aweyay, yetyay ithway everenceray ootay. Andyay, asyay Esterhay
Ynnepray adhay onay elfishsay endsyay, ornay ivedlay inyay anyyay easuremay orfay erhay ownyay
ofitpray andyay enjoymentyay, eoplepay oughtbray allyay eirthay orrowssay andyay
erplexitiespay, andyay esoughtbay erhay ounselcay, asyay oneyay owhay adhay erselfhay onegay
oughthray ayay ightymay oubletray. Omenway, oremay especially,—inyay ethay ontinuallycay
ecurringray ialstray ofyay oundedway, astedway, ongedwray, isplacedmay, oryay erringyay andyay
infulsay assion,—orpay ithway ethay earydray urdenbay ofyay ayay earthay unyieldedyay,
ecausebay unvaluedyay andyay unsought,—cameyay otay Ester’shay ottagecay, emandingday
ywhay eythay ereway osay etchedwray, andyay atwhay ethay emedyray! Esterhay omfortedcay andyay
ounselledcay emthay asyay estbay eshay ightmay. Eshay assuredyay emthay, ootay, ofyay erhay irmfay
eliefbay, atthay, atyay omesay ighterbray eriodpay, enwhay ethay orldway ouldshay avehay
owngray iperay orfay ityay, inyay Eaven’shay ownyay imetay, ayay ewnay uthtray ouldway ebay
evealedray, inyay orderyay otay establishyay ethay olewhay elationray etweenbay anmay andyay
omanway onyay ayay urersay oundgray ofyay utualmay appinesshay. Earlieryay inyay ifelay, Esterhay
adhay ainlyvay imaginedyay atthay eshay erselfhay ightmay ebay ethay estinedday ophetesspray,
utbay adhay onglay incesay ecognizedray ethay impossibilityyay atthay anyyay issionmay ofyay
ivineday andyay ysteriousmay uthtray ouldshay ebay onfidedcay otay ayay omanway ainedstay ithway
insay, owedbay ownday ithway ameshay, oryay evenyay urdenedbay ithway ayay ife-longlay orrowsay.
Ethay angelyay andyay apostleyay ofyay ethay omingcay evelationray ustmay ebay ayay omanway,
indeedyay, utbay oftylay, urepay, andyay eautifulbay; andyay iseway, oreovermay, otnay
oughthray uskyday iefgray, utbay ethay etherealyay ediummay ofyay oyjay; andyay owingshay owhay
acredsay ovelay ouldshay akemay usyay appyhay, ybay ethay uesttray esttay ofyay ayay ifelay
uccessfulsay otay uchsay anyay endyay!

Osay aidsay Esterhay Ynnepray, andyay ancedglay erhay adsay eyesyay ownwardday atyay ethay
arletscay etterlay. Andyay, afteryay anymay, anymay yearsyay, ayay ewnay avegray asway elvedday,
earnay anyay oldyay andyay unkensay oneyay, inyay atthay urial-groundbay esidebay ichwhay Ing’skay
Apelchay ashay incesay eenbay uiltbay. Ityay asway earnay atthay oldyay andyay unkensay avegray,
yetyay ithway ayay acespay etweenbay, asyay ifyay ethay ustday ofyay ethay otway eepersslay adhay onay
ightray otay inglemay. Yetyay oneyay ombstonetay ervedsay orfay othbay. Allyay aroundyay, erethay
ereway onumentsmay arvedcay ithway armorialyay earingsbay; andyay onyay isthay implesay abslay
ofyay ate—asslay ethay uriouscay investigatoryay aymay illstay iscernday, andyay erplexpay
imselfhay ithway ethay urport—therepay appearedyay ethay emblancesay ofyay anyay engravedyay
escutcheonyay. Ityay orebay ayay eviceday, ayay erald’shay ordingway ofyay ichwhay ightmay ervesay
orfay ayay ottomay andyay iefbray escriptionday ofyay ouryay ownay oncludedcay egendlay; osay
ombresay isyay ityay, andyay elievedray onlyyay ybay oneyay ever-glowingyay ointpay ofyay ightlay
oomierglay anthay ethay adowshay:—

               on“ay Ayay Ieldfay, Ablesay, Ethay Etterlay Ayay, Ulesgay.”
